dakṣādakṣabhujairdevīṃ vibhrāṇāṃ bhogibhūṣaṇāṃ |  
śavāsanāṃ sarpabhūṣāṃ kartrī vāpi kapālakaṃ ||  
  
vaṣakaṃ ca triśūlaṃ ca dadhatīṃ ca catuḥkaraiḥ |  
muṇḍamālāṃ dharā tryakṣāṃ nīlavārāhikāṃ bhajet ||  
  
padmāsanasthāmaruṇāmaruṇāṃvaradhāriṇīṃ |  
kuṃkumakṣeda liptāṃgīṃ protphulla kamalekṣaṇā ||  
  
maṃdasmitamukhī jeṣṭhāṃ sudhā pūrṇa navaṃghaṭaṃ |  
dhanapūrṇaṃ sṛṇīpāśaṃ dadhatīṃ bhujapallavai ||  
  
vālārkamaṇḍalābhāsāṃ trinetrā ca caturbhujāṃ |  
pāśāṃkuśa dhanuścāpaṃ suṃdarīṃ kālikāṃ bhajet ||  
  
p. 64a)  
  
iyaṃ devī mayā pūrvaṃ lalitā vaśya kāmyayā |  
upāsitā tadā japtā lalitā lalitā vaśā ||  
  
trayastriṃśat koṭi deva nāyikā lalitā tu yā ||  
  
khageṃdrinna * ndu śivaṃ pravadamṛtarasā plāvi cāṃgo trinetrā savyapāno   
kapāle galadasṛjamatho muktakeśā pivaṃtīṃ |  
vaddha kāṃcī * * * * maṇimayamukuṭodyaidyatā dīpta jihvā   
pāpānnīlotpalābhāravi śaśi vilasat kuṇḍalīlīḍhapādā ||   
  
caturbhujā kṛṣṇavarṇā muṇḍamālā vibhūṣitāṃ |  
khaḍgaśca dakṣiṇapārśvo vibhratīṃdrāvaradvayaṃ ||  
  
kartṛśca karparaṃ caiva kramā vāmena vibhratīṃ |  
maunikhaṃtī jaṭāmekī vibhratāṃ śirasā dvayaṃ ||  
  
muṇḍamālā parāṃ śīrṣe grīvāyāṃmapi cāparāṃ |  
vakṣasā nāgahāraśca vibhratīṃ raktalocanāṃ ||  
  
kṛṣṇavastradharī kaṭyāṃ vyāghrājina samanvitāṃ |  
vāmā pādaṃ śavahṛdi saṃsthāpya dakṣiṇaṃ padaṃ ||  
  
vilāpya siṃhapṛṣṭhe tu lelihānāṃ śavasvayaṃ |  
sāṭṭahāsa mahāghora rāvayukta subhīṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
mahāmegha prabhādevīṃ kṛṣṇavastra vidhāyinīṃ |  
lalajihvāṃ ghoradaṃṣṭrāṃ koṭarākṣī hasanmukhīṃ ||  
  
nāgahāranatopetāṃ caṃdrārddhakṛtaśekharāṃ |  
dyolikhaṃtī jaṭāmekāṃ lelihānāṃ śavatyayaṃ ||  
  
p. 64b)  
  
nāgayajñopavītāṃgaṃ nāgaśayyāniṣedutīṃ |  
paṃcāsanmuṃḍasaṃyuktaṃ naramālāmahodarīṃ ||  
  
sahasrahanamaṃyukta manaṃtaṃ śirasopari |  
caturdikṣu nāgaphaṇāveṣṭitāṃ guhyakālikāṃ ||  
  
takṣaka sarparājena vāmakaṃkaṇabhūṣitaṃ |  
anaṃtanāgarājena kṛta dakṣiṇakaṃkaṇaṃ ||  
  
nāgena rasanābhāra kalpitaṃ ratnanūpurāṃ |  
dvibhujāṃ ciṃtaye devīṃ nāgayajñopavītinīṃ ||  
  
naradeha samālabdhaṃ kuṃḍalaṃ śrutimaṃḍitaṃ |  
prasannavadanāṃ saumyāṃ navaratna vibhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
nāradādyai munigaṇaiḥ sevitāṃ śivagehiṇīṃ |  
aṭṭahāsāṃ mahābhīmāṃ sādhakābhīṣṭadāyinīṃ ||  
  
karālavadanāṃ ghorāṃ muktakeśī caturbhujāṃ |  
kālikāṃ dakṣiṇā divyāṃ muṃḍamālā vibhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
sadyacchinnaśiraḥ khaḍge vāmordhvādhaḥ kalāṃvujāṃ |  
abhayaṃ varadaṃ caiva dakṣiṇāddhorddhapāṇikāṃ ||  
  
mahāmeghaprabhāṃ śyāmāṃ tathā caiva digaṃvarīṃ |  
kaṃṭhe ca savamuṃḍālī galabhūṣiracarcitāṃ ||  
  
karṇāvanaṃ śavānītaṃ śavayugmabhayānakaṃ |  
ghoradaṃṣṭrā karālāsyāṃ pīnonnatapayodharāṃ ||  
  
gavānāṃkarasaṃghātaiḥ kṛta kāṃcī hasanmukhī |  
sṛkva dvaṃdva galadrakta dhārā visphuritānanā ||  
  
daṃturāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ vyāpi muktaraṃvitacorcayaṃ |  
śavarūpa mahādeva hṛdayoparisaṃsthitāṃ ||  
  
p. 65a)  
  
śivābhighorarāvābhiścaturdikṣu samanvitaṃ |  
sukhaprasannavadanāṃ smerānana saroruhāṃ ||  
  
evaṃ saṃciṃtayed devī śmaśānālayavāsinīṃ ||  
  
aṃbhodaḥ syāmalāṃgīmati vikaṭadatīṃ lolajihvā jaṭālī vāme muṃḍaṃ   
dadhānāṃ karakamalatale dakṣiṇe caṃdrahāsāṃ ||   
sṛkvadvaṃdāsradhārādvayadharavadane pretadorvallikāṃciṃ mādhvīkonmatta   
netrāṃ śavahṛdaya gatāṃ naumi kālīkarālīṃ ||  
  
asya maṃtrādikaṃ nyāsaḥ siddhamaṃtrasya vidyate |  
kṛṣṇatoyena saṃpūrṇe ghṛta vā homa kālikāṃ ||  
  
brāhmyādibhiśca dūtībhi yuktāṃ saṃpūjya bhaktitaḥ |  
aṣṭamī caṃḍikā stotra devīṃ dhyāyed gṛhe punaḥ ||  
  
paṃcavaktrāṃ mahāraudrīṃ prativaktraṃ trilocanaṃ |  
śaktiśūladhanurvāṇa kheṭakhaḍgavarābhayāt ||  
  
dakṣadakṣabhujairdevīṃ vibhrāṇāṃ bhogibhūṣaṇāṃ |  
varṇalakṣaṃ japenmaṃtraṃ vāmācāreṇa sādhakaḥ ||  
  
picumardasya samidho ghṛtāktā juhuyāt tataḥ |  
yadvā prajvalite vahnau tarpaṇādi tataḥścaret ||  
  
evaṃ siddhimaturmaṃtrī mārayedarirādripun |  
vinīta citi kāṣṭhāgnau aṣṭottarasahasrakaṃ ||  
  
saṃdhyāyāṃ homayet sapta dravyaṃ sapta dināvadhi |  
avaśyaṃ jāyate mṛtyuravevaddhāpuṣopi ca ||  
  
śmaśānakīkasaṃgrehe dhūmraṃ bhūtthaṃ viṣaṃ tathā |  
  
p. 65b)  
  
vibhītakaṃ rājikāṃ ca lājāsyā dravya saptakaṃ ||  
  
dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi sthitvā homayed dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade dvādaśaḥ paṭalaḥ || 12 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi maṃtrayaṃtrasya nirṇayaṃ |  
yasya vijñānamātreṇa vārāhī suprasīdati ||  
  
vakṣyāmi siddhametasyāt sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ |  
subhaktāya suśiṣyāya deyaṃ nānyatra kutracit ||  
  
tāramāyāramā kāma vīja pūrvaṃ tu nāmakaṃ |  
viprādyaiśca caturthyaṃtaṃ namoṃtaṃ prajapediti ||  
  
vṛddhāddhi prāṅgrāhyametadeka dātaṃ ca toṣayet |  
siddhoyaṃ maṃtra * 'diṣṭo gopyāmātaṭināravat ||  
  
na guruṃ nādimaṃ nāṃtaṃ na madhyapīṭhabhedikaṃ |  
kevalaṃ yadi labhyeta tadādyaṃ tu surādhipe ||  
  
dvīpākṣaraṃ tathā vālaṃ tithinakṣatrasaṃyutaṃ |  
sādhakādyakṣarairyuktaṃ maṃtrametat sudurlabhaṃ ||  
  
vālāśca ghaṭikāścaiva dina nityā tataḥ paraṃ |  
varṣamāsayugaścāpi parivṛttiriti kramāt ||  
  
a e ca taya iti sūtreṇa ghaṭikā parigaṇpate ||  
  
prakāsaśca virmasaśca ānaṃdo jñāna eva ca |  
satyapūrṇa svabhāvaśya patibhasubhagastathā ||  
  
navavārāni kathyaṃte pārāyaṇa parāyaṇā |  
tatvādi divasā caiva divasā parigaṇpate ||  
  
p. 66a)  
  
citrādi kāmeśvaryāṃ taṃ kāmeśvaryādi citratā |  
anuromaviromābhyāṃ divasāmiti kathyate ||  
  
trikoṇaṃ caiva ṣaṭkoṇaṃ na ca yoni punalikhet |  
vṛttaṃ cāṣṭadalaṃ caiva dvādaśādalameva ca ||  
  
ṣoḍaśālaṃ likhet paścā bhūpulaṃ ca punarlikhet |  
triśūlaṃ ca caturdikṣu catudvari susobhanaṃ ||  
  
suṃdarī kālikāyaṃtraṃ vārāhī ca prakīrtitā |  
tāramuktvā vajra nakha daṃṣṭrāye ca mahātataḥ ||  
  
siṃhāya huṃ phaṭ hṛcce maṃtraḥ saptadaśākṣaraḥ |  
tāraṃ ciṭi dvayaṃ paścāccaṃḍāli tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
mahat padādyāṃtāṃ vrūyādamukaṃ me padaṃ tataḥ |  
vaśamānaya ṭhadvaṃdvaṃ caturviṃśākṣaro manuḥ ||  
  
tāro namo bhagavate varāhādrupamuccaret |  
ṅeṃtaṃ vyāhṛtayaḥ proktā pataye padamuccaret ||  
  
bhūpatitvaṃ madehīti dāpayāṃtegni gehinī |  
trayastriṃśadvarṇakoyaṃ vārāhaḥ kathito manuḥ ||  
  
oṃ pārthive ca pṛthivītalacāriṇi vā pumā |  
tatolini ca tāruṇyaṃ kuru yugmaṃ cadhaṃ cadhaṃ ||  
  
svāhikona triṃśadarṇaḥ pārthivāyā manuḥ smṛtaḥ |  
aikaṃ kālī mahākālī kelikālābhyamuccaret ||  
  
svāhāṃta tithi varṇoyaṃ lakṣamasya japomataḥ |  
śuklāṃvarā śivā yasyā raktakaṃcuka dhāriṇī ||  
  
p. 66b)  
  
citrakaṃṭhī citranāda svaraṃ dehi yugaṃ tathā |  
bhī& rī& svāheti maṃtroyaṃ maṃtrārṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
oṃ hrī& namaśca vārāhi ghore svapnaṃ visarga yuk |  
ṭhadvayaṃ vahnijāyāṃto maṃtraḥ paṃcadaśākṣaraḥ ||  
  
tatorcaye nṛkapālaṃ japenmaṃtra catuṣṭayaṃ |  
kāli kapālāya namo hrī& hrī& pūrva * kaṃ vadet ||  
  
ekādaśākṣaro maṃtro'nena pūjādikā matā |  
strīṃ strīṃ strū tāriṇī tyuktvā kapālāya namoṃtikaḥ ||  
  
dvādaśārṇonena bhavet kapālārddhā dvitīyakā |  
hā& hrī& hū& procya nīlāka kapālāya nama ityayaṃ ||  
  
ekādaśārṇonenoktā kapālārcā tṛtīyakā |  
māyā strī& hū& svargakapālāya sarvāpadaṃ vadet ||  
  
tato rāya * sarvāya tathā sarvodbhavāya ca |  
sarvaśuddhamayāyeti sarvāsurarudhīti ca ||  
  
rācāruṇāya ca śubhrāya surābhājanāyeti ca |  
devī kapālāya namaścaturtho maṃtra īritaḥ ||  
  
ṣaṭpaṃcāśatkavarṇoyaṃ kapālasya tu pūjane |  
tatastasmin kapāle tu pūjayedarkamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
oṃ sūryamaṃḍalāyeti namoṃtoyaṃ navākṣaraḥ |  
sūryamaṇḍalapūjāyāṃ nṛkapāle manurmataḥ ||  
  
mūlamaṃtraṃ paṭhaṃ stasmin sudhā buddhyā surāṃ kṣipet |  
gaṃdhapuṣpākṣatā kṣiptvā trikhaṃḍākhyāṃ pradarśayet ||  
  
p. 67a)  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi tārakasya varāya tu |  
brāhmaṇopāsitāṃ tārāṃ dvādaśārṇāṃ sudurlabhāṃ ||  
  
vācaṃ lajjāṃ ramāṃ kāmaṃ haṃsarājai pratyayakāriṇaṃ |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahākālī mahāmanuṃ ||  
  
oṃ kṣre& kṣre& kre& ataḥ kreṃca paśuṃ gṛhāṇa coccaret |  
hū& phaṭ svāhā śakravarṇaṃ siddhamaṃtra udāhṛtaḥ ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi saptavarṇaṃ ramāmanuṃ |  
ai& hrīṃ śrīṃ rājyalati padamuktvā svayaṃbhuvaḥ ||  
  
hrīṃ jyeṣṭhāyai namaḥ proktvā maṃtra saptadaśākṣaraḥ |  
atha vakṣye mahāvidyāḥ kālikāyāḥ sudurlabhaḥ ||  
  
yāsāṃ vijñānamātreṇa jīvanmukto bhavennaraḥ |  
nātrarcitā viśuddhi syānnārimitrādi lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
navaprayāsa vāhulyaṃ samayā samayādikaṃ |  
na cittavyaṃ ya vāhulyaṃ kāyakleśakaraṃ sadā ||  
  
ya evaṃ ciṃtaye maṃtraṃ sarvakāryasamṛddhidāṃ |  
asya haste padevāsti sarvasiddhirna saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
gadyapadyamayī vāṇī sabhāyāṃ tasya jāyate |  
tasya darśana mātreṇa vādinonoḥ prabhāṃ gataḥ ||  
  
rājānopi ca rāsatva bhajaṃte piṃpare janā |  
divārātriṣṭhayaścaiva vaśīkartuṃ kṣamo bhavet ||  
  
aṃteṣa bhajate devyā gaṇatvaṃ durlabhaṃ naraḥ |  
kāmatrayaṃ vahni saṃsthaurati viṃdusamanviti ||  
  
kūrcayugmaṃ tathā lajjā yugalaṃ tadanaṃtare |  
  
p. 67b)  
  
dakṣiṇe kālike ceti dūrvavījāni coddharet ||  
  
aṃte vahni vadhūdadyā vidyā śakti prakīrtitāḥ |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi dakṣiṇā kālikā śubhaṃ ||  
  
kāmakṣaraṃ vahni saṃsthaṃ vāmanetra vibhūṣitaṃ |  
viṃdumetatsamāyuktaṃ vījametat trayaṃ likhet ||  
  
kūrcadvayaṃ tathā devi lajjā yogamanaṃtaraṃ |  
dakṣiṇe kālikāṃ ceti saṃvodhana padānvite ||  
  
sa savījaṃ puna prāha svāhāṃtamaṃtramuddharet |  
kevalaṃ mātṛkāṃ kṛtvā mātṛkāṃ tārasaṃpuṭāṃ ||  
  
mātṛkā puṭitaṃ tāraṃ nyaset sādhakasattamaḥ |  
śrīvījapuṭitānātu mātṛkāṃ puṭitaṃ tu yat ||  
  
kāmerapuṭitāṃ devī śaktiṃ ca tatpuṭāṃ nyaset |  
hrī& dvaṃdva punanyastvā ṛ ṝ ḷ ḹśca pūrvavat ||  
  
mūlena puṭitāṃ devī tatpuṭaṃ meva ca |  
anuloma vilomena nyastvā maṃtraṃ yathāvidhi ||  
  
mūle nyaṣṭa śataṃ kuryāt vyāpaka tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
iti guhyena durgāyā aṃgaṣoḍhā prakīrtitā ||  
  
tārāyā kālikāyāśca unmukhāśca tathā parā |  
etasminyāsa mātreṇa sarvapāpaṃ praṇaśyati ||  
  
mūlavidyāṃ trimaṃtreṇa praṇavādyairyathāvidhi |  
ātmavidyā śive caivastatvaṃ nyāsaṃ samācaret ||  
  
brahmaraṃdhre bhruvormadhye lalāṭe nābhideśake |  
guhye cakre ca sarvāṃgai saptavījaṃ kramān nyaset ||  
  
p. 68a)  
  
ādau yaṃtraṃ pravakṣyāmi yat jñātvā maratāṃ vrajet |  
ādau trikoṇaṃ vinyasya trikoṇaṃ tadvahi nyaset ||  
  
tato vai vilikhenmaṃtrī trikoṇa trayamuttamaṃ |  
vṛttaṃ vilikhya vidhivallikhet padmaṃ sulakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
pīṭhapūjāṃ tataḥ paścādādhāraśakti pūrvakaṃ |  
prakṛtiṃ kamaruṃścaiva śeṣaṃ pṛthvī tathaiva ca ||  
  
sudhāṃvudhimaṇidvīpaṃ ciṃtāmaṇi gṛhaṃ tathā |  
śmaśānaṃ pārijātaṃ ca tanmūlaṃ ratnavedikā ||  
  
tasyoparī maṇeḥ pīṭhaṃ nyaset sādhakasattamaḥ |  
caturdikṣu munīn devān śivāśca śavamuṇḍakān ||  
  
deveśi bhakti surabhe parivāra samanvitaṃ |  
yāvastvāṃ pūjayiṣyāmi tāvastvaṃ susthirā bhava ||  
  
gurupradṛṣṭamaṃtreṇa upacārāṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
oṃ jaya dhvani maṃtramātaḥ svāhā ghaṃṭāvādana pūjayet |  
devyāstu dakṣiṇe bhāge mahākāraṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
hū& kṣā& yā& vā& lā& ā& kro& mahākāra bhairava sa vighnānnāśaye 2   
hrī& śrī& phaṭ svāhā ||   
  
mahākālaṃ yajedyatnāṃ paścād devī prapūjayet |  
visṛjya parayā bhaktyā sannidhā yena mudrayā ||  
  
hṛdaye devi muddhāsya tanmayo bhavati dhruvaṃ |  
sarvasiddhi svarau bhūmau bhairavāvatsarād bhavet ||  
  
lakṣamekaṃ japed vidyā haviṣyāśī divā śuciḥ |  
rātrau tāṃvūlapuṃgāsya śayyāyāṃ lakṣamānavaḥ ||  
  
p. 68b)  
  
krameṇa lakṣayaṃ japtvā tad daśāṃśena maṃtravit |  
ayutaṃ homayed devi divārātri vibhedataḥ ||  
  
divālakṣa śucirbhūtvā haviṣyāśī japennaraḥ |  
tatastu taddaśāṃśena homayeddhaviṣā priye ||  
  
lakṣamekaṃ japen maṃtraṃ haviṣyāśī divāśuciḥ |  
aśuciśca tathā rātrau lakṣamekaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
daśāṃśaṃ homayen maṃtrī tarpayedabhiṣecayet |  
lakṣamekaṃ japed vidyāṃ haviṣyāśī divāśuciḥ ||  
  
rātrau tāṃvūla purāsyaḥ śayyāyī lakṣamāṇavaḥ |  
evaṃ lakṣadvayaṃ japtvā taddaśāṃśena maṃtravit ||  
  
aśvatthaṃ homayed devi divārātri vibhedataḥ |  
gate prathamayāme ca tṛtīyapaharāvadhi ||  
  
niśāyāṃ ca prajaptavyaṃ rātriśeṣaṃ japennaraḥ |  
vargādyaṃ vahnimadhyasthaṃ rativiṃdu samanvitaṃ ||  
  
ekākṣaro mahāmaṃtraḥ sarvakāma phalapradaḥ |  
triguṇaṃ tu viśeṣeṇa sarvaśāstra pravodhikā ||  
  
khadīrgha ṣaṭyutādyena praṇavādya na kalpayet |  
ṣaḍaṃgāni manorasya yāti yuktena deśikaḥ ||  
  
māyā dvayaṃ kūrcayugaṃ aiṃdrāṃtaṃ mādana trayaṃ |  
māyā dvayaṃścara yute dakṣiṇe kālike padaṃ ||  
  
saṃhāra kramayogena vījaṃ saptakamuddharet |  
ekaviṃśat paromaṃtrasmārādyaḥ kālikā manuḥ ||  
  
p. 69a)  
  
svāhāṃtaśca trayoviṃśakṣaroyaṃ maṃtrarājakaḥ |  
viṃśatparṇā mahāvidyā svāhā praṇavavarjita ||  
  
dhyāna pūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ dakṣiṇāvasamācaret |  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya kullukāvījamuddharet ||  
  
rativīja samuddhṛtya prapaṃcamasamanvitaṃ |  
ṭhadvayena samāyukto vidyārājñī prakīrtitā ||  
  
maṃtrasya bhairava ṛṣi virācchaṃdaḥ prakīrtitā |  
siddhikālī brahmarūpā viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
jape viṃśati sāhasraṃ saharaikena saṃyutaṃ |  
homaye taddaśāṃśena mṛtarūpeṇa maṃtravit ||  
  
mūlavījaṃ tato māyāṃ lajjāvījaṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
mahāvidyā kālyā mahākālena bhāṣitā ||  
  
vargādyaṃ vahnisaṃyukta ratiṃ viṃdu samanvitaṃ |  
etat trayaṃ vahnijāyā mūlatrayaṃ ca vahniyā ||  
  
nijavījaṃ pūrvavījaṃ lajjā ca vahni vallabhā |  
vāgbhavaṃ ca tato mūlaṃ kālikā vahni vallabhā ||  
  
asya maṃtrasya vā devi dakṣiṇāmūrti kīrtitaḥ |  
paṃkti chaṃda samākhyātā kālikā devatā smṛtāḥ ||  
  
lakṣmī dvayaṃ kūrca lajjā dakṣiṇe kālike ca phaṭ |  
mūlavījaṃ dvayaṃ lajjā pūrvavat vahni vallabhā ||  
  
nijavījaṃ kūrca lajjā dakṣiṇe kālike dvayaṃ |  
mūlavījaṃ kūrcavījaṃ nijavījaṃ vahni vallabhā ||  
  
nijavījaṃ dvayaṃ kūrca lajjā vā vahni vallabhā |  
mūlavījaṃ kūrca lajjā vahnijāyā ca suṃdarī ||  
  
p. 69b)  
  
mūlavījaṃ dakṣiṇā ca kālike vahni vallabhā |  
hṛdayaṃ vāgbhavaṃ mūlaṃ kālikāyai ca ṭhadvayaṃ ||  
  
vahnijāyāṃ tato maṃtra kālikāyā prakīrtitaḥ |  
atha paṃcakṣarī vidyā śṛṇuṣveka malānane ||  
  
prajāpatiṃ samuddhṛtya vargārūḍhaṃ tataḥ priye |  
caturthasvarasaṃyuktaṃ sarvataṃtrasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
vījatrayaṃ krameṇaiva tadaṃte vahnisuṃdarī |  
paṃcakṣaro mahāvidyā kathitā padma yoninā ||  
  
ṣaḍakṣarī mahākālī vakṣyāmi śṛṇu pārvatī |  
vījatrayaṃ krameṇaiva puna vījatrayaṃ sudhīḥ ||  
  
svāhāṃtā kathitā vidyā caturvarga phalapradā |  
ekādaśākṣarī vidyā kathyate śṛṇu pārvati ||  
  
vāgbhavaṃ hṛdayaṃ paścāt brahmārūḍhaṃ prajāpatiṃ |  
caturthasvarasaṃyuktaṃ nādaviṃduvibhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
dviguṇaṃ ca tataḥ kṛtvā ṅeṃtaśca kālikā padaṃ |  
svāhāṃtā kathitā vidyā priye ekādaśākṣarī ||  
  
ṛṣiḥ syād dakṣiṇāmūrti chaṃdaḥ paktirudāhṛdaṃ |  
parāt paratarā śaktiḥ kālikā devatā smṛtā ||  
  
ekādaśākṣarī vidyā kālikāyāḥ sudurlabhā |  
lakṣadva * ca ye vidyā puraścaraṇa karmaṇi ||  
  
anyāsāṃ varṇalakṣaṃ tu kathitā padmayoninā |  
mūlavījaṃ tato māyā lajjāvījaṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
dakṣiṇe kālike ceti astrāṃtā samudāhṛtā |  
athāparaṃ pravakṣyāmi vidyāviṃśati varṇakāṃ ||  
  
p. 70a)  
  
yasyā prasādamātreṇa bhave bhūmi puraṃdaraḥ |  
mūlavījaṃ dvayaṃ vrūyā tataḥ kūrca dvayaṃ vadet ||  
  
lajjā dvayaṃ samuddhṛtya saṃvodhyaṃta pada dvayaṃ |  
pūrvavat ṣatadhā vījaṃ nyaṃte ca vahnisuṃdariṃ ||  
  
ṛṣisyā dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ paṃkti chaṃdarudāhṛtaṃ |  
devatā kathitā sadbhiḥ kāli dakṣiṇa pūrvikā ||  
  
athāparaṃ pravakṣyāmi vidyā tribhuvaneśvarī |  
nijavījaṃ samuddhṛtya tadaṃte vahni suṃdarī ||  
  
ṛṣiṃsyā dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ paṃktiḥ chaṃda samanvitaṃ |  
aṣṭākṣarī mayā proktā sarvataṃtreṣu gopitā ||  
  
nijavījaṃ dvayaṃ kūrca dvayaṃ lajjā dvayaṃ tataḥ |  
svāhāṃtā kathitā kālī sarvakarma phalapradā ||  
  
nijavījaṃ tathā lajjā tadaṃte tava suṃdarī |  
paṃcākṣarī mahāvidyā paṃcavaktra ṛṣiḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
navākṣarī mahāvidyā śṛṇuṣva kamalānane |  
nijavīja trayaṃ kūrca yugaṃ lajjā yugaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
svāhāṃtā kathitā vidyā sarvasampatkarīmatā |  
athāparīn pravakṣyāmi vidyātāṃ ca navākṣarīṃ ||  
  
mūlavījaṃ samuddhṛtya saṃvudhyaṃtaṃ pada dvayaṃ |  
svāhāṃtā kathitā vidyā sarvaśatrukṣayaṃkarī ||  
  
atha cāṣṭākṣarī vidyā śṛṇuṣva kamalānane |  
nijavījaṃ tataḥ kūrcaṃ tato māyāṃ samuddharet ||  
  
p. 70b)  
  
punastāni samuccārya svāhāṃtā mokṣadāyinī |  
athāparāṃ pravakṣyāmi daśatatva samanvitāṃ ||  
  
mūladvayaṃ kūrcayuga tathā lajjā dvayaṃ tataḥ |  
punastāni samuccārya svāhāṃtā mokṣadāyinī ||  
  
athāparāṃ pravakṣyāmi daśatatva samanvitāṃ |  
mūla dvayaṃ kūrca yugaṃ tathā lajjā dvayaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
punastānyeva vījāni tadaṃte vahni suṃdarī |  
caturdaśākṣarī vidyā caturvarga phalapradā ||  
  
brahmā trayaṃ samuddhṛ * rati vahni samanvitaṃ |  
nādaviṃdusamāyuktaṃ lajjā kūrca dvayaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
punaḥ krameṇa coddhṛtya vahnijāyā vadhirmanuḥ |  
ṣoḍaśīyaṃ samāyuktaṃ lajjā kūrcaṃ dvayaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
punaḥ krameṇa coddhṛtya vahnijāyāvadhirmanuḥ |  
ṣoḍaśīya samākhyātā vidyā kalpadrumopamā ||  
  
hṛdayaṃ vāgbhavaṃ devi nijavījayugaṃ tataḥ |  
kālikāyai padaṃ proktā tadaṃte vahnisuṃdarī ||  
  
namaḥ pāśāṃkuśau dvedhā phaṭ svāhā kālikālike |  
dīrghatatvachadaṃ kālī manupaṃcadaśākṣaraḥ ||  
  
etāsā pūjanaṃ caiva dakṣiṇāvatsureśvari |  
atha vakṣye maheśāni vidyāṃ sarvaphalapradāṃ ||  
  
caturvargapradaṃ sākṣān mahāpātakanāśinīṃ |  
sarvasiddhipradā nityaṃ bhuktimuktipradāyinīṃ ||  
  
guhyakālīṃ mahāvidyā trailokya cāti durlabhā |  
kālī ca dakṣiṇā caiva guhyakāli tathaiva ca ||  
  
p. 71a)  
  
triśrīnāmapi vidyānāsādyaiva nāmata smṛtāḥ |  
iṃdrādirūḍhaṃ vargādyaṃ rativiṃdu samanvitaṃ ||  
  
triguṇaṃ ca tataḥ kṛtvā īkāraṃ ca samuddharet |  
ṣaṣṭhesvarasamāyuktaṃ nādaviṃdu vibhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
tadguhya kālikā proktā cātha vā dakṣiṇe vadet |  
saptavījaṃ tataḥ pūrva krameṇa yojayet tataḥ ||  
  
vahnijāyāvadhiḥ proktā vidyā trailokya mohanī |  
kāmavījaṃ tathā kūrca tadaṃte bhuvaneśvarīṃ ||  
  
guhyaṃ ca kālike cāpi tathā vīja dvayaṃ bhavet |  
svāhāṃtā kathitā vidyā sarvataṃtreṣu gopitā ||  
  
eṣā tu ṣoḍaśī proktā caturvarga phalapradā |  
saptavījaṃ purā proktaṃ guhya ca kālike punaḥ ||  
  
svāhāṃtā kathitā vidyā sarvataṃtreṣu gopitā |  
asyā nāmādikaṃ tyaktvāt tadā paṃcadaśākṣarī ||  
  
kāmavījaṃ parityajya athavā ṣoḍaśākṣarī |  
kāmavījasamuddhṛtya saṃvudhyaṃtaṃ pada dvayaṃ ||  
  
punakāmaṃ tadaṃte ca dadyād vahneśca suṃdarīṃ |  
eṣā navākṣarī vidyā guhya kālyā samanvitā ||  
  
dakṣiṇe padamābhāṣya bhave viyaṃ samuddharet |  
vāmākṣi vahni saṃyuktaṃ nādaviṃdu viṃbhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
tadguhya kālikā proktā cātha vā dakṣiṇe vadet |  
saptavījaṃ tataḥ pūrva krameṇa yojayet tataḥ ||  
  
vahnijāyāvadhiḥ proktā vidyā trailokyamohinī |  
kāmavījaṃ tathā kūrca tadaṃte bhuvaneśvarīṃ ||  
  
p. 71b)  
  
guhya ca kālike cāpi tathā vīja dvayaṃ bhavet |  
svāhāṃtā kathitā vidyā sarvataṃtreṣu gopitā ||  
  
eṣā tu ṣoḍaśī proktā caturvarga phalapradā |  
saptavījaṃ purāproktaṃ guhye ca kālike punaḥ ||  
  
svāhāṃtā kathitā vidyā sarvataṃtreṣu gopitāḥ |  
asyā nāmādikaṃ tyaktvāt tadā paṃcadaśākṣarī ||  
  
kāmavījaṃ parityajya athavā ṣoḍaśākṣarī |  
kāmavījasamuddhṛtya saṃvudhyaṃtaṃ pada dvayaṃ ||  
  
punakāmaṃ tadaṃte ca dadyād vahneśca suṃdarīṃ |  
eṣā navākṣarī vidyā guhyakālyā samanvitā ||  
  
dakṣiṇe padamābhāṣya bhave vidyā daśākṣarī |  
pūrvavatmāsavargaṃ tu pūrvavat pūjayecchivāṃ ||  
  
pūrvavacca japed vidyāṃ sarvaṃ pūrvavadeva hi |  
validānaṃ tathā maṃtrī pūrvavat parikalpayet ||  
  
bhadrakālyādayo maṃtra kathyaṃte śṛṇu suṃdarī |  
kāmavījādikaṃ vījaṃ sarvapūrvā pare yajet ||  
  
bhadrakālī tathā ṅeṃtāṃ vījamadhye niyojayet |  
svāhāṃtā kathiā vidyā viṃśadvarṇātmikā pare ||  
  
caturvarga prada vidyā bhadrakālī śubhānane |  
saptavījaṃ samuddhṛtya śmaśāna kālikā tathā ||  
  
punavījaṃ krameṇaiva svāhāṃtā sarvasiddhidā |  
viṃśatyekādhikā vidyā śmaśāna kālikā matā ||  
  
vījāni coccaret pūrve mahākalī padaṃ tataḥ |  
tadaṃte saptavījāni svāhāṃtā sarvasiddhidā ||  
  
p. 72a)  
  
viṃśatparṇā mahāvidyā mahākālyāḥ prakīrtitā |  
bhūpure lokapālāḥ syustadastrāṇi ca tadvahiḥ ||  
  
bhūpureṣu caturdikṣu pūjayet kramataḥ sudhīḥ |  
viṣṇuṃ śivaṃ tathā sūryaṃ gaṇeśaṃ pūjaye tataḥ ||  
  
trikoṇaṃ caiva ṣaṭkoṇaṃ navakoṇa manoharaṃ |  
trivṛttaṃ sāṣṭapatraṃ ca sukijjalka samanvitaṃ ||  
  
bhūpura tritayārūḍhaṃ yonimaṃḍalamaṃḍitaṃ |  
tripaṃcāramidaṃ pīṭhaṃ sarvataṃtrasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
valimaṃtraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ ||  
  
ehyehi jaganmātajaganmātāṃjjagatāṃ janani gṛhna 2 mama vali siddhiṃ dehi dehi   
śatrukṣayaṃ kuru 2 hū& 2 hrī& 2 hū& phaṭ oṃ kālikāyai namaḥ phaṭ svāhā ||   
ehi 2 guhyakālyai gṛhna 2 mama śatrun nāśaya 2 khādaya 2 turu 2 sphuru 2 siddhi   
dehi hu& phaṭ svāhā || oṃ hū& sadāśiva mahāpretāya guhyakālyāya namaḥ   
guhyakālyai namaḥ || mālāmaṃtraṃ pravakṣyāmi vārāhyā sarvasiddhayaḥ || hrī&   
śrī& ai& glau& ai& namo bhagavati vārtāri 2 vārāhamukhī 2 aṃdhe aṃdhinī   
namaḥ ruṃdhe ruṃdhinī namaḥ jaṃbhe jaṃbhinī namaḥ || mohe mohinī namaḥ   
staṃbhe staṃbhinī namaḥ || sarvaduṣṭa praduṣṭānāṃ sarveṣāṃ   
sarvavākcittacakṣunmukhāgati jihvāṃ staṃbhaṃ kuru 2 ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ   
hū& phaṭ svāhā vārāhī ratneśvarī svāhā ||  
  
p. 72b)  
  
iti te kathitā devyā maṃtrayaṃtra prakāśakaṃ |  
yasya vijñānamātreṇa vārāhī suprasīdati ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade trayodaśaḥ paṭalaḥ || 13 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
caṇḍī pāṭhaphalaṃ devī śṛṇuṣva gadato mama |  
ekāvṛttyādi pāṭhānāṃ yathāvat kathayāmi te ||  
  
saṃkalpa pūrvasaṃpūjyatyāsāṃgeṣu manun sakṛt |  
paraṃ vali pradānaṃ vā phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ||  
  
upasargau daśāvṛtyā trirāvṛttaṃ paṭhed vudhaḥ |  
grahadoṣa prakartavyaṃ paṃcāvṛttaṃ varānane ||  
  
mahābhayasamutpanna saptāvṛttaṃ paṭhet sudhīḥ |  
navāvṛtyā paṭhecchāṃti vājapeya phalaṃ labhet ||  
  
rājavaśyā ca bhūtyai ca rudravṛttamudīritaṃ |  
arkavṛttyā kāmasiddhi vairahāniśca jāyate ||  
  
manvo vṛttādi pūrvaśyāstathā strīvaśyatā bhavet |  
mokṣapaṃcadaśāvṛtyā śriya prāpnoti mānavaḥ ||  
  
karā vṛtyā putrapautra dhanadhānyāgamaṃ viduḥ |  
rājñābhīvivimokṣāya vairasyoccāṭanāya ca ||  
  
kuryāt saptadaśāvṛtyā yathā dvādaśakaṃ priye |  
mahāvraṇa vimokṣāya triṃśāvṛtta paṭhet sudhīḥ ||  
  
paṃcāviṃśāvartanāṃ tu bhavavaṃdhavimokṣaṇaṃ |  
saṃkaṭe samune prāpte ducikitsā mayestathā ||  
  
p. 73a)  
  
jātidhvaṃse kurocchede āyurānnāśanāgame |  
cauravṛddhau vyādhi vṛddhau dhananāśo prajākṣaya ||  
  
tathaiva trividhotpāte pāpeti pātake tathā |  
kuryād yatnācchatā vṛttaṃ tataḥ saṃpadyate śubhaṃ ||  
  
naśyaṃti vipadastasya aṃte yāṃti parāṃgatiṃ |  
śriyo vṛddhicchatā vṛtyād rājyavṛddhistathā parā ||  
  
manasā ciṃtitaṃ devi siddhyadaṣṭottaraṃchatā |  
śatāśvamedha yajñānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti suvrate ||  
  
sahasrāvartakaṃ lakṣmīrāviśoti svayaṃ sthiraḥ |  
muktvā manorathān kāmān bhogamokṣamavāpnuyāt ||  
  
yathāśvamedha kraturāt devānāṃ ca yathā hari |  
stavānāmapi sarveṣāṃ tathā saptaśatistava ||  
  
athavā vahunoktena kimetena varānane |  
caṃḍyāśatāvṛtti pāṭhāt sarvaṃ siddhyaṃtita priye ||  
  
ādhāre sthāpayitvā tu pustakaṃ prajapet sphuṭaṃ |  
hastasaṃsthāpanād devī ityaddhaṃ phalasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
jāvanna pūjyate dhyāya tāvanna ciramet paṭhet |  
atha kramaṃ paṭhed devī śiraḥ kaṃpādikaṃ tyajet ||  
  
patipramādadādhyāya vināso bhavati priya |  
punadhyāya samārabhya punaḥ sarvatato vidhī ||  
  
nātaḥ parataraṃ stotra kiṃcidasti varānane |  
bhuktimuktīpadaṃ puṇyaṃ pāpanāśaṃ ca pāvanaṃ ||  
  
tadravyajñaśca prathama dṛṣṭadevān praṇamya ca |  
  
p. 73b)  
  
praṇavaṃ ca tato dṛṣṭvā stotraṃ vā saṃhitān japet ||  
  
aṃte ca praṇavaṃ dadyāddhityuvācādi pūrvakaṃ |  
śuddhenācala kīrtena paṭhitavya prayatnataḥ ||  
  
namāna saṃpaṭhet stotraṃ vācikaṃ tu praśasyate |  
pustakaṃ vācane śastraṃ sahasrādvādikaṃ yadi ||  
  
ato nyūnaṃ bhaved yatra vācikaṃ pustakaṃ vinā |  
ādhāre sthāpayitvā tu pustakaṃ prajapet sudhīḥ ||  
  
hastasaṃsthāpanād devi yasmādalpa phalaṃ bhavet |  
na svayaṃ likhitaṃ tacca kṛtinālikhitaṃ bhavet ||  
  
ābrahmaṇe na likhitaṃ tatsarvaṃ viphalaṃ bhavet |  
na svayaṃ ca kṛtaṃ stotramananyapi kṛtena ca ||  
  
yasmāt kaṇau na prasāptaṃ ṛṣibhiḥ likhitaṃ paṭhet |  
ṛṣichaṃdādikaṃ nyasya paṭhet stotra vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
stotreṇa dṛśyate yatra prabhavaṃ tu samācaret |  
bhīṣma parvaṇi yogītaṃ supraśastā kalau matā ||  
  
viṣṇo sahasranāmākhyaṃ stotra pāpapraṇāśanaṃ |  
gajeṃdra mokṣaṇaṃ caiva kāruṇyastavameva ca ||  
  
narasiṃha sahasrakhyaṃ śrīrāma samasaṃjñaka |  
divyāḥ saptaśati stotra tathā nāma sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
tripurāyā prasādākhyaṃ sūryasyastavarājakaṃ |  
pautro rucistato yaśca iṃdrākṣī stotrameva ca ||  
  
vaiṣṇave ca mahālakṣmī stotramiṃdena bhāṣitaṃ |  
bhargavākhya narāmeṇa saptaśatyāni kāraṇā ||  
  
p. 74a)  
  
ityuktvā pārvatinātha sapta satyā mahāphalaṃ |  
tasya śravaṇamātreṇa sarvarogapraśāṃtaya ||  
  
mādhuryamakṣaravyakti padachedastu susvaraḥ |  
dhairyaṃ laghu guruścaiva ṣaḍete pāṭhakā guṇāṃ ||  
  
gītī śīghraṃ śiraḥ kaṃṭhī yathā likhita pāṭhakāṃ |  
anarthajñalpa buddhiśca ṣaḍete pāṭhakādhamā ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi cāmuṇḍāyā mahāmanuḥ |  
navadurgātmakaṃ yasya smaraṇād bhuktimuktayaḥ ||  
  
surathā yatprasādena rājyaṃ prāptya bhaven manuḥ |  
saṃsāravaṃdhanāsāṇi jñānaprāptaṃ samādhinā ||  
  
mārkaṃḍeyapurāṇoktaṃ caritraṃ tritayaṃ tavā |  
japādyasya phalaṃ dadyāt taṃ manuṃ vacmi sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
vāglajjā kāmavījāni cāmuṇḍāyai padaṃ vadet |  
vicce navārṇamaṃtroyaṃ śaktimaṃtrottamottamaḥ ||  
  
brahmāviṣṇu maheśāstu munayosya prakīrtitāḥ |  
gāyatryuṣṇiganuṣṭuṣma chaṃdastra yamudīritī ||  
  
daivyosya * mahākālī mahālakṣmī sarasvatī |  
naṃdāśākaṃbharī bhīmā śaktitrayamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
tisrosya śaktayo durgā bhrāmarī raktadaṃtikā |  
agnivāyu sūryastatvaṃ prāgvadṛṣyādikaṃ nyaset ||  
  
kṛtena yena devasya sāruṣya jātimānavaḥ |  
atha dvitīyaṃ kurvīta nyāsaṃ sārasvatābhidhaṃ ||  
  
vījatrayaṃ tu maṃtrādyaṃ tārādi hṛdayāṃtakaṃ |  
ṣaḍakṣaro bhaven maṃtro navasthāneṣu vinyaset ||  
  
p. 74b)  
  
kaniṣṭhānāmikā madhya tarjanyaṃguṣṭha yugmake |  
karamadhye hastapṛṣṭhe maṇivaṃdhe ca kūrpare ||  
  
hṛdayādi ṣaḍaṃgeṣu jātiyuktaṃ punaḥ nyaset |  
asmin sārasvata nyāse kṛte jāḍyaṃ vinaśyati ||  
  
nyāsaḥ kāryāḥ saptasatyāḥ pāṭhe kāmaviśeṣataḥ |  
tatastṛtīyaṃ kurvīta nyāsaṃ mātṛganādikaṃ ||  
  
māyāvījādikā brāhmī pūrvataḥ pātu māṃ sadā |  
māheśvarī tathāgneyyāṃ kaumārī dakṣiṇeva tu ||  
  
vaiṣṇavī pātu kāṣṭhāyāṃ vārāhī paścimeva tu |  
iṃdrāṇī pāvane koṇe cāmuṃḍācottareva tu ||  
  
aiśāne tu mahālakṣmīrūrddhaṃ vyomeśvarī tathā |  
saptadvīpeśvarī bhūmau rakṣmet kāmeśvarī tale ||  
  
tṛtīyasmin kṛte nyāse trailokya vijayī bhavet |  
nyāsa caturtha kurvīta nandajādi samanvitaṃ ||  
  
nandajāpātu pūrvāṃgaṃ kamalāṃkuśamaṃḍitā |  
khaḍgaṃpātra karā pātu dakṣiṇe raktadaṃtikā ||  
  
pṛṣṭhe śākaṃbharī pātu pṛṣṭhe pallavasaṃyutā |  
dhanurvāṇakarā durgā vāme pātu sadaiva māṃ ||  
  
śiraḥ pātu karā bhīmā mastakācaraṇāvadhi |  
pādādi mastakaṃ yāvavadbhrāmakāṃtikābhṛta ||  
  
turyaṃ nyāsaṃ naraḥ kurvan jalāmṛtyuṃ vyapohati |  
brāhmādyamatha kurvīta nyāsaṃ paṃcakamuttamaṃ ||  
  
p. 75a)  
  
pādādi nābhi paryaṃtaṃ brahmā pātu sanātanaḥ |  
nābhe viśuddhi paryaṃta pātu nityaṃ janārdanaḥ ||  
  
viśuddhe brahmaraṃdhrāṃtaṃ pātu rudrastrilocana |  
haṃsapātu pada dvaṃdvaṃ vainayeyaḥ karadvayaṃ ||  
  
cakṣuṣī vṛṣabhaḥ pātu sarvāṃgāni gajānanaḥ |  
pārāparau dehabhāgau yānvānaṃdamayo hariḥ ||  
  
kṛtesmin paṃcame nyāse sarvān kāmānavāpnuyāt |  
ṣaṣṭhaṃ nyāsaṃ tata kuryāt mahālakṣmyādi saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
madhya pātu mahālakṣmīraṣṭādaśabhujānvitā |  
ūrdhvaṃ sarasvatī pātu bhujairaṣṭābhiruṃjitā ||  
  
adhaḥpātu mahākālī daśavāhu samanvitā |  
siṃho hasta dvaye pātuḥ parahaṃsokṣi yugmakam ||  
  
mahiṣādi samārūḍho yamaḥ pātu pada dvayaṃ |  
mahiṣaścaṇḍikā yuktaḥ sarvāṃgāni maheśvari ||  
  
ṣaṣṭhesmin vihite nyāse sadgati prāpnuyānnaraḥ |  
mūlākṣare nyāsarūpaṃ tataḥ kurvīta saptamaṃ ||  
  
brahmaraṃdhre netrayuge śrutyornāsikayo mukhe |  
pāyau mūlamano varṇān tārādyānnamayo yutān ||  
  
vinyaset saptame nyāse kṛtvā tenokṣayo bhavet |  
pādayo brahmaraṃdhrāṃtaṃ punastāneva vinyaset ||  
  
yet tasminnaṣṭa medinyāḥ sarve duḥkhaṃ vinaśyati |  
kuvīta navamaṃ nyāsaṃ maṃtraṃ vyāpti svarūpakaṃ ||  
  
mastakārcaraṇaṃ yāvaccaraṇān mastakāvadhi |  
puro dakṣe pṛṣṭha deśe vāmabhāgeṣṭaśonyaset ||  
  
p. 75b)  
  
mūlamaṃtrakṛte nyāso navamo devatāpti kṛt |  
tataḥ kurvīta daśame ṣaḍaṃganyāsamuttamaṃ ||  
  
mūlamaṃtraṃ jātiyuktaṃ hṛdayādiṣu vinyaset |  
kṛtesmin daśame nyāse trailokyaṃ vaśamānayet ||  
  
caṇḍipāṭhepi kartavyā nyāsāḥ sveṣṭa pradāyakāḥ |  
dadyānnyāsokta phaladaṃ kuryādekādaśaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
khaḍginī śūlinītyādi paṭhitvā ślokapaṃcakaṃ |  
ādyaṃ kṛṣṇataraṃ vījaṃ dhyātvā sarvāṃgakaṃ nyaset ||  
  
śūlena pāhino devīṃ tyādi śloka catuṣṭayaṃ |  
paṭhitvā sūrya sadṛśaṃ dvitīyaṃ pṛṣṭhatāṃ nyaset ||  
  
tataḥ ṣaḍaṃga kurvīta vibhaktai mūlavarṇakaiḥ |  
ekenaikena caikena caturbhiyugmakena ca ||  
  
samaste naiva maṃtreṇa kuryādaṃgāni ṣaṭkramāt |  
śikhāyāṃ netrayoḥ śrutyo nāso vaktre gude nyaset ||  
  
maṃtravarṇo samastena vyāpakaṃ śreṣṭakaṃścaret ||  
tato devī tato dhyāyet kālikā dhyānamucyate ||  
  
daśāsyāṃdaśapādā ca daśahastāṃ vidhistutāṃ |  
indranīladyutiṃ khaḍgaṃ cakraṃ śaṃkhaṃ śiraḥ śarān ||  
  
dakṣahasteṣu dadhatīṃ gadāṃ śūlaṃ tu tuṃḍikāṃ |  
parighāṃśca dhanurvāṇaṃ dadhatīṃ brahmasaṃstutāṃ ||  
  
madhukaiṭabhanāśārthaṃ sālaṃkārāṃtrivīkṣaṇāṃ |  
tato dhyāyen mahālakṣmīṃ mahiṣāsuramardinī ||  
  
p. 76a)  
  
samastadevatā tejo jātī padmāsanasthitāṃ |  
aṣṭādaśabhujāmakṣamālāpadmaṃ ca sāyakaṃ ||  
  
khaḍgaṃ vajraṃ gadāṃ cakraṃ dakṣahaste kamaṃḍaluṃ |  
śaṃkhaṃ ca dadhatī vāme śaktiṃ ca paraśuṃ dhanuḥ ||  
  
carmadaṃḍo surāpātraṃ ghaṃṭāpāśaṃ triśūlakaṃ |  
sarasvatīṃ tato dhyāyeccharaścaṃdra samaprabhāṃ ||  
  
śaṃkhaṃ ca muśalaṃ cakre vāṇoṃ dakṣeṣu vibhratīṃ |  
ghaṃṭhāṃ śūlaṃ halaṃ cāpaṃ vāmahasteṣu vibhratīṃ ||  
  
gaurīdeha samudbhūtāṃ nṛṇāmānaṃdadāyinīṃ |  
ādhārabhūtāṃ jagataḥ śubhādika vimardinīṃ ||  
  
adhiṣṭhātrīṃ tṛtīyasya tricaritra smaret sadā |  
evaṃ dhyātvā japellakṣa catuṣkaṃ taddaśāṃśataḥ ||  
  
pāyasānnena juhuyāt pūjite hemaratnabhiḥ |  
jayādi śaktibhiryukte pīṭhe devī samarcayet ||  
  
etan maṃtrya nivṛttasya ṣaṭkoṇāṣṭa dalānvitaḥ |  
śriyā ca nai-ṛte viṣṇu vāyavye bhūmayā śivaṃ ||  
  
viḍārayaṃtaṃ mahiṣa prokkoṇe mṛgapaṃ yajet |  
ṣaṭkoṇeṣu ca pūrvādau naṃdayā raktadaṃtikāṃ ||  
  
śākaṃbharī tathā durgāṃ bhīmāṃ ca bhrāmarīṃ yajet |  
tārasvavīja pūrvāśca ṅentā hṛdayasaṃyutāḥ ||  
  
sarvāśāmeva śaktīnāṃ nāmamaṃtrājaye matāḥ |  
tataścāṣṭadale brāhmī māheśiṃ ca kumārikāṃ ||  
  
vaiṣṇavīṃ caiva vārāhīṃ nārasiṃhīṃ sureṃdrajāṃ |  
cāmuṃḍāmatha tadvāhye paṃcaviṃśaddale jayet ||  
  
p. 76b)  
  
viṣṇumāyāṃ cetanāṃ ca vuddhiṃ nidrāṃ kṣudhāṃ tathā |  
chāyāśaktiṃ parāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ kṣāṃtiṃ jātiṃ taduttalaṃ ||  
  
lajjāṃ śāṃtiṃ tathā śraddhāṃ kīrtilakṣmīṃ dhṛtiṃ tathā |  
vṛttiṃ śrutiṃ smṛtiṃ cāpi dayāṃ tuṣṭiṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
puṣṭiṃ ca mātaraṃ bhrāṃtimarcayed bhūpureṣu ca |  
catuḥkoṇeṣu gaṇapaṃ kṣetreśaṃ vaṭukaṃ tathā ||  
  
yoginīśca sureśāṃdyāṃstadvāhya cāyudhāni ca |  
mārkaṇḍeya purāṇoktaṃ nityaṃ caṃḍīstavaṃ paṭhet ||  
  
puṭitaṃ mūlamaṃtreṇa japennāpnoti vāṃchitaṃ |  
kalau na caṇḍī sadṛśī siddhidā bhuvane traye ||  
  
vāmadakṣiṇamārgabhyāmadhikāri phalapradā |  
tatrādimaṃ caritraṃ ca roganāśāya yojayet ||  
  
upasvarga vināśāya madhyamaṃ yojayed vudhaḥ |  
aṃtyaviṣayakāmastu caritraṃ paraśīlayet ||  
  
caritra dvaya śīlasya navaṃśaḥ chidyate kvacit |  
paṭhe dadyāt tricaritraṃ tu vipattistasya naśyati ||  
  
anādyaṃ paṭhate yastu mārayedacirādripūn |  
sārdhanusvāri padmaṃ ca saptasatyāsta yojayet ||  
  
yastanmaṃtraiśapuṭitaṃ praśākaṃśya ca saṃkhyayā |  
paṭheccaṃḍīṃ tathādyaṃte sakāmastasya siddhyati ||  
  
svaśatruṃ daitya bhāvena svamitrāṃ devatādhiyā |  
bhāvayen yojayeccaṇḍīṃ trisaṃdhyaṃ māsamātrakaṃ ||  
  
p. 77a)  
  
mṛtā vā mṛtakalpo vā śatravaḥ syūna saṃśayaḥ |  
sitapakṣātimārabhya cāṣṭasyaṃtamiyasa ca ||  
  
japellakṣaṃ manu homaṃ khādyaistrimadhuraplutaiḥ |  
pratyahaṃ pūjayed devī caṇḍīmādyaṃtaye paṭhet ||  
  
viprān guruṃ samārādhya vāṃchitaṃ labhate drutaṃ |  
saptaṃ satyāścaritre tu prathame padmabhū muniḥ ||  
  
chaṃdo gāyatramuditaṃ mahākālī tu devatā |  
vāgvījaṃ pāvakastatvaṃ dharmārthe viniyojanaṃ ||  
  
prayogānāṃ tu naiveti māraṇe mohanena tu |  
madhyamasya caritrasya munirviṣṇurudāhṛtaḥ ||  
  
uṣṇik chaṃdo mahālakṣmīddevatā vījamadrijā |  
vāyustatvaṃ dhanaprāptyai viniyoga hṛtaḥ ||  
  
uccāṭastaṃbhaṃne cātra prayogānāṃ śatadvayaṃ |  
uttarasya caritrasya muniḥ śaṃkara ucyate ||  
  
mahāsarasvatī devī triṣṭup chaṃda udāhṛtaṃ |  
kāmavījaṃ ravistatvaṃ kāmāptyai viniyojanaṃ ||  
  
vidveṣa vaśya yogaśca prayogādi kṛtairmitāḥ |  
evaṃ saptaśati cātra prayogāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||  
  
tasmāt saptaśatītyetra proktaṃ vyāsena dhīmatā |  
mahāvidyetyādi sapta satyaḥ kalpe tathā dine ||  
  
brahmeṃdra guruśakrāṇāṃ viṣṇu rudrasuradviṣāṃ |  
upāsya devatājātāstāṃścātra brahmaṇāstutāḥ ||  
  
tasmāt saptasatītyaiva vyāsena parikīrtitā |  
saumyāni yāni rūpāṇī yatrāpi parikīrtitāḥ ||  
  
p. 77b)  
  
upāsyā dakṣiṇe mārge lakṣmyādyāḥ saptaśaktayaḥ |  
lakṣmī ca lalitā kālī durgā gāyatryaruṃdhatī ||  
  
sarasvatī ceti sapta upāsyā vāmamārgataḥ |  
kālītārā chinnamastā sumukhī bhuvaneśvarī ||  
  
vālā kubjeti navamaḥ sucitānna prakīrtitāḥ |  
nāmnā saptasatī ceti madhyame carite dvidhā ||  
  
tattanmaṃtrokta saṃketairmaṃtravyaktiḥ prajāyate |  
evaṃ stavābhiyuktā nāmityārabhya tṛtīyake ||  
  
carite saptasabhyastu cāmuṃḍāṃtāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
haṃsayukta vimānāgre ityārabhya prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
brahmāṇyādyāḥ saptasatyo vartamānāstu tatra ca |  
vaivasvateṃtare prāpte ityārabhya ca sapta tu ||  
  
satyaproktāḥ svayaṃ devyā tasmāt saptasatī matā |  
saptasatyāstu sakalaṃ tatvāṃ brahmāhameva hi ||  
  
prādonaṃ śrīharidvarti koṭyaṃśamitare janāḥ |  
yathā maṃtrāsu siddhyarthaṃ yojyate kriyate nyathā ||  
  
vījādikaṃ tathā sadbhiḥ kāmanā vaśataḥ kvacit |  
varṇāṇā ca tadānāṃ ca vyaktāmastu prapaṃcitaḥ ||  
  
śabdaśāstra virūḍhoyaḥ pāṭhe sau'śubhakarmaṇiḥ |  
śabdaśāstra viruddhastu pāṭhaśāṃtika pauṣṭike ||  
  
p. 78a)  
  
sārthe sa tu paṭheccaṃḍī stavaṃ sveṣṭapadākṣaraṃ |  
samāptau tu mahālakṣmīṃ dhyātvā kṛtvā ṣaḍaṃgakaṃ ||  
  
japedaṣṭa śataṃ mūlaṃ devatāyai nivedayet |  
evaṃ yaḥ kurute saitranāvasīdati jātucit ||  
  
śatacaṃḍī vidhānaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi priye nṛṇāṃ |  
nṛpopadrava āpanne durbhikṣe bhūmikaṃpane ||  
  
ativṛṣṭyāmatī vṛṣṭau paracakra bhaye kṣaye |  
sarvavighnā vinaśyaṃti śatacaṃḍī vidhau kṛte ||  
  
rogāṇāṃ vairināśāya dhanaputra samṛddhaye |  
śaṃkarasya bhavānyā vā prāsāda nikaṭe śubhaṃ ||  
  
maṇḍapaṃ dvāravedyādyaṃ kuryāt sa dhvajatoraṇaṃ |  
tatra kuṃḍaṃ prakurvīta pratīcyāṃ madhyatopi ca ||  
  
snātvā ca nikṛtiṃ kṛtvā yojayed deśa vāḍavān |  
jiteṃdriyān sadācārān kulinān satyavādinaḥ ||  
  
vyutpannāṃścaṇḍikā pāṭhe ratān lajjā dayāvataḥ |  
madhuparka vidhānena vastra svarṇādi dānataḥ ||  
  
japārtha cāsanaṃ mālāṃ dadyāt tebhyopi bhojanaṃ |  
te haviṣyānnamaśnaṃto maṃtrārtha gatamānasāḥ ||  
  
bhūmau śayanāḥ pratyekaṃ japesaścaṃḍikāstavaṃ |  
mārkaṇḍeya purāṇoktaṃ daśakṛtyaḥ sa cetasaḥ ||  
  
navarṇe caṃḍikā taṃtraṃ japeyuścāyutaṃ pṛthak |  
yajamānaṃ pūjaye ca kaṃnyānāṃ daśakaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
dvivarṣādyāṃ daśābdāṃtāḥ kumārīṃ paripūjayet |  
nādhikāṃgī na hināṃgī kuṣṭinīṃ ca vraṇāṃkitāṃ ||  
  
p. 78b)  
  
aṃdhakānāṃ kekalāṃ ca kurūpāṃ rogayuktanuṃ |  
dāsīnāṃ bhogayuktāṃ ca duṣṭāṃ kanyāṃ na pūjayet ||  
  
viprā sarveṣṭa sa siddhyai yaśame kṣetriyodbhavāṃ |  
vaiśyajāṃ dhanalābhāya putrāptau śūdrajāṃ yajet ||  
  
dvivarṣā sā kumāryuktā trimūrtihāyanatrikā |  
caturābdā tu kalyānīṃ paṃcavarṣā tu rohiṇī ||  
  
ṣaḍābdā kālikā proktā caṃḍikā saptahāyanā |  
aṣṭavarṣāḥ śāṃbhavī syā durgā tu navahāyanā ||  
  
subhadrā daśavarṣoktā tā maṃtraiḥ paripūjayet |  
ekābdāyāḥ prītyabhāvau rudrābdā tu vivarjitā ||  
  
tāsāmāvāhane maṃtraḥ ślokarūpo nigadyate |  
maṃtrākṣaramayīṃ lakṣmīṃ mātṛṇāṃ rūpadhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
navadurgātmikā sākṣāt kanyāmāvāhayāmyahaṃ |  
kumārikādi kanyānāṃ pūjāmaṃtrān vruve'dhunā ||  
  
jagatpūjya jagadvaṃdye sarvaśakti svarūpiṇī |  
pūjāṃ gṛhāna kaumāri jaganmātre namostute ||  
  
tripurā tripurādhārāḥ trivajñāna svarūpiṇīṃ |  
trailokyavaṃditān devīṃ trimūrtiṃ pūjayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
kalātmikāṃ kalātītāṃ karuṇya hṛdayā śivāṃ |  
kalyāṇajananīṃ nityāṃ kalyāṇīṃ pūjayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
kāmacārīṃ śubhāṃ kāṃtāṃ kālacakra svarūpiṇīṃ |  
kāmadāṃ karuṇodārāṃ kālikāṃ pūjayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
p. 79a)  
  
caṇḍivījāṃ caṇḍimayīṃ caṃḍamuṃḍa prabhaṃjinīṃ |  
pūjayāmi sadā devī caṃḍikāṃ caṇḍavikramāṃ ||  
  
sadānandakarīṃ śāṃtāṃ sarvadeva namaskṛtāṃ |  
sarvabhūtātmikāṃ lakṣmīṃ śāṃbhavīṃ pūjayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
durgame duṣṭare kārye bhava duḥkha vināśinīṃ |  
pūjayāmi sadā bhaktyā durgādurgatināśinīṃ ||  
  
suṃdarīṃ svarṇavarṇābhāṃ sukhasaubhāgyadāyinīṃ |  
subhadrā jananī devī subhadrāṃ pūjayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
etaimaṃtrai lakṣanāḍhyāṃ tāṃ tāṃ kanyāṃ samarcayet |  
mahāmāyāyai vidmahe caṇḍikāyai dhīmahi tanno devī pracodayāt ||  
  
gaṃdhaiḥ puṣpairakṣya bhojyai vastrairābhaṇairapi |  
vedyā viracite ramya sarvato bhadramaṇḍape ||  
  
ghaṭasaṃsthāpya vidhivat tatrāvāhyārcayecchivāṃ |  
tadagre kanyakāścāpi bhojayed brāhmaṇānapi ||  
  
upacāraiśca vividhaiḥ pūrvoktā varaṇānyapi |  
evaṃ caturdinaṃ kṛtvā paṃcame homamācaret ||  
  
pāyasānnaistrimadhvaktaidrākṣā raṃbhā phalairapi |  
mātuluṃgairikṣu khaṇḍairnārikelaiḥ puraistilaiḥ ||  
  
jātīphalairāmra phalairanyairmadhuravastubhiḥ |  
saptasatyādaśāvṛttyā pratiślokaṃ hutaṃ caret ||  
  
ayutaṃ ca navārṇena sthāpitegnau vidhānataḥ |  
kṛtvā caraṇa devānāṃ homatannātra maṃtrataḥ ||  
  
p. 79b)  
  
kṛtvā pūrṇāhutaṃ samyag devamagniṃ visṛjya ca |  
abhiṣiṃccaya * * ṣṭāraṃ viprauḥ kalaśodakaiḥ ||  
  
niṣkaṃ suvarṇamathavā pratyekaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśet |  
bhojayeccāthavān viprān bhakṣyabhojyaiḥ pṛthag vidhaiḥ ||  
  
tebhyopi dakṣiṇāṃ datvā gṛhnīyādāśikhastataḥ |  
evaṃ kṛte jagadvaśyaṃ sarve naśyaṃtyupadravāḥ ||  
  
rājyaṃ dhanaṃ yaśaḥ putrān iṣṭamanyaṃ labhena ca |  
etad daśaguṇaṃ kuryāccaṃḍī sahasrajaṃvidhi ||  
  
vidyāvaṃtaḥ sadācārān brāhmaṇān vṛṇuyācchataṃ |  
pratyahaṃ caṃḍikā pāṭhān vighnadhvaste daśāmitān ||  
  
ayutaṃ prajape yuddhe pratyekaṃ navavarṇakaṃ |  
pūrvoktaḥ kanyakāḥ maṃtra pūrvamaṃtraiḥ śataṃ śubhā ||  
  
evaṃ daśāhaṃ saṃpādya homaṃ kuryuḥ prayatnataḥ |  
saptasatyāśatā vṛtyā pratiślokaṃ vidhānataḥ ||  
  
lakṣasaṃkhyaṃ navārṇaṃ ca pūrvokte dravyasaṃcayet |  
hotṛbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ datvā pūrvoktān bhojaye dvijān ||  
  
sahasrasaṃmitān sādhun devyārādhana tatparān |  
evaṃ sahasrasaṃkhyāte kṛte caṃḍī vidho nṛṇāṃ ||  
  
siddhyatyahīpsitaṃ sarvaṃ duḥkhaidyaśca vinaśyati |  
mārī durbhagarogādyā naśyaṃti vyasano ca yāḥ ||  
  
nemaṃ vidhiṃ vade duṣṭe khale caure gurudruhi |  
sādho jiteṃdriye dāṃte vadedvidhimimaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
p. 80a)  
  
evaṃ sā caṃḍikā tuṣṭāyastṛn śotṝnyarakṣati ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade caturdaśaḥ paṭalaḥ || 14 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
viprakṣatriyaviṭśūdracāṃḍālādi na bheda ca |  
kaulikeṣu ca karmeṣu siddhimaṃtro garīyasi ||  
  
mahāśūnyaṃ tatpravāhaṃ triśakti parimaṃḍitaṃ |  
tato viṃdu tataścaṃḍra tato yonyaṣṭamaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
tadadho yojayed vidvā yoni kuṇḍāt maheśvari |  
aṣṭāviṃśatimaṃ bhadre nādāt saptama saṃsthitaṃ ||  
  
tadveśma śirasābhinnanati praṇavavarjita |  
piṃḍametanmahābhāge sarvamaṃtrāraṇiṃ paraṃ ||  
  
piṇḍametanmahābhāge sarvamaṃtrāraṇiṃ paraṃ |  
sarvaśānnityakaraṇī sarvasiddhi bhayāvahaṃ ||  
  
bhogyamokṣyapradaṃ sāraṃ devyā piṃḍamanuttamaṃ ||  
  
hskhphre& ||  
  
sāṃtāṃtamādita kṛtvā ṣaṭviṃśaṃ tu samuddharet |  
adhorddhe vahni saṃrūḍhaṃ mūrddhni guhya niyojitaṃ ||  
  
ṣaṣṭhavargaṃtaṃ saṃbhinnaṃ devī ekākṣarā smṛtā ||  
  
kṣrjhrī& ||  
  
oṃ krī& kaṃkālī devī duṣṭamāriṇī mama kāryasādhinī devī hū&phaṭ svāhā ||   
  
kakārāt sarvamutpannaṃ tena sṛṣṭi svarūpiṇīṃ ||  
  
rephaḥ kārāgni rudraśca tena saṃhārarūpiṇī |  
īkāre ca mahālakṣmī lokatraya vibhāvinī ||  
  
teneyaṃ pālikā śaktiḥ sāmarasyaṃ ca viṃdunā |  
evaṃ ca veṣṭirūpeṇa sṛṣṭi sthitilayāmvikā ||  
  
p. 80b)  
  
evaṃ samaṣṭikā rūpe turīya brahmarūpiṇī |  
ciṃdānaṃdamayī sākṣāt vidyāśakti svarūpiṇī ||  
  
śabda brahma svarūpā ca nityānaṃda svarūpiṇī |  
sarvavedamayī sākṣāt nityānaṃda pradāyinī ||  
  
japasādhyāṃ parāśaktirnādamārga niyojitā |  
vāgmaṃdira padārūḍho bhairavī rūpadhṛk pradā ||  
  
tadā smaren mahāvidyāmiti siddhakamadhyagā |  
saptāviṃśati lakṣāṇi japtvā caiva tu siddhati ||  
  
yonirūṣmā tathānaṣkaṃ ṣaṭkoṇaṃ kuṇḍalī kulaṃ |  
māyā nārāyaṇaṃ haṃsa aṣṭadhā vāgbhava smṛta ||  
  
vāgbhavāṣṭaka madhyasthāṃ etadvargavibhedataḥ |  
pūrvavaktraṃ siddhi lakṣmī dakṣiṇaṃ guhyakālikā ||  
  
kālaśaṃkarṣanī vaktraṃmuttaraṃ samudāhṛtaṃ |  
paścimaṃ tu kujā vaktraṃ mūrddhaṃ pratyaṃgirābhidhaṃ ||  
  
dhyānamūrtimidaṃ jñeyaṃ saṃsārārṇavatāraṇaṃ |  
bhuktimukti pradātāraṃ sukhasaubhāgyavarddhanaṃ ||  
  
śmaśānādye mahāghore kṣattratyādhayatetha vā |  
laghvāśī dhyānasaṃyukto kṛṣṇāṃvaravibhūṣitaḥ ||  
  
dhyāyed ghorāṃ mahābhīmāṃ kṛṣṇarakta bhayānakāṃ |  
kṛśāṃgī pretasaṃrūḍhā digvāsāṃ vikṛtānanāṃ ||  
  
pretapreṃścātra saṃrūḍhāṃ śiśukarṇāvalaṃvinī |  
kapālahastāṃ vikṛtāṃ raktapūrṇā savodyatāṃ ||  
  
p. 81a)  
  
sarpābharaṇasaṃyuktāṃ vyālayajñopavītinīṃ ||  
  
aṣṭādaśabhujā raudrā paṃcavaktra tilocanaṃ |  
sarvāyudha dharā raudrī bhukti mukti phalapradā ||  
  
devīṃ pratyaṃgirā nāma sarvāpatti vighātinīṃ |  
oṃ a& ka& ca& tathā ḍha& ta& ya hma& bhā& hrī& samuccaret ||  
  
hū& sa uktvā hū& tathā straṃ svāhāṃtaḥ ṣoḍaśākṣaraḥ |  
munirvidhātācchaṃdoṣṭirdevatāḥ ṣaṭ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
mahāvāyu mahāpṛthvī mahākālastathaiva ca |  
mahāsamudranāmā ca mahāparvata eva ca ||  
  
mahāściśceti hū& vījaṃ hrī& śaktiḥ parikīrtitā |  
lajjāyā tu ṣaḍaṃgāni ṣaḍdīrghānvitayā caret ||  
  
maṃtra devāṃstato maṃtrī dhyāyet susthiramānasaḥ |  
nānāratnaccirākrāṃtaṃ vṛkṣāṃbhaḥ śravaṇairmataṃ ||  
  
vyāghrādi paśubhivyāptaṃ mānayuktaṃgiri smaret |  
matsyakūrmādi vījāḍhyaṃ navaratna samanvitaṃ ||  
  
ghanachayaṃ sa kallolaṃmakūpāraṃ viciṃtayet |  
jvālāvalī samākrāṃtaṃ jagattritayamadbhutaṃ ||  
  
pītavarṇaṃ mahāvahniṃ saṃsmarecchatruśāṃtaye |  
svarāsamuttharekādau malinaṃ ruddhabhūdivaṃ ||  
  
pacanaṃ saṃsmared viśva jīvanaṃ prāṇarūpataḥ |  
nadīparvatavṛkṣādikalitāgrāmasaṃkulā ||  
  
p. 81b)  
  
ādhārabhūtā jagato dhyeyā pṛthvīṃhamaṃtinā |  
sūryādi grahanakṣatra kālacakrasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
nirmalaṃ gaganaṃ dhyāyet prāṇināmāśrayapradaṃ |  
eva ṣaḍdevatāṃ dhyātvā sahasrāṇi tu ṣoḍaśā ||  
  
japen maṃtraṃ daśāṃśena ṣaḍ dravyai homamācaret |  
vrīhayastaṃḍulā ājyaṃ sarṣapāśca javāstilāḥ ||  
  
etai hutvā yathā bhāgaṃ pīṭhe pūrvodite yajet |  
aṃgādilaṃkyā vajrādyairevaṃ siddhā bhaven manuḥ ||  
  
śatrupadravamāyaṃto pūjyāt tatrannaye manuṃ |  
akāraṃ parvatākāraṃ dhāvaṃtaṃ śatrusaṃmukhaṃ ||  
  
pataronmukhamatyugraṃ prācyāṃdiśi viciṃtayet |  
kakāraṃ kṣucca kallolaṃ plāvitākhila bhūtalaṃ ||  
  
samudrarūpiṇaṃ bhīmaṃ praticyāṃdiśi saṃsmaret |  
turīya paṃcamādyaṇau pṛthvāgagaṇarūpiṇau ||  
  
śatruvargaṃ vaṃdhanaubdhiṃ yenniyajetatātmana |  
tadaśrīmaṃ varṇayuga śatro niśvāsapaddhatiṃ ||  
  
nirādhānaṃ smaren maṃtraṃ vidadhadriripumākulaṃ |  
māyādi varṇa tritayaṃ śatro netra śutīmukhaṃ ||  
  
pratyekaṃ tu niruṃdhyānaṃ ciṃtayet sādhakottamaḥ |  
varmasaṃkṣobhitaṃ tvastraṃ riporādhāradeśataḥ ||  
  
utthāpya vahni taddehaṃ pradehan sa manuṃ smaret |  
evaṃ varṇān smaren maṃtraṃ japed varṇa sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
maṃḍalaṃ tritayādarvāddhyārayatyeva vidviṣaṃ |  
evaṃ yaḥ kurute karma prāṇāyāmajayādibhiḥ ||  
  
p. 82a)  
  
evaṃ yaḥ kurute karma prāṇāyāma japādibhiḥ |  
saṃśodhayitvā svātmānaṃ svarakṣādyai hariṃ smaret ||  
  
aptyagnau hṛdaye sūrye sthaṃḍile pratimāsu ca |  
ṣaṭ sveteṣu hareḥ samyagarcanaṃ yogyatocyate ||  
  
āpo hyāya * maṃtasya tasmānnāsu sadā hariḥ |  
āgni kriyāvattāṃ viṣṇuryogināṃ hṛdaye hariḥ ||  
  
paṃḍitānāṃ hariḥ sūrye sthaṃḍile bhāvitātmanāṃ |  
pratimā svalpa buddhīnāṃ ṣaṭprakārāśca yāḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
  
akṛttimāḥ kṛttimāśca acalāśca calācalāḥ |  
nirjīvāśca sa jīvāśca tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇa ||  
  
akṛttrimā ca dvividhā sālagrāmoti pāvanaḥ |  
tadabhāve dvārakāyāścakraṃ tadvacca pāvanaṃ ||  
  
kṛttrimā daśadhā proktoḥ śreṣṭhāstāḥ pūrvapūrvataḥ |  
syād ratnaracitāstvādyā svarṇajā rūpyajāpi ca ||  
  
tāmrajā pittalī jātā sphāṭikī raktaśītajāḥ |  
kāṣṭhajā mṛttikā jātā citrarūpeti ca kramāt ||  
  
acalā kṣatrarūpāstu haridvāraṃ yathā gayā |  
devatābhiḥ kṛtāyāstu mūrtayastāścalācalāḥ ||  
  
jagannātho caikadeśa pāṃḍuraṃgādayastuto |  
sajīva brāhmaṇāgāvo nirjīvā pippalaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
maṃtraṃ nyāsaṃ purā kuryāt svadeha devatā su ca |  
gāyotryoṃkāranyastāṃgaḥ pūjayed viṣṇumavyayaṃ ||  
  
p. 82b)  
  
sarvasiddhipradā devi kāśyāṃ pūjā kṛte sati |  
tatopi dviguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ viṃdhyaparvata mūrddhani ||  
  
gaṃgāgayākurukṣetre prabhāse bhāskare yathā |  
naimikhāraṇyakādau ca viṃdhyaparvata yatphalaṃ ||  
  
tatopi dviguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ puruṣottama sannidhau |  
tataścaturguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ karatoyā nadījale ||  
  
tatopi dviguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ lohitya nadayāthasi |  
tata śataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ kāmākhyā yonimaṇḍale ||  
  
tatopi dviguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ nīlakaṃṭhasya mūrddhani |  
tataḥ koṭiguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ nepāle guhyamaṇḍale ||  
  
puṣpamātra pradānena sumeru sadṛśaṃ phalaṃ |  
jalaviṃdu pradānena saptasāgara yatphalaṃ ||  
  
guhyeśvarī samāpīṭhe nāsti brahmāṇḍa maṇḍale |  
homamudrā trayaṃ proktaṃ mṛgī haṃsī ca śūkarī ||  
  
śūkarīkara saṃkocī mṛgī mudrā kaniṣṭhikā |  
haṃsī syāt tarjanī muktā tridhā mudrā prakīrtitā ||  
  
śāṃtike pauṣṭike caiva māraṇoccāṭane tathā |  
vidveṣa staṃbhane caiva vaśye ca parameśvari ||  
  
śāṃtike ca mṛgī jñeyā haṃsī pauṣṭika karmaṇi |  
abhicāre śūkarī syād vidveṣoccāṭanādiṣu ||  
  
na devāḥ pratigṛhnaṃti mudrāhīnā mathāhutiṃ |  
mudrāhīnaṃ tu yo mohāddhotu micchati maṃdadhī ||  
  
p. 83a)  
  
vaśya śāṃtyoḥ svarṇapātraṃ mṛtpātraṃ staṃbhanena taṃ |  
vidveṣe khādiraṃ pātramuccāṭe loharirmitaṃ ||  
  
māraṇe kukkuṭāṃḍaṃ syāt pātrāṇīmāni tarpaṇe ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
mātardevī mahāmāye vaṃdhamokṣa pravartinī |  
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi gurupaṃkti manuttamaṃ ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
gurukramastu vahudhā maṃtra vistaragauravāt |  
kālānāmapyanāditvaṃ kathaṃ tatkathayāmite ||  
  
ajñātvā kulavargastu naṣṭamārgo bhaviṣyati |  
naṣṭamārge maṃtravidyā na tādṛg phalagocare ||  
  
gurūṇāṃ śiṣyabhūtānāṃ nāsti cetsaṃti kramaḥ |  
yaṃtra taṃtrāśca vidyāyā vihalā nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
viṃśati puruṣān yāpi navasaptastrayopi ca |  
ajñātvā guruvaṃśānāṃ śiṣyetya naṣṭasaṃtati ||  
  
svavaṃśādadhikaṃ jñeyaṃ guruvaṃśa mahādbhutaṃ |  
janakā dadhiko jñeyā maṃtradaśca maheśvara ||  
  
tasmāt sarvatra deveśa saṃkṣepāt śṛṇutān gurun |  
ādau sarvatra deveśa maṃtradaḥ prathamo guruḥ ||  
  
parāpara gurustvaṃ hi parameṣṭhī tvahaṃ tataḥ |  
sarvataṃtresu vidyāsu svayaṃ prakṛti nirūpiṇī ||  
  
p. 83b)  
  
tataḥ puruṣarūpaṃ ca tataḥ svaguru saṃtatiḥ |  
tevaiva hima daṃśāśva madbhaktāśca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
sarvamaṃtreṣu purato sarvatrasiddhidāyakāḥ |  
divyaighā guravo deva siddhaughā guravastathā ||  
  
mānavoghā samāsena kathayāmi tavāgrataḥ |  
tatrāsau kālikā devī tasyāḥ śṛṇu guru kramaṃ ||  
  
mahādevī mahādeva tripurā caiva bhairavaḥ |  
divyaugha guravaḥ proktā siddhaughān kathayāmite ||  
  
brahmānaṃdaśca pūrṇaścaścarataśca sulocana |  
kumāra krodhanaścaiva varadasmaradīpanaḥ ||  
  
māyāmāyāvatī caiva mānavaughān śṛṇu priye |  
vimalaḥ kuśalaścaiva bhīmasenaḥ sudhākaraḥ ||  
  
mīno gorakṣakoścaiva bhojadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ |  
mūladevovaṃti devo vighneśo vai hutāśanaḥ ||  
  
samayānaṃda saṃtoṣā kālikā guravaḥ smṛtāḥ |  
śūnyasya śūnyabhāvena nādarūpa kalāthinī ||  
  
tatrasthā paramā raudrā dharmabhūmistu sā vidu |  
rāvajñārācagārāvyārāvasthārāvadā sadā ||  
  
ravateyā idaṃ viśvamaṃtra bhūmistu sā vidu |  
uccayaṇa arucāryācāroccāra vivarjitā ||  
  
carate sarvanāṃ teṣāmaṃtra bhūmistu sā vidu |  
ko daṃḍe tu caturdaṇḍā daṃḍāta dvaya daṇḍagā ||  
  
varṇaistu samato bhinnā maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
kahīnākādyagāhastākālākālakṣayākulā ||  
  
p. 84a)  
  
kalāte sarvamaṃtrāṇi maṃtrabhūmistu sā vidu |  
vyāpi rūpā arūpasthā rūpātītā niriṃdriyā ||  
  
rūpakaistu śataibhinnā maṃtra bhūmistu sā vidu |  
prathamaṃ pratibhollā sādvavaṃtīccalācalaṃ ||  
  
niḥsvabhāvapadāṃvasthā maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
sphurate yāmadedikkā akṣarākṣaramadhyagā ||  
  
mahāsthāneṇa bhāvitā maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
amanāmānasai bhāvai hīnāmānonatā sadā ||  
  
mananetrāṇadharmitvā maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
kakalā kamalā rūḍhā kākacaṃca puṭiśritā ||  
  
yā kalā kālajananī maṃtra bhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
jhaṭityaṃtaḥ praviṣṭaṃ yā aṣṭakhaṃḍātra śūnyagā ||  
  
vyaṣṭikā tatsvarūpāṃtā maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
roṣāṃ tā sarvadāvānāṃgrāsate lālasā sadā ||  
  
sarvabhāveṣu saṃlīnā maṃtrabhūmistu sā vidu |  
vyāpti bhāvastu sarvasva haṭhāṃtu haragodyatā ||  
  
āśavaṃ paramānaṃdaṃ maṃtrabhūmistu sā vidu |  
aṃtapāniyakākacidṛśyādṛśyaṣuvarjitā ||  
  
sphuraṃti parame vyomni maṃtrabhūmistu sā vidu |  
adhyātma jñānarūpāsyahaśāṃtā paramāvyayā ||  
  
nisthūro acyutāśāṃtā maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
pakṣadvaya vinirmuktā madhyamādā amadhyagā ||  
  
p. 84b)  
  
kalate tatra saṃsthāyā maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
adhomukha nirākākālākālasya bhakṣakī ||  
  
maṃtrātītā amaṃtrajñā maṃtra bhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
amātrā dvidaśāṃ tāṃ tāṃ ṣoḍaśāṃtā punaḥ sadā ||  
  
mātrāhīnāṃ tu yā saṃdhi maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
tatvāstā tatva gahanī tatvā tatva vivarjitā ||  
  
tritatvabhāvatīyā tu maṃtra bhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
yatra nāsti paraṃ jñāna yatra jñānaṃ parāparaṃ ||  
  
yatra garbhātrayodvāma maṃtrabhūmistu sā viduḥ |  
rākākārākuhūrūpā kuhūrākāśa bhakṣakī ||  
  
parabhāva manuprītā maṃtra bhūmistu sā vidu |  
aṃta sūkṣma vahiḥ śūkṣmā carate yā carācare ||  
  
arūpā sarvadā rūpā maṃtra bhūmistu sā vidu |  
yo vā krameṇa tītāyā parārūpe khareśvari ||  
  
sarvamaṃtraraṇīyā vai maṃtrabhūmi sā vidu |  
anakṣaro maṃtrayoni mahāmaṃtra kulatraya ||  
  
sarvamaṃtrārtha janako mahāviṃduranakṣara |  
paṃcākṣaro mahāśūnyo viṃdu śūnyaḥ śatākṣaraḥ ||  
  
sarvakāro nirākāraḥ ṣoḍaśādvārddha viṃdudhṛk |  
akalaṃka kalātītaścaturtha dhyāna koṭi dhṛk ||  
  
sarvadhyānakalābhijñā samādhi kulagotravit |  
samādhikā yadā grāhyā sarvasaṃbhogakāranāt ||  
  
karavīra śmaśānasthāṃ kālasaṃkarṣaṇī parāṃ |  
caṃḍāṃ pratyaṃgirāṃ kālīṃ siddhilakṣmī namāmyahaṃ ||  
  
p. 85a)  
  
ānaṃdamayyanaṃ kuryācchatāṣṭāṃtamanu kramāt |  
caruṃ cāpi mahādīpaṃ pāraṃparya kramāgataṃ ||  
  
vinā trikena saṃsiddhiḥ kalpakoṭi śatairapi |  
mahāpātre dhānyapuṃjamadya pūrṇe ghaṭeṣu ca ||  
  
akṣayaṃ tadbhavet tasya nityapūjāratasya ca |  
mahātaila pradīptaṃ vā matsya tailena vā priye ||  
  
tatra devīṃ vidhānena yaṣṭvā cādhikataṃ śataṃ |  
śāṃtike puṣṭi rogādi nāśaneśceta vartikā ||  
  
uccāṭe dhūmravarṇā ca vaśyā kṛṣṇe ca lohitā |  
māraṇe kṛṣṇavarṇā ca rogārthe kṛṣṇavarṇikā ||  
  
vidveṣe ca paṃcavarṇā staṃbhane pītavarṇikā |  
jayārthe raktaśvetā ca melāpe kiraṇopamā ||  
  
sarvakāmānavāpnoti sādhako bhakti saṃyutaḥ |  
devikāmakalākāli dehyanujñāṃ maheśvari ||  
  
prayatiṣyemideśāṃte yogakṣemārtha siddhaye |  
śaktānāmatha śaivānāṃ tilaka dvitayaṃ priye ||  
  
bhasmanādau tripuṃḍaṃ syāccaṃdane nāparaṃ bhavet |  
sarvānana śriyo grīva sarvabhūta guhāśayaḥ ||  
  
sarvavyāpī ca bhagavāṃstasyāt sarvagataḥ śivaḥ |  
devimoprākṛtaṃ cittaṃ pāpākrāṃtamabhūtsadā ||  
  
tanniḥsārayavittātvaṃ pāpaṃ phaṭ racate namaḥ |  
sāmānyārgha viśeṣaṃ ca dvividhaṃ śodhanaṃ mataṃ ||  
  
p. 85b)  
  
sāmānyamalyaṃ kathitaṃ viśeṣo vahu vistaraḥ |  
kuṃḍalinyādi cājñāṃtaṃ cakraṃ ṣaṭkaṃ viśodhayet ||  
  
tacchodhanena sakalaṃ śuddhimeti kalevaraṃ |  
tadvi śuddhau viśuddhāḥ syurnyāsa pūjā japādayaḥ ||  
  
mahāphalguṣarūpeṇa mahāraktena pātrakaṃ |  
mahātailena dvīpādi dīpayet sarvathā niśi ||  
  
saptādaśākṣarā vidyā vidyāvidyeśvareśvarī |  
siddhikālīti vikhyātā siddhilakṣmī pareśvarī ||  
  
caru uttama madhyaṃ ca vāhyapūjya prayatnataḥ |  
vāhye uttama madhyasthaṃ carupūjya gṛhe sadā ||  
  
asmiṃ taṃtre samākhyātā siddhilakṣmī jayadratha |  
guhyakālī rājalakṣmī śivāpratyaṃgireti ca ||  
  
nānayā sadṛśī vidyā sarvakarmakarī śubhā |  
eṣāvidyā mahāvidyā mālāmaṃtragaṇā smṛtā ||  
  
na caiṣāṃ dīyate yuktā svabhāvena tu dīpitā |  
yathā devi tathā dehe mama tulyo bhaviṣyati ||  
  
samakāya śiro grīvā dhārayeda calasthitaṃ |  
sa paśyan nāsikāgre tu diśaśca nāvalokayet ||  
  
majjāmedāvasā aṃḍā māṃsaṃ rudhirameva ca |  
te dadyād yoginīmanyāṃ nāśayet sakalānvitaṃ ||  
  
gurudevāgni bhaktānāṃ maṃtra dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ |  
tatra tanmadhya dātavyā mityājñā pārameśvarī ||  
  
p. 86a)  
  
ājñāyāstripurā devī mūlādhārasya kubjikā |  
caṃḍeśvarī svādhiṣṭhāne'nāhate guhyakālikā ||  
  
maṇipūraka cakre tu chinnamastā prakīrtitā |  
viśuddhe rājamātaṃgī cakrāṇāṃ nāyikā imāḥ ||  
  
ūrddhva paścima pūrvottarā'dho dakṣiṇa saṃjñakāḥ |  
yathā tāleśvarī pūrṇā tathā pūrṇeśvarī nisā ||  
  
yathā niseśvarī kubjā tathā kubjeśca guhyakā |  
śrīmahātparā mahāvidyā mahātripurasuṃdarī ||  
  
praprāsāda mahāmaṃtraṃ sakalaṃ niṣkalā mayaṃ |  
svadehaṃ sakalaṃ proktaṃ niṣkalaṃ paramādibhiḥ ||  
  
sakalaṃ niṣkalaṃ jñātvā mokṣabhāvena pūjayet |  
ṣaḍāmnāyā amī proktāstatre mānāyikāḥ kramāt ||  
  
ekaiko maṃtra ekaiko nyāso dhyānamathaikakaṃ |  
japaścāṣṭottaraśataṃ tadarddhaṃ vātha pādikaṃ ||  
  
paścimāmnāya madhye tu mukhyā vai kubjikā matā |  
mūlādhāraṃ cakramasyāḥ sthityarthaṃ nilayā kṛti ||  
  
mūlādhāre mahācakre kubjikāṃ pariciṃtayet |  
asti kuṃḍalinī brahma śaktirādhārapaṃkaje ||  
  
ābrahmaraṃdhrā niyataṃ nīteyamamṛta pradā |  
kuṃḍalilyāḥ samutpannaṃ jagadetaccarācaraṃ ||  
  
dvitīya jagadākāraṃ bhautikaṃ dehameva ca |  
sāṃkhya yogaḥ samācaṣṭe prakṛtiṃ puruṣaṃ tathā ||  
  
p. 86b)  
  
jagataḥ kāraṇatvena tadvadvaivaṃdhamokṣayoḥ |  
tatrāpi prakṛti syādau puruṣastadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
prakṛtiḥ śaktirūpā hi puruṣaḥ śiva ucyate |  
ādyāśaktiḥ kuṃḍalinī cinmayī prakṛtiḥ kalā ||  
  
ityādyā vācakāḥ śabdā vahavaḥ śāstragocarāḥ |  
paramātmeśvaraḥ sākṣī māyeśaḥ puruṣaḥ śivaḥ ||  
  
paryāya śabdā etepi bhūyāsaḥ parameśituḥ |  
tasyāḥ kaṃdā gṛhaṃ proktaṃ mūlāsyādhāra hetutaḥ ||  
  
mūlādhāramiti khyātaṃ brahmagaṃthitayā tathā |  
sādhyaṣṭa valayā tatra prasupta bhujagākṛti ||  
  
ceṣṭayaṃtīṃ tanuṃ sarvāṃ tiṣṭhatyamṛtarūpiṇī |  
sadāśivasya bhavanaṃ brahmaraṃdhramiti smṛtaṃ ||  
  
sahasraṃ dalamaṃbhojaṃ taduriṣṭamadhomukhaṃ |  
brahmakāraiśūṣmaraṃdhai kuṃḍalinya hi rūpiṇī ||  
  
praviśya tiṣṭhati yāto brahmaraṃdhaṃ tato mukhaṃ |  
brahmaraṃdhraṃ śirasye ca brahmagraṃthi gudopari ||  
  
graṃthai vimocane mokṣo brahmagraṃthistataḥ smṛtaḥ |  
mūlādhāreśca kaṃdaśca brahmagraṃthiḥ sanātanaḥ ||  
  
brahmāṃḍaṃ brahmaśayyā ca śabdāḥ paryā ca vācakāḥ |  
kuṃḍalinye ca hi sadā gacchatyūrddhaṃ śivāṃtikaṃ ||  
  
na śivo'dhuḥ samāyāti kadāpi hi tadaṃtikaṃ |  
yatra yatra ca viśramya gacchatya mṛtaliṃgayā ||  
  
kramaṇorddhoddha saṃsthānāccakramityabhidhīyate |  
devi kāmakalā kāli sṛṣṭi sthityaṃta kāriṇī ||  
  
p. 87a)  
  
atrādhiṣṭhānamādhe hi parivāragaṇe saha |  
yathāśakti yathālābhaṃ tvadartha mu * kalpite ||  
  
dṛṣṭiṃ niveśayeśāni pūjopakaraṇe'khile |  
jale'nulepane puṣpe dhūpadīpe valau tathā ||  
  
naivedyepi ca tāṃvūle rājopakaraṇe tathā |  
adhiṣṭhitāyāṃ tvapyaṃva vighnān rakṣaṃti sarvaśaḥ ||  
  
bhūtāni vidraviṣyaṃti mama rakṣā bhaviṣyati |  
manorathāśca me sarve setsyaṃti tvat prasādataḥ ||  
  
pūjā ca saphalā devi bhavitrīte kṛpāvaśāt |  
nṛcarmamāsanaṃ kṛtvā narapātre prapūjayet ||  
  
yathā gurumukhoddiṣṭa nirvikalpena śodhayet |  
lākṣārasa nibhe naiva hetunā paripūritaṃ ||  
  
phalgu datvā tatra madhye pātre hetu prapūrite |  
aṣṭamyā vā caturdaśyāṃ navamyāṃ vā viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
śiva rātryāṃntathā pūjā niśāyāṃ paripūjayet |  
yathā śrīcakrapūjāṃ vai tathā sarvaṃ samācaret ||  
  
viṃducakre trikoṇe tu mahāpātraṃ tu sthāpayet |  
paṃcakālyāṃ tu paṃcāre carukaṃ paṃca vai kramāt ||  
  
nātaḥ parataraṃ bhadre kālikā kramapūjane |  
bhogyaṃ svargaṃ sukhaṃ mokṣaṃ ājñā siddhiṃ bhaveddhruvaṃ ||  
  
satyaṃ satyaṃ mahādevi satyametadvavīmyahaṃ |  
anyathā kurute yastu hetuvādakutarkataḥ ||  
  
pariśramaṃ kevalaṃ tu na sa siddhimavāpnuyāt |  
maṃgalā ca mahāmāyā caṃḍakāpālinī śivā ||  
  
p. 87b)  
  
cāmuṃḍā carcikā caṇḍā sṛṣṭi sthityaṃta kāriṇī |  
anākhyā ca mahābhāgā guhyaṃ kālī jayā parā ||  
  
siddhilakṣmī viśvalakṣmī mahāpratyaṃgirā smṛtā |  
suṃdarī tripurā cāru ugra caṃḍāprakāśinī ||  
  
vibhinnā vahudhā jātā nānābheda samāśritā |  
ekā sā vahurūpā ca jānīyād divya cakṣuṣā ||  
  
sa eva sādhakaśreṣṭaḥ siddhijñānasya bhājanaṃ |  
aṃvaraṃ pavanaṃ vahni āpaṃ ca dharaṇī tathā ||  
  
rāvaṇī nāma sā vidyā mokṣadā bhuktidā priye |  
ekākṣarī parāvidyā bhogamokṣapradā smṛtā ||  
  
śikhī ca madhuhā yuktā kālī prāṇamudāhṛtaṃ |  
khphre& mātmakamālikhya mahācaṃḍa matā likhet ||  
  
yogeśvarī padaṃ datvā vidyeyaṃ sā navākṣarī |  
maṃtramāteti vikhyātā trailokyaiśvarya dāyakaṃ ||  
  
samastamaṃtrajananī sarvamaṃtra pravāhinī |  
vahudhā varṇituṃ maṃtra mātā sa ca pravāhinī ||  
  
pratyaṃgirā mahākālī mokṣasaukhyapradāyinī |  
ṣoḍaśākṣariyā vidyā prāṇabhūtāśca tā śṛṇu ||  
  
yasyopadeśamātreṇa brahmabhūpāya kalpate |  
tripadaṃ tu samuddhṛtya mahārāvaṃ tato likhet ||  
  
p. 88a)  
  
niśā mādhavasaṃyuktaṃ jñeyaṃ tridaśavaṃdite |  
satyārūḍhe sāśvataścatuṣṭinā kavalīkṛtaṃ ||  
  
satyasatyā samārūḍho śekṣmeśa kevalī kṛtāḥ |  
tataścakrī jāṭharaṃ ca nārāyaṇa samanvitaṃ ||  
  
mādhavena samāyukto valānuja punarlikhet |  
māyācaṃḍī kūrcarakṣā mahārāva punarlikhet ||  
  
rati niyojayed devī śiramaṃtraṃ samuccaret |  
varṇa ṣoḍaśamākhyātaṃ maṃtrarājamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
ekoccāraṇa deveśi vājapeyasya koṭayaḥ |  
aśvamedha sahasrāṇi prādakṣiṇya bhuvastathā ||  
  
prayāge snānajatpuṇyaṃmakalasthe divākare |  
tasya śataguṇaṃ proktaṃ kālikā vidhinārcanaṃ ||  
  
pāturāśramayatpuṇyaṃ krameṇa parisevitaṃ |  
yatpuṇya varṇa dharmasya tatpuṇyaṃ kālikārcanāt ||  
  
kāśyadi tīrthayātrāṃ ca sārddhakoṭi trayānvitaṃ |  
tulādānāti deveśi satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
lakṣajāpena deveśi kiṃ punasiddhi bhāgbhavet |  
yasyāḥ sāmarthato devyā bhuvanāni caturdaśaḥ ||  
  
saumyasiddhikṛtāṃtena devī pratyaṃgirābhidhāḥ |  
nāradānumate naiva sajñā devyā dvidhā kṛtā ||  
  
śonitākhye pured devi hariśaṃkara vigrahe |  
nāradena munīṃdrena kṛṣṇāya sa pradattavān ||  
  
p. 88b)  
  
hariṇāṭṭāṃbhanāṣṭreṣu prayājya haramohitaḥ |  
vāsudevo priyārthāya rakṣārtha pradadau purā ||  
  
bhṛṃgopabhukta puṣpaṃ tu śivayogyaṃ yathā bhavet |  
tadvat nirakṣaraṃ vastu akṣarairapi saṃyutā ||  
  
noddhāraṃ lekhayed devi sākṣādvarṇeśvarī parā |  
śāpā bhavati vai nūnaṃ maṃtrahāni prajāyate ||  
  
vimukhā bhavate kālī pāyā nāmāśramo bhavet |  
karṇe karṇe tu deveśi hṛdisthaṃ kuru sarvadā ||  
  
guruvaktrā viniśkrāṃtā śrotramārge hṛdi sthitāḥ |  
udakaṃ likhitaṃ tadvat maṃtroddhāraṃ tathā bhavet ||  
  
bhogamokṣapradā vidyā pustake naiva lekhayet ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade paṃcadaśaḥ paṭalaḥ || 15 ||  
  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
divyārka vodhakamalādaragarbhasaṃsthaṃ visvātmakaṃ paramanirmala   
siddhanāthaṃ yenāvatārita mahārṇava madhyacaṃdraḥ dvīpāṃtaraṃ   
paramaciṃcini citprakāśaṃ |  
  
tanmadhya nirgata mahākulavedhayaṃti divyāṃtarikṣa gaganāṃtara bhūtareṣu |  
pātālacakra vicarāṃtara grāhayaṃtīṃ namāmi paścima kramātvaya śrīkukārāṃ   
||  
  
kālākāla viluptakaṃ daragharanityanuraktaṃ vrataṃ dvaitādvaita vibheda bhinna   
sadataṃ tyaktvāśca lābhādayaṃ |  
taṃ taṃ bhāvarasaṃparāmṛtaghanaṃ pītvāśca ghūrmodayaṃ krīḍaṃtīṃ   
raticakra carcita parāṃ saṃsparśa lakṣmī namaḥ ||  
  
p. 89a)  
  
yāśā śaktirbhagākhyaṃ prakaṭita nilaye dakṣiṇe caiva koṇe vāme   
śrīpūrṇapīṭhaṃ paśujanabhaya kṛt kāmarūpaṃ tadagre |  
evaṃ vyāptaṃ samasthaṃ sthitilayajananī rudraśaktistribhedaiḥ tanmadhye   
devadevaḥ makula * * mayaṃ tanmadādya svataṃtraṃ ||  
  
yasyājñā viṃdūbhūtā paśubhayaharaṇī siddhidā vodharūpā nitya klinnā   
svaraktā bhavamudita sadā naṃdadātrī svataṃtrā |  
tanmadhye divyaliṃgaṃ paramasukha'karaṃ viṃdurūpaṃ svarūpaṃ nityānaṃdaṃ   
svarūpaṃ tadubhayamathanaṃ ṣaṭprakārai vibhinnaṃ kurvaṃtī tatra māṃkṣubhita   
varatanuṃ śrīkubjikākhyaṃ namāmi ||   
  
namo nirṇāmanāmnāya bhagacakrabhagāyine ||  
  
namo ānaṃda daivyai ca bhagarūpe namostute |  
rajasvalāmukhaṃ dṛṣṭā sarvapāpai vimucyate ||  
  
saṃbhāṣanaṃ ca kurute rājasūyādikaṃ phalaṃ |  
tasyāḥ sparśanamātreṇa labhenmukti caturvidhā ||  
  
tasyāḥ saṃgamamātreṇa trailokyāt pāṭanai kṣamaḥ |  
śuddhayā pūjanet tasyāḥ bhagaṃsaṃrajasobhitaṃ ||  
  
nyāsaṃ kṛtvā svadeheṣu kulābhiḥ kāmapūjitaṃ |  
viśeṣaiḥ pūjitā yoniḥ puṇyasaṃkhyā na vidyate ||  
  
p. 89b)  
  
mahāyatnena deveśī puṣpavatīṃ sulakṣaṇā |  
pūjyate devatā buddhyā pisitālisu saṃyutāṃ ||  
  
javapātaṃ tu vidhivat svayaṃ bhaktyā yathaicchayā |  
pibe divyaṃ surajyoti jādyatā ca hare dhruvaṃ ||  
  
brahmabhūta svayaṃ bhaktyā niva jāpya sureśvarī |  
visarjane puna pūjāḥ punaḥ pātraṃ pivecchubhaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ kṛte tu vāreṇa śivatulyo bhave dhruvaṃ |  
anyata gopaye devi svayonimapane yathā ||  
  
na prakāśyaṃ kuputrāya gopyāt gopya kṛtaṃ śubhaṃ |  
pramādācca prakāśāti satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
triloke durlabhaṃ devi gopya pūjā phalaṃ mahat |  
bhaktyā ca paṭhate vīraḥ pūjāṃ tastavamuttamaṃ ||  
  
ratikāle viśeṣena śivaṃ tulyo bhavennaraḥ |  
iti dvādaśabhiḥ ślokai stavanaṃ paramādbhutaṃ ||  
  
rajasvalā samapitu pathyate sarvasiddhi kṛt |  
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyaṃ satyasatyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
sa puṣpa bhagapūjā ca brahmalokepi durlabhā |  
asya stotrasya māhātmyaṃ mayā vaktuṃ na śakyate ||  
  
viraṃjimaghayā viṣṇu paṭhate ca niraṃtalaṃ |  
stotrapāṭha prabhāvena sṛṣṭi sthiti bhaveddhruvaṃ ||  
  
tasmāt sarveṣu yatnena devī gopyakaraṃ śubhaṃ |  
  
smare prathama puṣpānī rudhila viṃdu nilāṃvarā gṛhita madhupātṛkāṃ   
madavipūrṇa netrānanāṃghanastanabharānatā galitanīvikā śyāmalāṃ kala   
sphurita varṇaviṃśadasaṃvatāṭaṃkiniṃ ||  
  
p. 90a)  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
śrutaṃ deva mayā sarvaṃ aśeṣa kramamuttamaṃ |  
pāraṃparya vibhāgena sarvaśāstra sutodbhavaṃ ||  
  
taṃtrasāraṃ kriyāsāraṃ kulasāraṃ suvistaraṃ |  
trikasāraṃ tathā nātha yoginī hṛdayāṃtaraṃ ||  
  
kālacakrodayannātha tejo rāsi samudbhavaṃ |  
yāmalaṃ tama siddhāṃtaṃ bhairavāṣṭa samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
gāruḍaṃ bhūtataṃtraṃ ca vidyāsāra suvistaraṃ |  
aṣṭāṣṭasadaṃ prastāraṃ vistāraṃ ca śrutanmayā ||  
  
paṃcaśrota vibhedena śaivaṃ śrutyā suniścayaṃ |  
maṃtrataṃtrātma bhedaṃ ca cakra bhedaṃ hṛdāṃtaraṃ ||  
  
sārabhedaṃ kalābhedaṃ nityābhedaṃ śrutanmayā |  
rudraśakti parāśakti svarāśaktiśca niścayaṃ ||  
  
svacchaṃda paramaṃ bhedamuttacottaranirṇayaṃ |  
saura vaiṣṇava paudhaṃ ca sāratarka vibhāvitaṃ ||  
  
sāṃbhavaṃ ānavaṃśaktaṃ bhedaṃ śrutvā mayā prabho |  
kaṣṭakaṣṭataraṃ kleṣaṃ sudhā sādhyayogacittakaiḥ ||  
  
dhyānayogarakecitkecijapyā parāyaṇāḥ |  
prāṇāyāma mayā kecit arddhacaṃdrakalākramaṃ ||  
  
viṃdubhedaratākecicchākhya jñāna sthitāḥ parāḥ |  
parakarmaratā keciccakṣunmīlita saṃsthitāḥ ||  
  
agnikarmaratāḥ keci pāgādi jajane ratāḥ |  
sarve kliṣyāṃtite nāthena kiṃcit pratyayo bhavet ||  
  
p. 90b)  
  
vinānvaya prabhedena ājñāsiddhi prakāśitaṃ |  
sarvaśāstrārtha hṛdayaṃ satānāmuttamottamaṃ ||  
  
śrīciṃcinīmatasārasya samuccaye vadasva me ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
ati guhyataraṃ praśnaṃ yoginī hṛdayāṃtaraṃ |  
duḥsādhyaṃ sarvadevānāṃ gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ ||  
  
ciṃcinīmatasāroyaṃ divyogha paramaṃ padaṃ |  
kathayāmi na saṃdeho vallabhatvādvarānane ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi sārasaṃgrahamuttamaṃ |  
siddhānvaya paraṃ kaulaṃ bhuktimukti phalapradaṃ ||  
  
kulākulamataṃ līnaṃ vyomavyomāṃta bhairavaṃ |  
visvonminirgataṃ śūnyaṃ śaktaviśrāṃtamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
tatotpannā parā deve kāminī kāmarūpiṇī |  
kumārī kāla pīṭhesthā mahādivyaughavarṣiṇī ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
divyoghaṃ tatkathaṃ nātha yantvayā codino hyahaṃ |  
kathayaṃ tva prasādena saubhāgyaṃ jananaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi paraṃ guhyaṃ sarvaśāstra samuccayaṃ |  
pāraṃparyakramaṃ sūkṣmaṃ divyakaulāvatārakaṃ ||  
  
kathayāmi na saṃdeha tava snehād varānane |  
divyogha paramānaṃdaṃ picu vaktrastu kaulikaṃ ||  
  
tanmadhyodita cidvṛkṣā mūlaśākhā suvistaraṃ |  
adṛṣṭa vigrahārūḍhaṃ siddhogha phalamuttamaṃ ||  
  
sthānāni deha vinyāsaṃ mahāpīṭha samudbhavaṃ |  
varṇarāsi paraṃ divyaṃ sarvavodima bhairavaṃ ||  
  
p. 91a)  
  
rudrān vīrāṃ tathā siddhāṃ kṣatrapālān svakṣetrajān |  
yoginī yogi vāmāṃtā sarvaśāstra kulāgamāṃ ||  
  
pīṭhodbhavā pīṭhasiddhāṃ pīṭhocārāpapīṭhajān |  
saṃdohaścanvaraṃ divyaṃ guhāvāsaṃ tu gahvaraṃ ||  
  
khyacaraṃ khecarāṃtasthā khasvarūpaṃ kṣabhakṣakaṃ |  
ekaikoṭhidhā bhinnaṃ kulaśākhā suvistaraṃ ||  
  
anāmāvarṇanāmaṃ tu vāgbhavaṃ khecarī sphuṭaṃ |  
akārādi kṣakārāṃtā prasuptannaṃdavigrahaṃ ||  
  
ciṃtāmaṇi samaprakhyaṃ vistaraṃ kulabhairavaṃ |  
sthānaṃ sthānāṃtaraṃ divyaṃ svasthānaṃ japa nirgataṃ ||  
  
adiṣṭavigrahānandamatītaṃ vimalānvayaṃ |  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi divyogha kramanirṇayaṃ ||  
  
bhuktimukti pradātāraṃ pūjāsiddhi phalapradaṃ ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
anvayaṃ kīdṛśīnnātha tvayoktaṃ praśnapūrvakaṃ |  
kathayasva prasādena yadi tuṣṭosi me prabho ||  
  
bhairavyuvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi anvayasyaiva lakṣaṇaṃ |  
mataṃ matantaraṃ guptaṃ śrīciṃcinīmatamuttamaṃ ||  
  
sārātsārataraṃ divyaṃ kathayāmi varānane |  
raviṃdu satvāmapadaṃ cidacit kamalodalaṃ ||  
  
ubhayānaṃda saṃdohaṃ pāraṃparya vijṛṃbhitaṃ |  
kulāmūlāmvayaṃ devi kulākaulaṃ vinirgataṃ ||  
  
p. 91b)  
  
kaulaṃ tu ṣaṭvidhaṃ satvā ṣaṭ kūṭa paritaṃ dhruvaṃ |  
ṣaṭ saṃjñā caḥ samudbhūtaṃ prasarāt paścimānvayaṃ ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
kathaṃ vai paścime saṃjñā anvayaṃ guru kīdṛśaṃ |  
lakṣaṇaṃ pratyayaṃ tasya kaulācāraṃ tu kīdṛśaṃ ||  
  
sādhakaṃ sādhanaṃ caiva dīkṣā samayameva ca |  
carūṃcāraṃ kathaṃ cāryā vrataṃ caiva tu kīdṛśaṃ ||  
  
dvaitaṃ caiva tathā dvaitaṃ dvaitādvaitaṃ tathaiva ca |  
pādukā darśanaṃ nātha kīdṛśaṃ vada tatvataḥ ||  
  
sālaṃvaṃ kiṃ nirālaṃvaṃ nistatvaṃ kiṃ sa tatvakaṃ |  
sānaṃdaṃ kiṃ nirānaṃdaṃ nilakṣaṃ ki salakṣakaṃ ||  
  
sākāraṃ kiṃ nirākāraṃ kīdṛśaṃ paścimakramaṃ |  
śāktaṃ ca sāṃbhavaṃ kiṃ vā jñānamānavameva ca ||  
  
maṃtravīryaṃ vimarthaṃ ca svarūpaṃ ca tathodayaṃ |  
vadanātha mahāmudrā pāśajālaśca drāvaṇī ||  
  
kathaṃ mūlaṃ ca saṃtānaṃ pāraṃparyaṃ ca kīdṛśaṃ |  
kathaṃ śāstraṃ ca vīryaṃ ca vidyāvaiśikameva ca ||  
  
ke pīṭhāḥ ke ca pīṭhā sāke siddhākāśca yogiṇī |  
catuṣkaṃ paṃcakaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ trikaṃścaiva tu kiṃ vidhā ||  
  
ādhāraṃ ca śvādhiṣṭhānaṃ maṇipūramanāhataṃ |  
viśuddhā ca tathājñā vai ṣaṭprakāra kathaṃ sthitaṃ sthitaṃ ||  
  
vyāptiśca kīdṛśī nātha bhedaṃ vai nirṇayaṃ tathā |  
divyabhaumāṃtarikṣaṃ ca trividhaṃ kīdṛśaṃ kramaṃ ||  
  
p. 92a)  
  
vṛkṣaṃ puṣpaṃ guhāgotraṃ saṅketaṃ ca gṛhaṃ tathā |  
sthitiṃ ca janma kīrtaṃ ca siddhiścaiva tu kīdṛśī ||  
  
adhikāra trayannātha javalli tritayaṃ tathā |  
ṣaṭśrotreṣu ca ko bhedaḥ pādukā darśanaṃ prabho ||  
  
maṇḍalottāraṇaścaiva maṃḍalaṃ maṇḍalakramaṃ |  
maṇḍalāṃtantathā nātha saptāviṃśati maṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
teṣāṃ pūjā kathaṃ nātha vyāptiścaiva tu kīdṛśī |  
kathaṃ dīpaṃ ca bhakṣāṃte pūjyate kena kāraṇe ||  
  
vidhiścaicārghapātraṃ ca keṣu dravyeṣu kārayet |  
nugrahe nigrahe nāthaṃ kathaṃ vyāptī parāpare ||  
  
kiṃ vījo bhaya ṣaṭkasya kasthānaṃ pūjanena tu |  
kiṃ caruṃ ca kamāmudrā dṛṣṭipātaṃ tu kīdṛśaṃ ||  
  
nityanaimittike nātha kā pūjā pādukā krame |  
dīkṣā jyaṣṭhe sthāna jyeṣṭhaṃ ājñā jyeṣṭha tṛtīyakaṃ ||  
  
krama jyeṣṭha caturthaṃ hi adhikaṃ kotra pūjyate |  
dīpaṃ caruṃ ca puṣpaṃ ca arghapātra kramaṃ tathā ||  
  
kīdṛśaśya tu deyeta pātukā darśanaṃ paraṃ |  
kramajñāna kramajñeyaṭkramalakṣa kramodayaṃ ||  
  
kramabhedaṃ kramoghaṃ ca kramātītaṃ tu kīdṛśaṃ |  
kramasiddhi kramābhyāsaṃ akulaṃ ca kulaṃ tathā ||  
  
navasaṃjñā trisajñā ca ṣaṭsajñā paṃcameva ca |  
trisaṃjñāmekasaṃjñā ca siddhadevī ca pāsthitā ||  
  
dvipaṃca viśa saṃjñā ca'teṣāṃ bhede vadasva me |  
kathaṃ parvadinā nātha ke siddhāstatra pūjyate ||  
  
p. 92b)  
  
kīdṛśeṇa krameṇaiva ājñā śiṣyasya dīyate |  
ṣaḍrasā deha saṃsthā ca paṃcaratnāni kīdṛśaṃ ||  
  
vīryamāharaṇannātha pratyayaṃ vyāptimeva ca |  
bhāṣācchummāśca melāsaṃ sa vāhyābhyaṃtaraṃ tathā ||  
  
kīdṛśasya prakāśyeta kaulācāraṃ sudurlabham |  
etat pṛcchāmyahaṃ nātha vadasva me matatvataḥ ||  
  
sarvaśāstrasamudbhūtaṃ praśna kṛtaṃ suvistaraṃ |  
yena nirbhrāṃta vuddhiśca bhavāmitpadanugrahaṃ ||  
  
niṣkampa kaulike mārge saṃvarāmi sadoditaṃ |  
nityaṃ śayaśca nirddhatvaṃ vitṛṣṇaṃ putra dārayoḥ ||  
  
jarāpalita hīnaṃ ca nityānaṃda bhayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi praśnakūṭa suvistaraṃ |  
ājñāsiddhikaraṃ divya bhuktimukti pradāyakaṃ ||  
  
sarvasaubhāgya jananaṃ sarvakāma phalapradaṃ |  
vakṣyāmi tava deveśi paścimaścaiva lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
lakṣāṃtaraṃ lakṣabhedaṃ lakṣapakṣa vivarjitaṃ |  
hyapakṣa vimalaṃ bhakṣa tadbhakṣa gṛhalakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
paścimaṃ tadvidurdevi ānvayaṃ ānvayānvayam |  
mānaseya parikṣīṇa nistaraṅga mahodadhiḥ ||  
  
gādhagaṃbhīra gahanantadānaṃda gṛha smṛtaḥ |  
svasvabhāva parāḥ kaścit pūrvacakrodaye sthitaḥ ||  
  
p. 93a)  
  
dakṣiṇottara taṃ bhedaṃ nityā kāli kramodayaṃ |  
sarvaṃ tyaktvā svabhāvena tallayaṃ paścime gṛhaṃ ||  
  
vaktravaktrī lalo lolī kaviḥ kaviḥ kulākulaṃ |  
cakracakrī kramākāmī guhāgūhī hṛdādikā ||  
  
kulakramārthakaṃ jñātvā yajed vimala bhairavaṃ |  
paścimamudayānaṃdaṃ utpatti kramaniścayaṃ ||  
  
siddhāmnāya rahasyaṃ tu kathitaṃ tava suvrate |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi anvayī ca mahāpriye ||  
  
trikulaṃ trikulātītaṃ tribhavaṃ tribhavāṃtaraṃ |  
trigarbhagarbharahitaṃ yo jānāti sa cāmvayī ||  
  
kāmakāmī tayedrūpa tadrūpa kulamālinī |  
cidacicciṃcinī garbhamvastutaṃ siddhanirmalaṃ ||  
  
ājñādhāraṃ tu taṃ devi nigrahānugrahe rataṃ |  
tīvrātīvrataraṃ jñeyo yo jānāti sacānvayī ||  
  
madaṃtpadāṃtaraṃ madyaṃ madātītaṃ madodbhavaṃ |  
madaṃ bhuktvā madaṃ divyaṃ yo jānāti sa cānvayī ||  
  
etad devi mayākhyātaṃ manvayī lakṣaṇaṃ paraṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi gurulakṣaṇamuttamaṃ ||  
  
yena saṃvodhayedvāpaṃ sarvaśāstra samudbhavaṃ |  
aṇoranīya yadbrahma kāraṇānāṃ ca kāraṇaṃ ||  
  
tatvaṃguṇa anādiṃ ca yasyorddhamaparannahi |  
sarvādayaṃ sarvagatiṃ sarvabhoga vivarjitaṃ ||  
  
p. 93b)  
  
sarvādhvā parivodhā ca ṣaḍrasāsvādalaṃ padaṃ |  
na graho yasya nirvāṇe tyāgo nāpi bhavārṇave ||  
  
dvābhyāṃ saṃspṛṣṭa yogena vartate socyate guruḥ |  
evaṃ vidhaṃ mahāguhyaṃ gurusarvārtha vodhataḥ ||  
  
bhrāṃti jñāna vicārāya gururityabhidhīyate |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇasyaivamuttamaṃ ||  
  
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaḥ sarvāgama vicārakaḥ |  
sarvabhūta dayāyuktaḥ kṛpāśīlān sa vatsalaḥ ||  
  
vodhakaścedako dakṣa śāṃtacittaśca varṇataḥ |  
tapasvī vratadhārī ca guhāvāsī jiteṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
kālacakrā na bhāvī ca bhikṣāsī vīravigrahaḥ |  
kulokālakulāmnāyī kramaśāstra vicārakaḥ ||  
  
vedhadīkṣāt sa saṃvodhaṃ tyāgī dhīrya parāyaṇaḥ |  
anudvija na śīlajña īdṛśaṃ gurulakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi gurupratyayamuttamaṃ |  
adṛṣṭavigrahaḥ śāṃto devatā siddhakhecarī ||  
  
paśyaṃti divya cakṣūṣāṃ trinetra gamanaṃ priye |  
maruciṃtāpahārī ca parakāya praveśanaṃ ||  
  
paravedha parākarṣa īdṛśi gurupratyayaḥ |  
etad devi mayā * khyaṃ gurupratyaya lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi kaulācāra manuttamaṃ |  
varṇadvāraṃ prajādvāraṃ mokṣadvāraṃ niraṃjanaṃ ||  
  
etad bhedavaraṃ divya kaulācāra prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
p. 94a)  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
varṇadvāraṃ kathaṃ nātha prajādvāraṃ kathaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
mokṣadvāraṃ mahādeva niraṃjana vadasva me ||  
  
etadbheda catuṣkaṃ tu kathayasva prasādataḥ ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi guhyaṃ kaulikamuttamaṃ |  
saṃpradāya catuṣkaṃ tu bhuktimukti phalapradaṃ ||  
  
khasvarāṃtasvaravisa muditaṃ vodhabhāskaraṃ |  
dhvani rūpa samāpannaṃ tālumadhyā valaṃvitaṃ ||  
  
prāṇasūtra pravāhena paṃcāśadvarṇa saṃyutaṃ |  
vaikharī vaktrayoktrī ca vīrāvali kulodbhavaṃ ||  
  
viṣālavaktra viṣadaṃ nirgataṃ kulabhairavaṃ |  
etad devi mayoktaṃ ca varṇadvāra manuttamaṃ ||  
  
prajāsūtimanohlādaṃ sravadanaṃdinirbharaṃ |  
triḥprakāraṃ triśanavaṃ tridhā ca kramamaṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
amṛtāgha plutaṃ divyaṃ tanmadhye cidacitsphuraṃ |  
trimūrti vadanandevi prajādvāraṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
nābhicakrāṃtara gataṃ cidacit teja maṃḍalaṃ |  
mahāyoni paraṃ divyaṃ brahmanāḍi prakāśakaṃ ||  
  
adha ūrddhva pravāhena vyāpakaṃ sarvato mukhaṃ |  
bhedayet tālu mārgaṃ tu drāvayeccit kalāmṛtaṃ ||  
  
mokṣadvāramidaṃ bhadre niraṃjana vadāmyahaṃ |  
śivamaṃḍala madhyasthaṃ mahākāli kramodayaṃ ||  
  
tatrodyogāmabhāṣaṃ tu carcitaṃ ca viropakaṃ |  
mahāsaṃhārasaṃhāraṃ grāśī kṛta kulārṇavaṃ ||  
  
p. 94b)  
  
niraṃjana sarvagataṃ sarvā bhāṣaikabhāṣakaṃ |  
mahākalpāṃtakalpāṃtaṃ mahāśiva layaṃ gataṃ ||  
  
mahātejo dharaṃ vīraṃ mahāpaśu priyā priyā |  
mahāsiddha padaṃ siddhaṃ mahādivyogha maṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
etat kramamanākhyaṃ ca yoginī yukti gocaraṃ |  
caturbheda vibhāgena kaulācāraṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
yo jānāti kramaṃ divyaṃ sa gururmokṣado bhavet |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi sādhanā sādhakaṃ priye ||  
  
yatra yatra parīkṣīṇo bhāvaṃ tallayatāṃ gataḥ |  
tatra tatra sthito yogī vivṛtti parabhāvitaḥ ||  
  
paśyate ca parāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ yadvastu manasepsitaṃ |  
tatkṣat prāpyate sohi aṃtarātmā śvabhāvataḥ ||  
  
harṣaśoka parityāgātidvate ca mahītale |  
sthirīya * hvamāpannā sādhanā sādhakaṃ priye ||  
  
samāgama vinirmukta svayastustatra tiṣṭhati |  
tatra viśrāma yogaṃdāṃ bhāvitaṃ vimalaṃ priye ||  
  
paśyate svakulaṃ tatvaṃ parabhāva prabhedanaṃ |  
paramākāsagamanaṃ sādhanāsādhanaṃ priye ||  
  
mudrā sphoṭakaraṃ devi dṛṣṭipāta nirīkṣaṇāt |  
pratimācāraṇaṃ kuryāt paṭadāha tathaiva ca ||  
  
yakṣiṇī sādhanaṃ caiva vilayaṃti prabhaṃjanaṃ |  
silā sphoṭastu bhūkampa maṃtra dhyānaṃ ca khecaraṃ ||  
  
jīvākṛṣṭikaraṃ devi paraciṃtā padāraṇaṃ |  
purapraveśakaraṇaṃ unmaṃta karaṇa priye ||  
  
p. 95a)  
  
apamṛtyu vināśāya jvararoga nivāranaṃ |  
sthirīkṛtya tanurdevi vāk staṃbhe karaṇaṃ priye ||  
  
dūrāśravaṇa vijñānaṃ prāṇināṃ ruditaṃ śutaṃ |  
gamana staṃbhanaṃ kṛtvā anagni jvalanaṃ tathā ||  
  
pakṣīkagagaṇākarṣayakṣa bhūtanivāraṇaṃ |  
evaṃ tu kathitandevi yogeṃdresya tu sādhanaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi dīkṣā kaulikamuttamaṃ |  
maṃtradīkṣā sa vījā ca ājyājyānnatilaihutaṃ ||  
  
nivījā kaulikī dīkṣā vedhamātma svarūpataḥ |  
sanmukṣīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā viśrāṃtargaganā priye ||  
  
tatrastho bhāvayed devi ājñā vimalabhairavaṃ |  
paśu vigrahayosphulyaṃ saṃkrāmakaraṇaṃ priye ||  
  
paramātmasvasaṃvodha hlādamānaṃdanirbharaṃ |  
vikalpabhedayuktā tu paśuvigrahanirmalaṃ ||  
  
hāhākāra krameṇaiva śithalīkṛta vigrahaṃ |  
te naiva yukti bhedena kādi saṃvidamāśṛtaṃ ||  
  
svasvabhāva svavodhena carcitaṃ ca'kulāmṛtaṃ |  
pītvā tu yuktibhedena kakaṃdara rasodbhavaṃ ||  
  
pakṣābhayavikāsogha svānaṃdapadanirbharaṃ |  
nirgatahāsya rāvena vedhaye snāna vigrahaṃ ||  
  
kathitaṃ devadeveśi vedhadīkṣā svavodhataḥ |  
saṃsārabhayabhicchinnā bhogamokṣapradāyinī ||  
  
p. 95b)  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi samayaṃ kaulikāgame |  
brahmādi svapacāṃtaśca sarvavarṇa vyavasthitāḥ ||  
  
paramātmā parāśaktiścidvatma parabhāvitaḥ |  
samatā buddhimāpanna satvastha samateṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
sarvabhūtāṃtaracarastiryaṅmānuṣa bhāvitaḥ |  
yatra yatrānubhāvena tatra tatra tu tallayaṃ ||  
  
gatvāṃtarātmā sarvajñāḥ kha svarūpa kha viśrutaḥ |  
sarvāvārasamopetaḥ samayaṃ samayeśvaraḥ ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade ṣoḍaśaḥ paṭalaḥ || 16 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi sārātsāraṃ varānane |  
caruṃ cāruṃ tathācāryā vratasyaiva tu lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
bhaktiyukto hi yogīṃdraścaryāparyatanerataḥ |  
sarakhatpara saṃyuktaḥ kaulavrataparāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
bhikṣācāraṃ ca gṛhnīyād yāgārthañjīvamaṃḍale |  
yogābhyāsa parā nityaṃ kramapūjāratatsadā ||  
  
ājñādhāraṃ gurorvākyaṃ sailisaṃketalakṣaṇaṃ |  
tasya siddhirbhaved devi kaulikī mokṣadāyinīṃ ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
caruṃ tu kīdṛśaṃ nātha ṣaṭparaścaiva kīdṛśaṃ |  
vratacaryo kramaṃ nātha adhyātma kathayasva me ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmiraraṣaṭ paralakṣaṇaṃ |  
vratacaryā samāyuktaṃ paścimānvayamuttamaṃ ||  
  
p. 96a)  
  
saraṃ ṣaḍunmi rahitaṃ ṣaṭpadārtha padārjhitaṃ |  
ṣaḍaṃtasthāna viśrāma pāraṇāsāramuttamaṃ ||  
  
sitāsitaparaḥ pakṣa sareyevagamuttamaṃ |  
praṇavasphulakaṃ yuktampaścimāmvayamuttamaṃ ||  
  
brahmāṃḍakhaṃḍa paramaṃ khatparaṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
sikṣānubhavacāreṇa ānaṃdagharamuttamaṃ ||  
  
khacaṃdracaṇḍikāryā ca hālānādāṃtare sthitaḥ |  
parāmṛta caruṃ divyaṃ dhārayet prāṇajīvitaḥ ||  
  
kathitaṃ tu varārohe vratacārasya lakṣaṇaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi dvaitaṃ cā dvaitalakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
khapadaṃ khapadātītaṃ svapadaṃ svapadāṃtaraṃ |  
kālacakrodayaṃ yatra tatra bhakṣayate paraṃ ||  
  
evaṃ krama vicāreṇa dvaitādvaitasya lakṣaṇaṃ |  
pādukādarśanaṃ devi kathitaṃ mama tatvataḥ ||  
  
yadvastu bhāvitaṃ devi viṃdunādāṃta madhyataḥ |  
dvaitaṃ samarasī bhūtaṃ advaitaṃ ca prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi praśnaṃ paramadurlabhaṃ |  
sālamvaṃ kinnirālamvaṃ nistatvaṃ kiṃ sa tatvakaṃ ||  
  
sānandaṃ kiṃ nirānandaṃ nirlakṣaṃ kiṃ sa lakṣakaṃ |  
sākāraṃ kinnirākāraṃ kīdṛśaṃ paścima kramaṃ ||  
  
sasvarūpaṃ cidākāśe sthitā viṃdutiyassukhaṃ |  
sālaṃvaṃ kiṃ vijānīyān nirālaṃvaṃ tu naṃtyajet ||  
  
bhāvanā bhāvyate bhāvyaṃ sphuṭaṃ prakaṭagocaraṃ |  
sphurat hlādodayaṃ nityaṃ satatvaṃ pari'kīrtitaṃ ||  
  
p. 96b)  
  
yaścadaṃti parannityaṃ tallayī bhūtavigrahaṃ |  
sarvasamarasānaṃdannistatpaṃca prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
cidacinmathanodbhūtaṃ svasvabhāvarasodbhavaṃ |  
sā naṃdaṃ taṃ vijānīyān nirānaṃdantu tanmanaṃ ||  
  
yatra sarvagataṃ sūkṣmaṃ tallayīkṛta vigrahaṃ |  
nirlakṣaṃ taṃ vijānīyāt sa lakṣaṅkathayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
citprakāśaṃ paraṃ jyoti buddhyā paramayābhyaset |  
dṛśyate parayā dṛṣṭā sālamvamiti kathyate ||  
  
tatvād para kalā kāla vyāptaṃ yena carācaraṃ |  
sākāraṃ taṃ vijānīyān nirākāraṃ tu taṃ tyajet ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi sāktaṃ sāmbhava mānavaṃ |  
lakṣaṇaṃ devadeveśi mahājñānodayaṃ priye ||  
  
icchājñānaṃ kriyā caiva tathā kuṇḍalinī parā |  
mātṛkā paṃcamī ceti śaktiḥ paṃcakamiṣyate ||  
  
icchāyā prasarodbhūta jñānaṃ tatrāvalokanaṃ |  
kāryākārya kriyā caiva kuṃḍalinyā?nmavodhanaṃ ||  
  
mātṛkāmīyate viśvaṃ paṃcadhāśakti lakṣaṇaṃ |  
anunātma svarūpaṃ ca cicchaktiṃ parabhāvitaḥ ||  
  
ādhārabheda yogena kulaśākhā samāśritaḥ |  
sthānaṃ sthānāṃtaraṃ devi viśramaṃti parasparaṃ ||  
  
pṛthagbhedaṃ pṛthak siddhi nadhubhāvena bhāvitaṃ |  
etad devi mayākhyātaṃ ānavaṃ tatprakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
p. 97a)  
  
ādhāraṃ tu kathannātha pṛthak siddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavet |  
viśrāmayogabhedena pṛthak sthānaṃ pṛthak kramaṃ ||  
  
kathayasva prasādena yena siddhāraho bhavet ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi śākhājñānaṃ suvistaraṃ |  
pṛthak siddhiḥ pṛthagbhedamanubhāvena bhāvitaṃ ||  
  
kathitaṃ tava deveśi sarvasiddhiphalaṃ bhavet |  
ādhāraṃ caiva saṃkocaṃ turyajanma tathaiva ca ||  
  
kaṃdaṃ kuṃḍalinī devi kuṃbhākhyaṃ ca tathaiva ca |  
tacai saṃjīvanī sthāna bhūtālāṃ jīvasaṃpuṭaṃ ||  
  
kurmodhāraṃ sparśagaṃ ca lolākhyaṃ laṃvikodaraṃ |  
guruvaktraṃ tathā devi aṃjavaktraṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
viśuddhaṃ ca paraṃ sthānaṃ vaisargika mataḥ paraṃ |  
visargāṃtan tathā devi ṣoḍaśaita prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
ete ṣoḍaśa cādhāre pṛthak siddhi vadāmyahaṃ |  
udgataye viṣadharā svālayecca mahīdharā ||  
  
kampayedakhilā corvī sarvādhāra sthitaḥ priye |  
ākṛṣya sarvalokānāṃ pātāla vicaraṃ viset ||  
  
staṃbhayet sarvasainyāni saṃkocasthena saṃśayaḥ |  
dhvaṃsayed duṣṭa cetāsi unmūla pratipādapān ||  
  
darpe harati nāgānāṃ mārutasyastu sādhakaḥ |  
drāvayed poṣitaḥ sarvān vasī kuryāccarācaraṃ ||  
  
paraṃ saubhāgyamāpnoti janmacakresusaṃsthitā |  
cālayet pratimādīni ākarṣet sūrayoṣitāḥ ||  
  
p. 97b)  
  
plavatetkhatalaṃ yogī kandacakrāvalaṃvakaḥ |  
kuṃḍalyādhāramārūḍha āhvayeta yogiṇī gaṇaṃ ||  
  
vedhayet paravādīni sādhayed yadyadīpsitaṃ |  
pūrayed viśvamakhilaṃ svāraṃdodya? na sādhakaḥ ||  
  
sarvasaṃkrāmaṇaṃ kuryād kuṃbhastho nānya gāminaḥ |  
cittakṣobhavaṣākṛṣṭi apamṛtyu nivarhaṇaṃ ||  
  
vedhadīkṣātma saṃvodhaṃ kuryāt saṃjīvanī gati |  
kūrmādhārasamādhistho yogī parapuraṃ vrajet ||  
  
sarūjāṃ nirūjāṃ caiva nirūjāṃ sarūjāṃ priye |  
sthito jīva puṭādhāre sādhako yogacittakaḥ ||  
  
nidhanaṃ pasthate sarvaṃ sarvasiddhīśvaro bhavet |  
lolākhyaṃ sthānamāsādya bhogāni vividhāni ca ||  
  
prāpnoti sādhakaḥ kṣiprannātra kārya vicāraṇāt |  
laṃvikāṃta sthito yogī kṣutpipāsapalaṃdaret ||  
  
rasaṃ rasāyanaṃ siddhaṃ labhate mṛtyujid bhavet |  
guruvaktraguhāṃtastha sādhako vigatatpṛha ||  
  
avināsa tanurbhūtvā prāpnoti paramaṃ padaṃ |  
visuvasthā mahādevo jagaduddharanakṣamaṃ ||  
  
bhavate nātrasaṃdehaṃ pūjaye yogiṇīgaṇaiḥ |  
vaisargika samārūḍhaṃ sarvajñādi guṇāllabhat ||  
  
hartākartā bhavad yogī yathā deva sadāśivaḥ |  
paracitta gata jñānamatītānāgataṃ ca yet ||  
  
p. 98a)
