rūditaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tatvatovetti sādhakaḥ |  
visargāṃta yathāvasthāni kampā deha varjitaḥ ||  
  
kalākalaṃkārahito bhrājate divi sūryavat |  
sarvakāmeśvarī vīro yogiṇībhiḥ parāvṛtaḥ ||  
  
svānaṃda rasasaṃpūrṇaṃ krīḍatenaṃta varcasaḥ |  
iti me kathitastubhyaṃ harasyaṃ śivabhāvitaṃ ||  
  
ṣoḍaśādhāra yogādhyāṃ svāna bhūtyaika lakṣaṇaṃ |  
sadyaḥ pratyaya kṛddevi vīrāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā ||  
  
svagopyaṃkāra yennityaṃ yathānyonāvadhārayet |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi śāṃbhavasyaiva lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
samaṃ gataṃ layaṃ caiva avabaudhaṃ caturthakaṃ |  
caturddhāṃ bhedabhinnaṃ tu śāṃbhavaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi rahasyaṃ bhuvi durlabhaṃ |  
maṃtravīryaṃ vimarṣaṃ ca svarūpaṃ ca tathodayaṃ ||  
  
etat prasnavaraṃ divyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ ca vadāmyahaṃ |  
mananaṃ sarvavetyatvaṃ trāṇaṃ saṃsāranugrahaṃ ||  
  
mananatrāṇadharmatvā maṃtramityabhidhīyate |  
yasya mūlaṃ parāmṛṣya śaktimūlaṃ tu sarvagaṃ ||  
  
tatpuṃjabharitākāraṃ mahāvyāpti parodayaṃ |  
udito maṃtrarājānāṃ tadvīryaṃ tatsvarūpakaṃ ||  
  
tadvimartha parāmṛṣya maṃtrarājā manusmaret |  
sādhanāt sādhanaṃ devi anyathā jaḍavadbhavet ||  
  
p. 98b)  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi mudrāvaṃdhavarānane |  
svasvarūpa parādṛṣṭirvikāsya nayanodbhavaṃ ||  
  
vadhvāṃjali nābhigataṃ hṛdiciṃtaṃ nidhāya ca |  
vadhvā tu khecarī mudrāmpāśajālasya drāvaṇīṃ ||  
  
sarvaduṣṭa praśamanī sarvavighna vināśinī |  
brahmādi devatāssarvāṃ vadhvā tuṣyaṃti yogiṇī ||  
  
nṛtyaṃti'khecarī cātra khecarī siddhamātarā |  
mātṛkāyogiṇī tasya siddhaṃ dadāti bhairavi ||  
  
pūjākāle tu deveśi pādukā darśanaṃ priye |  
yo vadhvā khecarī mudrāṃ tasya mokṣo dhruvaṃ bhavet ||  
  
punanmūlāvatāraṃ tu kathitaṃ ca varānane |  
yā śrībhagāṃtare sthitvā bhagarūpā bhagodayā ||  
  
bhagadrāvaka yonityāṃ mūlasthānīditāparā ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
kathaṃ tu bhagamityuktaṃ nicaiva tu * kiṃ vidhā |  
bhaganityānvayaṃ divyaṃ kathayasva prasādataḥ ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi bhagannityā ca nirṇayaṃ |  
kathayāmi na saṃdeha tava snehād varānane ||  
  
bhagastrikoṇa vikhyātaṃ dhiyasthaṃ guptamaṃḍalaṃ |  
icchājñāna kriyākoṇaṃ tanmadhye ciṃcinī kramaṃ ||  
  
khasudhārṇava niryātā svabhāsānaṃdarūpiṇī |  
sarvāhlādakarī tṛptā sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
viśvasya jananīyā sā kālagrāsā valaṃvinī |  
pītvā kāmarasaṃ śuddhi sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
p. 99a)  
  
kha kalākhecarāṃtasthā kha caṃdrakalabhakṣiṇī |  
tena pānaparonmatta sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
nirvīja vījayā sattā svavījodbhavarūpiṇī |  
kulakaulāṃtaragatā sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
saṃkocanna vikāsaṃ ca hansaṃ yaṃtra na vidyate |  
tadaṃtarlīna cittasya nityānaṃda pravartate ||  
  
sūryāgni cakramathitaṃ galitaṃ kulacaṃdriṇī |  
tadasaṃyatra saṃtṛpti sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
mahācakriṇi cakrāṃto bhagaliṃgā samāgame |  
prasphūrat tatra madhyesthā sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
āsvāditapicuṃ vaktrairbhagamadhye cidāṃkurāṃ |  
drāvitaṃ viśvajananī sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
parākāya praviṣṭasya paracittasya drāvaṇī |  
parabhūmiṃ parākṛṣya sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
sarvavṛtyāditāyā sā trikabhedaṃ trigarbhiṇī |  
triprakāra triśravaṇī sā nityā bhagarūpiṇī ||  
  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi bhagamūlasya nirṇayaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi praśnaṃ paramadurlabhaṃ ||  
  
paraṃparye tu saṃtānaṃ kathayāmi varānane |  
kulavīrodayaṃ yatra tatra sāṃtodyamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
vyomavyomāṃtaraṃ śaiva mudita taṃ vodhabhāskaraṃ |  
bhāskarādravisaṃjātaṃ rave jātaṃ divākaraṃ ||  
  
p. 99b)  
  
divākarāsadmagarbhaṃ padmagarbhaṃditaṃ jagat |  
cidmayo cidacit teja sarvagaṃ śivavīryakaṃ ||  
  
sarvabhūtāṃtarāvasthaṃ pāraṃparya prakīrtitaṃ |  
kramaṃ cakrāmakaṃ caiva krama oghavinirgataṃ ||  
  
krama oghaṃ tu saṃtāna nirācārapade sthitaṃ |  
ṣaḍiṃdriya parityāgamastraṃ divyaughamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
tadgarbhaciṃcinī sthānaṃ viśramaṃti ramaṃti taṃ |  
tacchāstramiti vikhyātaṃ naṃtu vāgjāla saṃgrahaṃ ||  
  
anyaṃ ca kathitāṃ devī vījasyaiva tu nirṇayaṃ |  
parivārāṃgavistāraṃ nāmajāti * varjitaṃ ||   
  
evaṃ mūlaṃ smṛtaṃ maṃtraṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ vidhisādhanaṃ |  
śabdāvasthā parityajya vodharūpena saṃsthitaṃ ||  
  
cittānaṃdāgra saṃpūrṇaṃ vījasṛṣṭimayaṃ sthitaḥ |  
adhyātmagarbhiṇī vidyā svaprakāsatvamarṣiṇī ||  
  
svavījamaṃtravīryaṃ ca janmakarma kṣayaṅkarī |  
anacchavarṇavikhyātaṃ kaṇṭhatālvoṣṭhavarjitaṃ ||  
  
arghāsyaṃ ca anuccāryaṃ nākṣaraṃ kṣarate kvacit |  
na kṛṣṇavarṇa rakṣaṃ ca tadvarṇaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi pīṭhaṃ pīṭheśarakṣaṇaṃ |  
prathamaṃ kaulikaṃ pīṭhaṃ dvitīyaṃ vinaya kaulikaṃ ||  
  
tṛtīyaṃ siddhakaulaṃ tu divyakaula caturthakaṃ |  
ādi ṣoḍaśakaṃ caiva kādisāṃta dvitīyakaṃ ||  
  
p. 100a)  
  
yādiphāntaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu rūhamaṃ tu caturthakaṃ |  
somākhyaṃ kaulinī pīṭhaṃ sauraṃ vinaya kaulikaṃ ||  
  
siddhakaulaṃ tathāgneyaṃ vidyākhyaṃ divya kaulikaṃ |  
evamātmani saṃsthāni vāhyataḥ kathayāmi te ||  
  
śrīśailaṃ śrīmaheṃdraṃ ca canda dvīpaṃ varānane |  
kailāśaṃ ca caturdevi śivapīṭhamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
pīṭhaśaṃ ca pravakṣyāmi bhuktimukti phalapradaṃ |  
caṃdraṃ kumāra śikharaṃ mahānaṃdaṃ caturthakaṃ ||  
  
guptaṃ guptataraṃ divyaṃ pīṭheśaṃ ca prakīrtitaṃ |  
siddhānāṃ yoginīnāṃ ca śṛṇu vakṣyāmi suvrate ||  
  
ādhāraṃ ca svacakraṃ ca kuraṅgīśaṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
madandanāma deveśi pīṭhasiddha prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
raktākalālā caṃḍākṣī mahocchuṣmā caturthikā |  
pīṭhasiddhā mayākhyātā devyā kaulika rūpiṇī ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
punaranya pravakṣyāmi pūjākrama manuttamaṃ |  
catuṣkaṃ paṃcakaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ trikañca parameśvaraṃ ||  
  
kathayāmi catuṣkaṃ tu sa vāhyābhyaṃtaraṃ priye |  
vuddhistu prathamaṃ pīṭhaṃ manaścaiva dvitīyakaṃ ||  
  
ahaṃkālaṃ tṛtīyaṃ syādeva pīṭhantu unmanaḥ ||  
  
oṃkāraṃ prathamaṃ pīṭhaṃ jālapīṭhaṃ dvitīyakaṃ |  
pūrṇapīṭhaṃ tṛtīyaṃ syādevapīṭhaṃ tu kāmarūpaṃ ||  
  
ete śaktimayāpīṭhā sa vāhyābhyaṃtarāṇi ca |  
pūjanīyaṃ vidhānena siddhānāṃ yogi yutaṃ ||  
  
p. 100b)  
  
oṃkānaṃdaṃ tathā siddha visvānaṃda dvitīyakaṃ |  
tṛtīyaṃ ca kulānandaṃ caṃdragarbha caturthakaṃ ||  
  
pūjānāmaṃ tu deveśi devīputraṃ tu mānasaṃ |  
raktākṣītāra jihvā ca karākṣī somajihvikā ||  
  
caṇḍākṣī agnijihvā ca ucchuṣmā sūryajihvikā |  
pūjanīyā vidhānena guruvaktrā gataṃ priye ||  
  
catuṣkaṃ kathitaṃ devi devyā paṃcaka tacchṛṇu |  
anādi sarvajñatā devī muktayogeśvarī tathā ||  
  
samarī siddha saṃjñā ca kubjikā samayī smṛtā |  
paṃcakaṃ kathitan devi yogaṣaṭkaṃ śṛṇu priye ||  
  
vimalātha prakāraṃ tu kubjikādyā varānane |  
mātaṃgī sikhinīṣasvīsuhirānaṃda suṃdarī ||  
  
nugrahaṃ ṣaṭka kathitaṃ jñānaṣaṭkaṃ śṛṇu priye |  
ājñā tu kubjikā devi māṃtagī śuddhameva ca ||  
  
anāhataṃ mālinī ca maṇipūra khageśvarī |  
svādhisthāne tu jibhrā ca ādhāraṃ tu vijibhrikā ||  
  
jñānaṣaṭkaṃ tu kathitaṃ trikaṃṭha śṛṇu suvrate |  
pāraṃparyavibhāgena trimūrti paravyāpiṇī ||  
  
taṭasthaṃ pūjayed yuṅmaṃ ekavāmaṃ tu bhairavi |  
oṃ miṣaṃ ca punardevi oṃ vali tritayaṃ tathā ||  
  
navasaṃketakaṃ bhadre guruvaktrāṃ tu labhyate |  
gurupaṃkti tathā pūjya saṃtatipyasya yādṛśī ||  
  
p. 101a)  
  
unmūlamūlamāśritya ājñātenāṃtu saṃsphura |  
tatra śrīkramavikhyātaṃ yogiṇīnāṃ tu vallabhaṃ ||  
  
gaditaṃ tatkrama saṃjñā paṃcaratnāni viśrutaṃ |  
trikaṃ ca kathitaṃ devi ṣaṭprakāramataḥ śṛṇu ||  
  
ādhāraṃ guḍamityuktaṃ svādhisthānaṃ tu liṃgakaṃ |  
maṇipūraṃ nābhidaṃtaṃ hṛdaye tu anāhataṃ ||  
  
viśuddhaṃ kaṃṭhadeśe tu ājñā bhrūmadhyasaṃsthitaḥ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi praśnaṃ guptaṃtaraṃ priye ||  
  
divyaṃ bhaumāṃtarikṣāṃ ca trividhaṃ kramanirṇayaṃ |  
bhāṇḍapṛṣṭhe tu deveśi navasaṃketakaṃ priye ||  
  
pūjayet parayā bhaktyā divyaṃ caiva varānane |  
catuṣkā pūrva caivoktaṃ pūjāsaṃtati vistaraṃ ||  
  
vāhyamaṃḍalamadhye tu yathāvibhavamarcayet |  
bhaumānaṃta vijānīyā bhuktimukti phalapradaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi aṃtarikṣa kramaṃ śubhaṃ |  
khacaraṃ khecarāṃtasthaṃ kha svarūpaṃ khamuttamaṃ ||  
  
tejopi vṛṃhitaparaṃ kālicakra kramodayaṃ |  
pūjayecca mahācakraṃ bhāsvaṃtaṃ parameśvari ||  
  
marīci dvādaśayutaṃ bhūriśūrya samaprabhaṃ |  
pūjāparasavodhena kha svabhāvena bhāvitaṃ ||  
  
kha puṣpamaṇḍale pūjya kha mudrāmvanvaye priye |  
kha svarūpānubhāvena pūjayet kha padāṃtaram ||  
  
p. 101b)  
  
khagāṃtarāsane sthitvā viśrāṃtaṃ sūryamaṃḍalaṃ |  
cicchaktigalitānaṃda pūjaye khamarīcayaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi aṃtarikṣa kramaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade saptadaśaḥ paṭalaḥ || 17 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi vṛkṣanāthasya lakṣaṇaṃ |  
rahasyaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ gopitaṃ tāṃtrike kramaṃ ||  
  
guptāguptataraṃ devi paśusaṃgaṃ vivarjayet |  
pravakṣyāmi paraṃ divyaṃ navasaubhāgya bhājane ||  
  
mahākaulārṇavaṃ divyaṃ anaṃtaṃ vimalodakaṃ |  
tanmadhya madhya deveśi caṃdadvīpa samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
paṃcaratnaśilā caṃdradvīpamānaṃdaśeṣaraṃ |  
tatra madhye trikoṇākṣaṃ sthāna yogini vallabhaṃ ||  
  
śṛṃmātamaṃḍarāṃtasthāṃ tadgarbha hṛdayāṃtaraṃ |  
uditaṃ ciṃcinīnātha sarvakāma phalapradaṃ ||  
  
mūlaśākhā suvistīrṇaṃ divyogha phalasaṃbhavaṃ |  
kaulākulaṃ kulonmūlaṃ utpatti śivamaṃḍale ||  
  
svasvabhāvarasāṃ dhyāya sā naṃdāmṛtasaṃbhavaṃ |  
sākhya tritaya vistīrṇaṃ vedavedāṃga patravaṃ ||  
  
puṣpeṃdriya samākīrṇa viṣayāmugamuttamaṃ |  
tatra viśraṃti paramaṃ sukhaduḥkhavivarjitaṃ ||  
  
cidāmodaphalaṃ divyaṃ aṃtavibhavamuttamaṃ |  
evaṃ kramāgataṃ devi kathitaṃ vṛkṣanirṇayaḥ ||  
  
p. 102a)  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi puṣpasaṃketakaṃ priye |  
caturbhṛmānase puṣpaḥ paṃcamaṃ ubhayaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
paṃceṃdriyaṃ paṃcabhūta dvāraṇaṃ paṃcameva ca |  
etat puṣpavaraṃ divyaṃ sarvasādhāraṇaṃ priye ||  
  
purāṇāṃ puṃgalādyānāṃ yoṣayaṃti paraspara |  
pārayaṃti jagatsarvaṃ tasmāt puṣpāḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi puṣpasyaiva tu lakṣaṇaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi guhāgotrayamuttamaṃ ||  
  
guhā ca trīṇī vikhyātā dehasthā tu varānane |  
guptāguptataraṃ divyaṃ akathyaṃ kathayāmi te ||  
  
kadaṃva prathamā devi siddhā caiva dvitīyakaṃ |  
tritayā devi guhāṃ caiva saivyate sarvasiddhiṣu ||  
  
kadaṃva mukhamadhyasthā nābhau siddhavarānane |  
bhagaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi guhādevyāmudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ tubhyaṃ guhā caiva varānane |  
gośabdamamṛtaṃ divyaṃ paṃcaratna samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
tatra madhye mahādevi aparikāgotramuttamaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃketasya tu lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
ūrddhvadṛṣṭi nirīkṣeta dṛśeddivyoghamaṃḍalaṃ |  
saṃketa eṣa vikhyāto jyeṣṭhanāthasya suvrate ||  
  
nāsāgramaṃḍalāṃtasthaṃ divyatejodgavaṃ priye |  
adho dṛṣṭi nirīkṣeta hṛdicittavidhāya ca ||  
  
saṃketa eṣa vikhyāto vālanāthasya suvrate |  
aṃguṣṭhe madhyamāṃgulyā kaniṣṭhā ca varānane ||  
  
p. 102b)  
  
mudrā tritaya saṃketa siddhanāthamudāhṛtaṃ |  
pūjākāle tu deveśi darśanānmokṣado bhavet ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi pīṭhasaṃketalakṣaṇaṃ |  
vyomāvartamukhe kṛtvā nimeṣasthāgata priye ||  
  
oṃkāra pīṭhasaṃketaṃ yogiṇī priyamuttamaṃ |  
karṇaṃ tu dakṣiṇe devi parāṃ dṛṣṭi nipātayet ||  
  
jālapīṭhasya saṃketaṃ siddhayogiṇi vallabhaṃ |  
vāmakarṇa nyased dṛṣṭi pūrṇapīṭhodayaṃ priyaṃ ||  
  
saṃketa eṣa vikhyāta siddhayogeśvarī mate |  
ghrāṇāṃta kāmarūpī ca tatra dṛṣṭi nyaset priye ||  
  
sarvakāma phalat tasya yasya saṃketakaṃ viduḥ |  
pīṭhasaṃketakaṃ bhadre kathitaṃ tava durlabhaṃ ||  
  
sarvasiddhipradaṃ devi saubhāgyajananaṃ paraḥ |  
gopitavyaṃ prayatnena tatrājñā pārameśvarī ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi pīṭhamudrā varānane |  
muṣṭiṃ vadhvākarau devi prasāyāṃguṣṭhakaṃ priye ||  
  
oṃkāra pīṭhamudraiṣā siddhayogini sevitaṃ |  
prasāryahastau deveśi aṃgulyā viralā kṛtaṃ ||  
  
jālapīṭhasya mudraiṣā vadhvā tuṣyaṃ tu yogiṇī |  
hastau tu kuṃbhavat kṛtyā aṃgulyā saha vallabhe ||  
  
pūrṇapīṭhasya mudraiṣā vadhvā dahati kalmaṣaṃ |  
hastau trikoṇavat kṛtvā dvau aṃgulyā samānataḥ ||  
  
kāmarūpīṭha mudraiṣā kāminīnāṃ priyo bhavet |  
tarjanī ūrdhvagā kāryā kiṃcidurnāma pṛṣṭhikaḥ ||  
  
p. 103a)  
  
devī saṃketa mudraiṣā khecarī samadarśanaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi gṛhaṃ sthiti varānane ||  
  
trigarbhagarbhaviśrāṃtaṃ raticakra samudbhavaṃ |  
bhāvitaṃ kulakaulākhyastadgṛhamparikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
sthitvā tadvodha manasā bhāvābhāvavivadvaye |  
krīḍayeṃti kulāmnāye avilupta cidālaye ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi janmasyaiva tu lakṣaṇaṃ |  
caturmādvaravyomnāye avatāra pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
devyāṃvaye prabhāvaṃ ca pūrvapaścimadakṣiṇaṃ |  
uttaraṃ ca tathā devi kāmayārūpamāsṛtaṃ ||  
  
pravakṣyāmi samāsena vallabhatvād varānane |  
guptaṃ guptataraṃ praśnaṃ gopanīyaṃ ca yatnataḥ ||  
  
rahasyaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ āmnāya hṛdayaṃ paraṃ |  
vaktrāvaktragataṃ jñāna yoginī mukhasaṃsthitaṃ ||  
  
khecarācāraguptaṃ ca kalācāramanuttamaṃ |  
bhogamokṣapradaṃ nityaṃmetasārasamuccayaṃ ||  
  
paścimāmnāya deveśi ājñā krama varānane |  
gopanīyaṃ prayatnena tathāpi kathayāmi te ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi gharaṃ pūrvasuvistaraṃ |  
yogiṇī matasāraṃ tu āmnāyaṃ kulaśāsanaṃ ||  
  
pravakṣyāmi samāsena devatā sasvabhāvajaṃ |  
kulakaulāṃtaragataṃ kumudodayakuṃkuṇaṃ ||  
  
p. 103b)  
  
sthānaṃ tatroditā devī svavodhānaṃdarūpiṇī |  
kulācāracaraṃ divyaṃ kulagarbhakulodayaṃ ||  
  
tasmāt kuleśvarī devī kumārī kulabhakṣiṇī |  
yatra vīravaraṃ siddhā vāṃchayaṃti punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
vyomāṃtavyodhamaṭhikā tatra sthānāvatārakaṃ |  
kṛtvā tu devatā devi pūrvānvayamanukramaṃ ||  
  
triprakāragatā sā tu devī tribhuvaneśvarī |  
caṃdriṇī bhāskarī caiva tejotkaṭa varānane ||  
  
caṃdriṇī caṃdragarbhasthā bhāskarī ravi madhyataḥ |  
tejotkaṭā vahnigarbhā maṭhikātrika kīrtitāḥ ||  
  
caṃdriṇī nirgatā devi mīnanāthaṃ varānane |  
bhāskarī meṣapādaṃ ca avatāraṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet ||  
  
tejotkaṭā kūrmanāthamutpannaṃ svasvabhājanaṃ |  
khageṃdranātha sā devi vyomārddhamaṭhikaṃ priye ||  
  
nirgatā tatra madhyā tu paramānaṃdabhairavaṃ |  
tena cādhyāpitaṃ viśvaṃ divyoghaṃ jñānamuttamaṃ ||  
  
maṭhikā siddhasaṃtānaṃ vṛddho vallirudāhṛtaṃ |  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi maṭhikā mūlamuttamaṃ ||  
  
āmnāya siddhanāthaṃ tu avatārayutakramaṃ |  
pravakṣyāmi samāsena śṛṇu svāyatalocane ||  
  
ādyayuge khageṃdraṃ tuṃvijādūbhyāsahāgataṃ |  
mānuṣyaṃ siddhimicchaṃti kaulinī parameśvarī ||  
  
yatra krīḍā prakurvāṇaṃ saṃtatī saṃbhavaṃ tadā |  
visalaśca suśubhaśca teṣāṃ datvā bhiṣecanaṃ ||  
  
p. 104a)  
  
gatvāścakaṃ padaṃ devitasvasmaṃtanabhaṃkṛtaṃ |  
kṛtvā vai moditā loke yo sthitā kulagocare ||  
  
dvitīya kūrmanāthaśca maṃgalā jyotireva ca |  
krīmānāṃ vai kulāmnāyai jātāsteṣāṃ dvayassutau ||  
  
ajito vijiteścaiva teṣā saṃtānakaṃ kṛtaṃ |  
tṛtīyaṃ meṣapādaṃ tu kāmamadga * yā saha ||  
  
krīḍāvāraṃ milītaṃ ca dvayossaṃpadyayostathā |  
vicitraṃ vidhiṃdunāsaṃsaṃ saṃtānaṃ tu śatadvayaṃ ||  
  
eteṣāṃ triṣu lokeṣu parimānaṃ tu saṃtatiṃ |  
kṛtvākha kulanāthena catuḥṣaṣṭhyādhikaṃ kulaṃ ||  
  
siddhastu adhikāraṃ ca saṃtatīmelakaṃ tathā |  
oṃ vallī ca sureśāni vistaraṃ kathayāmite ||  
  
kalāyuge mahāghore caturthamānapādakaṃ |  
piṃgalaṃ nāmatannātha tamāgama * nāmayaṃ ||  
  
gṛhītaṃ jñānasarvasvaṃ mokṣahetu carācaraṃ |  
taṃ jñānaṃ kartike yena sāgare nyasitaṃ tathā ||  
  
tadā saptaṃ tu taṃ krodhā siddheśvara varārcite |  
yāvat koṭyā catuḥṣaṣṭhi muktigā tu bhavārṇavaṃ ||  
  
tāvat kṣatrādhipaṃ vaṃhi vaṭukaṃ ca na saṃśayaḥ |  
anyaṃ ca kathitaṃ devi saṃkṣepānna tu vistaraṃ ||  
  
rājakanyā mahābhāge kuṃkumā tena pūjite |  
jyātitve vimalā'śuddhā tayā krīḍitameva ca ||  
  
utpannā dvādaśā putrā rājaputrā mahāpriye |  
teṣānnāmāni vakṣyāmi yathāvat sva maheśvari ||  
  
p. 104b)  
  
bhaṭṭasvāmarapāpaśca maheṃdravaradevakaḥ |  
āheṃdraśca khageṃdraśca mahīdhara tathaiva ca ||  
  
guḍikānātha pādaśca dvādaśaite prakīrtitaḥ |  
amaro varadevaśca citranāthastathaiva ca ||  
  
alinā cidvapādaṃśca guṭikā ṣaṭprakīrtitāḥ |  
eteṣāṃ sādhikāraṃ tu saṃtatīkṛta suvrate ||  
  
jñānāni tava vakṣyāmi pratyeko saiva suvrate |  
tripurottarasaṃketa siddhasthānaṃ tu taṃ viduḥ ||  
  
amarasya varārohe varadevasya kāmadaḥ |  
citrasya aṭṭahāsaṃ vaidaivikoṭaṃ alisya ca ||  
  
dakṣiṇādi sa viṃdhyasya kolāgiyyāṃ tu goḍikaḥ |  
sarveṣāṃ ca duhārthaṃ vai saṃvisthānaṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi ṣaṇā caiva varānane |  
vrataṃ bhikṣākramaṃ sthānaṃ pṛthak pṛthak vadāmyahaṃ ||  
  
vodho vallīparannātha vrata sā carati priye |  
śrīsailadakṣiṇadiśāṃ dubhālanagaraṃ tathā ||  
  
caryā karoti tatrasthāḥ siddhanātho vara priye |  
vrataṃ datvā munibhi'khya vanannaramuṃ * gīyate ||  
  
śraṃvilpāṃ vāṭikā madhye rugrahītaṃ varānane |  
tenaiva munibhistatra vrata sā caritaṃ priye ||  
  
dvādaśaiva tu varṣāṇi paścāt kaumārikuṃkune |  
gatvā tena mahādevi caryā kuryād varānane ||  
  
śrīvaradeva prabhāḥ valyāṃ vrataṃ sā caritaṃ priye |  
śrīsailapaścime diśā kuṃḍīna nagaraṃ tathā ||  
  
p. 105a)  
  
caryā karoti tatrastho yogābhyāsa mahāmuniḥ |  
tatra sthānaṃ vrate datvā vidyānaṃdasya sā varaḥ ||  
  
divyasiddhivaraṃ devi vīracaryānupālakaḥ |  
yogiṇīvṛṃda sahita krīḍate yatra yatra ca ||  
  
śrīcitranāthaṃ mahādevi pādovallī prakīrtitaṃ |  
śrīsaila uttaradiśāṃ caṃdanannagaraṃ tathā ||  
  
caryā karoti vatrasthā citranātho mahāpriye |  
vilvārkṣaṃ ca phalaṃ yatra vāṭikā tatra madhyataḥ ||  
  
vrataṃ datvā mahādevi kaulasiṃhamunistathā |  
ta kuryād vratacaryāstu svasthāne tu mahātmane ||  
  
dvādaśaiva tu varṣāṇi siddhyate tatra maṃḍale |  
śrī alinātho mahādevi ānaṃdo vallisaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
śrīsailapūrvadiśāyāṃ nagalaṃ vālakaṃ priye |  
puṃgavṛkṣaphalaṃ tatra vāṭikā tatra madhyataḥ ||  
  
vrataṃ datvā varārohe śṛṃgālamuniruttamaṃ |  
tadgatā tu mahādevi kāmarūpīṭhamuttamaṃ ||  
  
tasya dakṣiṇadigbhāge caryāṃ kuryād varānane |  
trikhaṃḍī sthānamāśritya yatra siddho vijṛṃbhati ||  
  
tatra sthāne vrataṃ kṛtvā saptavarṣāṇi suvrate |  
siddhyate paramānaṃda dhyānayukta mahāmuniḥ ||  
  
viṃdhyanātha mahānmāyo yogovallī prakīrtitaṃ |  
śrīsaile tu mahāsthāni pūrvadakṣiṇamadhyataḥ ||  
  
p. 105b)  
  
piṃḍā ca nagaraṃ devi vratacaryā karoti ca |  
khaira vṛkṣavāṭikāyā madhye caiva varānane ||  
  
vrataṃ datvā varārohe sāṃḍilasya mahāmuniṃ |  
paścāṃgatvā sahāviddhaṃ vrataṃ caryā karoti ca ||  
  
khecarī bhūcarī yukta sākiṇī vallabha priye |  
śrīguḍikānātha āvalyāṃ oṃvallī parikīrtitā ||  
  
śrīsaile tu mahādevi pūrva uttaramadhyataḥ |  
goḍikānagaraṃ tatra tatra caryāṃ tapodhanaḥ ||  
  
nārikela phalaṃ yatra tatra madhye tu vāṭikā |  
vrataṃ datvā varārohe caṃdaviṃva munistathā ||  
  
tena tatraiva deveśi aṣṭau varṣāṇi suvrate |  
caryāṃ karoti yogeṃdro vrata yuktā mahāmuniḥ ||  
  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi ṣaḍovalli vratakramaṃ |  
pāraṃparya vibhāgena pūrvāmnāyaṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi dakṣiṇaṃ ghoramuttamaṃ |  
mahāsiddhipradaṃ divyaṃ bhuktimukti phalapradaṃ ||  
  
kāmeśvaryāvatārastu kathayāmi varānane |  
tripīṭhodbhava madhyasthā satsvabhāvānurūpiṇī ||  
  
vālārka satate jāḍyā vidyutkoṭi samaprabhā |  
kāmataḥ kāminīkāmā bhakṣayaṃti svakāminīṃ ||  
  
tasmāt kāmeśvarī devi kumārī kumārī kulabhakṣiṇī |  
kāmapīṭhavaraṃ divyaṃ paradhāmeśvamaṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
kāmeśvaryāvatāraṃ tu kṛtvā kaumāri rūpadhṛk |  
sa svabhāvastu tejena drāvitaṃ janmamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
p. 106a)  
  
tena svavīrya saṃkalpā yāyate kulayogiṇī |  
divyarūpadharāśāṃta śuddhasphaṭikanirmalaḥ ||  
  
jñānasaṃkrāmadivyoghaṃ sphuraṃtī paratejasā |  
dvibhujā ekavaktrā ca trinetrā nimnamadhyagā ||  
  
bālarūpā tu kaumārī yoginī siddhapūji * |  
mahāpīṭha parasthānaṃ gatvā mālini parvataṃ ||  
  
vāmabhāge sthitā devī tasya pṛṣṭhe tu gahvaraṃ |  
kokilākhyammahāsthānaṃ divyaṃ paramanoharaṃ ||  
  
haṃsakāraṃḍavākīṇaṃ cakra vākopa śobhitaṃ |  
khecarī bhūcarī siddhāssākiṇī divyarūpiṇī ||  
  
nivasaṃti mahādevi yogadhyāna parāyaṇāḥ |  
tatra sthāna mahāramye trikoṇe divyamaṃḍale ||  
  
caṃdraviṃvaguhāsreṃ vā caṃdrakāṃti samaprabhaṃ |  
tatra tiṣṭhaṃti sā devī kumārī śukravāhinī ||  
  
pūrvasiddhā mahādevi munīnāṃ ca tapasvinaḥ |  
muniḥ krodhaśucapala mahāraudra varaṃ priye ||  
  
divyaṃ varṣa sahasraṃ tu tapamārādhitaṃ kṛtaṃ |  
kṣīṇagātra mahāvṛddhe vāyubhakṣamanonsanaṃ ||  
  
ūrddhvadṛṣṭi nirīkṣeta sthitvā cāṃtamukhaṃ priye |  
dṛṣṭvā tu devadeveśi śukradevi mahātape ||  
  
ghūrmāvasthāgato devī munibhirdivya tejasā |  
jñānasaṃkrāmanaṃ divyaṃ kṛtvā devāṃ varānane ||  
  
p. 106b)  
  
kāmadevagataḥ sākṣyā divyarūpadharāstute |  
kāmeśvaryā prabhāvena dravanvaṃ bhavate tadā ||  
  
dvauvījāvekataḥ kṛtvā rudrayāmalasaṃbhavaṃ |  
divyatejot kaṭaṃ devi divyakāma phalapradaṃ ||  
  
jñānayogavalautkarṣā kṛtvā tena varānane |  
lakṣapādādhikaṃ devi rudrayāmala saṃhṛtaḥ(?) ||  
  
svasvabhāva svayogena(?) vāgīśvaryāṃ prabhāvakaṃ |  
tasya putrammahādevi kaulīśaṃ tu varānane ||  
  
tenāvatāritaṃ divyaṃ jñānaṃ paramadurlabhaṃ |  
karmasaṃsāravaṃdhānāṃ narāṇāṃ kathitaṃ priye ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi devatānāmanuttamaṃ |  
kāmeśvaryāvatāraṃ tu parivārena saṃsthitaṃ ||  
  
hṛllekhā kledanī kaṃṭya(?) kṣobhayet ma * nāturā |  
niraṃjanā rāgavatī tathānyā madanāvatī ||  
  
khecarā drāvanī caiva tathā vegavatī smṛtā |  
ekāvasaitā devyāstu madano dvādaśa smṛtā ||  
  
cakravyāptaṃ mahādevi ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vahnimaṇḍale |  
arakairatarālaiśca pūjayitvā varānane ||  
  
pārśve tu madanaṃ divyaṃ pūrvārāṃta vyavasthitaṃ |  
madhye kāmeśvarī devīṃ pūjayed divyamaṃḍale ||  
  
ekādaśākṣarā vidyā vajraprastāra coddhṛtā |  
madanaṃ sarasaṃyuktaṃ guruvaktragataṃ priye ||  
  
kāmaṃ vaṃtagakaṃ devi ratiśukraṃ varānane |  
vāmadakṣiṇakaṃ pūjya dvārapālaṃ tu suvrate ||  
  
p. 107a)  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
kathayaśca mahānātha devatālakṣaṇaṃ paraṃ |  
sthānaviśrāṃti paramaṃ saṃjñā caiva pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi devatānāṃ ca saṃvidaṃ |  
nāmasaṃjñā svabhāvosthā adhyātmaṃ kathayāmi te ||  
  
hṛdyāt sausāṃtaragataṃ sāmāsomārkamaṃḍalaṃ |  
tatroditā parā devī hṛllekhyā tu cidāskṣarī ||  
  
śivaśaktistathā rudrā trividhaṃ kledano mayaṃ |  
parāmṛtarasaṃ sāraṃ śravaṃtī kledanī mataṃ ||  
  
ṣaṭkoṇa kuharāṃtasthāṃ śṛṃgāṭa parimaṃḍalaṃ |  
viśrāṃtavaranārāvaṃ tadānaṃdasvanaṃdanī ||  
  
icchāviccakramadhye tu bodhayed gaganāṃtaraṃ |  
tatra kāmakalā nityā kṣobhayet kṣobhanī smṛtā ||  
  
śūnya dvaya samāveśāṭkivaṃdravati nirbhavaṃ |  
yadā pūrṇe pūrṇamāsā tadā sā madanāturā ||  
  
mahāyonyāṃtaraṃ cakraṃ trikāra rasasodbhavaṃ |  
niraṃjanā tatra madhye uditā bodhabhāskarī ||  
  
vahnibhāskara yormadhye caṃdraviṃvaṃ guhāṃtare |  
kāminī rasahot kṛtvā tadārāśravatī priye ||  
  
kāmaṃ kāmāṃtaragataṃ kāmamaṃḍalamadhyagaṃ |  
carcitaṃ hlādamatulaṃ madanāvati saṃkulaṃ ||  
  
ānaṃdasyaṃdinī devī yā rasā sarvagāminī |  
khakalā sā tu vijñeyā caṃdra tu garbhasya garbhiṇī ||  
  
p. 107b)  
  
tridhāgodayamadhye tu viśrāṃtaṃ ravimaṃḍalaṃ |  
baṃdhayeccitkalācaṃdraṃ dravitaṃ drāvaṇī smṛtaḥ ||  
  
caṃdrasya yo bhayaliṃgaṃ mathitaṃ manmathoditaṃ |  
yathānubhāva divyoghaṃ tadā vegavatī smṛtā ||  
  
śivacaṃdrakalābhedaṃ galitaṃ madanodayaṃ |  
tenāhlādita viddhakti praśūtadivyamaṃkuraṃ ||  
  
aṃkurā bhedabhinnaṃ tu nānāḥ prakṛti saṃbhavaṃ |  
tadāsau vyāpako nityaṃ madanotmādarūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
kathaṃ vāgīśvarī divyā tripuraṃ ca kathaṃ bhavet |  
vāgbhavīti kathaṃ devī nityā vai sava bhogiṇī ||  
  
bhagamālini kathannātha liṃgaṃ tritaya bhedinī |  
kāmeśvaryā prabhāvaṃ tu kathayasva prasādataḥ ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
atiguptataraṃ praśnaṃ sarvanityā samudbhavaṃ |  
dakṣiṇaṃ ghoramātmāyaṃ kathayāmi tava priye ||  
  
trikamedāṃtaraṃ kuryāt sphurachṛṃgāṭamaṃḍalaṃ |  
niḥsvabhāvodayaṃ yatra tatra vādodbhavaṃ priye ||  
  
caturbhedā parādyena uditā viśvamālinī |  
tasmād vāgīśvarī sā tu aṣṭadhā kulabhedinī ||  
  
trisvabhāva parāśakti viṣakāmaniraṃjanā |  
aliṃgāliṃginī sā tu tribheda parikīrtitā ||  
  
tripurā sāṃtavijñeyā nirānaṃdasvabhairavī |  
caṃdraviśvaguhāṃtasthā retodyarasavarṣiṇī ||  
  
p. 108a)  
  
svānaṃda svasvanityā ca liṃgabheda dravāvinī |  
śṛṃgāṭamaṃḍalāṃtasthā bhagabhokṣyābhagodayā ||  
  
bhagamālini sasānityā paṃcakāraṇa bhakṣiṇī |  
itaraṃ viṣamityuktaṃ kāmavāṇaprakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
svayastu bījamutpatti tridhālakṣaṃ japaṃ kuru |  
paścābhimukhabhedena yasya liṃgasya yādṛśaṃ ||  
  
tataṃ sthānasamāsṛtya kāmaiśvaryā pravartakaṃ |  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi ghoradakṣiṇamuttamaṃ ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi āmnāya dyaramuttamaṃ |  
śāṃtasvarodaya padaṃ janmādhāraṃti khaṃḍinī ||  
  
tatroditā devi kalā kālī kaulika bhakṣiṇī |  
kaulācāraṃ kaulagarbhaṃ kaulādaya trikaulakaṃ ||  
  
tasmāt kāmeśvarī devī kumārī kulabhakṣiṇī |  
tatrāvatāraṃ kṛtvā tu yatra sthānamaso muni ||  
  
khaṃḍinī sthānaparamaṃ niṣkriya jñānamuttamaṃ |  
kathitaṃ krodharājasya vedhasaṃkramaṇaṃ kṛtaṃ ||  
  
paramāmnāya divyoghaṃ karṇātkarṇa kramaṃ sthitaṃ |  
ślokadvānirbhinnaṃ saṃpradāya parisphuṭaṃ ||  
  
guruvaktragataṃ devi svānubhūtyaika lakṣaṇaṃ |  
kāliḥ kaṃkalasaṃkrāma anākṣapadamuttamam ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade aṣṭādaśa paṭalaḥ ||  
  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
kālibheda kathaṃ nātha dvādaśaiva kathaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
mukhāmnāya kathaṃ nātha kenopāyena saṃkramaṃ ||  
  
kathayasva prasādena yena tuṣyāmyahaṃ prabho |  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi kālikā kramamuttamaṃ |  
dvādaśaiva paraṃ bhadre saṃpradāyaṃ vadāmyahaṃ ||  
  
aviluptaparāvyāpti bhedabhinnā tu svaprabhaṃ |  
vācāmatīta viśāṃti yoganidrā gurormukhāt ||  
  
labhate ca mahājñānaṃ vidyārājena suvrate |  
krodharājena vikhyātam paścād vidyāṃ parityajet ||  
  
kathayāmi mahājñānaṃ nikriyaṃ śṛṇu suvrate |  
ravipradīpako loke sūryamadhyādvinirgataḥ ||  
  
raviraṃtargato bhānu bhāsayatyakhilaṃ jagat |  
bhānavī kaulinī yā sā tatpuṃja paritaṃ jagat ||  
  
tatrotpannā mahāmaṃtrā bhairavāṣṭāṣṭayonayaḥ |  
ravibhānu mayī devī kauleśākula gahvarī ||  
  
kṣobhānaṃda virāmā tu paśyate kulasaṃtati |  
mahāvyomārṇave śaive bhānave kuṃḍamadhyataḥ ||  
  
tatra pralīnāssarve te bhairavāṣṭāṣṭayonayaḥ |  
bhānavī kuṃḍamadhye tu layacakraṃ svabhāvataḥ ||  
  
vilīne svasvabhāvākhyaṃ tatsvabhāvodayaṃ tataḥ |  
bhāvābhāva kṣayo kṣīṇaṃ paścinobhyaśarīriṇaḥ ||  
  
sācidāniśca bhāvatvācchuryākulikṛṣodarī |  
  
p. 109)  
  
tatsvarūpoditaṃ cakraṃ cidbhānvarka gati sthitaḥ |  
pratabiṃbamivābhāti viṃvagrāsaika laṃpaṭaṃ ||  
  
nakulaṃ kaulinī śaktirna svabhāvodayaṃ tataḥ |  
na saṃhārasya saṃhāraṃ divyāsau sarvabhogabhuk ||  
  
icchā cinmātra dharmeṇa apṛthagbhāvavartinī |  
sṛṣṭissarva gatasyaiva saṃhārakathayāmite ||  
  
rasenānaṃdajaṃ rūpaṃ yadā grāhya na gṛhyate |  
yadā pratyastamastatra sa ca taṃ vṛtti gocaraṃ ||  
  
kṣīṇavṛttiḥ pralīnatvājjāyate paramādbhutaṃ |  
trikoṇaṃtatrikoṇasthaṃ suśiraṃ suśirāprataṃ ||  
  
śūnyaśūnyasukhailīnaṃ cittaṃ cittāṃtaro citaṃ |  
cidanādi cidāhānau cuṃvanādi lihāgṛhaṃ ||  
  
kadeṃdriyāṇi saṃyojya parasparavidhi krame |  
hitvā bhāvanna gṛhnāti yada bhāvāṃtara citiḥ ||  
  
tadā tatparamaṃ brahma svasvabhāvaṃ pravartate |  
etat kaulāmṛtaṃ siddhaṃ yoginībhirudāhṛtaḥ ||  
  
niṣkriyānaṃda pādaiśca bhūtale saṃprakāśitaṃ |  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
kathitaṃ kasya vai nāthaṃ niṣkriyānaṃdabhūtale |  
mahākālikramaṃ divyaṃ saṃkrāṃtaṃ kasya saṃkramaṃ ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi saṃkrāmaṃ yasya saṃkramaṃ |  
śilācitinmunivaraṃ tasya putra tapodhanaṃ ||  
  
yogābhyāsarataṃ devi siddhasāvararūpadhṛk |  
vidyānaṃdeti vikhyātaṃ mahādhīravaraṃ priye ||  
  
śmaśānavāsi nityastho nisāṭana rataḥ paraṃ |  
siddhayogeṃdra vīrāśca cakracāra rati priye ||  
  
śivapīṭhaṃ mahādevi śrīsailaṃ devatā priyaṃ |  
tasya uttara digbhāge nānāśikharaparvataḥ ||  
  
tatra hemaṃ mayaṃ divyaṃ guhāsiddhasurārcitā |  
tatrārādhanataṃ kṛtvā vidyā sa viramuttamaṃ ||  
  
karoti bhakti yogīṃdro niṣkriyajñāna vāṃchinaḥ |  
bhaktistīvratarādivyā kṛtvā sāvararūpadhṛk ||  
  
tasya tuṣṭaṃ munivaraṃ śrīniśkriyānaṃdamuttamaṃ |  
amoghavāṇī tasyaiva saṃkrāmaṃ kālikā kramaṃ ||  
  
vāmājñānaṃ tu kathitaṃ paṃcaṣaṭbhūmikā kramaṃ |  
teṣāṃ bhedaṃ ca diṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvaṃ tu pārvati ||  
  
vibhaktād bhava cakrāṃtaṃ gaganaṃ gaganoditaṃ |  
dvādaśāṃka prabhākālī vyomarūpāśca bhakṣaṇī ||  
  
sphurat kṣīṇāsvaraṃ naṃ tatkṣīṇaṃ * divyagocaraṃ |  
kramaṃ saṃhārasaṃhāraṃ pāraṃparyakramānugaḥ ||  
  
svakulaṃ svakulātītaṃ svapadaṃ svapadāṃtaraṃ |  
spṛṣṭvā kālikramaṃ divyaṃ uditaṃ oṃghamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
umanmana padāṃtasthaṃ cidarkodaya maṃḍalaṃ |  
tadbhāvabhāvitaṃ rasaṃ visvogha sphurate krame ||  
  
bhitvā bodhapadaṃ divyaṃ bodhabhāskaravecitaṃ |  
drāvitaṃ cinmarīcībhiḥ pītvā tu rasamuttamaṃ ||  
  
p. 110a)  
  
citsvarūpaparākāśaṃ sadasadbhāvavarjitaṃ |  
tadaṃtaraḥ sararasaṃ parākāsaṃ vijṛṃbhitaṃ ||  
  
ataḥ svollāsaviṣaya nānā vaicitrya citritaḥ |  
avināsaparo kāmi kāli teja samudbhava ||  
  
anaṃta sapta viśrāṃta gaganodita citsvayaṃ |  
sphurat tejo vikāsogha saṃkrāmaṃti paśuṃ valā ||  
  
bhagabhagapadātīta mataṃ tanmatamuttamaṃ |  
kramaṃ kulakulāmnāyaṃ yogiṇī yukti gocaraḥ ||  
  
kāmaṃ kāmāṃtaraṃ kāmaṃ tejaṃ tejeṣu maithunaṃ |  
bhogabhogāṃtaraṃ bhogaṃ matayukti prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
rudraśca rudraśaktiśca yugapadmena bhaktitaṃ |  
sa rudraṃ drāvaka khaṃ khe kaṃ kā ke kulakaulikaḥ ||  
  
śaktimaṃḍadravāṃtasthaṃ bhāvayoge śivāṃtake |  
sa piṃḍassiddhyate rūpī rūpālaya padāṃta kṛt ||  
  
ālamūlottarāsaṃgavottarottaratāṃtaraḥ |  
rudraśaktisamāvesān siddhokto manasāsane ||  
  
guruvaktragataṃ jñāna labhyate svamate mate |  
bodhabhāskaravijñānaṃ karṇāt karṇa krame sthita ||  
  
aṃtargaganayākānitsaṃvidānaṃdanaṃdinī |  
tatsvarūpaparollāsa vikāsaṃ sphurat kaulinī ||  
  
kaulakaṃkālakalayā grāsaghasmararūpiṇī |  
kālīkālāṃjanī bhīmā dvādaśaudita bhānavī ||  
  
kramākramaparaṃ krāma saṃkrāmaṃ kālikākramaṃ |  
sphuratyaṃtargato gharmiranākhyaṃ spaṃdamuttamaṃ ||  
  
cidaciccakramadhyastho yoganidrānubhāvitaḥ |  
śūnyaṃ śūnyāṃtaragato na viṃdati kulātmakaṃ ||  
  
aṃtargalitacidvāma svabhāvapadasaṃvidaḥ |  
anaupamya parollāsa kālicakravijṛṃbhitaḥ ||  
  
brahmādi devatāssarvān bhairavāṃta prakīrtitaḥ |  
līyate ca paraṃ teja kālavahnighanīkṛtaṃ ||  
  
cidākāsaparaṃ guhyaṃ oṃ ditaṃ kulabhāskaraṃ |  
dvādaśāra sutejāḍhyaṃ bhūrisūryasamaprabhaṃ ||  
  
jīvasya jīvasaṃjīvamprakāśayati tanmanaṃ |  
te naiva yukti bhedena pasuṃ vadhayate valaṃ ||  
  
śivādvāmāṃtaraṃ devi saha modita bhāvaṃ na |  
haṭhakramya parāśakti vadhayaṃsmānavigrahaṃ ||  
  
vyomātītaṃ vyomapadamuditaṃ bhānavī kramaṃ |  
jvālā sahasra tejoḍhyaṃ trailokyaṃ grāsaghasmaraṃ ||  
  
tridhāmādaṃyamadhye tu citteja parabhāvitaḥ |  
nirviṣaṃ viṣamākramya kālakūṭavibhakṣitaḥ ||  
  
kulaṃ kulaṃ kulāmnāyaṃ rasaṃ rasasamudbhavaṃ |  
padaṃ padapadātītaṃ sthānakaulikamuttamaṃ ||  
  
garbhasthā garbhaṇī garbhā paṃcagarbha prasūyinī |  
ekāsiddhi trayo nīca udyoga kramamālinī ||  
  
svarādi varṇavimalaṃ sthānaṃratavibhakṣitaṃ |  
tadviśrāma parābhūmiḥ kālitejaḥ prakāśitaḥ ||  
  
bodhābodhayate bodha svabodhānya ravodhitaṃ |  
cakracāravibhedena saṃkrāmaṃti parasparaṃ ||  
  
svabhūmibhūmimākrāṃta khecanmūrddha khamuttamaṃ |  
tadvadvīryā vahāsena piṃḍapiṃḍataradgataṃ ||  
  
kālākālasvakālaṃ ca tyaktvā viśrāṃtayassukhaṃ |  
tatsukhaṃ krīḍate yogī spṛṣṭvā citteja maṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
rūpārūpāṃtaraṃ rūpaṃ svarūpaṃ rūpavarjitaṃ |  
bhāvābhāvavinirmuktaṃ sarvataudita niṣkalaṃ ||  
  
tatroditā parā devī kālī kaṅkālabhakṣiṇī |  
kaṃkālakaṃdalampātraṃ pītvā vyomāmṛtodbhavaṃ ||  
  
ghūrmitā vamitā ye ca tena viśva samudbhavaṃ |  
nijadhāmasvarūpastho yogīyoga valāvṛtaḥ ||  
  
kaṃdakaṃdaraso kṛṣya mahākramavicārakaḥ |  
paraṃbhuktvā paraṃpātvā paraṃ dṛṣṭvā parodbhavaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ samarasaṃ bhūtvā kālikramaṃ vicārakaḥ |  
kalpāṃtakalpitaṃ kalpaṃ kulakalpavikalpitaṃ ||  
  
kālicakramabhedaṃ ca uditā vyaktamaṃḍalaṃ |  
sthūlasūkṣma tathā śūnya tricaitanya layadgataḥ ||  
  
tatradhāmoditā kācidviśvākhya samarīdhinī |  
biṃdunādakṣaye kṣīṇe sthāne citpadamaṃḍale ||  
  
bhāvayed divya yonī ca siddhānāṃ paṃcagarbhinī |  
mahākāla kalāṃtasthā kālacakra karīkalā ||  
  
p. 111a)  
  
tena kālīti vikhyātā kaṃkālakālabhakṣiṇī |  
bhāvābhavasubhāvasya viccakra cidacarvitaḥ ||  
  
svādasaṃbodha hlādena sphurat kālikramodayaḥ |  
bhramadbhramaranirghoṣaṃ līyate yatpare pade ||  
  
tatrodgalita yogeṃdro yogiṇīnāṃ priyo bhavet |  
viśrāṃtabodhavimalo vedhayetkasvamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
kulakāli vibhedena nisroni kramamāśritaṃ |  
kulakāli vibhedena niśroni kramamāśritaṃ ||  
  
garbhādivadgarbha padaṃ bhagabhaṃbhagadrāvakaṃ |  
mahācitkamalānaṃdaṃ vikasadbodhabhāskaraṃ ||  
  
hāsyalāsavilāghā tatadbhrāmya bhrāmya codakaṃ |  
vīrādārahatā karṣa kāli pūjā kramoruhaḥ ||  
  
hānādānavibhedena tyāga grahaparikṣaye |  
narīkṣamānatatvajño jñānārkasaṃprakāśayet ||  
  
viśvākāroditaṃ cakraṃ viśvā sthityāvabhāsrakaṃ |  
viśvasaṃhāriyaṃ tejastastejo grāsaghasmaraḥ ||  
  
vividhena vimārgena haṭhākramya manukramaṃ |  
karoti kramiko yogī sadyogī yoginī priyaḥ ||  
  
khapakṣabhakṣarī bhakṣakakṣa'kṣīṇākṣalakṣagaḥ |  
sphurad ghūrmiratānaṃda nityādita vijṛṃbhitaṃ ||  
  
svasvabodhaparāmṛkṣa bhāvābhāva viparyaye |  
  
p. 112a)  
  
viśrāṃtasutkacidyuktā guruvaktrā turabhyate |  
nādhonorddhena madhye vā na vāhye bhyaṃtarepi ca ||  
  
vismṛtasmayate yatra tatra kāli kramodayaḥ |  
śrīniṣkriyānaṃdanāthena sāvarasaiva bhūtale ||  
  
uktāpaṃcāsikā devi kālikākramamuttamaṃ |  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
śrutaṃ devamayā sarve kālikākramapaddhatiṃ |  
siddhasaṃdohavijñānaṃ pāraṃparya kramāgataṃ ||  
  
adyāpi saṃśayānātha tvayoktaṃ praśnapūrvakaṃ |  
dvādaśārka prabhākālī nāmasaṃjñā kathaṃ bhavet ||  
  
etadākhyā hi me nātha maṃtrapūjā samanvitaṃ |  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi rahasyaṃ kālikāgamaṃ |  
gopanīyaṃ mahābhadre tathāpi kathayāmi te ||  
  
sṛṣṭikāli sthitikālī saṃhāraṃ ca tṛtīyakaṃ |  
raktakālī ca caturthī ca sūkālī paṃcamī smṛtāṃ ||  
  
yamakālī tathā ṣaṣṭha mṛtyukālī ca saptamī |  
aṣṭamī bhadrakālī ca paramārkā navasmṛtāḥ ||  
  
mahāmārtaṇḍakālī ca daśamī parikīrtitaḥ |  
ekādaśī rudrakālī mahākāli dvādaśī ||  
  
etad bhedakramaṃ devi nāmasaṃjñā prakīrtitāḥ |  
svabhāvā svasvarūpā ca vyomāṃte vyomabhakṣaṇī ||  
  
hrī& śrī& maṃtreṇa saṃpūjya dvādaśāre sadoditā |  
madhye tu paramā devi kumārī kulabhakṣaṇī ||  
  
p. 112b)  
  
dvādaśāṃtaṃ tu saṃpūjya pūrvokta vidhi vallabhe |  
gurupaṃkti tathā pūjya pāraṃparya kramāgataṃ ||  
  
vāhye tu madhya pṛṣṭhe ca evameva kramaṃ nyaset |  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi paścimānvayamuttamaṃ |  
kulaparvakulodbhūtamakulaṃ kulavarjita ||  
  
sthānaṃ tatroditā devi pida cicciścinī sphuṭaṃ |  
oghamogha kalānaṃdaṃ sa ca garbhavinirgataṃ ||  
  
tasmāt kubjeśvarī devī kumārī kulabhakṣaṇī |  
kṛtvāvatāraṃ deveśi nugrahārthaṃ varānane ||  
  
caṃdradvīpāvatārasya nirgatā parameśvarī |  
kathitaṃ devadeveśi saṃkṣepānna tu vistaraṃ ||  
  
śrīkubjikāmatasāroyaṃ vistaraṃ kathitasvayā |  
janmāmnāya rahasyaṃ tu catugharasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
kathitaṃ paramaṃ divyaṃ mahisnehād varānane |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi siddhakīrtimanuttamaṃ ||  
  
trigarbhodaya nāthasya śṛṇukīrti vadāmyahaṃ |  
mātrīvanena mahāsthāne ciṃcinī yena pāṭitaṃ ||  
  
punaścotthāpanaṃ kuryā kīrtikhyātimanukramaṃ |  
dvitīya kīrtināthasya bilvavṛkṣa vidāritaṃ ||  
  
punaścotthāpanaṃ kuryād divya kaulena suvrate |  
tṛtīyaṃ kīrti nāthasya vidyādharasupāṭitaṃ ||  
  
guṭikā grāhayed devi kṣiptvā caiva mahātape |  
taḍāge ciṃcinī nāmnā snātvā khagati māpnuyāt ||  
  
p. 113a)  
  
vidyādharaṃnugrahītaṃ paścāt tatraiva suvrate |  
khegatiḥ kurute tena kīrti syāt parameśvarī ||  
  
anyāni ca taḍāgāni kṛtvā nāgavaraṃ priye |  
anugrahītaṃ phaṇi varaṃ vitaṃkaṭanu nāmakaṃ ||  
  
akhaṃḍamaṇḍalākāraṃ ājñāsiddhi prakīrtitaṃ |  
śatayojanakaṃ devi paśuṃ vedhayate kṣaṇāt ||  
  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi siddhakīrtimanukramāt |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi adhikāra trayaṃ priye ||  
  
ovalli tritayaṃ devi śṛṇusvāyata locane |  
trimūrtiṃ ca trigarbhaṃ ca ṣaṭprakāramudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
kramasaṃtati kṛd devi jyeṣṭhamadhyavavālakaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi ṣaṭśrotasyaiva lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
śabdaṃ sparśaṃ tathā rūpaṃ rasaṃ gaṃdhāśca paṃcamaṃ |  
manaḥ ṣaṣṭhavijānīyācchotavyaṃ tat prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
mayā tu vyāpinī śaktissarvadehāṃtare sthitāḥ |  
ṣaṭ prakāra gatā sā tu ṣoḍaśādhārabhedinī ||  
  
paṃcavyomāṃtare devi trilakṣapathamadhyagā |  
ṣaṭcakra vyāpinī sā tu sarvabhāṣamana smṛtā ||  
  
nāḍi madhyagataṃ vāyu vāyurmadhyagataṃ nabhaṃ |  
nabho madhyagataṃ śaktiḥ śaktimadhyagataṃ śivaḥ ||  
  
śivāt paratarannāsti ityājñā pārameśvarī |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi paṃcapraśnaiva nirṇayaṃ ||  
  
p. 113a)  
  
maṃḍalottāraṇaṃ devimmaṃḍalaṃ maḍalakramaṃ |  
maṃḍalārtiṃ tathā devi saptāviṃśati maṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
pravakṣyāmi samāsena śṛṇusvāyata locane |  
maṃḍavrajanamityukta svarūpottaraṇaṃ priye ||  
  
viśrāmamaṃḍalaṃ jñeyaṃ kramānaṃdakramodayaṃ |  
artiṃ prakāśavijñānaṃ kramāgrena tu yojayet ||  
  
evaṃ vidhavidhānena sarvasiddhāraho bhavet |  
maṃḍale madanannāma paścime siddhi pūjayet ||  
  
uttare sahajannāma bhāvamaṃḍalapūrvakaṃ |  
abhāvamaṃḍalannāma dakṣiṇaṃ diśi pūjayet ||  
  
kramamaṃḍalamadhye tu pūjayet paṃcakaṃ tathā |  
anaṃtaṃ mahataṃ vyoma śūnyaṃ akhaṃḍamaṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
trailokya ghaṭapūrṇaṃ ca akṣayaṃ ca tathaiva ca |  
prabhāmaṃḍalasūryaṃ ca somamāgneya maṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
paṃcaratna trikoṇaṃ ca paṃcatatva punaḥ priye |  
paṃcavyomaṃ tridhāśūnyaṃ ātmamaṃḍalameva ca ||  
  
vyāpti maṇḍalakaṃ devi ajapavijayaṃ tathā |  
kulakaulaṃ guru siddhaṃ yogiṇī maṃḍalaṃ priye ||  
  
evaṃ vidhivicāreṇa nāma bheda na suvrate |  
pūjayet kramavākyaṃ tu ityājñā pārameśvarī ||  
  
īṣat pakvasupiṣṭhena kuryād vedā gulonnataṃ |  
dīpāṃ tu marukākārāṃ trikoṇāṃnati śobhanān ||  
  
karṣājyagrāhiṇaḥ kuryānnava saptātha paṃca vā |  
  
p. 114a)  
  
aṃtastejo vahisteja ekīkṛtya mitaprabhān |  
tridhādevya paribhrāmya kuladīpaṃ nivedayet ||  
  
samastacakracakreśi yute devi tathāṃvike |  
ārātrikamidaṃ devi gṛhāṇa mama siddhaye ||  
  
kuladīpān pradaśyātha śaktipūjāṃ samācaret |  
punaranya pravakṣyāmi dīpabhakṣaṇapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
arghapātra kramaṃ devi śṛṇu vakṣyāmi suvrate |  
caṃdrasūryodayāṃtasthaṃ dīpaṃ viśvāvatārakaṃ ||  
  
uddīpa snehamamṛtaṃ parānaṃda rasodbhavaṃ |  
sukhavartī chayā devi dhāraṇā dhāramaṇḍale ||  
  
jñānadīpaṃ svavimalaṃ biṃdunālokabhāṣakaṃ |  
tat teja tejayet teja vāhya dīpaṃ prakāśayet ||  
  
sālicūrṇena saṃskṛtya dāpayet kramasannidhau |  
susṛṣṭannirmalaṃ śuddhaṃ snehapūrṇaṃ suśobhaṇaṃ ||  
  
pūjayecca vidhānena krameṇa kramavallabhe |  
tuṣyaṃti khecarī siddhā mahābhairavabhairavī ||  
  
dīpaṃ prajvālya deveśi sannidhānaṃ bhavaṃti hi |  
gītavādyaṃ tathā nṛtyaṃ stotrabhakti parāyaṇa ||  
  
aṣṭāṃga praṇipātena prārthayeccarukaṃ priye |  
grahayecca punardevi vaṃdayecca muhurmuhuḥ ||  
  
prāśayed divya carukaṃ paraṃ saubhāgyadāyakaṃ |  
janmāṃtaragataṃ pāpannāśayecca varānane ||  
  
paścād dīpaṃ pravakṣyeta parādṛṣṭi nirīkṣataṃ |  
dvautejo ekata kṛtvā kṛtakarma daheddhruvaṃ ||  
  
vastramāchādyajatnena nirvighnaṃ ca yathā bhavet |  
tadya tu bhakṣayed dīpaṃ yo mārga prakāśakaṃ ||  
  
śālicūrṇena kartavyaṃ guḍasenva ca saṃyutaṃ |  
vyomāvartaṃ trikoṇaṃ vā uchvāyā caturāṃgulaṃ ||  
  
athavā tryaṃgulaṃ devi trikoṇaṃ kārayet priye |  
sarvavighnopraśamanaṃ sarvaduḥkhanivāraṇaṃ ||  
  
sarvopatāpasamanaṃ kramadīpaṃ samuddharet |  
kumārī pūjitaṃ devī śyāmavarṇaṃ sulocanaṃ ||  
  
vyomāsanasthaṃ ghūrmāṃtaṃ vīrapānapariplutaṃ |  
pūjayettavidhānena puṣpasagdāmabhūṣitam ||  
  
caturbhujāmekavaktrā trinetraṃ divyarūpiṇī |  
idṛgrūpa dharāṃ devi ciṃtayed vyomamaṇḍale ||  
  
kumārīṃ sukumārīśca kulakaulakramāgataṃ |  
prārthayed vividhai stotrairaṣṭāṃgaiḥ praṇipātayet ||  
  
paścādājñā gṛhītaṃ tu dīpaṃ prajvālya suṃdarīṃ |  
tadvaktroditatatteja tatteja dīpamuccaret ||  
  
kramamaṇḍaladātavyaṃ sannidhānaṃ tu devatāṃ |  
karoti vividhākārā bhuktimukti phalapradā ||  
  
vāmālāmā tu sākinyā khecarī bhairavī smṛtā |  
nṛtyamānā tu tā devi prakāśakramamaṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ vidhi kramāyātaṃ kathitaṃ dīpalakṣaṇaṃ |  
gopanīyaṃ prayatnena na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit ||  
  
p. 115a)  
  
pālanāt samayācārā siddhirbhavati sāsvatī |  
pātraṃ tu alinā pūrvaṃ śivapuṣpasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
ubhayānaṃdajaṃ devi yadi yogyā bhavet sukhī |  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
jyotī ca kīdṛśī nātha kartavyā sādhakena tu |  
kathayasva prasādena * ye niḥsaṃśayaṃ bhavet ||  
  
bhairavovāca ||  
  
jyotī ca subhagākāyā śīlaśuddhā tapasvinī |  
svabhāvaratasā naṃdā sukrādyā śubhagā priye ||  
  
kṣemāśīlā kritakrodhā satyavāk priyavādinī |  
kramabhakākramaratā kramavedha kramodayā ||  
  
kramacāra ratā devi suśvāra kramavartinī |  
suguptāyāgakāle ca samayedyadi puṣpitā ||  
  
tadā siddhimavāpnoti ityājñā pārameśvarī |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi nigrahānugrahaṃ priye ||  
  
piṃḍādhāraṃ piṇḍagarbha piṃḍāṃtaṃ piṇḍanirgataḥ |  
tatpiṇḍavyāpakaṃ viśvaṃ sarvaṃ jānāti sarvagaṃ ||  
  
saṃcārakramabhedena saṃkrāmaṃti parasparaṃ |  
mukhāmnāya rahasyaṃ tu yoginī saṃpradāyakaṃ ||  
  
mahāmaṃthānamathitaṃ kālacakra vibheditaṃ |  
svasvarāṇi ca tejoṃtu ciṃciṇī kramasaṃsphuraṃ ||  
  
sphuranmānogha vimalaṃ paramātmā sa ceṣaṇaṃ |  
nirāveśa svarūpeṇa spṛśed divyoghamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
yanmukhaṃ jayate bhadre tanmukhaṃnugrahaṃ pare |  
  
p. 115b)  
  
nigrahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi maṃtrabhedena suvrate |  
devyānāmādi varṇaṃ ca uddhṛtaṃ parameśvari ||  
  
ulakaṃ sahavarṇaṃ ca paṃcaviṃśayutaṃ priye |  
tejarūḍhaṃ vāyuyutaṃ rudraśakti samanvitaṃ ||  
  
arddheṃdu vindasaṃyuktaṃ bījaṃ saṃhāramuttamaṃ |  
sudhivarṇaṃ tridhā kṛtvā sarveṣāṃ varavarṇinī ||  
  
ati dīrghaṃ triyayuktaṃ maṃtraṃ tridaśamuttamaṃ |  
devyāmādyakṣarāssarvaṃ pānujena samanvitaṃ ||  
  
tena yuktā mahādevi ekādaśasamanvitaṃ |  
śrīpūrveṇa samāyuktaṃ devyānāmasamuccaret ||  
  
etanmaṃtravaraṃ divyaṃ maṃtramaṃtreśvarādhipaṃ |  
mahāsaṃhārasaṃhāraṃ devaṃ tribhuvaneśvarī ||  
  
nigrahaṃ ṣaṭkamityuktaṃ viśvagrāseka laṃpaṭaṃ |  
bījobhayaṃ ca ṣaṭkaṃ ca vakṣyāmi tava suvrate ||  
  
dvādaśāṃtargatā śakti bījarūpā tapasvinī |  
sṛṣṭisaṃhārabhedena hrasvadīrgha kramodayaṃ ||  
  
dvādaśasvarabhedena hrasvadīrgha pariplutaṃ |  
hrasvaṣaṭkañcandrakramaṃ dīrghasūryamiti priye ||  
  
ubhayaṃ bījaṣaṭkañca kathitaṃ tava suvrate |  
  
iti śrīvārāhītantre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade unaviṃśati paṭalaḥ || 19 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi carumudrāṃ ca vallabhā |  
dṛṣṭipāta tathā divyaṃ śṛṇuvakṣyāmi suvrate ||  
  
cullasthānaṃ tu saṃsodhya gomayenopalepitaṃ |  
  
p. 116a)  
  
arghapuṣpaṃ dadeddhūpaṃ tilasarṣapa prastaret |  
prakṣyālya carukaṃ divyaṃ saṃskārāgniṃ pradīyate ||  
  
kapilākṣī lamādāya taṇḍulaṃ śobhanaṃ kṣipet |  
athavā ye naddravyeṇa carukaṃ sādhayet priye ||  
  
uttamādhamamadhyena nirvikalpena sādhakaḥ |  
kartavyaṃ divyacarukaṃ punaprakṣyālyate priye ||  
  
lepanaṃ śobhanaṃ datvā puṣpadhūpārghamarcaye |  
vastramāchādyayatena ānītaṃ yāgamaṃḍape ||  
  
astramaṃtreṇa prokṣata svamudrāṃ vandayet priye |  
parā dṛṣṭi nipātena sarvavighnanivāraṇaṃ ||  
  
kramamaṇḍalanaivedyaṃ mūlamaṃtreṇa sādhakaiḥ |  
paścādājñā gṛhītaṃ tu carukaṃ grāhayet priye ||  
  
śiraśca vatkamāchādya tadā carukamāharet |  
sarvavighnavināśāyaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃ bhavet ||  
  
acirāt siddhimāpnoti ityājñā pārameśvarī |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi nityanaimityalakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
ciccakracarcitā nityaṃ carubhakṣārati priye |  
viśrāṃtrotpadasaṃcāra nityameva prakīrtitā ||  
  
sarvasaṃpūrṇaciddhṛtti bhāvayet svasvamaṇḍalaṃ |  
yāvanna kiñcittajñeya bhallayī bhūtavigrahaṃ ||  
  
bodhabhāskaramārūḍhanaimittikamudāhṛtaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi praśnānāñcatura smṛtaṃ ||  
  
dīkṣā jyeṣṭhaṃ sthāna jyeṣṭhāṃ ājñā jyeṣṭhaṃ tṛtīyakaṃ |  
kramaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ caturthaṃ hi adhikaṃ kotra ucyate ||  
  
p. 116b)  
  
dīkṣānirvājanagarbhe ājñāsaṃsphura nityasaḥ |  
sthānaṃ viśāṃti paramaṃ jīvamukti kramaṃ labhet ||  
  
evaṃ vicārayed devi jyeṣṭhānukramakārakaḥ |  
tasmāt sarva prayatnena krama jyeṣṭhā hi pūjyate ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu svāyata locane |  
dīpaṃ caruṃ ca puṣpaṃ ca arghapātravidhi kramaṃ ||  
  
kīdṛśasya ca dīrye tat sādhakasya varānane |  
śiṣyasya ca suvītasya gurubhaktasya dhīmataḥ ||  
  
sraddadhānasya vīrasya jitakrodhasya nispṛhaṃḥ |  
satyavāk priyavādinya abhayaṃ bhaya bhāvitaḥ ||  
  
kramabhaktānubhāvā ca tyāgī dharma parāyaṇa |  
bindunādāntara gatajñāna yoga sadātyasaḥ ||  
  
vinayī devatā saktā aṣṭāṃga praṇipātita |  
yajñapājīnityaraṃta svādhyāyī ca tapasvināḥ ||  
  
samayācāra yuktasya guruvākyaratasya ca |  
nityānaṃda svabhāvajño dhīro vīrakramānvitaḥ ||  
  
yuktaṃ yuktarataṃ divya cakrāchiṣṭasya bhājanaḥ |  
siddhasaṃtānapārajñā paścimāmnāya bhājanaḥ ||  
  
kṣemāparaśca tejasvī dhairyavān bodhabhāskara |  
mānāvamānanirmukto vīradravyābhilāsikaṃ ||  
  
śīlasaṃketaniratā divyakaulavicārakaḥ |  
īdṛśasya tu dātavyaṃ carudīpaṃ varānane ||  
  
puṣpakramavidhānena yena siddhāraho bhavet |  
deśikaḥ siddhimichaṃti tadā guṇavicārayet ||  
  
p. 117a)  
  
nirguṇe yadi tadātavyaṃ siddhihānirbhaviṣyati |  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena deśikaśca vicārayet ||  
  
punaranyaṃ prvakṣyāmi śṛṇusamyak vadāmyahaṃ |  
ekādaśa prasnaparaṃ tvayoktaṃ prasnapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
vakṣyāmi tava deveśi paścimānvayamuttamaṃ |  
kramajñānaṃ kramajñoyaṃ kramalakṛṃ kramodayaṃ ||  
  
kramabhedaṃ kramoddāṃ cakramātītastu kṛṣyate |  
kramasiddhi kramābhyāsamakulaṃ ca kulaṃ tathā ||  
  
etad vakṣyāmyahaṃ bhadre vallabhātvadvarānane |  
prāṇāpānadvayonmadhye yatkiṃcidupalabhyate ||  
  
kramajñānaṃ vijānīyāt svarūpasthopalakṣaṇaṃ |  
tasmānubhavabhāvena tallayī kṛtavigrahaṃ ||  
  
yadā na viṃdate kiṃcit kramajñeya * dā bhavet |  
yā dṛṣṭi dṛṣṭi tatvānāṃ bhedatrayavivarjitaṃ ||  
  
sā dṛṣṭvā sarvagāyena sa yogī kramalakṣakaḥ |  
vastvaṃtaraṃ vastu śūnyaṃ bhāvagrāhya bhavādbhavaṃ ||  
  
bhāvācāracaraṃ nityaṃ tatvacāraṃ kramodayaṃ |  
ṣaṭprakāra kramaṃ bheda vimalaṃ sarvatodayaṃ ||  
  
viśuddhi ṣoḍaśai bhedairdvādaśaistu anāhataṃ |  
daśabhirmunibhirbhinnaṃ svādhisthānaṃ ṣaḍātmakaṃ ||  
  
ādhāra bhedāścatvāra ājñā bhedaṃ dvikantathā |  
etadbhedavaraṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kramabhedaṃ samucyate ||  
  
kramogha śṛṇu deveśi yathā sampa * dāmyahaṃ |  
vidyādharottara gate anugarbheśca maṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
p. 117b)  
  
vyāpakaṃ vyāptimakulaṃ ciṃcinī sphuravigrahaṃ |  
kramoghaṃ kramasaṃtānaṃ śivaśakti samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
saṃturājñā sphuraṃti ca vedhayen mātṛmaṃḍalaṃ |  
hṛdayaṃ yogiṇī padmaṃ prasphuraṃ jīvamaṃḍalam ||  
  
hlādayeccetanā śakti paratatvan prakāśayet |  
paṃcatatva layaṃ tatvā drāvitaṃ vyomamaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
labdhvā tu hṛdayānaṃda paṃcāvasthā pravartate |  
ānaṃdoścodbhavaḥ kampa nidrā ghūrmistu paścimaḥ ||  
  
tatvavidvasya deveśi paṃcāvasthā pravartate |  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
avasthā kīdṛśī nātha svānubhāvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet |  
kathayasva prasādena yena tuṣyāmyahaṃ tava ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi avasthā lakṣaṇaṃ śubhaṃ |  
ānaṃda jananaṃ pūrvaṃ parāhlādaṃtaraḥ sukhaṃ ||  
  
divyogha ūrddharomāni ājñāsiddhi pravartate |  
marīci cakra dravitaṃ nābhiraṃdhravikāśitaṃ ||  
  
ddhaniṣṭampaplavo nityaṃ hāsyarāvaṃ pramucyate |  
eṣāvasthodbhavā yogī ājñāsiddhi pravartate ||  
  
dvāsaptati sahaḥsrāṇi nāḍīraṃdhraprapūrayet |  
svānaṃdāghana divyena mahāpiṇḍaṃ prakampayet ||  
  
vyomavadbhramate bhūmau bhavavaṃdhavimardayet |  
kampāvasthā bhaveddhyeṣa ājñāsiddhi pravartate ||  
  
sarvabhāvaparityajya śāṃtabhūmau samāviśet |  
  
p. 118a)  
  
grāhyagrāhyagrahāśreṣṭā vyomavyomāṃtara sthitā |  
tadā hlāda parānandā yoganidrātmabodhakaḥ ||  
  
nidrāvasthā bhavet hyeṣa ājñāsiddhiḥ pravartate |  
caturbhivasthāsaṃtṛpto yogī brahmāṇḍabhedakaḥ ||  
  
parānaṃdarase pūrṇaṃ puṇyamānāpi nityasaḥ |  
ājñāsaṃkramaṇaṃ divyaṃ nityānaṃdakaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
eṣāghūrmodayāvasthā ājñāsiddhiḥ pravartate |  
avasthā kathitaṃ devi rudraśaktiḥ prabhāvataḥ ||  
  
rudraśaktisamāveśāt siddhyate svātmamaṇḍalaṃ |  
anākhyaṃ ca nirābhāṣaṃ tritatvaṃ ca nirāśrayaṃ ||  
  
avyaktamaṇḍalāṃtasthaṃ kramātītaṃ kramodayaṃ |  
vikāśya nayanonmeṣa yatra dṛṣṭirnirīkṣate ||  
  
tatra bhāva parikṣīṇe kramabhyāsasya ucyate |  
sarvasaṃkalpakṣīṇepi nityānaṃdaḥ pravartate ||  
  
nivartate citsvabhāvaṃ mokṣalakṣmīśca siddhyati |  
avyaktamaṃḍalaṃ jñeyaṃ vyaktijasya na labhyate ||  
  
paṃcabhautikanirmuktaṃ makulaṃ ca prakīrtitaṃ |  
tasya chāyā parāśakti śuddhātaddharma dharmiṇī ||  
  
sā kuleti samākhyātā parānaṃda phalodayā |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃjñā bhedasya lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
ātulanavasaṃketa kukāratritameva ca |  
nugrahaṃ ṣaṭkavijñeyād devī saṃjñā ca paṃcakaṃ ||  
  
trimūrti trikasaṃjñā ca pāraṃparyakasaṃjñakaṃ |  
  
p. 118b)  
  
saptāviṃśati saṃjñā ca etad bheda varānane ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi parvāṇāṃ catulakṣaṇaṃ |  
kṛṣṇapakṣe tu aṣṭamyāṃ phālguṇe pūjayen mudā ||  
  
jyeṣṭha nāthasya ovalli varyānāthasya saṃjñikā |  
tasya parvāti taṃ devi pūjanīya prayatnataḥ ||  
  
bhukti mukti pradaṃ devi ājñāsiddhi phalapradaṃ |  
tasya parva idaṃ devi sarvachidranivāraṇaṃ ||  
  
nichidro bhavate sopi devatā priya naṃdanaḥ |  
caitramāse tu cāṣṭamyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe tu pūjayet ||  
  
madhyamā valli nāthasya padmānaṃdasya khecaraḥ |  
tasya parva idandevi sarvachidra nivāraṇaṃ ||  
  
vijñāna lābha paramaṃ devatānāṃ priyo bhavet |  
siddhasādhanamartyānāṃ dātavyaṃ pūrvapūjanaṃ ||  
  
kṛṣṇapakṣe tu aṣṭamyāṃ śrāvaṇe pūjayet priye |  
vālovalli kramaṃ siddhaḥ kamalannāma sundari ||  
  
parva'saubhāgya jananaṃ pūjanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ |  
parvaṇastasya māhātmyaṃ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi suvrate ||  
  
siddhakhecaramātṝṇāṃ vāmā * lā tu sākinī |  
vīrāmukte śikhāraudrī gaurīkāmasukhā smṛtā ||  
  
ekanetra trinetrā ca caturvaktrānyanekadhā |  
viḍālī siṃhavaktrā ca nānārūpadhara priye ||  
  
tuṣyaṃti siddhimichaṃti sādhakasya varānane |  
ekācānvaya vīrāṇāṃ ājñāsaṃsphuritā bhavet ||  
  
p. 119a)  
  
duḥkhaśokavinirmuktaṃ bhogamokṣaphala pradaṃ |  
doṣadāridrya samanaṃ parvacaitra prapūjayet ||  
  
trayovallikramaṃ divyaṃ sarvaṃ ca kathitaṃ priye |  
punaranya pravakṣyāmi ājñāśiṣyasya lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
deśikena pradātavyaṃ sādhakasya varānane |  
ājñābhiṣeka deveśi śṛṇu vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
triprakārābhiṣekaṃ tu kulaṃ tatra kramaṃ priye |  
ādau tatra kramaṃ vakṣyadabhiṣekaṃ tu deśikaiḥ ||  
  
dātavyaṃ sādhakeṃdrasya vakṣyāmi tava pārvati |  
yāgaṇehaṃ tu saṃsodhya bhūmibhāgaṃ suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
kṛtvā tu deśikeṃdreṇa yāgaṃ prastārya suvrate |  
māṃgalyaṃ sarvato bhadre tatra pūjāṃ tu kārayet ||  
  
kalaśa paṃcabhiḥ pūjya toyapūrṇaṃ varānane |  
sarvoṣadhi samāyuktaṃ saptavrīhi samanvitaṃ ||  
  
vacākuṣṭa hiraṇyaṃ ca sarṣapātilameva ca |  
sahadevena saṃyuktaṃ lājyapuṃgahalānvitaṃ ||  
  
caṃdanaṃ raktamaillepya arghapuṣpādi pūyakaṃ |  
maṃtramūrti tathābhyarcya kalaṣaṃ paṃcakaṃ priye ||  
  
hiraṇya raupyatāmraṃ ca alāṃbunmṛmayaṃ kṛtaṃ |  
pūjayed devi keṃdraistu ekacitta samāhitaḥ ||  
  
svastikaṃ maṃḍalaṃ kṛtvā paṃcaratna yutendriya |  
tatropaviśya deveśi pūrvābhimukhasādhakaṃ ||  
  
adyārgha paṃcabhirdevi kalasaṃ paṃcasaṃyutaṃ |  
gītavāditrasaṃyuktaṃ śaṃkhaduṃdubhireva ca ||  
  
p. 119b)  
  
maṅgalaṃ maṅgalārthañca gīyate ca varānane |  
paścādabhimukhācāryaṃ abhiṣakaṃ tu dāpayet ||  
  
yajñopavītakaṃ te ca pādukā dīyate priye |  
svastikañcākṣamālā ca homabhāṇḍa tathaiva ca ||  
  
samayo śrāvayet paścād gachatvaṃ deśiko bhavaḥ |  
paśunistāraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhūtamārge carācare ||  
  
taṃtrābhiṣekaṃ kathitaṃ kulācāryastu kathyate |  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi vastu yogaṃ suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
catuṣkoṇaṃ caturdvāraṃ kṣetrapālasamanvitaṃ |  
madhye tu vartulaṃ kṛtvā lohitaṃ bhrāmakārayet ||  
  
tatpṛṣṭhapaṭṭamādāya vastreṇa chadyasuvrate |  
punalohitavastreṇa tatpṛṣṭhe pūjayet kulaṃ ||  
  
madhye kuleśvarī devī kulanāthena saṃyutaṃ |  
paścāt kulāṣṭakaṃ devi pūjayecca prasannadhī ||  
  
aṣṭāṣṭakaṃ tataḥ pūjyaṃ siddhasaṃtāna pūjayet |  
kṣatrapālaṃ tu vaṭukaṃ vighnaśaṃ tu varānane ||  
  
evaṃ kramavicāreṇa kulapūjāṃ tu kārayet |  
paścāṃ tu pūjayed devi aṣṭau kalaṣapaṃktibhiḥ ||  
  
maghādi vīradravyena pūjayecca varānane |  
jāyaphalaṃ puṃgaphalaṃ bilvaṃ caiva hiraṇyakaṃ ||  
  
sahadeva vacākuṣṭaṃ sarvoṣadhi samanvitaṃ |  
siddhārthakaṃ tathā vrīhi cūtapallavasobhitaṃ ||  
  
caṃdanaiḥ kuṃkumailepya arghadhūpasugandhibhiḥ |  
  
p. 120a)  
  
puṣpairnānā vidhairdevi arcayeta yathāvidhiṃ ||  
  
brahmādyā devatāścāṣṭau kalaśe pūjayet priye |  
hrī& śrī& maṃtreṇa saṃpūjya aṣṭottaraśataṃ japet ||  
  
devatā pūjayeccāṣṭau aliphalguṣabhojanaṃ |  
sa tṛptā tu varārohe nānābhojanabhojitaṃ ||  
  
sānaṃdaṃ nṛtyamānā ca sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā |  
akārarāvaravakāmuktakeśāvarānane ||  
  
kalaṣagrāhayeddastau samāviṣṭavara priye |  
sādhakasyābhiṣekaṃ tu datvā ca varavarṇini ||  
  
gachaputra kulācārya vicaratvaṃ mahītale |  
anuprahaṃ ca martyānāṃ yathechaṃ kuru deśikaḥ ||  
  
bhukti mukti pradannityaṃ devatākulayoginī |  
dadaṃti sādhakasyaiva ityājñā pārameśvarī ||  
  
kulābhiṣekaṃ kathitaṃ rahasyaṃ paramaṃ padaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi karmācāryābhiṣecanaṃ ||  
  
ājñāsiddhi pradaṃ nityaṃ divyasparśa svarūpakaṃ |  
kathayāmi na saṃdeho vallabhatvād varānane ||  
  
sa jīvamīnayuktena surayā pūritena tu |  
paṃcāmṛtena saṃpūrṇaṃ śaṃkhena kalaśena vā ||  
  
pūjitā tu kumārībhirāmnāyagharasaṃtati |  
kuleśvarī kubjikā ca kālī kāmeśvarī smṛtāḥ ||  
  
puṣpadhūpasugaṃdhaiśca caṃdanai kuṃkumaiḥ priye |  
tāṃbulavadanai divyairnānā bhojanabhojitaḥ ||  
  
muktakeśā kumārī ca kalaśaṃ sthāpayet priye |  
  
p. 120b)  
  
sādhakasya varārohe ājñāsiddhi pradāyakaṃ |  
gacha putra mahāprājñā ājñāsaṃsphuritā bhavet ||  
  
yajanaiḥ satamātreṇa paśuvakṣeyase kṣaṇāt |  
vāhya tu kathitaṃ devī adhyātma śṛṇu suvratre ||  
  
mīnaṃ tu laṃbikā devī rudraṃ kalaṣamucyate |  
alināmṛtasaṃpūrṇaṃ śiṣyaṃtanābhiṣecayet ||  
  
mīnākhyaṃ mīnapādau sā tasmāt tenābhiṣecanaṃ |  
ayaṃ siddhābhiṣekaṃ tu ājñāsiddhi pravartate ||  
  
iti tatkathitaṃ devi abhiṣekasya lakṣaṇaṃ |  
dīkṣitasya svaśiṣyasya yogiṇī tilakāṃkitaṃ ||  
  
nāmaṃ kuryād varārohe pūrvanāmākṣarairyutaṃ |  
āvalīnāṃ pravakṣyāmi mātṛkā bhedamuttamam ||  
  
a prabhūtānanda || ā lokānanda || i lalitānanda || ī pratimānaṃda || u capalānanda || ū   
siṃhānanda || ṛ ṛktānanda || ṝ līlānanda || ḷ klinnānanda || ḹ locanānanda   
|| e śubhagānanda || ai manmathānanda || o paramānanda || au vijayānaṃda || aṃ   
khecarānanda || aḥ bhaṣānanda || ka kulānanda || kha suśivānanda || ga gagaṇānanda   
|| gha saṃpūrṇānanda || ṅa śikhānanda || ca mātrānaṃda || cha bhuvanānaṃda || ja   
paramānaṃda || jha vaktrānaṃda || ña tejānaṃda || ṭa vāmānanda || ṭha   
bhāsurānaṃda || ḍa madanānaṃda || ḍha rudrānanda ||   
  
p. 121a)  
  
ṇa śavarānanda || tha vairāgyānaṃda || da devānanda || dha saṃkhyānaṃda || na   
vitānanda || pa sūkṣmānanda || pha sarvānanda || va siddhānanda || bha   
bhāsvarānanda || ma marutānanda || ya yogānanda || ra citānanda || la rūpānanda || va   
asitānanda || śa bhogānaṃda || ṣa naktānanda || sa kirāṇānanda || ha jñānānaṃda ||   
kṣa jvalitānaṃda ||   
  
saṃsthāpyakulanāmaivaṃ kuladravyaṃ tu dāpayet |   
kulābhiṣecanaṃ paścāt kartavyaṃ nirvikalpataḥ ||   
  
kramadīkṣā samākhyātā ājñāsiddhi pravartakaṃ |   
mahāsaṃsārapāpaughāmācaraṃ tu karaṃ paraṃ ||   
  
iti te kathitaṃ devi ājñāśiṣyasya lakṣaṇam ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītantre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade viṃśati paṭalaḥ || 20 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi ṣaḍrasaṃ dehasaṃsthitaṃ |  
paṃcaratna paraṃ devi vīryaṃ pratyayalakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
raktaṃ māṃsaṃ vasāmedo majjāśukra tathaiva ca |  
ṣaḍrasaṃ dehasaṃdhiṃ tu āhāryaṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
ichāratnaṃ tu prathamaṃ dvitīyākāyasaṃsthitaṃ |  
tṛtīyaṃ mamṛtaṃ saṃjñā caturthaṃ vaindavaṃ smṛta ||  
  
paṃcamaṃ paramānandaṃ sukhasaṃdeha kārakaṃ |  
eta ratnamayākhyātā maṃtravīryaṃ śṛṇu priye ||  
  
gasapavana deveśi indrarūpavarānane |  
ṣaṣṭhasvarasamāyuktaṃ biṃdumastakabhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
p. 121b)  
  
ete maṃtra varādivyā amarigotramuddharet |  
vīryapūjāvidhānaṃ tu śṛṇu svāyata locane ||

maṃtapūjā vidhi proktaṃ paṃcaratnāni suvrate |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi āhāryaṃ pratyayaṃ tathā ||  
  
yasya ratnasya yaṃ sthānaṃ āhāryaṃ tatra suvrate |  
tatra śrī bhavate sohi tadā vyāpti pravartate ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
bhāṣāsaṃketakaṃ nātha lakṣaṇaṃ ca vadasva me |  
yathā samyagahaṃ vetmi sa vāhyābhyaṃtarāṇi ca ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi bhāṣāsaṃketa lakṣaṇaṃ |  
sthānāni kramabhedaṃ ca khecarī kṛta vigrahaṃ ||  
  
kuvākuṣī kuvaiḥ kuryā kubhe kukṣe kuli kṣamaḥ |  
aṣṭau saṃketakaṃ bhadre pāraṃparyatvamāvataḥ ||  
  
pākahā bhākahā devi ākahā gukahā tathā |  
makahāmaṃkahā devi nokahā taṃkahā tathā ||  
  
aṣṭasaṃketakaṃ bhadre yogiṇī mukhasaṃsthitā |  
sa vāhyābhyaṃtaraṃ devi śṛṇu sthāni * vakṣyase ||  
  
kukāre kubjikā devi aṣṭasaṃketasannidhau |  
sthānāni tava pūjyata sa vāhyābhyaṃtarāṇi ca ||  
  
vā śabda vamate nityaṃ svapacīgharapūjitaṃ |  
  
p. 121a)  
  
savādhāraṃ tu tatraiva sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
ṣīśabde śṛṇu deveśi kukkaśīgharapūjitaṃ ||  
  
turyasthānāṃtadargataṃ sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
vai śabdaṃ vaṣate devi māṃtaṃgī gharapūjitaṃ ||  
  
nābhi cakrāṃtara gataṃ sthitvā cāṃtara |  
ya śabde yogiṇī sthānaṃ oṃvīgharamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
hṛdaye hyādi madhyasthaṃ sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
tu śabde bhukti vijñeyā ghaṇṭhakīghara pūjitaṃ ||  
  
kaṇṭhasthānaṃ gataṃ devi sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
kṣeśabde paramaṃ kṣetraṃ veśyāghara supūjitaṃ ||  
  
ājñādhāraṃ tu tatrasthaṃ sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
niśabde śṛṇu deveśi trailīgharasunirmalaṃ ||  
  
brahmabrahmavilāṃtasthaṃ sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
kṣamāsthānaṃ dvādaśāṃtaṃ kaṃdakīgharapūjitaṃ ||  
  
vāmāsthānavaraṃ divyaṃ sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
evaṃ tu kathitaṃ devi aṣṭau saṃketadurlabhaṃ ||  
  
khecarī matasaṃdehampāramparya kramāgataḥ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi yogiṇīmukhasaṃsthitaṃ ||  
  
pāruhāpārumūlaṃ tu savādhārodayaṃ priye |  
kalpapālīgharaṃ tatra sthitvācāṃtaramālinī ||  
  
logahābhagamūlaṃ tu spṛṣṭvā svayakramaṃ śubhaṃ |  
vacakīgharamāśritya sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī ||  
  
āyātaṃ sarvatatvānāṃ janmādhāraṃ tu āhakā |  
  
p. 122b)  
  
mlechīghara valaṃ divyaṃ sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
okahāguptavijñeyaṃ janmādhāraṃ tu dhīvarī ||  
  
gṛhaṃ nirvāṇa paramaṃ sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
makahā sarvasaṃketaṃ śmaśāna hṛdayaṃ para ||  
  
yogiṇīsaṃgamaṃ tatra sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
maṃkahā maṃgalaṃ devi kaṃthakūpaṃ catuṣpathaṃ ||  
  
kṣutpipāśā parityāgā sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
nākahāmekavṛkṣaṃ tu nāsāgra parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
viśrāṃti sukhasaṃsthānaṃ sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
suṃkahācumbakaṃ devi dvādaśāṃtaṃ tadūrddhagaṃ ||  
  
kumārī kulabhoktī ca sthitvā cāṃtaramālinī |  
āmnāyaṃ kathitaṃ devi rahasyaṃ kaulikā game ||  
  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi chūṣmāmelāpakaṃ priye |  
pīṭhasiddhakramaṃ sthānaṃ mātṛmaṃḍalamuttamaṃ ||  
  
guptāguptataraṃ divyaṃ tarjanyāgre tu saṃspṛśet |  
tasmāchūṣmā vijānīyānnirdiṣṭaṃ kulaśāsane ||  
  
calanaṃ spandasaṃghaṭṭa viśrāṃtagaganāṃtare |  
labdhāmṛtarasaṃ divyaṃ pītvānaṃdamayo bhavet ||  
  
ānaṃdaghūrmaviśrāṃta tadā melāpakaṃ bhavet |  
sa vāhyābhyaṃtaraṃ devi praśnaṃ sārasamuccayaṃ ||  
  
śataṃ viṃśatikaṃ devi kathitaṃ tava vallabhe |  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
p. 122a)  
  
āsanaṃ devadeveśi matasārasamuccayaṃ |  
mahāṃtari paṃcakannātha cakramakṣyanyameva ca ||  
  
kṣetrapālamahāvīraḥ kathayasva maheśvaraḥ |  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
ati praśnavaraṃ divyaṃ ciṃcinīmata saṃbhavaṃ |  
āsanaṃ parameśāni śṛṇu vakṣyāmi suvrate ||  
  
ādhāraśaktyānaṃtaṃ ca kālāgniṃ ca punastathā |  
bījākula tathā devi mahārṇava tathaiva ca ||  
  
pretapadmāsanaṃ devi siṃhāsanamataḥ phalaṃ |  
siddheśvaraṃ tathā guhyaṃ nābhau vīreśvaraṃ tathā ||  
  
hṛdi kuleśvaraṃ caiva kulakhaṃ vātu kaṃṭhake |  
lalāṭe narkanāthaṃ tu ete āsanamuttamaṃ ||  
  
hṛtkamalā kuladdīpā varvarāvakurūpiṇī |  
mahāṃtārī paṃcamī ca sarveṣāṃ vimalaṃ dadet ||  
  
pūjanīyā mahādevi dvārapāraṃ varānane |  
caturbhujā ekavaktrā trinetrā ghorarūpiṇī ||  
  
gānāsā bharaṇā devī sarvakulavibhūṣitāḥ |  
mahājvālā samākīrṇa ūrddhakeśāṭṭahāsinī ||  
  
khaḍgatriśūlahastā ca śaktimudgaradhāriṇī |  
daṃṣṭrākarālavadanā gajacarmottarīyakaṃ ||

rakṣitavyaṃ mahāsthānaṃ caṃdradvīpaṃ varānane ||

akacaṭatapayasa vargavidyā prakīrtitāṃ ||  
  
pūjanīyā vidhānena aṣṭau devyāṣṭavargakau |  
  
p. 122b)  
  
diśā cāṣṭau tathā devi pūrvādyāsurasuṃdari |  
brāhmī māheśvarī caiva kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā ||  
  
vārāhī ca tathā aiṃdrī cāmuṃḍā ca parāḥ smṛtā |  
etad devyā mayākhyātā akṣayā ca varānane ||

bhukti mukti pradātāraṃ kuladevyāśca pārvati ||

varvaraṃ piṃgakeśaṃ ca piṅgaḥ piṃgalalocanaṃ ||  
  
daṃṣṭrākarālamatyugra kapālābharaṇojvale |  
vakakṣetrapālamahāḍāmarādhipate valiṃ ||

śrutaṃ devamayā sarvaṃ mattanāmuttamottamaṃ ||  
  
ciṃcinī matasāroyaṃ tvat prasādāt mayāśrutaṃ |  
adyāpi saṃśayo nātha hṛdi me vartaṭe sphuṭaṃ ||  
  
kathaṃ vīravṛtannātha kumārī vratameva ca |  
tadākhyā hi ca me nātha prasādaṃ kuru satkara ||

śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi kumārī vratanirṇayaṃ |

p. 123a)  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepā na tu vistaraṃ ||  
  
khaṭparaṃ pūrvakathita camaraṃ śṛṇu suvrate |  
sarvādhāroditā devi kakaṃdara parā kalā ||  
  
cāracakra pravāhena bhedayet paramaṃ padaṃ |  
tridhāmodayamadhyasthaṃ drāvitaṃ citkalāmṛtaṃ ||  
  
carcitaṃ carcikāmnāyaṃ tasmāccāmarakatpriye |  
dhāritā paramā devi kumārī brahmacāriṇī ||  
  
kāmākhyapīṭhamadhye tu vratamācaritaṃ priye |  
dvābhyāṃ sakhī parā devyā vallabhā parameśvarī ||  
  
divyarūpā kumārī ca rūpikāratnasuṃdarī |  
camaraṃ dhārayed ratnā khaṭparaṃ rūpasuṃdarī ||  
  
madhye tu khecarī devyā caṃdrarekha taḍijjvalaṃ |  
caryācāryaṃ samuccāryaṃ divyogha kramamaṃḍala ||  
  
acaleti padaṃ divyaṃ caṃcaleti pada dvayaṃ |  
pavaneti mahāvege nirmāṃse vyomabhakṣaṇī ||  
  
carukaṃ ca disiṃhī ca bhāṣitaṃ ca muhurmuhuḥ |  
sthāne sthāneṣu gaṃtavyaṃ krīḍākulamanuttamaṃ ||  
  
etad devi mayā khyātaṃ kumārī vratanirṇayaṃ |  
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi vīravratamanuttamaṃ ||  
  
nisāṭanaṃ vīradharaṃ haste pākarasaṃyutaṃ |  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
pākaraṃ kathitaṃ nātha saṃkṣepānna tu vistaraṃ ||  
  
bhrāṃti jñānavināśāya sarvasiddhāraho bhavet |  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi vīrapānakalakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
p. 123b)  
  
svaprakāśaprabodhena cārasaṃcāracarcitaṃ |  
bhavaccedaṃ parollāsa viśramaṃti padaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
vyomātīta parāyukti kaulopāyena saṃvidaḥ |  
vyaktavyakta padaṃ divyaṃ tatra pākajasaṃsmaret ||  
  
bhagamadhya cidākāraṃ ravimadhya rati priye |  
dvābhyāṃ madhya śivaḥ sākṣāt tatra pākarasaṃsmaret ||  
  
aṃvarāṃtargataṃ devi bhānavī kalasaṃsthitaṃ |  
jīvādibhyoditaṃ yatra tatra pākalasaṃsmaret ||  
  
gatvā svarūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca krodhaśca bhagasāgaraṃ |  
drāvitaṃ ca mahāghora pītvā saha sa bhairavaṃ ||  
  
vīre vīravaraśreṣṭha saṃcaraṃti carācaraṃ |  
na bhayaṃ vidyate tasya yasya mukti svayaṃ vidaḥ ||  
  
parādeva parāvasthā svabhāvaḥ sarvagovyayaḥ |  
vadaṃtyayannaṃto vīra kulakolādhipaḥ prabhoḥ ||  
  
kathitaṃ devadeveśi vīrapākaralakṣaṇaṃ |  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
śrutaṃ deva mayāsarvaṃ matasārasamuccayaṃ |  
adyāpi saṃsayo nātha maṃtravidyā daśasva me ||  
  
vattrī sāṣṭarikannātha bījapaṃcakameva ca |  
khaṭikā bhavaprastāraṃ vadasva mama śaṃkara ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi maṃtravidyā samuddharan |  
bhūpradeśe same śuddhaṃ alinā lepayet priye ||  
  
puṣpadhūpavaliṃ devi madyanaivedyamuttamaṃ |  
prasanna vadano bhūtvā uddhared bīja paṃcakaṃ ||  
  
p. 124a)  
  
vāgbhavaṃ prathamaṃ devi māyābījaṃ dvitīyakaṃ |  
śrībījaṃ tu tṛtīyaṃ syāt caturthaṃ śṛṇu suvrate ||  
  
pānajaṃ vahnimārūḍhaṃ ekādaśa yutaṃ priye |  
biṃduyuktaṃ paraṃ devi yoginībījamuttamaṃ ||  
  
sṛṣṭisaṃhārasaṃyuktaṃ caturdaśa yutaṃ priye |  
kādiyuktaṃ paraṃ devi paṃcamaṃ bījamuttamaṃ ||  
  
bījapaṃcakametaddhi sarvasādhāraṇaṃ priye |  
namo bhagavati padamuddhṛtaṃ prathamaṃ priye ||  
  
saṃhāraṃ sṛṣṭisaṃyuktaṃ pānajaṃ tejasaṃyutaṃ |  
ekādaśaṃ biṃduyutaṃ ekatraṃ saptamaṃ priye ||  
  
śrīkubjiketi padaṃ divyamekādaśa prakāśitaṃ |  
saṃhāraṃ ca tṛdhā kṛtvā tena yuktaṃ varānane ||  
  
dvitīyaṃ svarabiṃdu ca prathamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
caturthasvarasaṃbiṃduṃ dvitīyaṃ bījamuttamaṃ ||  
  
caturthasvarabiṃduṃ ca tṛtīyaṃ varavarṇini |  
caturdaśa paraṃ bījaṃ uddhṛtya parameśvari ||  
  
ṅa ña ṇa nameti padāṃ kona viṃśati uddharet |  
aghoramukheti padaṃ caturviṃśa varānane ||  
  
chā& chī& ti paramaṃ divyaṃ kiṇi kiṇi padaṃ paraṃ |  
vicceti maṃtrasaṃdohaṃ dvātriṃśadvarṇamuddhṛtaṃ ||  
  
ekavaktreśvarī devī sarvakāmaphala pradā |  
pūjate sarvadevebhyo lokapālā mahāvalāḥ ||  
  
brahmeṃdraviṣṇurudrāṇā nityaṃ pūjayate priye |

p. 124b)  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
dakṣiṇāmnāya vakṣyāmi mahāvīryā mahāvalā |  
aghorabhairavo dṛṣṭvā niśveśī ca nilaṃ galā ||  
  
nirālaṃveśvarī nityā aghoraṃtachivaṃ viduḥ |  
siṃhāsana gatā nityā niśeśī rakta carcikā ||  
  
caitanya bhairavī kecid raktakālīti kecana |  
suṃdarī kālikā kecidaghoreśvarikena ca ||  
  
dhyānarūpaṃ tu vakṣyāmi bhairavyāyāmyadigsthitāḥ |  
nityā niraṃjaniratā niḥśreśī nirguṇāśrayā ||  
  
kratu nārādhitā devi dharmarājāya vai purā |  
saṃpradāya krameṇaiva devī caitanya bhairavī ||  
  
caturvedāsanā devī mahāphetkārasaṃsthitā |  
prajvalaṃtī citā madhye dakṣiṇye dakṣadakṣayā ||  
  
alāta cakravadyasyā bhramaṃtī śiramālikā |  
snāyu lakṣākṛśāṃgī ca asthicarmavaśevitā ||  
  
vyāghracarma kaṭi vṛtā naracarmottarīyakā |  
sahasrāditya saṃkāśāṃ taptakāṃcana saṃprabham ||  
  
paṃcavaktrā cātibhīmā tripaṃcanayanairyutā |  
iṣaddhāsya lalajjihvā nimnanābhi kṛśodarī ||  
  
vikalālāsanakhyātā cakra vaktrāsana sthitā |  
raudrī bhayā parāghorā caṃdrārddhakṛta ketanā ||  
  
varvarārddhamuktakeśī nāgarājavirājitā |  
  
p. 125a)  
  
kavaṃdha uṣṇīṣa yutā brahma śīrṣaśikhāmaṇi |  
sadyaśchinna galadraktaḥ śiromālāvibhūṣitā ||  
  
bhujaṣoḍaśasaṃyuktā gajakaṃcukakiṃkiṇī |  
pāśāṃkuśa kapālaṃ ca khaṭvāṃgaṃ muṇḍatriṃḍimaṃ ||  
  
khaḍgapheṭavāṇadhanu cakra daṇḍakamaṃḍaluṃ |  
abhayaṃ varadaṃ caiva tarjanī vidhṛtā karaiḥ ||

pracaṇḍā ugra caṇḍā ca ugratārā kapālinī ||

nīlā sarasvatī bhīmā trailokya ḍāmareśvarī ||

tasyāṃga devatāḥ sarve vahubhedā mahojvalā ||

dakṣiṇāmnāya deveśī nānābhedavisāriṇī ||

p. 125b)  
  
mahācaṃḍāṭṭasaṃrāva pūjayaṃto digaṃ tathā |  
vetālā vahulā tatra ḍākinīgaṇasaṃvṛtā ||  
  
vālalīlā samāpannā niśācara gaṇāvṛtā |  
daṇḍapāśe dharadyatā sarvasādhakasiddhidā ||  
  
śākapuṣkara dvīpeṣu sādhakābhedadarśinī |  
cauhāregaṃkare pīṭhe yonimaṇḍalamārgagā ||  
  
vāmācāraratā pūjyā hyaṇimādyaṣṭasiddhidā |  
sūtrīyatā mayā proktā dakṣiṇāmnāya tāṃ gata ||  
  
nīlavārāhikā dhyānaṃ kathayāmi tavādhunā |  
nīlatoyadasaṃkāśāṃ nīlakuṃḍalaśobhitām ||  
  
nīlapuṣpavibhūṣāḍhyāṃ nīlālaṃkārabhūṣitāṃ |  
nīlāṃgavāgasaṃśchaṃtāṃ nīlavaiḍūryamālinīṃ ||  
  
indranīlanivadhāṃśu mahārghamaṇi bhūṣaṇāṃ |  
nīlavājisamārūḍhāṃ nīlakhaḍgāyudhāṃ parām ||  
  
nidrāpaṭena nīlena bhuvanāni caturdaśa |  
mohayati mahāmāyāṃ dravyaniṃdakabhakṣiṇīṃ ||  
  
vīrapānaratāṃ vīrāṃ pālayaṃtīṃ samaṃ tataḥ |  
saṃketamaṃḍalaṃ divyaṃścādayaṃtī svavāsasā ||  
  
paramānaṃdavapuṣīṃ paramānaṃdabhairavīṃ |  
paramānaṃda jananīṃ praṇamāmi parāṃvikāṃ ||  
  
māyālakṣmī dvayasyāṃte namo bhagavatīti ca |  
māheśvari svarūpāṃte sarvapaśujaneti ca ||  
  
manaścakṣustirakaraṇaṃ kuru dvaṃdvaṃ ca ṭha dvayaṃ |  
tathānyatitaskaraṇīṃ lajjāṃ kāmeśvarīṃ tataḥ ||  
  
p. 126a)  
  
vāṇīṃ glauṃ tiraskariṇīṃ sakalajaneti vai tataḥ |  
vāgvādinīti sakalapaśuvrata janeti ca ||  
  
manaścakṣuḥ śrotrajihvā ghrāṇe kṣitiraskaraṇaṃ |  
kuru dvayaṃ ṭha dvayaṃ ca savisarga śiromanuḥ ||  
  
ugrāmnāyamuttaraṃ tu kālikākulasaṃbhavā |  
koṭi koṭi pramadosti kālikātīrvanāyikā ||  
  
ājñāsiddhi pradā devī viṣṇutejopavṛṃhitā |  
nārāyaṇī mahākālī jagadrakṣaṇa tatpara ||  
  
kālikāli mahākāli caṇḍayogeśvarīti ca |  
tiṣṭha śṛchansmarannityaṃ mucyate mahato bhayāt ||  
  
ābrahmasthāvarāṃtā ca kālena kalayaṃti ca |  
taṃ kālaṃ kalayet kālī tataḥ sā kālikā smṛtāḥ ||  
  
ānega cakracakreśī nānā bhedo mahāgamā |  
śakyate kālikā devyā devā brahmādayopi hi ||  
  
tathāpi leśamātrastu kumārīṃ kramata śṛṇu |  
nīlavarṇā mahākālī trimukhānavalocanā ||  
  
pītaṃ tu dakṣiṇaṃ vaktraṃ muttaraṃ pāvakopamaṃ |  
maṃḍalaṃ vitanetrāśca aṣṭavāṅkī tanuddharā ||  
  
piṃgalorddha jaṭāṭopa caṃdrārddhakṛtaśekharā |  
saptāviṃśati muṃḍaṃśca raktavipluṣasaṃyutā ||  
  
asthikuṃḍalaśobhāḍhyā maulīkāpālamālinī |  
kiṃkiṇī naupurārāva vīraghaṃṭāravottamā ||  
  
śivāpretā samārūḍhā mukhaśonita nirjharāḥ |  
  
p. 126b)  
  
iṃdrādyā brahmaviṣṇuśca rudreśvara sadāśivaḥ |  
pītaśyāmaraktadhūmra śvetābhā paṃcakālakāḥ ||  
  
vajradaṃḍaśaktiśūla khaṭvāṃgāyudhadhārakāḥ |  
tarjanīmukhanikṣiptvā śivādhasthā trilocanā ||  
  
vaddhapadmāsanā devī pīnonnata payodharā |  
vāmahaste kapālaṃ ca raktapūrṇāni śobhane ||  
  
dhārayaṃti triśūlaṃ ca śabdaṃ dakṣiṇe kare |  
cakraṃ ca dakṣiṇe haste aṃkuśaṃ mudgaraṃ tathā ||  
  
vāme pāśaṃ ca khaṭvāṃgaṃ mṛtavālaṃ ca dhāriṇaṃ |  
citkalā kalanātasthāṃ jyotirūpāśca kevalā ||  
  
nirvāṇapadadātītā bhāvātītāmagocarā |  
asminmūrtau mahādevyā navavatkāni pūjayet ||  
  
vahudhā bhedarūpāṇi kālikāyā maheśvarī |  
ājñāsiddhi pradānityā kaulamārgapravartakā ||  
  
mahākulālikāyātā viṣṇuḥ kālitvamāgatā |  
yasyāprabhāvāmatulaṃ varṇituṃ naiva śakyate ||  
  
durvāsānāradovyāsaḥ vaśiṣṭhaḥ kauśikastathā |  
triścatuḥ paṃcakagrehādekāhāt siddhimāgatā ||  
  
animādyā mahāsiddhi tasyāṃga siddhi yaḥ smṛtāḥ |  
mokṣadā siddhidā kālī nirvāṇeśīśvarī śivā ||  
  
kaivalyamekāsiddhisyā mahājñāna prakāśinī |  
sādhako bhairavaḥ sākṣājjarāmaraṇavarjitaḥ ||  
  
p. 127a)  
  
dhanadasya samābhūmin na śakrasya prajāyate |  
yā bhūti sādhakasyaiva bhavatrailokya durlabhā ||  
  
paṃcavaktrakramaṃ devī paṃcakālyānuśāsitā |  
guhyakālī mahādevī vaiṣṇavī brahmarūpiṇī ||  
  
vāmadevāśritā sarve mahābhairava koṭayaḥ |  
gaṇeśavaṭuyoginyaḥ śatakoṭi sahasrakā ||  
  
bhūtavetālaḍākinyo cetakā rākṣasa khagāḥ |  
pheravākākagṛdhrāśca ulūkā garuḍāvakāḥ ||  
  
śṛṃgālīkaṃ kaṭiyugā nānārūpā mahāvalā |  
āmnāyajñāvadaṃtīha uttaraṃ tu niruttaraṃ ||  
  
anekaśatasāhasra śrīnāthenāvatāritaṃ |  
maṃtraṃ nānārahasyaṃ ca jāmalaṃ lakṣasammitaṃ ||  
  
tvanābhimathanād devī svakīya rasanāpurā |  
brahmāṃḍaṃ garbhatastasyā jātaṃ divyeta yoninā ||  
  
tadārabhya maheśāni kujādevīti viśrutā |  
jyeṣṭhavālaprabhedena kubji kālīka pūjitā ||  
  
sadyojātamukhodgītā paścimāmnāya devatā |  
kubjikā jagatāmādyā mahārarūpiṇī ||  
  
anaṃta deśikaḥ sevyā nityāśivasamāgataḥ |  
jyeṣṭhavāla prabhedena vahumārgapravāhinī ||  
  
dvātriṃśatā bhedayuktā kubjikā bhairavāśritā |  
vṛṣabhe saṃsthitaṃ devaṃ khavarṇaṃ rūpaśobhitaṃ ||  
  
ekavaktraṃ trinetraṃ ca bhujāṣṭādaśadhāriṇaṃ |  
ḍamarūṃ paraśuṃ vāṇaṃ khaḍgamaṃkuśavajrakaṃ ||  
  
p. 127b)  
  
śaṃkhaṃ ca veṇuvādyaṃ ca varadābhayadakṣiṇe |  
vāme khaṭvāṃga śūlaṃ ca dhanuḥ phelakapāśakaṃ ||  
  
ghaṃṭākalaśaveṇūṃ ca abhayābhayanāśanaṃ |  
paṭṭeṇa vaṃdhitaṃ jānu vāmorusthā ca kubjikā ||  
  
ekavaktrā trinetrā ca aruṇāvarṇavarṇitā |  
dvibhujāvaradā devī siṃhasthā bhayasavyasu ||  
  
nāgābharaṇabhūṣāṃgī khaṃdendukṛtamastakā |  
varvaro keśapāśena cārupīnaghanastanī ||  
  
sarvābharaṇasaṃśobhā lakṣaṇeśca suśobhitā |  
evaṃ dhyeyā kujāmātā paścimāmnāya bhairavī ||  
  
tatraiva vahu bhedosti kubjikākulamārgatā |  
vibhinnasiddhināthena śrīnāthenāvatāritā ||  
  
kujeśanātha vīreṇa kujāmnāya prakāśitāṃ |  
navātmā śrīśikhānātha svachandalaliteśvaraḥ ||  
  
krameśī ca trikhaṃḍā ca mahaṃtāri trikhaṇḍikā |  
triśūddhi ugracaṃḍā ca caṇḍācaṃḍākapālikā ||  
  
annapūrṇā kalālī ca jvālāmālini kāminī |  
brāhmyādyāmātaragaṇā asitāṃgādi bhairavā ||  
  
brāhmī māheśvarī caiva kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā |  
vārāhī caiva māhendrī cāmuṃḍāsaptamī smṛtā ||  
  
aṣṭamī ca mahālakṣmī etāḥ sarvatra pūjitā |  
asitāṃgo ruruścaṃḍa krodhīśotmattakastathā ||  
  
kapālī bhīṣaṇākhyāśca saṃhāraścāṣṭamastathā |  
  
p. 128a)  
  
ṣaḍāmnāye prapūjyā vai mātṛkā sahabhairavaiḥ |  
gaṇeśā vaṭuko kṣetra yoginīsaṃghakā smṛtā ||  
  
ḍākinī bhūtavetāla ceṭikāgaṇasaṃvṛtāḥ |  
ḍākinyādi mahā * * ṣadyoginyaḥ prakīrtitā ||  
  
ḍākinī yākinī ghorā lākinī kākiṇī tathā |  
sākiṇī hākiṇī proktā yākiṇyaḥ saptadhāravaḥ ||  
  
saṃsthitā devatā vidyā carurūpeṇa bhairavaḥ |  
sadyojātaḥ sādhitā sā kubjikā cakranāyikāḥ ||  
  
aṃgirāsādhitā vidyā dakṣāya pratipāditā |  
raghuṣāya tato datvā tato caṃdrā tvayāya ca ||  
  
pārthivānāṃ ca saumyānāṃ kuladevīti kīrtitā |  
aneka siddhidā sarve kriyāṃ tu vahava smṛtā ||  
  
durvāsārādhitā vidyā nirācārā karāśritā |  
vāmamārge ratānityā dakṣiṇāphalavarjitā ||  
  
makārapaṃcakaiḥ pūjyā nānyathā phaladā bhavet |  
saucācāranirācāra niḥkalaṃkānirāśrayā ||  
  
animādi mahāsiddhi sādhanā chighrasiddhidā |  
mokṣadā bhogadā devī kubjikā kulamātṛkā ||  
  
bahudhā varṇitā devi tavāgre śrīmahādiṣu |  
maṃthānabhairave cāsti caturviṃśamateṣu ca ||  
  
sarvacakreśvarī nityā sarvāmnāya prapūjitā |  
sarvasiṃhāsanamayī īśānāsanasaṃsthitā ||  
  
paraṃ brahmeśvarī māyā devī nārāyaṇī smṛtā |  
  
p. 128b)  
  
nidrābuddhi kṣamākhyāṃti kṣudhā lajjā smṛti dhṛti |  
prajñāśāṃti prabhājjātimasyāpādāṃgulīnakhe ||  
  
yasyādṛgdhātamātreṇa sākṣālakṣmī patirbhavet |  
yasyā vā karmasuratā yasya mārgānusāriṇī ||  
  
rājārājasamo bhūtvā surarājasamopi vā |  
bhuktvā tu vipulān bhogān naṃte nirvāṇamāpnuyāt ||  
  
kadācid yoṣito bhūttā kadācit puruṣo bhavet |  
viṣṇurūpena sakalaṃ duṣṭān sarvā vināśayet ||  
  
jagavyāptavatī māyā mohayet sasurāsurān |  
arūpārūpiṇī bhūtvā suṃdarī kathayāmi te ||  
  
padmarāgapratīkāśaṃ kuṃkumodaka saṃnibhā |  
subhravāṃ ca sunetrā ca sustanī cāruhāsinī ||  
  
kṛśamadhya caturdvāhu khaṃḍeṃdu kṛtaśekharāṃ |  
trinetrāṃ sarvabhūṣāḍhyāṃ cāruveśāmanoramā ||  
  
pāśāṃkuśekṣu cāpaṃ ca paṃcavāṇadhanurddharā |  
brahmāviṣṇurudra īśāmaṃ ca maṃḍapādikā ||  
  
sadāśivākhya paryaṃke saṃsthitā parameśvarī |  
parāśaktāṃ suṃdarīti tripureśīti gīyate ||  
  
mahāmokṣapradā devī paraṃ brahmasvarūpiṇī |  
bahubhedā viśālākṣī vahurūpā prakāśinī ||  
  
kāmeśvarī rudraśaktī pūrṇapīṭhāvatāriṇī |  
vajreśī vaiṣṇavī nityā kāmarūpanivāsitā ||  
  
śāktīśvarī bhageśī ca jālaṃdhara pratiṣṭhitā |  
  
p. 129a)  
  
brahmāśaktī samullāsa pīṭhagahvaravigrahā ||  
  
udyānapīṭhanilayā paraṃ brahmātmikā śivā |  
sarvacakreśvarī sarva pīṭheśrī maṃtravigrahā ||  
  
sarvamaṃtreśvarī sarva deveśī divya vigraha |  
udyānapīṭha nilayā paraṃ brahmātmikā śivā ||  
  
ṣaḍāmnāyeśvarī nityā niraṃsāni parigrahā |  
nityāṣoḍaśavidyāyā navacakre vyavasthitā ||  
  
navacakreśvarī nityā navakoṇāgrata sthitaḥ |  
trailokya mohanaṃ cakraṃ sarvāśāparipūrakaṃ ||  
  
sarvasaṃkṣobhanaṃ cakraṃ sarvasaubhāgyadāyakaṃ |  
sarvārthasādhanaṃ cakraṃ sarvarakṣākaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
sarvakāma pradā cakraṃ sarvasiddhi pradāyakaṃ |  
sarvānaṃda mayaṃ cakraṃ navamaṃ cakranāyikāṃ ||  
  
sarvaitadvaindave līnā tacchrī cakramudāhṛtaṃ |  
tripurā tripureśī ca suṃdarīpuravāsinī ||  
  
śrīmālinī ca siddhāmvā mahātripurabhairavī |  
aneka devatāvṛṃda līnā cakreṣu saṃsthitā ||  
  
vaindave ca trikoṇe ca aṃtalāle'ṣṭakoṇake |  
dvidaśāre ca manvastre nāgapatreṣu sarvataḥ ||  
  
patraṣoḍaśasaṃkhyāte caturasre guṇaspṛhaṃ |  
rekhāyukta caturdvāre trailokyaṃ tatra pārvati ||  
  
hiraṇya rajate tāmre maṇopatretha bhūrjake |  
kauśeya sthaṃḍile vāpi dṛṣṭā tu praṇamet priye ||  
  
p. 129b)  
  
sarvatīrtheṣu sasnāta sarvayajñeṣu dikṣitaḥ |  
sarvadaḥ sarvatasākṣāt maheśvara samo bhavet ||  
  
śrīcakraṃ kālayitvā tu yo dadyāt sādhakāya ca |  
bhūcakraṃ tena dattaṃ hi sa śaila vanakānanā ||  
  
sa vai mahāpāśupataḥ savai vaiṣṇavasattamaḥ |  
sarvadaḥ sarvadarśī ca brahmajñānī sa vai sudhī ||  
  
mahādānāni ye proktā munibhi brahmavādibhiḥ |  
tatphalaṃ labhate nūnaṃ śrīcakrasya prabhāvataḥ ||  
  
koṭiliṃga pratiṣṭhasya yatphalaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ |  
tatphalaṃ labhate nūnaṃ śrīcakrasya ca pūjane ||  
  
viṣṇo hi * pratiṣṭhāyāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti niścitaṃ |  
hiraṇye rajate tāmre maṇaubhūrje ca paṭṭake ||  
  
aṃ kiṃ bhyādhārayed yastu kale kaṃṭhe bhujepi vā |  
yāni kāni ca pāpāni brahmahatyā samāni ca ||  
  
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ śrīcakrasya ca dhāraṇāt |  
pāpāṇi vilayaṃ yāṃti jñānājñāna kṛtāni ca ||  
  
sarvaṃ sa dahyate śīghraṃ cakrarājasya dhāraṇāt |  
bhūtapretapiśācaiśca śvāpadai brahmarākṣasaiḥ ||  
  
ḍākinī sākiṇībhirvā vīkṣituṃ naiva śakyate |  
mahākrūragrahairvāpi janmasthāna sthitopi vā ||  
  
gocare lagnago vāpi sarvaṃ śubhagrahaṃ bhavet |  
akālamṛtyuṃ harati sadāsannihitā parā ||  
  
parāsannihitā tatra kiṃ kurvaṃ nyasya devatāḥ |  
  
p. 130a)  
  
śrīcakradhārayitvā tu yastu prāṇāt parityajet |  
kīkaṭe cāṃtarikṣe vā nikhiddhe kaśmalepi vā ||  
  
kṛtvā ceṃdriya laulya na pāpāni subahūnyapi |  
sa kaivalyaṃ labhennūnaṃ na pūrvajanmabhāg bhavet ||  
  
yamadūtā palāyaṃte dṛṣṭvā śrīcakradhāraṇaṃ |  
brahmajñāna na vā mokṣaḥ kāśyāṃvāsaḥ stanu tyajet ||  
  
śrīcakraṃ dhāraṇādvāpi trayo mokṣasya kāraṇaṃ |  
sarvadevagaṇāstatra sarvadharmaśca tatra vai ||  
  
gaṃgādyā saritāḥ sarve puṣparādyā jalāśritāḥ |  
puruṣottamamukhyāśca kṣatrānaṃdavavarādayaḥ ||  
  
vājimedhādi yajñasya phalatvarikalaṃ bhavet |  
vāmadakṣiṇa yogena suṃdari dvividhā smṛtāḥ ||  
  
suṃdarī dvividhā proktā vāmadakṣiṇasāśane |  
acirena bhaved vāmaḥ sarvakāmānna saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇācāra yogena bhikṣunāṃ pāramā smṛtā |  
tadanyācāra yogena āśusiddhiphalaṃ labhet ||  
  
vedoktaid dakṣiṇācāraiḥ kaivalyaṃ kevalaṃ phalaṃ |  
ata eva mahādevi sākṣād brahmasvarūpiṇī ||  
  
śabdabrahmaparaṃ brahma rūpiṇī parameśvarī |  
śabdabrahmavijānā hi sākṣāvarṇa svarūpiṇīṃ ||  
  
ṣoḍaśārṇā mahādevī vācyarūpeṇa saṃsthitā |  
turīyā sā mahāvidyā sākṣājjāgrat svarūpiṇī ||  
  
p. 130b)  
  
vaktrakoṭi sahasraistu jihvākoṭi śatairapi |  
varṇituṃ naiva śaknoti śrīvidyā ṣoḍaśākṣaraṃ ||  
  
brahmavidyā svarūpā sā bhuktimukti phalapradā |  
ekoccāraṇa * devi rājasūryasya koṭayaḥ ||  
  
ṣoḍaśārṇā mahāvidyā na prakāśyā kadācana |  
vināguruprasādena śrīvidyā ṣoḍaśākṣarī ||  
  
dṛṣṭvā prajapyate yastu sa bhakṣo yogiṇī gaṇaiḥ |  
śrīguro kṛpayā labdhā na pradāśyā kadācana ||  
  
vinā guru prasādena japannaiva kadācana |  
śrīgurokṛpayālabdhā sarvasāmrājyadāyinī ||  
  
sudhātaraṃginī vega śabdacārya dāyinī |  
saubhāgya bhogasaṃpanno kalākuśaladāyinī ||  
  
bhuvanatrayasaubhāgyaṃ trailokyo karṣaṇaṃ tathā |  
paraṃ brahmaṇi līnatvaṃ dadāti jaga uttamaṃ ||  
  
ṣoḍaśārṇā mahāvidyā bhuktimukti phalapradā |  
niḥsaraṃti mahāvidyā visphuliṃgā yathā priye ||  
  
sākṣāt saṃcinmayī nityā visphuliṃgā yathā priye |  
sākṣāt saṃcit mayī nityā jñānamokṣapradāyinī ||  
  
mahāsaṃpatpradāvidyā sākṣādakṣararūpiṇī |  
ṣoḍaśārṇā mahāvidyā śrīvidyā kathitā purā ||  
  
nidhānāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ caurebhyastu yathā priye |  
prāṇenāpi rakṣaṇīyā śrīvidyāṣoḍaśākṣarī ||  
  
na deyā yasya kasyāpi deyā prāṇapradāyinī |  
  
p. 131a)  
  
rājñerājya pradeyāni prāṇebhyopyadhikāya ca |  
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ śreṣṭhamadhyamathādhanaṃ ||  
  
tāmralakṣaguṇaṃ proktaṃ raupyaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet |  
sauvarṇaṃ naṃtaphaladaṃ athāsau kiṃ vravīmite ||  
  
vālā sā prathamā vidyā tato vāgmaravī smṛtā |  
saṃpat pradāśrī pradāśca tato tripurabhairavīṃ ||  
  
viṃdumālini * llekhā hṛllekhā śrīparākalā |  
ṣaṭkūṭānavakūṭā ca lopāmudrā trikūṭikā ||  
  
paṃcamī paṃcakāminye vidyāśrī kāmarājakaṃ |  
ṣoḍaśārṇā mahāvidyā sā vai śrī paramā parā ||  
  
parāyuktā ca prāsādaḥ sāṃbhavaṃ samudāhṛtaḥ |  
aṇimādyā mahāsiddhi aṃtarāya prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
paṃcasiṃhāsane devyā mahātripurasuṃdarī |  
sākṣājjāgra svarūpā ca vaiṣṇavī paradevatā ||  
  
sarvasvarūpiṇī satyā prakṛti parameśvarī |  
sarvajīvasvarūpā ca vyāpya sarvatra saṃsthitā ||  
  
śivaśakti vayo nāsti pumānnastī napuṃsakaḥ |  
sarvajīva svarūpā ca dātmaliṃga svarūpiṇī ||  
  
sarvotpatti hetu bhūtā yonirityavidhīyate |  
siṃhāsana svarūpāyā ūrddhāmnāya mayoditaṃ ||  
  
leśamātraṃ mahādevi sākṣājjāgra svarūpiṇī |  
prathamaṃ pūrvavaktrena rūpaṃ tatpuruṣena ca ||  
  
kathayā māsa prāciṃ tu siṃhāsana mahoddhataṃ |  
  
p. 131b)  
  
nāyikā rudraśaktīryā śivaṃ tatpuruṣaṃ paraṃ |  
pūrṇeśvarī mahaṃ go sā pūrvāmnāya prakīrtitā ||  
  
cakreśvaryāṃ tu vakṣyāmi sādhakānāṃ hitāya vai |  
dhyānaṃ tu citte dhiṣṭhāya dhyātavyā parameśvarī ||  
  
iṃdranīlasamaprakhyaṃ daśadorddaṃḍadhāriṇīṃ |  
varābhaya karaṃ ramyaṃ sa triśūlaṃ kapālakaṃ ||  
  
ḍamaruṃ cākṣamālāṃ ca śaktīṃ caiva karāṃbuje |  
indu cāpaṃśaraṃ caivaṃ khaḍgahastaṃ suśobhanī ||  
  
mahāpretoparitatau sūrya caṃdrāsanāsthitāṃ |  
pratyālīḍhā trinetrā ca muṇḍamālā vibhūṣitā ||  
  
vāsukī śaṃkhapālau tau taukarṇabhūṣatāṃ gatau |  
anaṃtahāramālāṃ ca hāḍālaṃkārabhūṣitā ||  
  
viśāla prayanetrātva caṃdrārdhakṛtaśekharā |  
eṣā pūrṇeśvarī devī hāhārāvavara priyā ||  
  
pūrṇeśvarīti vikhyātā sāhaṃkārārajo yutā |  
śirau pūrṇā laye pīṭhe lakṣmī vana śmaśānake ||  
  
iṃdre nārādhitā nityā vahurūpāvatāriṇī |  
pūrvāmnāyati vikhyātā pūrvadevarṣi pūjitā ||  
  
īśvarī sarvavidyānāṃ mahābhāgyabharāvahā |  
nānārūpadharā nityā vahurūpāvatāriṇī ||  
  
jayājayaṃtī vijayā ajitānārasiṃhikā |
