vyāghreśvarī karālā ca rājeśī bhuvaneśvarī ||  
  
p. 132a)  
  
raktadaṃtāviśālākṣī kāmeśī caṃḍamālinī |  
vidyujjihvā ḍāmareśī nāṭeśrī nṛtyanāyikā ||  
  
naṃdī caiva mahākāla bhaṃginī ca kulālikā |  
navanāṭeśvarī tatra catuḥpaṃcarasānvitā ||  
  
vahubhedā deva devī bhairavāṣṭaka mātṛkā |  
nāṭeśvareti vikhyātā bhairavo cakra pālakaḥ ||  
  
kṣetravighneśa vaṭuka yāgiṇī mātṛkāṣṭakaḥ |  
brahmāṇyādyā prapūjyaṃte kumārī kāmadā sadā ||  
  
nṛtyamāne purā deve bhairavo mātṛbhirvṛtaḥ |  
nṛtyabhairava nāmā tu pūrvacakre vyavasthitā ||  
  
gaṇeśakṣatra ḍākinyo gaṇāstatpuruṣāśritā |  
vāmamārgaiḥ samārādhya na taddakṣiṇataḥ kriyā ||  
  
plakṣadvīpe kuśadvīpe vahudhā ca tadaṃvagā |  
vaśyākarṣastaṃbhanaṃ ca siddhayatvanimādayaḥ ||  
  
marīcinā samārādhya śakrāya ca pradattavān |  
ityeṣa pūrvacāmnāya prāci siṃhāsana sthitā ||  
  
adhāmnāya śṛṇuṣva tvaṃ sā valījina mātṛkā |  
aśeṣakarma nirmāṇā kalauśīghra phalapradā ||  
  
bauddhamārge nirāṭaṃkānilaṅgaṃ lanala prabhā |  
āmnāyāṃtarasārāṇi khyātā sā vajra yogiṇī ||  
  
trivaktrā raktavarṇā ca nṛtyapādā sa vāsanā |  
trinetrā maṃḍalaṃ vīta hāḍā bharaṇabhūṣitā ||  
  
p. 132b)  
  
muṃḍamālāvibhūtāṃgī vyālayajño pavītinī |  
vyāghracarmāmvarāṃ devī siṃhacarmottarīyakā ||  
  
vairocanī vajrapūrvā vajraghaṃṭhāvara priyā |  
caturbhujā pretasaṃsthā varvarorddha śiroruhā ||  
  
kartṛkapālakhaṭvāṃgaṃ ḍamaruṃ ca dhṛtākarai |  
saugatānugamāsākṣāt kalau śīghraphalapradā ||  
  
ihaiva phaladā nityārāpavargaphalaprabhā |  
saugatānugamā sarvā nānā bheda samāśritā ||  
  
kālacakraṃ saṃvaraṃ ca haye grīvākhya bhairavaṃ |  
yogāṃvaraṃ ca kāleśaṃ śāvalī saugamāśritā ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāya nirvāṇapade dvāviṃśati paṭalaḥ || 22 ||  
  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
yathā saṃsādhayed deva prayogādi jagatpate |  
sādhakaḥ saṃvibhāgena tathā kathaya śaṃkaraḥ ||  
  
śrīsadāśiva uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi yathāsaṃsiddhisūcakaṃ |  
yena saṃsādhayed vīro vīrācākulasaṃtate ||  
  
akṛtvā tu puraścaryā prayogaṃ kartumichati |  
mahāpāṭaka koṭīnāṃ bhājanaṃ sa bhaviṣyati ||  
  
nātaḥ parataraṃ devi kulamārgasya dūṣakā |  
tasmāt sarvavyayenāpi prāṇāṃte nāpi sarvadā ||  
  
karmaṇā manasā vācā puraścaraṇamācaret |  
varṇalakṣajapenmaṃtrī haviṣyāsī jiteṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
divā ca brahmacaryeṇa rātrau kuryād yathechayā |  
  
p. 133a)  
  
pūjayed vidhinā devī mapaṃcaka puraskṛtaḥ |  
sāṃgaṃ sa parivāraṃ ca tatra nūnaṃ na kārayet ||  
  
daśāṃśa havanaṃ kuryā bilvapatrai ghṛtaplutaiḥ |  
chāgamāṃsaistimadhvaktairdevī saṃtuṣṭa hetave ||  
  
tarpayet sudhayā devī daśāśai havanasya vai |  
tarpaṇasya daśāṃśena mārjanaṃ hyamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
taddaśāṃśena vai kuryāt kumārī bhojanaṃ mahat |  
kalau catuguṇaṃ kuryāt puraścaryaṃ tu sādhakaḥ ||  
  
dīkṣā prāpyamakuryād vai puraścaryāṃ tu sādhakaḥ |  
dīkṣāprāpya na kuryād vai puraścaryā vilaṃvanaṃ ||  
  
āyūścaṃcalatāṃ jñātvā svātma śreyastu ciṃtayet |  
dīkṣāprāpya puraścaryā makṛtvā mriyate yadi ||  
  
brahmabhūtā bhavennūnaṃ śatavarṣamanāśraye |  
caṃdrasūrya parāge vā puraścaraṇa kārayet ||  
  
sparśān muktiṃ tu saṃpūjya puraścaraṇamucyate |  
daśāṃśaṃ sarvakarmāṇi kāraye pūrvacoditaṃ ||  
  
tataḥ prayoga karmāṇi śṛṇu vakṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ |  
vīradīkṣā na śaktāya saṃpūjya vidhivat purā ||  
  
śmaśāna śivadakṣe vā gṛhe vāvāhane sthitā |  
dīpādi trividhainnitya mahāparvataparvaṇi naḥ ||  
  
satyavāk dhairyasampannaḥ kāmakrodha vivarjitaṃ |  
śaktisaṃhāyasaṃyukto vīraḥ saṃhāyakothavā ||  
  
sahāya dravyahīnāya bhīkṣāsī ca niśāgame |  
sahasraikaṃ japeccādau kāyaśuddhārtha hetave ||  
  
p. 133b)  
  
devī tuṣṭā hune caiva yathāpūrva mayāditaṃ |  
tato lakṣa japenmaṃtrī divācāra vivarjitaṃ ||  
  
bhuktorddhabhāvanāśakte saṃdhyāyāṃ śatamekakaṃ |  
gāyatyāṃ tu japed yugmaṃ nyastvā caiva ṣaḍaṃgakaṃ ||  
  
tato rātrau japaṃ kuryād yathāśaktyā krameṇa tu |  
daśāṃśena hunet paścā maṃtrasaṃsiddhiṃ hetave ||  
  
homāṃte kanyakā pūjyā kṛtasiddhi bhaveddhruvaṃ |  
athavā dviguṇaṃ jāpya yāvad vai saptavāsaraṃ ||  
  
kurādau cāṣṭame sevāddhomāṃte grahaśāṃtikaṃ |  
trisaṃdhyaṃ madhyarātrau ca ekadvitricaturdinaṃ ||  
  
vātādisekate śāṃti homādroga pramucyate |  
aṣṭāmyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ samārabhya śivāvali ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
atha vidhāsya taṃtrasthaṃ samyak ṣaṭkarmalakṣaṇaṃ |  
sarvataṃtrānusāreṇa prayogaphalasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
śāṃti vaśya staṃbhanāni vidveṣoccāṭane tathā |  
māraṇaṃ ca * ti saṃti ṣaṭkarmaṇi manīṣiṇaḥ ||  
  
rogagrahādi pīḍānāṃ nāśanaṃ śātirīritaṃ |  
vaśyaṃ janānāṃ sarveṣāṃ svādhīne tvamudīritaṃ ||  
  
nivṛtti kāraṇaṃdiśca staṃbhanaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ |  
lokānā dveṣaṇamitho vidveṣaṇamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
uccāṭana svadeśāhaṃ bhraṃśanaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ |  
prāṇināṃ prāṇahananaṃ maraṇaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
p. 134a)  
  
sva devatā dikkālādīn jñātvā karmāṇi sādhayet |  
ratirvāṇī ramājyeṣṭhā durgākālī yathā kramāt ||  
  
ṣaṭkarma devatāḥ proktā karmādau tāḥ prapūjayet |  
īśacaṃdrendra ni-ṛtivāmvagnīnāṃ diśaḥ kramāt ||  
  
ṛtavasyurvasaṃtādyā ahorātraṃ dine dine |  
vasaṃtagrīṣmavargāśca śaraddhemaṃtaśaiśilāḥ ||  
  
hemaṃtaśāṃtike proktā vasaṃte vaśyakarmaṇi |  
śiśire staṃbhane prokto vidveṣa grīṣma īritaḥ ||  
  
prāvattuccāṭane jñeyo śaranmāraṇa karmaṇi |  
padmaṃ ca svastikaṃ vāpi vikataṭkukkuṭaṃ kramāt ||  
  
vajraṃ ca bhadramityāhurāsanāni maṇīṣiṇaḥ |  
ṣaṇmudrāḥ kramato jñeyāḥ padmapāśa gaḍā api ||  
  
muśalāḥ śani khaḍgāśca śāṃtikādiṣu karmasu |  
jalaṃ śāṃti vidhau proktaṃ vaśye vahnirudāhṛtaḥ ||  
  
staṃbhane pṛthivī proktā vidveṣavyomakīrtitaṃ |  
uccāṭane mato vāyurbhūyognimāraṇe mataḥ ||  
  
tattadbhūtodaya saṃmyak tattanmaṃḍalasaṃyutaṃ |  
tattat karmavidhātavyaṃ maṃtriṇāniścitātmanā ||  
  
śītāṃśoramṛtakṣoṇī vyomavāyurhavirrujāṃ |  
varṇāsyu maṃtravījāni ṣaṭkarmasuyathākramaṃ ||  
  
graṃthanaṃ ca vidarbhāśca saṃpuṭaśca virodhanaṃ |  
yogaḥ pallava ityete prayojyā ṣaṭsu karmasu ||  
  
maṃtrāṇāṃtaritā kuryān nāmavarṇānyathā vidhi |  
  
p. 134b)  
  
grathanaṃ tadvijānīyāt praśastaṃ śāṃti karmaṇi |  
maṃtrārṇa dvaya madhyastha madhyanāmākṣaraṃ likhet ||  
  
vidarbha eva vijñeyo maṃtribhirvaśya karmaṇi |  
ādāvaṃte ca maṃtrasyān nāmosau saṃpuṭa smṛtaḥ ||  
  
sa eṣa staṃbhane śasta ityukto maṃtravedibhiḥ |  
rāmna ādyaṃta madhyeṣu maṃtra syād rodhanaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
vidveṣaṇavidhāneṣu praśastamidamīritaṃ |  
maṃtrasyāṃte bhaven nāma yoga uccāṭana smṛtaḥ ||  
  
aṃte nāmno bhaven maṃtra pallavo māraṇe mataḥ |  
sitaraktaśvetakṛṣṇa kṛṣṇadhūmrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
varṇato maṃtrasaṃproktā devatāḥ ṣaṭsu karmasu |  
maṃtrāṇāṃ likhane dravyaṃ caṃdranarocanādikaṃ ||  
  
gṛhadhūmaścitāṃgāro māraṇeṣṭaviṣāṇi ca |  
śyenāgni loṣṭapittāni dhūrtūrarasasau tathā ||  
  
gṛhadhūmastrī kukkuṭau viṣāṣṭakamudāhṛtaṃ |  
devatā kālamudrādīn samyak jñātvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
ṣaṭkarmāṇi prayujīta yathoktaphalasiddhaye |  
śāṃtyāstu meṣa carma syādūrṇā carmaraśobhanaṃ ||  
  
śvetacaṃdanādi lipte śītāṃśu bījaśobhite |  
śvetapuṣpābhirdevīnāṃ pūjanīyātha devatā ||  
  
caṃdrakoṭi prabhā bhāsā suddhādṛṣṭyā susādhakaḥ |  
saṃprapaśyaṃti sādhyayāmaṃtribhiḥ śāṃtikarmaṇi ||  
  
p. 135a)  
  
vyāghrasya vā khaḍgino vā carmavaśya praśasyate |  
caṃdanādi yute yaṃtre sudhābījopaśobhite ||  
  
raktapuṣpādibhirdevi pūjanīyātha devatā |  
raktavarṇaṃ vibhāvyai ca vaśyākarṣaṇa sādhaka ||  
  
vaśyakarma yathā devi tathā karṣaṇamucyate |  
gajacarmapradhānaṃ syāt staṃbhane maṃtriṇāṃ sadā ||  
  
caṃdanādi yute yaṃte bhūbījenāpaśobhite |  
sitapuṣpādibhirdevi pūjanīyātha devata ||  
  
kaṃvalaṃ tu praśastasyādāsanaṃ dveṣakarmaṇi |  
citāṃgārasunirmāṇe vyomabījopaśobhite ||  
  
kṛṣṇapuṣpādibhirdevi pūjanīyatha devatā |  
vāyubījasamāyukte uccāṭane tathaiva ca ||  
  
turaṃgasasya carme tu māraṇa syāt praśasyate |  
viṣāṇaṣṭakādi yukte vahni bījena saṃyute ||  
  
devatāṃ pūjayet paścā sādhakeṃdraśiromaṇi |  
śāṃtivaśyākarṣaṇeṣu staṃbhane sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
aṃguṣṭhanāmikābhyāṃ tu yathākālaṃ japenmanūn |  
vidveṣaṇoccāṭanayostarjanyaṃguṣṭhayogataḥ ||  
  
manu japed yathā kālaṃ dhyātvā niścala mānasaḥ |  
kaniṣṭhāṃguṣṭha yogena māraṇe samājjapovaraḥ ||  
  
paścāt kalpoktavidhinā pūjayed diṣṭa devatāṃ |  
nānāprakārakusumairvastrālaṃkārabhūṣaṇaiḥ ||  
  
karpūrāgurukastūrī caṃdanādi vilepanaiḥ |  
  
p. 135b)  
  
dhūpai dīpaistathā vādyai bhairīvādyaravaiḥ sahaḥ |  
caryādi paṃcabhojyāni tasyai devyai nivedyasaḥ ||  
  
chāgaiśca mahiṣādyaiśca valiṃ dadyād yathā vidhiḥ |  
puraścaryā vidhāneṣu śāṃtikādiṣu pārvati ||  
  
paścāt saḥ sthira citte san japellakṣaṃ yathāvidhiḥ |  
gurave dakṣiṇādeyā gobhumyanu ḍuhādikā ||  
  
siddhyarthamaṃtrarājasya puraścaraṇa kāriṇā |  
kṛtvā śāṃtau puraścaryā triṃśatsvarṇaṃ tu lāṃghanaṃ ||  
  
gurave praṇipratyārtha deyād bhakti puraḥsaraṃ |  
athavā viṃśati tulān dadyāt sādhakasattamaḥ ||  
  
triṃśat svarṇa tulāvāpi vaśyakarmaṇi śasyate |  
catvariṃśat svarṇa tulā ākarṣe tu vidhīyate ||  
  
paṃcāśat svarṇa tulā tu staṃbhane saṃpraśasyate |  
ṣaṣṭhisvarṇa tulāyāṃ turiporuccāṭane smṛtā ||  
  
saptati svarṇa tulā tu ripuṇāṃ māraṇe smṛtā |  
śāṃtirvaśyastathā karṣeḥ staṃbhanaṃ ca tathā punaḥ ||  
  
uccāṭanaṃ māraṇaṃ ca ṣaṭkarmāṇi vidurbudhāḥ |  
parātparatarā deva vṛddhānāṃ daśadakṣiṇā ||  
  
adatvā dakṣiṇāṃ samyagaṃ smṛtvā gurupādukāṃ |  
maṃtraprabhāvā deveśa kṛtaṃ tannisphalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
ṣaṭkarmāṇāṃ vidhānaṃ tat kathitaṃ mama durlabhaṃ |  
yeṣāṃ śravaṇamātreṇa svāṃtamūlasitaṃ mahat ||  
  
p. 136a)  
  
yadi snehosti te mātaḥ kadācidabhimāṃ prati |  
tarhi me kathayā svāśu validānaṃ vidhiṃ mudā ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu putra pravakṣyāmi validānaṃ vidhiṃ śubhaṃ |  
nadītīre prāṃtare vā catuspathetha vā punaḥ ||  
  
matsyamāṃsādi saṃyuktaṃ valiṃ dadyā tu sādhakaḥ |  
ehyehīti ca maṃtreṇa vaṭukāya valiṃ bhavet ||  
  
gaṇapatya tu maṃtreṇa valiṃ tasya pradāṃpayet |  
yoginī manunā vatsa tāsāmatha valirbhavet ||  
  
kṣetrapālaśca maṃtreṇa valikasya pradāpayet |  
vāyayādi caturdikṣu dadyād valiṃ catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
ni-ṛtirvaruṇarmadhye sarvabhūta valiṃ bhavet |  
mahāniśi valiṃ datvā tataḥ karma samācaret ||  
  
iṣṭadevīṃ prapūjyātha upacārai suśobhanaiḥ |  
svarṇādi kusumairdeva paṭṭavastrādibhiḥ punaḥ ||  
  
grathanādi vibhedena karmabhedena putrakā |  
iṣṭa devīṃ manuṃ japtvā kramādvāmādikaṃ caret ||  
  
homakarma tataḥ kṛtvā tarpaṇaṃ samupācaret |  
abhiṣekaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā bhojayedvijapuṃgavān ||  
  
subhojiteṣu vipreṣu sarvaṃ hi saphalaṃ bhavet |  
yadi na syād vipra bhojyaṃ tarhi nisphalatāṃ bhavet ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
yathā yadṛṣṭi prakhyatya bhinnaṃ sukapayomṛtaṃ |  
śavamānīya kartavyaṃ nāharet svechayāmṛtaṃ ||  
  
p. 136b)  
  
strīvaśya patitā spṛśyāmayavarjahataṃ naraṃ |  
avyakta liṃgakuṣṭhānāṃ pretarārcāśavaṃ haret ||  
  
na durbhikṣamṛtaṃ varddhaṃ na paryuṣitameva ca |  
strījanaṃ ca dṛśaṃ rūpaṃ sarvathā parivarjayet ||  
  
śūnyāgāra maraṇyaṃ vā nīlāddhṛtyavibhūṣayet |  
saṃsthāpyaśavaśayyāyāṃ puruṣaṃ divyarūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
tataḥ śavaṃ kṣālayitvā snāpayecca prayatnataḥ |  
yadi raktāktakaṃ tiṣṭhe bhairavācca bhayaṃ bhavet ||  
  
elālavaṃgakarpūrā jāti khadira sārddhakaiḥ |  
tāṃbūlaṃ cathukhe kṣiptvā śavaṃ kuryādidho mukhaṃ ||  
  
snāpayitvā ca tatpṛṭhe caṃdanena vilepayet |  
vāhumūlāṃta kaṭyāṃtaṃ caturasraṃ vidhāya ca ||  
  
madhye padmaṃ caturdvāraṃ dalāṣṭaka samanvitaṃ |  
tataścaileyamajitaṃ kamalāṃtarita nyaset ||  
  
pūjā dravyaṃ sannidhau ca dūre cottara sādhakaḥ |  
saṃsthāpya śavamabhyarcya tatraścārohaṇaṃ viśet ||  
  
kuśānyāvatale datvā śavakeśān prasārya ca |  
dṛḍhaṃ nivadhya juṭikāṃ tacca devasya rūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
tasyā devaṃ susaṃspṛśya paṭhedrakṣāya saṃmukhe |  
sarve bhavecca deveśi siddhiṃ śavakṛtāṃvare ||  
  
paṭṭena rajake naiva caraṇau vaṃdhaye dṛḍhaṃ |  
oṃ bhīmabhīru bhayābhāva bhāvyalocanabhāvuke ||  
  
trāhi māṃ devadeveśa śavāśarādhipādhipa |  
iti pādatale tasya trikoṇaṃ tu samālikhet ||  
  
p. 137a)  
  
tenotsvātuṃ na śakroti śavastu niścalo bhavet |  
upaviśya punastatra vāhubhiḥ sārya pādayoḥ ||  
  
hastayoḥ kuśanāstīrya pādau tatra nidhāpayet |  
oṣṭhau saṃpuṭakau kṛtvā sthira citta sthireṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
sadā devaṃ hṛdi dhyātvā maunau japamathācaret |  
carāsanodbhayaṃ nāsti bhayajāte vadet tataḥ ||  
  
yanprārthate valitvena dātavyaṃ kuṃjarādikaṃ |  
dināṃtare tadā syāmi svanāma kathayasva me ||  
  
ityuktvā saṃskṛtoktyā ca nirbhayastu na pūjayet |  
tataśca madhuraṃ vākyaṃ vaktavyaṃ līlayā naraiḥ ||  
  
tataḥ satyaṃ kārayitvā varaṃ ca prārthayet naraḥ |  
yadi satyaṃ na karoti varaṃ vāna prayachati ||  
  
tadā punarjapeddhimānekāgra yatamānasaḥ |  
satyaṃ kṛte varaṃ labdhve saṃtyaje tu japādikaṃ ||  
  
phalaṃ jātamiti jñātvā jūṭikāṃ mocayet tataḥ |  
śavaprakṣālya saṃsthāpya mocayet pādavaṃdhanaṃ ||  
  
pādarajjūṃ mocayitvā pūjādravyaṃ jale kṣipet |  
śavaṃ jale vā garte vā nikṣipya snānamācaret ||  
  
tatastu svagṛhaṃ gatvā valiṃ dadyād dināṃtare |  
yajamāno pragṛhnaṃ tu mayādattamimaṃ valiṃ ||  
  
arthai yeryācitān svānu narakuṃjara śūkarān |  
datvādiṣṭa mayīkena kartavyaṃ samupoṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
parahni nityamācārya paṃcagavyaṃ pivet tataḥ |  
  
p. 137b)  
  
brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayet tatra paṃcaviṃśati saṃkhyakān |  
paṃcapaṃca vihīnāṃ vā krameṇaiva daśāṃvadhi ||  
  
tatra snātvā tu bhuktvā tu nivaseduttamaṃ sthalaṃ |  
yadi na syād viprabhojyaṃ tadā nirddhanatāṃ vrajet ||  
  
tena cennidhanaṃ tasyāt tayā devaḥ prakupyati |  
trirātraṃ vāpi ṣaḍrātraṃ navarātraṃ tu gopayet ||  
  
triśaryo yadi śayena tadā vyādhi vinirdiśet |  
śītaṃ śrutvā ca vadhiro niścakṣurnṛtya darśanāt ||  
  
yadi vekti dine vākyaṃ tadāsyaṃ mūkatā bhavet |  
paṃcadaśadinaṃ yāvad dehe devasya saṃsthitiḥ ||  
  
śeṣāt kuryād gaṃdhapuṣpaṃ vahiṣīti yadā yadā |  
go brāhmaṇānāṃ niṃdāṃ ca na kuryāt tu kadācana ||  
  
deva go brāhmaṇādiśca pratyahaṃ saṃspṛśet suciḥ |  
prātarnitya kriyāṃte ca bilvapatrodakaṃ pibet ||  
  
tataḥ snānaṃ tu gaṃgāyāṃ saṃprāpte śeṣa vāsare |  
svāhāṃte maṃtramuccārya proktā tārā namaḥ padaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ śatatrayaṃ mūrdhna devānvai tarpayejjalaiḥ |  
snāna tarpaṇaśūnyasya na syād devasya tarpaṇaṃ ||  
  
ityanena vidhānena siddhiṃ prāpnoti sādhakaḥ |  
iha bhuktvā carāṃ bhogānaṃte yāṃti hare padaṃ ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
kathayāmi na saṃdehaḥ kumāryā pūjanaṃ śubhaṃ |  
yasyā pūjanamātreṇa trailokyaṃ pūjanaṃ bhavet ||  
  
p. 138a)  
  
kumārī pūjanaṃ nātha tridhāmūrti vyavasthitā |  
parā caivāparā caiva tṛtīyā yā parā parā ||  
  
yatre kālena kiṃcit svād devāsura mahoragāḥ |  
trailokyannatvayādvaṃ ca tadā jātā kumārikā ||  
  
ādyā sṛṣṭi karī yā tu pratyakṣā sā bhavesvidhā |  
umā kalā tu sā jātā sṛṣṭirūpā bhavārṇavai ||  
  
ekavarṣā bhave caṃḍi dvivarṣā tu sarasvatī |  
trivarṣā tu tridhā mūrtiścaturvaṣā tu kālikā ||  
  
śubhagā paṃcavarṣā tu ṣaṣṭhavarṣā umā bhavet |  
saptabhirmālinī sākṣādaṣṭavarṣā tu kubjikā ||  
  
navabhiḥ kālasaṃkarṣā daśabhiścāparājitā |  
ekādaśe tu rudrāṇī dvādaśābde tu bhairavī ||  
  
trayodaśe mahālakṣmī dvisaptā pīṭhanāyikā |  
kṣatrajñā paṃcadaśabhiḥ ṣoḍaśe caṃḍikā matā ||  
  
evaṃ krameṇa saṃpūjya yāvat puṣpaṃ na vidyate |  
pratipadādi pūrṇāṃtaṃ vṛddhibhedena pūjayet ||  
  
mahāparvasu parveṣu viśeṣācca pavitrake |  
mahā navamyāṃ deveśi kumārī ca prapūjayet ||  
  
piṃgalāṃ pūjayed yastu ṣoḍaśaiścaiva bhaktimān |  
bhaktitaḥ pūjayitvā tu sarvasaṃpattimān bhavet ||  
  
pūjayet kulavidyānāṃ me kathā navabhairavīṃ |  
evaṃ praṇavayogena caitanya tanumarcayet ||  
  
evaṃ dvābhyāṃ tribhiścaiva saptāṣṭa navadhā punaḥ |  
  
p. 138b)  
  
nitya krameṇa deveśi pūjayed vidhipūrvakaṃ ||  
  
ghnaṃti vighnān pūjitāstāstathā śatruṃ mahotkaṭaṃ |  
vyādhayaḥ sarvariṣṭāni durnimittāni nāśayet ||  
  
grahāyakṣāḥ kṣayaṃ yāṃti bhūtavetālapannagāḥ |  
asurā guhyakāḥ pretā yoginī guhya ḍākinī ||  
  
mahābhayāni durbhikṣa utpātāni kuleśvari |  
duḥsvapnamapamṛtyaṃ ca anye ye ye samudbhavā ||  
  
kumārī pūjanā deva na tasya prabhavaṃti hi |  
animādeṣṭa siddhāni pātālaguṭikāṃjanaṃ ||  
  
uddiṣṭaṃ divyavetālo bhavet kumārikārcanāt |  
aiṃkāreṇa jalaṃ dadyā hrī&kāre pāda śaucanaṃ ||  
  
śrīṃkāre nārghaṃ dadyāt kūrcabījena caṃdanaṃ |  
śaktibījena puṣpāni ṣaṣṭhe dhūpaṃ ca dāpayet ||  
  
ai& hrī& śrī& kro& stau& imāṃ kulakumārike hṛdayāya namaḥ |  
hsai& hrai& śrī& hrī& ai& svāhā kulakumārike śirase svāhā ||  
  
oṃ hrī& sa& śikhāyai vaṣaṭ || ai& kulavāgīśvarī imāṃ kulakumārike kavacāya   
hū& || hrī& phaṭ svāhā || imāṃ kulakumārike netra trayāya vauṣaṭ || ai& hrī&   
siddhayāya pūrvavaktrāya namaḥ || e ai& jayāya uttaravaktrāya namaḥ || ai& hrī&   
śrī& kubjike paścimavaktrāya namaḥ || ai& phre& kālike dakṣiṇa vaktrāya   
namaḥ ||   
  
vāgbhavena purakṣobhaṃ māyābīje guṇāṣṭakaṃ |  
śriyo bīje śriyālābhaṃ hrī& bījena visaṃkṣayaṃ ||  
  
bhairavena tu bījena khagasvamamarādibhiḥ |  
  
p. 139a)  
  
kumārikā hyahannātha sadā tvaṃ ca kumārikā |  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ vāpi ekāṃ kanyāṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
pūjitā pratipūjyaṃte nigrahaṃtyapamānitā |  
kumārī yogiṇī sākṣāt kumārī sarvadevatā ||  
  
bhūrbhuvo mūrtipādaikā kumārī trikapūjitā |  
asurāduṣṭarogāśca ete duṣṭa grahādapi ||  
  
bhūtavetālagaṃdharva ḍākinīyakṣarākṣasāḥ |  
hṛdaye devatāḥ sarvā bhūrbhuvaścaiva devatā ||  
  
pṛthvivyādīni sarvāṇi brahmāṃḍaṃ sa carācaraṃ |  
brahmāviṣṇuśca rudraśca īśvaraśca sadāśivaḥ ||  
  
bheruṃḍāḥ sarvatuṣṭāśca yastu kanyāṃ prapūjayet |  
kālāgni śivaparyaṃtaṃ tathā gauryādi saṃsthitāḥ ||  
  
saptadvīpāḥ samudrāśca bhuvanāni caturdaśaḥ |  
vidhiyuktaṃ kumārī ca bhojayet kulabhairavaḥ ||  
  
pādyamargha tathā dhūpaṃ kuṃkumaṃ caṃdanaṃ śubhāṃ |  
bhaktibhāvanasaṃyukta sarvaṃ tasyai nivedayet ||  
  
pradakṣiṇa trayaṃ kuryā pādi madhye śubhaṃ bhavet |  
paścācca dakṣiṇā deyā rajata svarṇa mauktikaḥ ||  
  
vivāhayet svayaṃ kanyā brahmahatyāṃ vinaśyati |  
gohatyāṃ caiva strī hatyā sarvapāpaṃ praṇaśyati ||  
  
mātā ca pitarau caiva bhrātaraścaiva sarvataḥ |  
ye tu peca punaḥ sarve kanyādānaṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
bhuktimukti phalaṃ tasya saubhāgyaṃ sarvasaṃpadaḥ |  
rudraloke vasennityaṃ trinetro bhagavān haraḥ ||  
  
p. 139b)  
  
ṣaṣṭhikoṭi sahasrāṇi aśvamedha phalaṃ labhet |  
etat phalaṃ labhessadya kanyāṃ yadi divākaraṃ ||  
  
kanyādānaṃ mahādānaṃ sarvadāneṣu cottamaṃ |  
daurbhāgyaṃ ca pranaśyaṃti kṣipraṃ saubhāgya vartate ||  
  
rājadvāre labhet pūjāṃ rājyamadhye nareśvaraḥ |  
sarveṣāṃ ca kumārīṃ ca pūjayecca prayatnataḥ ||  
  
marudbhaya samutpane pūjyate hyati dāruṇe |  
kroṣṭuke sārameye vā droṇakāke ulūkike ||  
  
gṛdhraikāke ca pārāye yajñāṃte śāṃti karmaṇi |  
mahāpūjā prakartavyā kumārī bhojayed vidhi ||  
  
nātaḥ parataraṃ śāṃti nṛṇāṃ kanyāṃ pacet paraṃ |  
mahābhaya samutpanne kanyaḥ kāṃcaiva pūjayet ||  
  
tatkṣaṇāṃllabhate saukhyaṃ satyaṃ satyañca bhairavī |  
  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāya nirvāṇapade trayoviṃśati paṭalaḥ || 23 ||  
  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
devadeva mahādeva sarvajña parameśvara |  
atyadbhutamidaṃ manye kālikramakulodbhavaṃ ||  
  
mānasaṃ kaṃpate tīva lomaharṣaśca jāyate |  
kathaṃ sā kālikā devīṃ śatakoṭi prabhedataḥ ||  
  
etad bheda trayaṃ kvāpi na śrutaṃ parameśvara |  
sarvaṃ kāli kramāśritya sthiteva bhāsate manaḥ ||  
  
cakreśvarī cakrabhedaṃ kā ca sarvādhikāśritā |  
kramabheda kulodbheda kathaṃ pūjā kramaṃ prabho ||  
  
tasyārcanena deveśa labhed vā kiṃ mahāphalaṃ |  
  
p. 140a)  
  
idaṃ vā mutra kiṃ bhukte sādhakaḥ parameśvaraḥ |  
kathaṃ kālī hyanālaṃ vā sālaṃ vā kāla ghasmarā ||  
  
nirguṇā niṣkalā nityā niraśeti tvayoditā |  
koṭi bhede lakṣabhede vaktuṃ yadi na śakyate ||  
  
mukhya mārgānuśā devya nāyikā vadaśaṃkara |  
yasyārcanena sakalaṃ kālikāṃ pūjitaṃ bhavet ||  
  
eka eva parā nityāṃ yā devī citi rūpiṇī |  
sarvasvarūpā sarveśī citirūpāśritā parā ||  
  
yasyā mutpadyate viśvaṃ līyate sthiyate punaḥ |  
vada deva maheśāna namaste śaśiśekharaḥ ||  
  
tāsāṃ cakreśvarī nityā kā rūpā kati saṃkṣakā |  
amṛtasyaiva pānena yathā tṛpyaṃ tu devatā ||  
  
nāyitāṃ kramabhedaṃ ca śrutvā tṛpyāmi puṣpalaḥ |  
vadaṣyedo na te deva sarvajña śarva sarvataḥ ||  
  
śrīsadāśiva uvāca ||  
  
brahmāṇḍakoṭi lakṣāṇi bhasma sā kurute yayā |  
tāṃ kālagrāsanaratāṃ kālasaṃkarṣaṇīnnamaḥ ||  
  
yasyā krīḍārthamakhilaṃ brahmāṃḍaṃ kaṃdukāyate |  
tāṃ kālagrāsanaratāṃ kālasaṃkarṣaṇīnnamaḥ ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi yastvayā manu pṛchate |  
nitvā niraṃta sā devī brahmasatya prakāśinī ||  
  
vaktrakoṭi sahasraistu jihvākoṭi śatairapi |  
varṇituṃ naiva śaknoti śatābde nāpi suṃdarī ||  
  
paṃcavaktra na jihvābhiḥ paṃcabhiḥ parameśvarī |  
  
p. 140b)  
  
lakṣakoṭi prabhedeṣu deśamātraṃ vadāmite |  
kālikā kramabhedeṣu yā śreṣṭhā mokṣadāyine ||  
  
tāni te kathayiṣyāmi kramapaṃca vinirṇayaṃ |  
paraṃ brahmamayī nityā sākṣājjāgra svarūpiṇī ||  
  
nillepānirguṇā nityā guṇaiḥ saṃkrīḍate jagat |  
na pumān na striyaḥ sākṣāt na khaṃḍo prākṛtena ca ||  
  
avyaktavyaktarūpā ca jāgrad guṇaguṇālayā |  
pṛthivī vāyurāpogni khapaṃcabhūtasammatā ||  
  
tasmārūpamidaṃ sarvaṃ sṛṣṭārthaṃ sṛjate guṇaiḥ |  
dhāraṇī paramā devī dharaṇyādi śivāṃ tathā ||  
  
pṛthak tvāt pṛthivī tyuktvā tataḥ sarvaṃ sahā hyabhūt |  
sarvajīvaṃ prāṇayaṃtī sarvatra caraṇa kṣamaḥ ||  
  
sama sarvatra pratyāyu guṇairvāyo samarpitaḥ |  
caturvidhaṃ jīvanātsva? jagatsthāvarajaṃgamaṃ ||  
  
jalaiḥ saṃvarddhayet sarvaṃ tadguṇaṃ sā jalerpitaṃ |  
dahatya * jagat sarvaṃ mamedhyaṃ medhyameva vā ||  
  
tejasā prajvalatneva tejasā syāḥ smāśritā |  
vyāpakatvāt mahatvā ca niraṃgatvād guṇāgrayāt ||  
  
ākāśa hyarpitā devyā sarvasaṃdhāryate guṇā |  
mahāsaubhāgya jananī mahāsārasvataḥ sadā ||  
  
mahāsaundarya śubhagā mahāmṛtyuvināśinī |  
brahmāviṣṇusureṃdrādi vaṃditā pāpahāriṇī ||  
  
sarvatīrthamayī devī sarvadharma mayī śivā |  
  
p. 141a)  
  
sarvakṣetramayī puṇyā sarvakāryārthasādhinī |  
mahābhogapradāśāṃtā mahāmokṣaphalapradā ||  
  
mahāprabhāvato devī sarvaṃ śuddhyati nānyathā |  
vāmācāraratā vāpi dakṣiṇācāra kṛd bhavet ||  
  
nirācārāpi sā cārāyāpodharma na vidyate |  
kimācāra vicārena yadi kālyārcane rataḥ ||  
  
kimācāra vicāreṇa yadi kālyā na dīkṣitā |  
nirācārā kriyā sarvā sā cārā kriyate yayā ||  
  
śvechatra bhakṣa niyamā nirāhārasamasmṛtaṃ |  
kālināmākṣara padaṃ japanyāpāni naśyate ||  
  
mahāpāṭaka koṭīnāṃ līlayaiva vinaśyate |  
dahyate sarvapāpāni mūlarāśimivānalaḥ ||  
  
cakroddhāraṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣveka manā śive |  
bindu trikoṇapaṃcāra navakoṇa punallikhet ||  
  
aṣṭāraṃ cāṣṭa dalakaṃ daśadvādaśakaṃ tathā |  
ṣoḍaśaṃ dalasaṃlikhya muṇḍaprākālasaṃlikhet ||  
  
catuḥpaṃcāśakaṃ devī kavaṃdhasamudāhṛtaṃ |  
triśūlāgre muṇḍamālā catuḥpaṃcāśake priye ||  
  
aṣṭadikṣu śmaśānāṣṭa vilikhe jvaladayake |  
citāṣṭadikṣu pralikhet mahāpātaka nāśanaṃ ||  
  
hiraṇyarājate vāpi maṇau vāpi ca ṭaṃkite |  
  
p. 141b)  
  
caṃdanāṃ gurukarpūra nābhikāśmīra siṃduraiḥ |  
raktacaṃdana yuktena hetunā ghṛṣṭayet sudhī ||  
  
bhājane lepayet tena likheddhema śalākayā |  
ṛjurekhā surekhena ramyadṛṣṭi manohara ||  
  
pratimāyāṃ paṭe vāpi sthaṃḍile pustake hṛdi |  
khaḍge vātha triśūle vā mahāpātrethavā striyaṃ ||  
  
etena vasu vai pūjyā navayoni parā priyā |  
divāyāṃ brahmacaryaṃ vai maṃgalāyāḥ prapūjayet ||  
  
rātrau yathechayā pūjyā kālikākulaśāsinī |  
kūṭastha prakṛti svāsyā līlābhuvana pāvanī ||  
  
vṛhadvṛha devi proktāreṇṭhādapi mahāmanu |  
arūpāyāṃ tu vakṣyāmi rūpamavyaktarūpiṇiṃ ||  
  
vinādhyānena vai pūjyā sakalāpi kalāsmṛtā |  
tasmāt sādhaka siddhyarthaṃ dhyānayogaṃ vadāmi te ||  
  
pitāmahena devena māṃsamorādhya pārthivā |  
tuṣṭena vai mayā prādād brahmaṇe loka sajjane ||  
  
brahmaṇāpi pulastyā yadattaṃ kāli kulakramaṃ |  
tena viśravase prādād viśravādhanadāya ca ||  
  
tato laṃkādhipāḥ sarvaṃ vaṃśākālikramānugā |  
daśāsyaṃ kuṃbhakarṇaṃ ca vibhīṣaṇa maheṃdrajit ||  
  
hiraṇyakaśipūrvāṇo valirjālaṃdharastathā |  
aṃvarīṣothamāṃdhātā nahuṣohahaiyādayaḥ ||  
  
nāradādyā munigaṇo durvāsāgādhinaṃdanaḥ |  
  
p. 142a)  
  
virūpākhyādayaḥ siddhāremire svechayāmudā |  
tasyā prasāda leśena trailokya vijayī bhavet ||  
  
brahmaṇā preritaḥ paścāllaṃkeśvara vadhāya ca |  
viśvāmitra vaśiṣṭhābhyāṃ rāghavāya pradattavān ||  
  
sarayūtīra tīrthe vai daśonābhṛśatākṣarī |  
triṃśatākṣari maṃtro vai trilokyaiśvarya dāyinī ||  
  
daśāvarṇa mayā devi gopitā yatnataḥ purā |  
yadi pūrṇaṃ bhaved devi maṃtraṃ vai triṃśatākṣarī ||  
  
yojānāti sa puṇyātmā bhairavohaṃ na saṃśayaḥ |  
maṃtramāteti vikhyātā trailokyaiśvarya dāyakaṃ ||  
  
samastamaṃtrajananī sarvamaṃtraṃ pravṛṃhiṇī |  
vahudhāvarṇitaṃ maṃtra mātā sarva pradāyinī ||  
  
pratyaṃgirā mahākālī mokṣasaukhya pradāyinī |  
nānayāsadṛśī vidyā vidyate bhuvanodare ||  
  
rājyadā dhanadā mokṣadabhṛkaivalya dāyinī |  
tenāstreṇa ca rāmeṇa rāvaṇo vinipātitaḥ ||  
  
tadā prabhṛti sā devī sūryavaṃśā nṛpeśvarāḥ |  
iṣṭatvena ca saṃpūjya sarvatasyānugāśritā ||  
  
ādyākālī kramaṃ paṃca ekā sā paṃcadhā gatā |  
kālikulasamudbhavaṃ pulastyenāvatāritā ||  
  
kumārī trimukhākālī nava ekākṣarā sthitā |  
ādyā yā sṛṣṭi kālī ca dvitīyā sthiti kālikā ||  
  
p. 142b)  
  
saṃhārakālikā ugrā bhṛtiyā divyarūpiṇī |  
anākhyā kālikā devī caturtha paramāśritā ||  
  
bhāsā kālī paṃcamī tu advaitabhāvamāsthitā |  
abhinnarūpāstāḥ sarvā guhyakālīstanauśritā ||  
  
śarīrāvayavā vaktrā vyahvādīnāśanādikā |  
paṃcakālī mahogrā sā ekā sā bhinnarūpiṇī ||  
  
ātmā vaiśvarabhūtāyā guhyakālī prakīrtitā |  
tāsāṃ dhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu pāpa bhayāpahaṃ ||  
  
atha vakṣye mahādevyā dhyānayogamanuttamam |  
yogavijñānamātreṇa sādhakasiddhi bhāgbhavet ||  
  
nīlotpaladalaśyāmā nīlaratnavinirmitā |  
jñānaraśmi chaṭāṭopā jyotirmaṃḍalasaṃbhavā ||  
  
daśavaktrā mahākālī saptāviṃśati locanā |  
aṣṭottaraśatārddhaṃ ca bhujādaṃḍairnarānanā ||  
  
dīpakaṃ ūrddhakaṃ vaktra caṃḍayogeśvarī mataṃ |  
jyotirmaya mahāvaktraṃ nirvāṇapada dāyinī ||  
  
tadadhaḥ siṃhavadanaṃ śvetavarṇaṃ subhāsvataṃ |  
pheruvaktraṃ ca tadadhaḥ kṛṣṇa trailokya ḍāmaraṃ ||  
  
kapindrasya mukha vāme raktavarṇa mahojvalaṃ |  
kolavaktraṃ bhaverdakṣaṃ dhūmravarṇaṃ bhayānakaṃ ||  
  
tākṣavaktraṃ ca vāmaṃ ca piṃgavarṇa sa caṃcakaṃ |  
dakṣiṇe makarāsyaṃ ca haritābhaṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
gajāsyaṃ vāmake proktaṃ gauravarṇaṃ mahojvalaṃ |  
hayāsyaṃ dakṣiṇe kālyā śyāmavarṇaṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
p. 143a)  
  
sarve draṣṭrākarālā ca trinetrābhīmanādinī |  
bhrūbhaṃgakuṭilā bhīmā kālāsyā śrīmukhottamā ||  
  
piṃgalorddha jaṭāṭopa caṃdrārddhakṛtaśekharā |  
nānāratnaiśca ghaṭitā śvetaṃ kādyāli mālinī ||  
  
saptāviṃśati muṃḍaiśca raktavipluṣasaṃyutā |  
vajrāli puṣpasaṃyuktaṃ śiromālā prakīrtitā ||  
  
cidratna ca ṭikākādyaṃ khaḍgapāśaṃ ca śaktikaṃ |  
khaṭvāṃgaṃ muṃḍadhanuṣaṃ cakraghaṃṭā ca susvanā ||  
  
vālapretaṃ ca śailaṃ ca kaṃkāra nakulaṃ tathā |  
sarpaṃ ca kuṭṭanī vaṃgaṃ ṣaḍamraṃ oḍikā punaḥ ||  
  
vahni pātraṃ ca daṃḍaṃ ca śruvamaṣṭāra keśarī |  
vastramudgara ḍamaruṃ vibhratī vāmavāhubhiḥ ||  
  
cidratna caṭikā kartṛ tarjanyaṃ kuśadaṃḍakaṃ |  
ratnapūrṇaṃ ca kalaśaṃ triśūlaṃ duṣṭanāśanaṃ ||  
  
paṃcaparśu paṭāvāṇaṃ padmadvīpamatāṃgamaḥ |  
kuṃtaṃ ca pārijātaṃ ca churikā tomaraṃ tathā ||  
  
puṣpamālā ḍiṃḍimaṃ ca gṛdhraṃ svastika varddhanīṃ |  
kamaṃḍalu śruvāścaiva paśupuṣṭibhayāpahaṃ ||  
  
nadyāvarta kuṃḍalaṃ ca māṃsakhaṃḍasuśobhanaṃ |  
bījapunaphalaṃ śūcī vibhratī dakṣavāhubhiḥ ||  
  
vyāghracarmaparīdhānā kālacarmottarīyakā |  
kiṃkiṇī jālaśobhākhyā vīraghaṃṭhāninādinī ||  
  
naupurārāvanirghoṣā ghargharārāvabhīṣaṇā |  
  
p. 143b)  
  
kanakādgadakeyūrā mahāsthi kṛtaśobhanā ||  
  
muṃḍamālā gale devyā āpadāṃtā vilaṃvinī |  
raktapadmamayī mālā śuṣkakādyālikāstathā ||  
  
kāṃcī kaṭṭārako petā kaṭi devyā virājitā |  
brahmasūtrī jvalatkaṃṭhā yogapaṭṭottarīyakā ||  
  
saumyāgrabhūṣaṇairyuktā nāgarājadyalaṃkṛtā |  
ratnakuṃḍalakarṇaśrīpaṃcakālāsana sthitā ||  
  
śivāsanaṃ tadūrddhaṃ ca nīlaṃ nādaurddhalaṃchanaṃ |  
mahārgharatnamāṃsaṃ ca kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ caturbhujaṃ ||  
  
ekavaktraṃ trinayanaṃ bhairavābharaṇānvitaṃ |  
kartṛkāpālahastaṃ ca ḍamaru khaṭvāṃgadhāriṇaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ bhairavapīṭhaṃ tu devyā āsanamuttamaṃ |  
paṃcapretraṃ ca tadadhaḥ brahmādyā paṃcakāraṇāḥ ||  
  
brahmāviṣṇuśca rudraśca īśvaraśca sadāśivaḥ |  
pīṭhaśyāmaṃ raktadhūmraṃ śvetābhā paṃcakāraṇāḥ ||  
  
daṇḍacakra śaktiḥ śūla khaṭvāṃgāyudhadhārakāḥ |  
tarjanī mukhaniḥkṣiptā śivādhasthā trilocanā ||  
  
piṃgaraktatrigusyā hi phetkāraravabhīṣaṇā |  
vajradaṃṣṭrā nakhasparśā padmapṛṣṭhe śivottamā ||  
  
śacīpatyādi ratnaṃ ca digavarṇaśavarṇakaṃ |  
iṃdrapītābha vajraṃ ca vahniraktaṃ sa śaktikaṃ ||  
  
yamaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca daṃḍāḍhyaṃ dhūmraṃ nai-ṛtyakhaḍgakaṃ |  
varuṇaṃ pāśaśubhrāsyaṃ vāyuśyāmakare dhvajaṃ ||  
  
p. 144a)  
  
kuberaṃ kuṃkuma gadāṃ śuklamīśānaśūlakaṃ |  
digaṣṭapatayo jñeyamāsanaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
śuklaṃ kṛtayugaṃ jñeyaṃ pītaṃ tretāyugaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
dvāparaṃ cāruṇaṃ varṇa śyāmaṃ caiva karismṛtaṃ ||  
  
ṛgvedaṃ śuklavarṇaṃ ca yayupītaṃ suvarṇavat |  
sāmaraktamiti khyātaṃ kṛṣṇātharvaṇa ucyate ||  
  
upavedastathā varṇā navamāsa na mucyate |  
sahasrasūrya jvālāgramāsanaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
padmopari sthitā devī nṛtyamānā sadoditā |  
athavā sukhamāsīnaṃ sarvadevādhi yaṃtritā ||  
  
sahasrasūrya pratibhā durnirīkṣāṃdurāsayāṃ |  
sarvadevāśrayā nityā mālinī jayamaṃgalāṃ ||  
  
nūkuhūṃkāra jihvāgraṃ lālayaṃ taṃ viciṃtayet |  
pratyālīḍha padāvāpi nṛtyamānāpi vā smaret ||  
  
sarvamaṃtramayī dhīrā sarvalakṣmī jayeśvarī |  
evaṃ dhyeyā mahākālīmudbhinna navayauvanā ||  
  
bhāsākramasya madhyasthā cakreśī parameśvarī |  
paṃcakālī prabhedāstu viśeṣaṃ śṛṇu pārvati ||  
  
navavaktrā mahākālī saptāviṃśati locanā |  
ūrddhvajyotirmayaṃ vaktraṃ caṃḍayogeśvarī bhidhāṃ ||  
  
cidratna vaṭiko mudrā mūladevyāstu evasā |  
vaktraikaṃ ratnamudrāṃ ca vihīnā paṃcakālikā ||  
  
vakraśastraṃ bhujaṃ mālā māsanāni kramāni ca |  
  
p. 144b)  
  
bhūṣaṇādīni varṇāni yathā śrīguhyakālikā |  
sṛṣṭi sthiti ca saṃhāra anākhyāyāṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
bhāsākālyā tulyarūpā viśeṣaṃ saccatān śṛṇu |  
viśeṣikā viśeṣeṇa tadvakṣyāmi krameṇa tu ||  
  
nīlajīmutasaṃkāśā navavaktrā maheśvarīṃ |  
pūrvokte dhyānarāje tu tulyācānyā maheśvarī ||  
  
vaddhapadmāsanā devī pīnonnatapayodharā |  
jihvāgre ca vāmadaṃṣṭrāṃ darśayaṃtīṃ tribhaṃgikāṃ ||  
  
madaghūrṇita dīrghākṣī dhyānā locana tatparā |  
cidratna vaṭikāstajyā varadā bhayapāninī ||  
  
tarjanyagre sthitaṃ vajra mūrti jvalana sa prabhāṃ |  
raśmi dvādaśasaṃyuktamanākṣeśīṃ smṛret sadā ||  
  
saṃhāracakramadhyasthāṃ nirmāṃsā koṭarāṃvikāṃ |  
pratyālīḍha padā devī daṃtoṣṭaghṛṣṭapiṃḍikāṃ ||  
  
lelihānā lalajihvā mukta huṃkārarāvinī |  
varadānaṃ parityajya vibhrāṇāmajakeśavau ||  
  
daśaśakti samāyuktaṃ viśvasaṃhārakāriṇī |  
sthiti kramasya * mastha īṣat prahasitānanā ||  
  
kharvālaṃvodarī devīṃ rājalīlāsanasthitāṃ |  
ajakṛṣṭau parityajyaṃ brahmakaṃkālavallakī ||  
  
vādayaṃtī mahākālī sthitisthāṃ ṣoḍaśātmikāṃ |  
sṛṣṭikramadhyasthāmaṣṭahāsasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
ūddhāsamayadācāru lalitā tanuvigrahā |  
  
p. 145a)  
  
vihāya brahmavīṇāṃ ca vibhratī caṃdrabhāskarau |  
yonipaṃcakramadhyasthāṃ dhyāyet sṛṣṭaika hetava ||  
  
anākhyā cakramadhyasthāṃ dhyāyet sṛṣṭaika hetava |  
anākhyā cakramadhyasthā bhāsā devī jagatmayī ||  
  
sarvākālī stutā devī ṣoḍaśāre pratiṣṭhitā |  
caṃdrasūrya parityajyāmaṃjīra dvaya dhāriṇī ||  
  
jagadbhāsayate bhāsā kālī viṣṇu samudbhavā |  
vālākumāri yā kālī sarvāsaṃsṛtarūpiṇī ||  
  
trimukhāṣṭabhujā devī kapālamālasaṃyutā |  
pivaṃ tu rudhiraṃ divyaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ trilocanaṃ ||  
  
pāśāṃkuśaṃ vajraśūlaṃ khaṭvāṃgaṃ mudgalaṃ tathā |  
mṛtavālamuṃḍahastaṃ kapālaṃ rakta pūrituṃ ||  
  
evaṃ dhyātvā mahādevī nānābhoga phalapradā |  
etadeva hi bhedoyaṃ paṃcakālasya kāraṇaṃ ||  
  
tataḥ samasta rūpāṇi kālikā krama udbhavā |  
vidhivat pūjaye nityaṃ vidhilopaṃ na kārayet ||  
  
yathā guropadiṣṭaṃ tu tadaiva vratamācaret |  
devatāmaṃtrarūpāni guruveva na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
śive rūṣṭe gurutrātā gururuṣṭe kadāścanaḥ |  
gurureva sadāpūjā kālikā tuṣṭi hetave ||  
  
aṃdhatamasisaṃmagne gurureva parāgati |  
vadhaputra sahasreṣu mātuḥ pituḥ śateṣvapi ||  
  
etebhyo gaurava tvācca gururityabhidhīyate |  
  
p. 145b)  
  
brahmahatyādi pāpānāṃ niḥkṛti samudāhṛtaṃ |  
gurudrohi kṛtānāṃ tu niḥkṛti nāsti pārvatī ||  
  
gurośca devatāyāśca dvaita bhāvaṃ na kārayet |  
svātmavikrayato vāpi gurureva prapūjayet ||  
  
guru tuṣṭe jagat tuṣṭe mityājñā pārameśvarī |  
na mātā na pitāputrā bhrātāvaṃdhu suhṛnnṛpaḥ ||  
  
gurorgurutaraṃ devi na kuryāt tribhiḥ sarvathā |  
yasya prasādājjānīyāt trailokyaṃ sa carācaraṃ ||  
  
na toṣitā gururyena tasya syānniphalā kriyā |  
yasya vaktrādviniryātā devī śabda mayī parā ||  
  
na guruṃ vaṃcaya chiṣyaiḥ prāṇaiḥ kaṃṭhagatairapi |  
devatā maṃtrasakalaṃ laṃghitaṃ tena bhairavaḥ ||  
  
guru daivatamaṃtrāṇi manāgbhedaṃ na kārayet |  
bhedena nilayaṃ yāṃti samūlaṃ vinihaṃti vai ||  
  
gurusaṃtoṣayed yatnaiḥ svaprāṇenāpi śraddhayā |  
dvīpakasyaiva vetāla parāgatimavāpnuyāt ||  
  
gurusaṃtoṣito yena rakṣitaṃ bhuvana trayaṃ |  
nātaḥ parataraṃ kiṃcid gurorabhyadhikaṃ priye ||  
  
aśarīrāvarṇa rūpā brahmāṃḍa vyāpinī śive |  
piṃḍadānādi saṃskāraṃ yathā pitro tathā guro ||  
  
akṛtvā narakaṃ yāti ṣaṣṭhivarṣa śatādhikaṃ |  
śarīradāpitā devi jñānadā gurureva ca ||  
  
piṃḍadānādi saṃskāraṃ yathā pitro tathā guro |  
  
p. 146a)  
  
akṛtvā narakaṃ yāti ṣaṣṭhivarṣaśatādhikaṃ |  
śarīra dāpitā devi jñānadā gurureva ca ||  
  
gurorgurutaraṃ nāsti saṃsāraduḥkhasādhane |  
yasya vaktrādviniryātā varṇaṃ brahmamayaṃ vapuḥ ||  
  
tārayet nātrasaṃdeho narakārṇa vrate dhruvaṃ |  
atohaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sāraṃ sarvārtha kāmadaṃ ||  
  
ekākṣarī navākṣarīṃ ca ṣoḍaśākṣari vāruṇi |  
catupaṃcāśavarṇaṃ ca śatākṣari viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
dviśatākṣari maṃtraṃ ca daśānā tṛśatākṣarī |  
sahasrākṣari deveśi prāṇabhūtāstu kālikā ||  
  
ambaraṃ pavanaṃ vahni āpaṃ ca dharaṇī tathā |  
rāvaṇī nāma sā vidyā mokṣadā bhuktidā priye ||  
  
ekākṣarī parā vidyā bhogamokṣapradā smṛtā |  
śivaśakti samāyogo bhavedatra ca pārvati ||  
  
mahākuṇḍalinī devī mahārāveti pūjitā |  
vahni śivākṣarāṃtaṃ ca kālaṃ kālamavāruṇaṃ ||  
  
śikhī ca madhuhā yuktā kālī prāṇamudāhṛtaṃ |  
kha phre& mātmakalālikhya mahācaṃḍamatā likhet ||  
  
yogeśvarī padaṃ datvā vidyayaṃ sā navākṣarī |  
ṣoḍaśākṣari yā vidyā prāṇabhūtāśca tā śṛṇu ||  
  
yasyopadeśamātreṇa brahmabhūyāya kalpate |  
tripadaṃ tu samuddhṛtya hāmāravaṃ tato likhet ||  
  
p. 146b)  
  
niśāmādhavasaṃyuktaṃ jñeyaṃ tridaśavaṃdite |  
satyārūḍhasāsvataśca tuṣṭinā kavalī kṛtaṃ ||  
  
satyamatyāsamārūḍhā śūkṣmeśa kavalī kṛtā |  
tataścakrī jāṭharaṃ ca nārāyaṇa samanvitaṃ ||  
  
mādhavena samāyukto valānujapunarlikhet |  
māyācaṃḍī kūrca rakṣā mahārāva punarlikhet ||  
  
na tiṃ niyojayed devī śivamaṃtraṃ samuccaret |  
varṇaṣoḍaśamākhyātaṃ maṃtrarājamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
paṃcapiṃdāgrato datvā mahāsaptadaśī bhavet |  
anādima mahāmaṃtraṃ varṇarājamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
śatākṣaraṃ maṃtrarājaṃ tathā paṃcaśatākṣaraṃ |  
paṃcākṣaramādi maṃtraṃ tathāṣṭākṣara maṃtrakaṃ ||  
  
daśonātriṃśatā vidyā mahāmaṃtra udāhṛtā |  
dviśataṃ tu mahādevī navatyadhika suvrate ||  
  
vaśiṣṭha heto hi purā sahasrākṣaramālikā |  
etat parataraṃ devī kulācāra krame vidhiḥ ||  
  
paraṃ brahmasvarūpaṃ tu nādabiṃdu kalātmikā |  
sakalārṇava madhyasthā sakalārṇava rūpiṇī ||  
  
śrīguroḥ kṛpayā devi saṃpradāya kramāgataṃ |  
labhyate yadi bhāgyena konyadhanyatarau bhuvi ||  
  
manuṣyavapurāchannā sa śivo nātrasaṃśayaḥ |  
varṇituṃ naiva śaknoti kālikāyā kulakrama ||  
  
p. 147a)  
  
varṇaṣoḍaśakaṃ vidyā rājyadā prāṇadā smṛtāḥ |  
mahāsaukhya pradāśāṃtā sā kālī prāṇadāyinī ||  
  
vaikharī cānya bhāvatvādaśaktā guṇavarṇane |  
brahmavidyā svarūpā sā bhuktimukti phalapradā ||  
  
ekoccāreṇa deveśi vājapeyasya koṭayaḥ |  
aśvamedha sahasrāṇi prādakṣiṇyabhuvastathā ||  
  
prayāge snānayat puṇyaṃ makarastha divākare |  
tasya śataguṇaṃ proktaṃ kālikā vidhinā caran ||  
  
cāturāśramya yatpuṇyaṃ krameṇa parisevitaṃ |  
yatpuṇyaṃ varṇadharmasya tatpuṇyaṃ kālikārcanāt ||  
  
kāśyādi tīrtha yātrāṃ ca sārddhakoṭi trayānvitaṃ |  
tulānāyati deveśi satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
lakṣajāpena deveśi kiṃ punaḥ siddhabhāgbhavet |  
yasyāmartha tato devyā bhuvanāni caturdaśaṃ ||  
  
abhavatyarameśāni teṣāṃ kāraṇarūpiṇī |  
puraścaryā kṛtā yena teṣāṃ vidyā phalāṃ gamaṃ ||  
  
akṛtvā tu puraścaryā na maṃtraṃ phalado bhavet |  
brahmāṃḍakoṭi jananī mahāmokṣa pradāyinī ||  
  
niḥsaraṃti mahāmaṃtrā visphuliṃgā yathā priye |  
agne sakāśādvahavā bhedā vidyā prakāśitā ||  
  
praṇavā sarvamutpannā paraṃ brahma mayī tu sā |  
  
p. 147b)  
  
yāmāhartā rakṣitā ca nānyā tu bhuvaneśvarī |  
nānāmnāya svarūpeṇa nānārūpeṇa māyayā ||  
  
mohayaṃtī jagatsarvaṃ putrapautra pravarddhinī |  
strīpuṃbhāvena satataṃ graṃthitaṃ kāmasūtrake ||  
  
sarvatra vyāpinī cāpi brahmasthāna nivāsinī |  
saubhāgya vaṃdhagrahaṇā viśvayoniritīrita ||  
  
caturvāṅmaya niṣṭheyaṃ trailokyavaśakāriṇī |  
sākṣātsaṃcinmayī devī rūpiṇī bhāgyadāyinī ||  
  
mahāsaṃpat padānityā sākṣādakṣararūpiṇī |  
ṣoḍaśākṣararūpeṇa viśvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitā ||  
  
navākṣarī mahāvidyā paṃcacāṣṭākṣarī tathā |  
ekākṣarī daśārṇā ca śatārṇā ca sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
eteṣva maṃtravargeṣu viśvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitā |  
caturvedeṣu yatsāraṃ tadaṃgeṣu ca ya smṛtaṃ ||  
  
purāṇe smṛti sāreṣu yastu sāratamaṃ mahat |  
tatsarvebhyādhikaṃ sāraṃ sārātsārataraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
navanītaṃ yathā dadhnā sāroddhṛtya ghṛtaṃ bhavet |  
tadeva amṛtaṃ nāma devānāṃ prāṇadhāraṇaṃ ||  
  
tathā samasta śāstreṣu vede maṃtreṣu cāgnaye |  
uddhṛtya sarvasārebhyo brāhmaṇe pratipāditā ||  
  
brāhmaṇopi vaśiṣṭhāya vaśiṣṭhorāghavāya ca |  
dattaṃ sarvātmane tena tato martyā vatāritā ||  
  
advaito dvividhā kṛtvā muninā jñānadṛṣṭinā |  
daśonātriṃśatā kuryā maṃtravīryā prakāśitā ||  
  
saumyasiddhi kṛtā tena devī pratyaṃgirābhidhā |  
nāradānumate naiva saṃjñā devyā dvidhā kṛtā ||  
  
nidhānaṃ mivacaurebhyo rakṣaṇīyo prayatnataḥ |  
na deyā yasya kasyāpi deyā prāṇapradāyine ||  
  
nirmalāya praśāṃtāya prāṇebhyopi priyāya ca |  
jñānaniṣṭhā yadātavyaṃ sārametan maheśvari ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade caturviṃśati paṭalaḥ || 24 ||  
  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
namo devādhidevāya sarvajñāya mahātmane |  
sṛṣṭisthityaṃta kartre ca sarvavyāpi namostute ||  
  
jayadeva jagannātha kiṃci praṣṭuṃ mama prabho |  
manometaralaṃ jāto bhayāvaktuṃ na cotsahe ||  
  
prasīda parameśānaṃ saṃśayaṃ chetu marhasi |  
  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
mā śaṃkā kuru deveśi tvadanyo nāsti mat priyāṃ |  
niḥśakaṃ svachayā devī pṛchayaṃ hṛdi vāṃchitaṃ ||  
  
yaṃ yaṃ tvat saṃśayaṃ devi taṃ taṃ pṛchayathechayā |  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
namastubhyaṃ namastubhyaṃ namastubhyaṃ maheśvarī |  
  
p. 148b)  
  
cidrūpiṇī parā devī kālikā tvaṃ gatā yadā ||  
  
tasmādvaidha gatā deva nāradānumatena ca |  
sarvāgama vidaḥ śūraḥ sādhakānāṃ varo muni ||  
  
kiṃ bhadaṃ caiva kārathavaśiṣṭhanāradau purā |  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
dhanyosi kṛtakṛtyāsi śrotuṃ jānāsi tatvataḥ |  
etat sūkṣmāti bhedena punaḥ śrotuṃ matistava ||  
  
jātā paramikā buddhi namaste parameśvari |  
saptādaśākṣarī vidyā vidyāyā paramā kalā ||  
  
khaṃḍasya khaṃḍinī khaṇḍā khaṇḍakhaṃḍāgakhaṇḍinī |  
khaṃḍacakra gatā kālī vidyāsaptadaśākṣarā ||  
  
phaṇirūpasya kālasya akulā viṃdubhakṣaṇī |  
tṛdhā cāruhatā lakṣmī vidyāsaptadaśī smṛtā ||  
  
akalākalamadhyasthā kalāsthā akalākalā |  
akarāparamānaṃdā siddhi saptādaśākṣarī ||  
  
rāvasthaṃ rāvamadhyasthaṃ rāvarāvaniyojitā |  
rāvalīrāvarājñeyā mahāsaptādaśākṣarī ||  
  
kāṃtagādi chāṃtajātaṃ mahāhṛllola huṃkṛtaṃ |  
rāvalolakarākrāṃtaṃ etā saptadaśī kalā ||  
  
akṣarākṣara yogena kāli śabde naya sthitā |  
yogeśvarī padaṃ nāsti vidyāsapta daśākṣarī ||  
  
hahahāhahalalīnā vilīnāṃ hahane hasā |  
  
p. 149a)  
  
hanādānā padaillīnā vidyāsaptadaśīkṣarī |  
evaṃ saptadaśaṃ varṇaṃ varṇayaṃ parameśvarī ||  
  
kramasarvāturaṃ tīvraṃ nirguṇaṃ parameśvarīṃ |  
śatadvayaṃ tu varṇānāṃ navatyadhika kīrtitaṃ ||  
  
triguṇai rahitā vidyā trikhaṃḍā parikīrtitā |  
navaṣoḍaśavarṇānāṃ bhedānātraiva vidyate ||  
  
anayā vidyayā devī janmamṛtyu vihāya ca |  
nāradādyā muniḥ śreṣṭhā yoginaḥ kapilādayaḥ ||  
  
trilokavijayī bhūtvā svechayā vicaraṃti vai |  
avyāhatagatiḥ prāptattrikālajño bhavat tadā ||  
  
śoṇitākhye pure devi hariśaṃkara vigrahe |  
nāradena munīndrena kṛṣṇāya saṃpadattavān ||  
  
hariśājṛṃbhanāstreṣu prayojyā haramohitaḥ |  
vāsudevopi pārthāya rakṣārthaṃ pradadau purā ||  
  
bhṛgopabhuktapuṣpaṃ tu śivayogyaṃ yathā bhavet |  
tadvat nirakṣaraṃ vastu akṣarairapi saṃyutā ||  
  
noddhāraṃ lekhayed devi sākṣāvarṇeśvarī parā |  
śāpo bhavati vai nūnaṃ maṃtrahāni prajāyate ||  
  
vimukha bhavate kālī pāpā nāmāśrayo bhavet |  
karṇe karṇe tu deveśi hṛdisthaṃ kuru sarvadā ||  
  
guruvaktrā viniḥkrāṃtā śrotramārge hṛdi sthitāḥ |  
udake likhitaṃ yadva maṃtroddhāraṃ tathā bhavet ||  
  
p. 149b)  
  
bhogamokṣapradā vidyāṃ pustake naiva lekhayet |  
saṃvachalakṛtā vāse jñātvā karmaśubhāśubhaṃ ||  
  
tato maṃtra padeṣṭamyāyadyānmaśubhamichati |  
aparichita śiṣyāya yastu maṃtraṃ prayachati ||  
  
niraye niyataṃ vāso bhaviṣyati sudāruṇe |  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena na prakāśyaṃ kadācana ||  
  
astikya buddhi yasyāsti tasmai devī prasīdati |  
suṃkāyā jāyategnāni saṃkāyā duḥkhabhājanaṃ ||  
  
saṃkāyā siddhi hāni syāt nirvikalpaṃ samāśriyet |  
kartavyaṃ vāpyakartavyaṃ naiva tatra vicārayet ||  
  
mayāpi viṣṇunā sārddhaṃ brahmaṇā munibhiḥ saha |  
ekapātraṃ gṛhītvā tu nirvikalpa yathāśritā ||  
  
devagaṃdharva daityādīn rakṣapannagamānavā |  
saptadhātubhiḥ saṃklinnai malamūtraśravāvahe ||  
  
teṣāṃkita dvicāreṇa nirvikalpa samācaret |  
sūryodaye kiṃ tamāsi tiṣṭhaṃti bhuvanodate ||  
  
tathā devyā prabhāvena kimācāra vicārayet |  
kiṃ vahuktena deveśi gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ ||  
  
sarvasiddhin maheśāni gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ |  
prakaṭe mṛtyumāpnoti siddhi hāniśca jāyate ||  
  
yasmin maṃtre yadācārastatra dharmastu tādṛśaḥ |  
kṛtārthastena jāye tṛsvargaṃ vāmo kṣameva vā ||  
  
p. 150a)  
  
nāḥ dharmā naiva pāpādi jāyate tat krameṇa ca |  
kiṃ ca dharmo mahānvāpi purāparāśi pravarddhate ||  
  
śaktā sarvasamutpannaṃ yatkiṃcijjagatī gataṃ |  
tasmāchuddhamaśuddhaṃ vā śakti brahmasvarūpakaṃ ||  
  
sarve vedavido vipra sadācāriṇi suvrate |  
cāṃḍālaṃ vapace pāpe hyātmā sarvatra vartate ||  
  
ātmā brahmavijānā hi bhrāṃti jñānaṃ parityaja |  
jñānameva paraṃ tatvaṃ tasmājñānaṃ samāśraye ||  
  
jñānamārgena sakalaṃ vikalpaṃ parivarjayet |  
sa vikalpā mahādoṣa pāpabhāk jāyate dhruvaṃ ||  
  
śivaśaktī mayaṃ dehaṃ rajaṃ śukraimajāyate |  
paraṃ brahmaṇi saṃlīnā parāvācyā pareśvari ||  
  
nīrājya madhumaireyai dravya bhedā bhavaṃti hi |  
sarvajñe tve varārohe yajñe doṣā na vidyate ||  
  
aśvamedhe mahāyajñe vājihatyā kathaṃ bhavet |  
jalaṃ kṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ caivaṃ madhumaireyamaikṣavaṃ ||  
  
pauṣpaṃtaru bhavaṃ dhānyaṃ saṃbhavaṃ takra nirmitaṃ |  
sahakāra bhavaṃ caiva vividha vahubhedataḥ ||  
  
ajñānaiḥ saṃskṛtaṃ sadyo mahāpātaka kṛdbhavet |  
brahmahatyāsurāpāna svarṇasteyādi pātakān ||  
  
pūjanād devanirvatya nirvikalpa sa maṃtravit |  
jalaṃ jalacaṃlaṃ sarvaṃ ghaṭapūrṇaṃ samānaye ||  
  
sthāpite dina saptāhe jalaṃ jīva samanvitaḥ |  
  
p. 150b)  
  
anāmikhaṃ nāsti kiṃcit sarvakṣīrādikaṃ priye |  
samavṛkṣaḥ samo vahnistathā suṃdari tiṣṭhati ||  
  
sarvabhūteṣu vijñānaṃ jñātavyaṃ deśikottamaiḥ |  
kāṣṭhadi mathanād devi prakaṭā vahnirucyate ||  
  
tatkāṣṭhaṃ dahyate tena tena brahmamayaṃ jagat |  
dharmādharmaparityāgāt sakalepi paratra ca ||  
  
viṇmutra strīrajaṃ vāpi yaccāsti sakalaṃ priye |  
vicārayet sumutrādi bhrāṃtireva hi kāraṇaṃ ||  
  
annaṃ brahmavijānīyāt tena yasya samudbhavaṃ |  
nānā jīvāśrayaṃ taṃ tu purīṣaṃ kena duḥkhyate ||  
  
gomūtraṃ prāṇanaṃ devi gomūtrasyāpi bhakṣaṇaṃ |  
prāyaścitteṣu kathitaṃ brahmahatyādi mocana ||  
  
malamūtreṣuje bhrāṃti doṣa eva na saṃśayaḥ |  
strīraja parameśāni dehaste naiva jāyate ||  
  
kalpitaṃ dūṣitaṃ tena prāpyate paramaṃ padaṃ |  
puruṣasya tu bījaṃ tu kha?durityavidhīyate ||  
  
biṃdustu parameśāni kāyoyaṃ śivarūpadhṛk |  
śivatatvena śāsthādi dūṣaṇaṃ nāsti vai tadā ||  
  
sūtaḥ pavitraṃ dehasya kāraṇaṃ kena vidyate |  
jñānamārgena sakalaṃ nirvikalpasya suṃdari ||  
  
vikalpasya maheśāni pāpabhāg jāyatena ca |  
  
p. 151a)  
  
nirvikāla tayā yasya rasenā kutsitā bhavet |  
taṃtu dūṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ manyatsarvaṃ śubhaṃ bhavet ||  
  
brahmānaṃda mayaṃ jñānaṃ paraṃ brahmamayo bhavet |  
taṃ jñātvā parameśāni kathayāmi varānane ||  
  
na brahmaṇastura brāhmyai nakṣatraṃ kṣattriyastathā |  
vaiśyo na vaiśyaḥ śūdreṇa śūdrastu parameśvarī ||  
  
vicāre parameśāni puṣkaso naiva puṣkaśaḥ |  
sarvasāṃtu vijānī hi paramātmā viniścayāt ||  
  
ākāśāt patitaṃ toyaṃ nimnamārgena gachati |  
grāmamadhya gataṃ sarvaṃ viṣṭhāmutrādi pūritaṃ ||  
  
mṛtagośvā hi mārjāra kharāti rudhirānvitaḥ |  
samastamapi deveśi gaṃgāyāmilitaṃ yathā ||  
  
gaṃgāmṛtaṃ tadevāsti kāluṣyaṃ naiva tiṣṭhati |  
malamūtreṣu ye doṣā bhrama eva hi kāriṇī ||  
  
pavitraṃ strī rajaṃ proktaṃ yato deha viniḥsmṛtaṃ |  
rudhirādi vidhānena prāpyate paramaṃ padaṃ ||  
  
puruṣasya tu yadbījaṃ biṃdurityabhidhīyate |  
sarvasya kāraṇaṃ reto taṃ dehaṃ kena nindyate ||  
  
bhagaliṃgasya saṃsparśād garbhādviniḥsṛtaḥ pumān |  
yadā tadā janmakāle kona syād guru talpagaḥ ||  
  
puṇyapāpavinirmuktaṃ jñānametacchṛṇu priye |  
brahmāṃḍakoṭi jananī ekaivāhaṃ svarūpiṇī ||  
  
p. 151b)  
  
bhuktvā nānāvidhairvāhaṃ krīḍārthaṃ sakalaṃ jagat |  
kulālacakra bhedena ghaṭākālaṃ yathā ghaṭe ||  
  
dṛśyate parameśāni ākāśa vyāpya tiṣṭhati |  
ghaṭe bhavati bhinnatvenākāśe bhinnatā bhavet ||  
  
yathā dehagato jīvā dehanāśe varānane |  
vyāpyati sarvatra * * tasmād brahma padaṃ mahat ||  
  
ata eva maheśāni nirvikalpa sadā bhavet |  
evaṃ samvinmaye jñānaṃ samatā sarvajaṃtuṣu ||  
  
sarvavarṇeṣu cābhāvat samatā nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
yathāsūrya prakāsebhya samatvena pravartate ||  
  
dattamavyāpi cānyasya tamasaṃ * hate kṣaṇāt |  
śoṣayet sarvamūtrādi caṃdanaṃ naiva kardamaṃ ||  
  
ata eva maheśāni saṃti sarvamayo bhavet |  
siddhistu devi vijñeyu śrīguro kṛpayā priye ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
yathāsaṃsādhayed deva prayogādīn jagatpate |  
sādhakaḥ saṃvibhāgena tathā kathaya śaṃkara ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi yathāsaṃsiddhi sūcakaṃ |  
yena saṃsādhayed vīro vīrācākulasaṃtate ||  
  
akṛtvā tu puraścaryā prayogaṃ kartumicchati |  
mahāpāṭaka koṭīnāṃ bhājanaṃ sa bhaviṣyati ||  
  
nātaḥ parataraṃ devī kulamārgasya dūṣakā |  
tasmāt sarva vyayenāpi prāṇāṃtenāpi sarvadā ||  
  
p. 152a)  
  
karmaṇā manasā vācā puraścaraṇamācaret |  
varṇalakṣaṃ japen maṃtrī haviṣyāsī jiteṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
divā ca brahmacaryena rātrau kruyād yathechayā |  
pūjayed vidhinā devimapaṃcaka puraskṛtaḥ ||  
  
sāṃgaṃ sa pacivāraṃ ca tatra nūnaṃ na kārayet |  
daśāṃśaṃ havanaṃ kuryā bilvapatrai ghṛtaplutaiḥ ||  
  
chāgamāṃsaistrimadhvaktairdevī saṃtuṣṭahetave |  
tarpayet sudhayā devī daśāṃśai havanasya vaiḥ ||  
  
tarpaṇasya daśāṃśena mārjanaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ |  
taddaśāṃśena vai kuryāt kumārī bhojanaṃ mahat ||  
  
kalau caturguṇaṃ kuryāt puraścaryāṃ tu sādhakaḥ |  
dīkṣā prāpya na kuryād vai puraścaryā vilaṃvanaṃ ||  
  
āyuścaṃcalatā jñātvā svātma śreyaṃ tu ciṃtayet |  
dīkṣā prāpyapuraścaryāmakṛtvā mriyate yadi ||  
  
brahmabhūtā bhaven nūnaṃ śatavarṣamanāśraye |  
tasmāt sarvātmanā devī puraścaryā samāśrayet ||  
  
candrasūryoparāge vā puraścaraṇa kārayet |  
parśānmuktiṃ tu saṃjapya puraścaraṇamucyate ||  
  
daśāṃśaṃ sarvakarmāṇi kāraye pūrvacoditaṃ |  
tataḥ prayoga karmāṇi śṛṇu vakṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
vīradīkṣā na śaktāye saṃpūjya vidhivat purā |  
śmaśāne śivadakṣe vā gṛhe vā vāhane sthitā ||  
  
dīpādi trividhairnityamabhāvāt parvaṇi punaḥ |  
  
p. 152b)  
  
satyavāk dhairyasampannaḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ |  
śaktisaṃhāyasaṃyukto vīraḥ sahāyakothavā ||  
  
sahāya dravyahīnotha bhīkṣāsī ca niśāgame |  
sahasraikaṃ japeccādau kāyaśuddhyartha hetava ||  
  
devī tuṣṭā hune caiva yathā pūrvamayoditaṃ |  
tato lakṣaṃ japen maṃtrī divā cāhāravarjitaṃ ||  
  
bhuktorddhabhāvanāśaktaḥ saṃdhyāyāṃ śatamekakaṃ |  
gāyatryā tu japed yugmaṃ nvastvā caiva ṣaḍaṃgakaṃ ||  
  
tato rātrau japaṃ kuryād yathāśaktyā krameṇa tu |  
daśāṃśena hunet paścāt maṃtrasaṃsiddhi hetave ||  
  
homaṃ te janyakā pūjyā kṛta siddhirbhaveddhruvaṃ |  
athavā dviguṇaṃ jāpyaṃ yāvad vai saptavāsaraṃ ||  
  
krūrādau cāṣṭamesekāddhomāṃ te grahaśāṃtakaṃ |  
trisaṃdhyaṃ madhyarātrau ca ekadvitricaturdinaṃ ||  
  
vātādi sekato śāṃti homādrogapramucyate |  
aṣṭamyāṃ vā caturdaśyāṃ samārabhya haraśataṃ ||  
  
daśāṃśa homataḥ sekāt mahāśāṃti bhave sphuṭaṃ |  
japa paṃcaśataṃ maṃtrī yachagyaṃ triśataṃ hunet ||  
  
homāṃte sekataḥ paśya puṣṭi caiva samāpnuyāt |  
triśataṃ triśataṃ hutvā japtvā caivāṣṭa me hani ||  
  
hāmāṃte sekato japtvā puṣṭimāpnoti mānavaḥ |  
japtvā caiva tu sahasraṃ hunet paṃcaśatāni vai ||  
  
p. 153a)  
  
nāgāśca goṣṭalokānāṃ puṣṭimāpnoti saikataḥ |  
nirgalādgala yaṃtrāṇi ātmano vā parasyatha ||  
  
trisaṃdhyāvartanādvaścā trisaptāhāt prajāyate |  
śmaśāna śarkarā gṛhya maṃtrairaṣṭa śataṃ japet ||  
  
yatra yatra kṣiped gauri nigaḍā sphoṭanaṃ bhavet |  
bhūtāṃkuśaspadaṃdena tridhābhimaṃtritāṃ dadhān ||  
  
nāvāśakaṭa yaṃtrāṇi staṃbhayet mocayeślathāt |  
dūrvātaṃ tu viṣakṣobhaṃ duḥkulaṃ duṣṭajaṃtuṣu ||  
  
vālukā saptajaptvā tu mahāmeghyāṃ tu vārayet |  
rājikā saptajaptvā tu grasta bhūtādi bhinnaraḥ ||  
  
tāḍayeddhṛti mudrāyāṃ kṛtvā saṃtyajyate dhruvaṃ |  
jvarā cāturthakādyāśca saptajaptodakena tu ||  
  
atyukṣaṇonivartaṃte citrāgugguludhūpataḥ |  
lutāgardabhavisphoṭa vyādhayo vividhāstathā ||  
  
saptajapto dakṣasekāt pānālopa dvināśayet |  
ekaviṃśati vāraistu jalaṃ caivābhimaṃtritaṃ ||  
  
sthāvaraṃ jagamaṃ vāpi viṣapānādvināśaye |  
puṣpānna siddhisiddhārtha śmaśānasya ca bhasmakaṃ ||  
  
saptamaṃtrāhane chatruṃ saśatruṃ mohanāya ca |  
mahāpātre dhānyapuṃje madhyapūrṇaghaṭeṣu ca ||  
  
akṣayaṃ tadbhavet tasya nitya pūjāratasya ca |  
arthakoṣe bilvagatāṃ sauliṣya paṭake japet ||  
  
p. 153a)  
  
dhanadena samaṃdravyaṃ na kadācid vinaśyati |  
gajaśāle muktadāme pūjayet paṃkajātpalaiḥ ||  
  
na kadācid vinaśyaṃti gajāvṛddhiṃ prajāyate |  
kṛtvā ca navakoṇaṃ thāmaśvasthānakadaṃvakaiḥ ||  
  
saṃpūjyā śvāna naśyaṃti vṛddhimāyāṃti śobhanāṃ |  
śitaguṃjaṃ ca sarpokhāṃ dhāmavyāghravarāṭikā ||  
  
saptajapto mukhe dhāryā astranaṃgo na jāyate |  
vālānāṃ sarṣapā maṃtrya śatayvenāmasaṃkhyayā ||  
  
kaṇṭhe vaddhā vṛddhiyāṃti āyu vā prajñayā dṛḍhaḥ |  
puṣpārke śrīphalaṃ pakvaṃ sahasrārddhena maṃtritaṃ ||  
  
tarjaleḥ secitā nārī aputro sūyate sutaḥ |  
ahorātroṣito bhūtvā anudigdho jape tu yaḥ ||  
  
svārtha vātha parārthaṃ vā apamṛtyurvinaśyati |  
puṇḍarīkāṃśunā vartyā kā guhyaṃ dīptasaṃmukhe ||  
  
vane jāyāt sahasreṇa aṃjanī paśyate nidhiṃ |  
catuḥpatha mṛdaṃ gṛhya gṛhārddhe paṃcaviṃśati ||  
  
japtvā saṃkṣapayennidrāṃ vaṃdho bhavati durbhagā |  
tilataṃḍulasiddhārthaṃ pratyekaṃ daśamaṃtritaṃ ||  
  
ekīkṛtya kṣiped yastu padaṃ nā kramate ari |  
phalvālivaṃsikaṃ paṃcaviṃśādhikaśatābhidhaṃ ||  
  
bhūtāyāṃ saṃkṣiped yatra tatra rogī bhavejjanaḥ |  
lājā cākṣata siddhārthaṃ sa bhasmaśatamaṃtritaṃ ||  
  
p. 154a)  
  
yatra yatra kṣipen maṃtrī tato rogyaṃ pravartate |  
kaṃṭhamātrodake sthitvā japet paṃca gataṃ yadi ||  
  
varuṇena tathā homān mahāvṛṣṭi bhaveddhruvaṃ |  
śatārddhaṃ tu japen maṃtrī śatārddhaṃ homayet priye ||  
  
vaśī kuryāt na saṃdeho saptāhena śacī patiṃ |  
japtvā paṃcaśataṃ maṃtrī śatārddhaṃ homayet punaḥ ||  
  
punapaṃcaśataṃ japtvā siddhārthaṃ cākṣataṃ tathā |  
mastake kaṇṭha vāho vā dhṛtā dīvyasya staṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
apāmārga śataṃ hutvā tatkāraṃ tasya dīyate |  
durbhago jāyate nityaṃ prīti nāśo mavāpnuyāt ||  
  
siddhārthaṃ gugguluṃ caiva ekīkṛtya śatatrayaṃ |  
homāṃte ca mahāprīti viprīti sa prajāyate ||  
  
haimabījaḥ śatāṣṭau ca homayet saptavāsaraṃ |  
unmattau jāyate śīghraṃ vartulaṃ vā ghṛtānvitaṃ ||  
  
saptāhā ca niśārātrau japecchuddhā samanvitaḥ |  
divā ca brahmacaryena rātrau kuryā yathechayā ||  
  
karpāsāsti tuṣā taila yuktaṃ paṃcaśataṃ hune |  
ekaviṃśa dineṃ devi śakrasyāpi śriyaṃ haret ||  
  
guruśukla tṛtīyā * pūjākuṃbhe śataṃ japet |  
hutvā trimadhuraṃ sekād bhaṣṭa śrīlabhate śriyaṃ ||  
  
piṣṭhena prākṛtiṃ kṛtvā maṃguṣṭhāmaṣṭakāvadhi |  
chitvāpaṃcaśataṃ hutvā svakulāṃ parineṣpati ||  
  
p. 154b)  
  
siṃdūramakṣatāṃ yuktaṃ śatāṣṭaparimaṃtritaṃ |  
kṛtvā kanyākare datvā āviṣṭāveṣṭakaṃ bhavet ||  
  
rājikā dhūmajaṃ kṣāraṃ daśadhā vābhimaṃtritaṃ |  
mahoragapraśamanaṃ snāna mātreṇa niścitaṃ ||  
  
tailaṃ vātha ghṛtaṃ vātha aṣṭadhā cābhimaṃtritaṃ |  
pānātnābhi pradānācca prasūteṃ mukhanidrayā ||  
  
śirasthāne ghaṭaṃ pūjya aṣṭottaraśataṃ japet |  
hitāhiteṣu kāryeṣu svaparai codayaṃ labhet ||  
  
hatāmvarasamādāya kṛṣṇamāvartya lakṣakaṃ |  
tathaivā dṛśyakaḥ satyaṃ krīḍate vasudhā tale ||  
  
paṃcaviṃśati sāhasraṃ kare kṛtvā vacā japet |  
japāṃte bhakṣayet prājñā vāgīśvara samo bhavet ||  
  
lakṣārddha homayed vīraḥ kadaṃvakusumairyadā |  
kuṃḍoduttiṣṭhate śīghraṃ vetālāḥ siddhyate tadā ||  
  
kākinī vīrahomena tuṣṭā bhūtapiśācikā |  
lakṣārddhārddhana homena nityaṃ dadyātpalaikikā ||  
  
kanyāhastaṃ talaṃ gṛhna śatārddhaṃ tu śmaśānake |  
japtvā bhūtabhaviṣyaśca vartamāna bhavattvaliṃ ||  
  
nṛgolocanakau gṛhya salālaśata * nvitaṃ |  
lalāṭe tilakaṃ kṛtvā yaḥ paśyet sa vaśo bhavet ||  
  
kuṃkumā gurukarpūra rocanāmi sumiśritaiḥ |  
śatābhimaṃtritaṃ kṛtvā tilakaṃ yaḥ karikṣati ||  
  
p. 155a)  
  
raṇe rāja kule dyūte vivāde sa jayī bhavet |  
siddhartha kavacāśvetā pratyuṣe kalaśodare ||  
  
kṛtvā prāta caturdaśyāṃ saṃpūjya madhusaṃyute |  
mukhe prakṣipya japtvā tu paravāde jayo bhavet ||  
  
śritaśrapuṃkhikā mūlaṃ śatāṣṭa parijāpitaṃ |  
śiroveṣṭikaye vadvā paravāṇa nivāraṇaṃ ||  
  
ācāravārabhedena tatra devī na vidyate |  
nirācāro piśācārā tasmā devyāpa bhāvataḥ ||  
  
viśeṣa kiṃ bahuktena sārametad vadāmyahaṃ |  
nṛ carmamāsanaṃ kṛtvā narapātre prapūjayet ||  
  
yathā guru mukhod dviṣṭa nirvikalpena sādhayet |  
lākṣārasanibhenaiva hetunā paripūritaṃ ||  
  
phalguṃ datvā tatra madhye pātrahetu prapūrite |  
aṣṭamyāṃ vā caturdaśyāṃ navamyāṃ vā viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
śivarātryāṃ tathā pūjā niśāyāṃ paripūjayet |  
yathā śrīcakrapūjā vai tathā sarvaṃ samācaret ||  
  
biṃducakra trikoṇe tu mahāpātraṃ tu sthāpayet |  
paṃcakālyāṃ tu paṃcāre carukaṃ paṃca vai kramāt ||  
  
nātaḥ parataraṃ bhadre kālikā krama pūjane |  
bhogyaṃ svargaṃ sukhaṃ mokṣaṃmājñāsiddhirbhaveddhruvaṃ ||  
  
satyaṃ satyaṃ mahādevī satyameta vravīmyahaṃ |  
anyathā kurute yastu hetavāda kutarkataḥ ||  
  
p. 155b)  
  
pariśramaṃ kevalaṃ tu na sa siddhimavāpnuyāt |  
ityatat te samākhyātaṃ kālikāyā kulakramaṃ ||  
  
vidhānaṃ paramaṃ divyaṃ śāstraikāli kramāgataiḥ |  
gopanīyaṃ prayatnena na dadyād yasya kasyacit ||  
  
guru bhakti rato yo hi mahāśāstramayī tu sā |  
ramyapuṣpaphalaṃ dṛṣṭvā vastrālaṃkārameva ca ||  
  
svātma priyā nibhavyāni yat kiṃcid bhuvi durlabhaṃ |  
guravai prathamaṃ datvā tataḥ svātmani dhārayet ||  
  
gurvāgamakramārīśā pūjakāya pradāpayet |  
guru saṃtuṣṭamāne tu saṃtuṣṭā kālikā kramaṃ ||  
  
yenedaṃ likhyate śāstraṃ yasya hasteṣu tiṣṭhate |  
yatra sthitaṃ prapūjyaṃte vidhivat parameśvarīṃ ||  
  
sanirvighnaṃ tu ṣaṇmāsaṃ yāvajjivati caiva hi |  
pustakaṃ pūjitaṃ yena idaṃ kāli kulakramaṃ ||  
  
samagraṃ pūjitaṃ yena kālikākālanāśinī |  
ābrahmastaṃbha sakalaṃ kālena kalayet sadā ||  
  
taṃ kālaṃ kālikā devī kalayet sāyuge yuge |  
na kālī sadṛśī yajño na kālī sadṛśī tapaḥ ||  
  
na kāli sadṛśī dharmo na kālī sadṛśī bhuvi |  
jīvanmuktaḥ sa vijñeyo mahāpāśupataḥ sa vai ||  
  
mahāyogī vijānī hi kālikā pathasaṃśritāḥ |  
ahaṃ mṛtyuṃjayo devo maṃgalārcanato bhavet ||  
  
p. 156a)  
  
kalau viśeṣato kālī pūjitavyā prayatnataḥ |  
devatā saṃyutaṃ vighnaṃ varjitasthānakaṃ priye ||  
  
yo'jñātā bhairavo devo śrotārudra samo bhavet |  
sa eva kadhā ca bahudhā sākānāṃ hitāya ca ||  
  
nānātaṃtra pravāhāstu nānāmnāyatvamāgatāḥ |  
taṃtra bhede nāma bhedā ekāśakti sahasradhā ||  
  
maṃgalā ca mahāmāyā caṃḍakāpālinī śivā |  
cāmuṃḍā carcikā caṃḍā sṛṣṭi sthityaṃta kāliṇī ||  
  
anākhyā ca mahābhāvā guhyakālī jayā parā |  
siddhilakṣmī viśvalakṣmī mahāpratyaṃgirā smṛtā ||  
  
suṃdarī tripurā cāru ugracaṃḍā prakāśinī |  
vibhimnā vahudhā jātā nānābhedasamāśritā ||  
  
ekāsā vahu rūpā ca jānīyād divya cakṣuṣā |  
sa eva sādhakā śreṣṭhaḥ siddhijñānasya bhājanaṃ ||  
  
anusthānaratā sarvaṃ siddhibhāgī bhaveddhruvaṃ |  
  
iti śrīvārāhī taṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade paṃcaviṃśati paṭalaḥ || 25 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
kuryāt tadāsanaṃ tasmādārogyaṃ cāṃgalāghavaṃ |  
vaśiṣṭhādyaiśca munibhirmatsyaiṃdrādyaiśca yogibhiḥ ||  
  
aṃgīkṛtānyāsanāni kathyaṃte kāni citsadā |  
jānurcoraṃtare samyak kṛtvā pādatale ubhe ||  
  
ṛtukāyaḥ samāsīnaḥ svastikaṃ tan pracakṣate |  
  
p. 156b)  
  
savye dakṣiṇagulphaṃ tu pṛṣṭāpārśve niyojayet |  
dakṣiṇe'tathā savyaṃ gomukhaṃ gomukhaṃ tathā ||  
  
ekaṃ pādaṃ tathaikasminvinyasyoruṇi saṃsthitaṃ |  
itaraśmiṃ tathā caikaṃ vīrāsanamitiritaṃ ||  
  
gudaṃ niṣpīḍā gulphābhyāṃ vyuktameṇa samāhitaḥ |  
kūrmāsanaṃ bhavedetaditi yogavidovidaḥ ||  
  
padmāsanaṃstu saṃsthāpya jānurvoraṃtare karaiḥ |  
vinyasya bhūmau saṃsthāpya vyomasthaḥ kukkuṭāsanaṃ ||  
  
kukkuṭāsanamadhyasthoddaurbhyāsaṃ vaṃdhyakaṃ dharā |  
sate kūrma vaduttāna etadutāna kūrmakaṃ ||  
  
pādāṃguṣṭhau tu vāhubhyāṃ gṛhītvā śrīvaṇāvadhi |  
dhanurākarṣaṇaṃ kuryāddhanurāsanamucyate ||  
  
vāmorumūlārpita dakṣapādaṃ jānorvahi veṣṭhita vamapādaṃ |  
pragṛhya tiṣṭhet parivetti tāgraḥ śrīmatsyanāthodita māsanaṃ syāt ||  
  
matsyeṃdra pīṭha jvalana pradīptaṃ pracaṃḍarugmaṃ na * khaṇḍanāstraṃ |  
abhyāsataḥ kuṃḍalinī prabodhaṃ daṃḍasthiratvaṃ vadadāti puṃsāṃ ||  
  
uttānaśavavadbhūmau śamanaṃ ca savāsanaṃ |  
savāsanaṃ śāṃti haraṃ citta viśāṃti kārakaṃ ||  
  
caturāśīti bhyāsanāni śivena kathitāni tu |  
  
p. 157a)  
  
tebhyaścatuṣkamādāya sārabhūtavravīmyahaṃ |  
siddhaṃ padmaṃ tathā siṃhaṃ bhadraṃ ceti catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
śreṣṭha tatra dvayaṃ tiṣṭhet padmasiṃhāsane sadā |  
  
yoni syātakamaṃghrimūlaghaṃṭitaṃ kṛtvā dṛḍhaṃ vinyase meḍhe   
pādamathaikameva niyataṃ kṛtvā samaṃ vigrahaṃ ||   
sthānu saṃpratiteṃdriyau caladṛśā paśyannuvoraṃ * caitanmokṣa *   
kapāṭabhedajanakaṃ siddhāsanaṃ procyate ||  
  
meḍhrāduparinikṣipya savyagulpha tathopari |  
gulphāṃtara ca niḥkṣipya siddhāsanamidaṃ bhavet ||  
  
etat siddhāsanaṃ prāhuranye vajrāsanaṃ viduḥ |  
suktāsanaṃ vadaṃtyeke prāhurguptāsanaṃ pare ||  
  
yameṣvivamitāhāraḥ ahiṃsā niyameṣviva |  
mukhyaṃ sarvāsaneṣvekaṃ siddhāsiddhāsanaṃ viduḥ ||  
  
caturāśīti pīṭheṣu siddhameva sadābhyaset |  
dvisaptati sahasraiṣu nāḍīnāṃ mala śodhane ||  
  
ātmadhyāyī mi * hārī yāvadvādaśavatsaraṃ |  
sadā siddhāsanābhyāsād yoginī prāptimāpnuyāt ||  
  
kimādyairbahubhiḥ pīṭhaiḥ sadāsiddhāsane sati |  
prāṇānitye sāvadhāne varddha kevalakuṃbhake ||  
  
urudyaṃte vinibhyāsā svayamevotmanī yathā |  
tathaikasminneva dṛḍhe vaddhe siddhāsane sadā ||  
  
baṃdhatrayasanāyāsāt svayamevopajāyate |  
na cāsanaṃ siddhasanaṃ na kuṃbhasadṛśo nila ||  
  
p. 157b)  
  
na khecarī samāmudrā na nāda sadṛśo layaṃḥ |  
  
vāmorūparidakṣiṇaṃ ca varaṇaṃ saṃsthāpya cāmaṃ tathā jānu   
bhūparipaścimena vidhinā dhṛtvā karābhyāṃ dṛḍhaṃ || aṃguṣṭhau hṛdaye   
nidhāya cibukaṃ nāsāgramālāṃkaye tadvyādhivināśanāya yamināṃ   
padmāsanaṃ procyate ||   
  
uttānau caraṇau kṛtvā urū saṃdhau prayatnataḥ |  
urū madhye tathottānau pāṇau kṛtvā tato dṛśau ||  
  
nāsāgre vinyased dṛṣṭī daṃtamūlaṃ ca jihvayā |  
uddhṛtya cibukaṃ vakṣye sthāpayet pacanaiśanaiḥ ||  
  
idaṃ padmāsanaṃ proktaṃ sarvavyādhi vināśanaṃ |  
durlabhaṃ yena kenāpi dhīmatā labhyate bhuvi ||  
  
kṛtvā saṃpuṭitau karau dṛḍhataraṃ badhvā tu padmāsanaṃ gāḍhaṃ vakṣasi   
sannidhāya cibukaṃ dhyānaccataccetasi ||  
vā svā * rasapārdamūrddhamanilaṃ prollāsa yat pūritaṃ muṃcan   
prāṇamupaiti bodhamatulaṃ śaktiṃ prabodho dayāt ||  
  
padmāsane sthito yogī nāḍī dvāreṇa pūrayet |  
mārutaṃ yastu pibati samukto nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
gulpho ca vṛṣaṇasyādhaḥ sīvanyāḥ pārśvayoḥ kṣipet |  
dakṣiṇe savya gulphaṃ tu dakṣagulphaṃ tu savyake ||  
  
hastau bhujānunoḥ sthāpya svāṃgulīḥ saṃprasārya ca |  
vyāttavaktrau nirīkṣeta māsāgre nyasta locanaḥ ||  
  
p. 158a)  
  
siṃhāsanaṃ bhavedetat pūjitaṃ yogibhiḥ sadā |  
baṃdha tritayasaṃdhānaṃ kurute cāsanottamaṃ ||  
  
gulpho ca vṛṣaṇa syādhaḥ sīvanyāḥ pārśvayoḥ kṣipet |  
pārśvapādau ca pāṇibhyāṃ dṛḍhaṃ badhvā suniścalaṃ ||  
  
bhadrāsanaṃ bhavedetatat sarvaṃ vyādhi nāśanaṃ |  
gorakṣāsanamityāhuridaṃ vai siddha yoginaḥ ||  
  
evamānavaṃdhaṇeṣu yogiṃdro vigataṃ śramaḥ |  
athābhyasennāḍi śuddhaṃ mudrādi pavana kriyāṃ ||  
  
kriyāyuktasya siddhiḥ syādakriyasya kathaṃ bhavet |  
na śāstra pāṭhamātreṇa yogasiddhi prajāyate ||  
  
na veṣadhāraṇaṃ siddhe kāraṇaṃ na ca tatkathā |  
kriyaiva kāraṇaṃ siddhaḥ satyameva na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
siṣṇodararatā ye he na deyo veṣadhāriṇaḥ |  
mayi bodhī budho svasthe tuchoyaṃ viśvabudbudaḥ ||  
  
malīna udito vetti vikalpāvasaraḥ kutaḥ |  
āsanaṃ kuṃbhakaścitraṃ mudrādi karaṇāni ca ||  
  
athādānānu saṃdhena syādabhyāsān kramo haṭhe |  
brahmacārī mitāhārī tyāgī yogaparāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
abdādūrddhaṃ bhavet siddhinnātra kāryāvicāraṇāt |  
susnigdhā madhurāhāra caturthāṃśavivarjitaḥ ||  
  
bhujāvimāṃsadadhitakra kulatthakolapi |  
nadyākahiṃgulaśunādyamapaśyamāhuḥ ||  
  
bhojanamahitaṃ vidyāt punaraghulīkṛtaṃ |  
rukṣaṃ atilavaṇaṃ tilapiṃḍakadaśanam ||  
  
p. 158b)  
  
varjayeddhurjana prīti vahnistrī paṭhasevanaṃ |  
prātasnānopavāsādi kāyakleśādikaṃ tathā ||  
  
godhūmaśāli javaṣaṣṭhikaśobhanāntaṃ kṣīrājya khaṇḍa navanītasitāmadhūni ||  
sūḍhīpaṭolaphalakādi ca śākamuktaṃ muṃgādi divyamudakaṃ ca   
yamīndrapaṃthāṃ ||  
  
iṣṭaṃ sa madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ gavyaṃ dhātu prapoṣaṇaṃ |  
manobhilaṣitaṃ yogyaṃ yogībhojanamācaret ||  
  
yuvāvṛddho'ti * ddho vā vyādhito durvalastathā |  
abhyāsāt siddhimāpnoti sarvayogeṣṭa taṃdritaḥ ||  
  
pīṭhāti kuṃbhakaścitraṃ mudrādi karaṇāni ca |  
sarvasya viha *? bhyāse rājayogaphalāvadhi ||  
  
athāsane dṛḍhe yogī vaśīti hamitāsanaḥ |  
gurūpadiṣṭamārgena yogamārga samabhyaset ||  
  
calavātejalaṃvittaṃ niśca niścalate tathā |  
yogīsthāṇutva māpnoti tato vāyuṃ niruṃdhayet ||  
  
yāvadvātāsthito dehe tāvajjīvanamucyate |  
marana tasya niḥkrāṃti tasmād vāyu na ruṃdhayet ||  
  
malākulāsu nāḍīṣu mārutī naiva madhyagaḥ |  
kathaṃ syādutmanī bhāvaḥ kāryasiddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavet ||  
  
śuddhimeti yathā sarvaṃ nāḍī cakraṃ malākulaṃ |  
tadaiva jāte yogī prāṇasaṃgrahaṇe kṣamaḥ ||  
  
prāṇābhyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryānnityaṃ sātvikayādhiyā |  
  
p. 159a)  
  
yathā sukhemavasthāyamalāḥ śauṣaṃ prayāṃti ca |  
vaddhapadmāsane yogī prāṇaṃ caṃdreṇa pūrayet ||  
  
dhārayitvā yathā śaktyā bhūyaḥ sūryeṇa recayet |  
prāṇaṃ sūryeṇa cākṛṣya pūrayedudaraṃ śanaiḥ ||  
  
vidhivat kuṃbhakaṃ kṛtvā punaḥ caṃdreṇa recayet |  
yena tyejettenā pūryadhārayedavirodhataḥ ||  
  
recayecca tato'nyenaśanaireva na vegataḥ |  
  
prāṇaṃ trayāpitenniyamitaṃ bhūyo'nyayāracayet pītvā piṃgalayā samīraṇamatho   
vadhvā tyajed vāmayā ||  
sūryāccaṃdramasoranena vidhinā viṃvadvayaṃ dhyāyatāṃ śuddhānāḍi gaṇā   
bhavaṃti yamināṃ māsatrayādūrddhataḥ ||  
  
prātarmadhye dine śāya madhyarātre ca kuṃbhakān |  
śanairaśīti paryaṃtaṃ caturvāraṃ samabhyaset ||  
  
adhamaṃ jāyate svedaḥ kaṃpo bhavati madhyame |  
uttiṣṭha cottame prāṇā vaddhe padmāsane muhuḥ ||  
  
jalena śramajātena gātramardana mācaret |  
dṛḍhatā laghutā vāpi tena gātrasya jāyate ||  
  
abhyākāle prathameśasmakṣīrājya bhojanaṃ |  
tatobhyāse sthirī bhūtena tādṛg niyamagrahaḥ ||  
  
yathā siṃho gajo vyāghro bhaved vaśya śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |  
tathaiva sevito vāyuranyathāhaṃti sādhanaṃ ||  
  
prāṇāyāmena yuktena sarvarogakṣayo bhavet |  
ayuktābhyāṃsayogena sarvarogasamudbhavaḥ ||  
  
hikkākāśastathā śvāsa śiraḥ karṇākṣi vedanā |  
  
p. 159b)  
  
bhavaṃti vividhā doṣāḥ pavanasya vyati kramāt |  
yuktaṃ yukta tyajed vāyuḥ yuktaṃ yukta ca sevayet ||  
  
yuktaṃ yukta ca vadhnīyādevaṃ siddhimavāpnuyāt |  
yadā nāḍi viśuddhiḥ syāt tadā cihnāni vāhyataḥ ||  
  
kāyasya kriyate kāṃtistathā jāyeta niścitaṃ |  
yathāṣṭaṃ dhāraṇaṃ vāyorānalasya pradīpanaṃ ||  
  
nādābhivyaktirārogyaṃ jāyate nāḍi śodhane |  
medaḥ śleṣmādi nāśārthaṃ ṣaṭkarmādi samācaret ||  
  
anyathā nācaret jñāni doṣāṇāṃ samabhāvataḥ |  
dhotīvartiśca netiśca trāṭakaṃ naulikaṃ tathā ||  
  
kapālabhāthī caitāni ṣaṭkarmāṇi pracakṣyate |  
karmaṣaṭkamidaṃ gopyaṃ ghaṭaśodhanakārakaṃ ||  
  
vicitraguṇasaṃdhāyī pūjyate yogapuṃgavaiḥ |  
caturaṃgulavistāraṃ hastapaṃcadaśena tu ||  
  
gurūpadiṣṭamārgeṇa siktaṃ vastraṃśanaigraset |  
tataḥ pratyāhare caiva duditau dhauti karma tat ||  
  
śvāsaḥ kāśaḥ plīha kuṣṭāṃ kapharogāśca viṃśati |  
dhautī karma prabhāvena śuddhyaṃte ca na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
nābhi daghnena lepāyunyasanālotkaṭāsanaḥ |  
ādhārāt kuṃcanaṃ kuryāt kṣālanaṃ vasti karma tat ||  
  
gulpaplihodalaṃ vāpi vātapittakaphodbhavaṃ |  
vastikarma prabhāvena kṣīyaṃte sakalā malā ||  
  
p. 160a)  
  
dhonviṃdriyāṃtakaraṇaprasādaṃ dadhāsvakāṃtiṃ dahanapradīptiṃ |  
aśeṣadoṣopacayaṃti hanyādatyasya mānaṃ jalapasti karma ||  
  
mutraṃ vitasti susnigdhanāsānāsapraveśayet |  
mukha nirgamanā deva neti siddhairnipādyate ||  
  
kapālaśodhinī kāryā divya dṛṣṭi pradāyinī |  
yattūrddha jātarogodyānetirāśunihaṃti ca ||  
  
nirīkṣyaniścalā dṛṣṭyā sūkṣmalakṣaṃ samāhitaḥ |  
aśrusampataparyaṃtamācāryaistāṭakaṃstataṃ ||  
  
sphoṭanaṃ netrarogī ca taṃdrānāṃ tu kapāṭakaṃ |  
prayatnāttrāṭakaṃ gopyaṃ yathā hāṭakapetakaṃ ||  
  
amaṃdāvartavegena tuṃdasavyāpasavyataḥ |  
ataśo bhrāmayedeṣā naulī gaulaiḥ praśasyate ||  
  
maṃdāgnisaṃdīpanapācakādi saṃdhāpakānaṃdakarī sadaiva |  
aśeṣadoṣāmalaśoṣaṇīva haṭakriyāso jayatīhanaulī ||  
  
lohakālasya bhastrīvat kuryāt savyāpasavyataḥ |  
kapālabhāṣyaṃ vikhyāta kaphadoṣaviśodhinī ||  
  
ṣaṭkarmabhirgatasthaulyaṃ kaphamedo valādhika |  
prāṇāyāma tataḥ kuryādanāyāsena siddhyati ||  
  
prāṇāyāmai sukhāt sarve praśuddhyaṃti malāśayāḥ |  
ācāryānāṃ tu keṣāṃcidanyat karma na sanmataṃ ||  
  
ṣaṭkarma yogamāpnoti pacanābhyāsa tatparaḥ |  
brahmādayo'pi vidaśāḥ prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇā ||  
  
p. 160b)  
  
tena siddhiṃ gatāste ca tasmāt pavanamabhyaset |  
sumanākāṃtakābhavya tasmāt pavanamabhyaset ||  
  
yāvad vaddhaumarud dehe yāvaccittaṃ nirāmayaṃ |  
yāvat paśyadbhuvaurmadhyaṃ tāvat kālaṃ bhaye kutaḥ ||  
  
vidhivatprāṇasaṃyāme nāḍīcakre viśodhite |  
suṣumnā vadanaṃ bhitvā sukhadvigatimārutaḥ ||  
  
mārutamadhyasaṃcāre manasthairya prajāyate |  
yo manaḥ susthiro bhāva saivāvasthā manonmanī ||  
  
tatsiddhaye vidhānajño citrāt kurvaṃti kuṃbhakā |  
vicitrakuṃbhakāsādvicitrāṃ siddhimavāpnuyāt ||  
  
sūryabhedanamukhyāyī tathāśītkā * *? talī |  
bhastīkā bhramarīmūrchā kevalaścāṣṭakuṃbhakāḥ ||  
  
pūrakāṃte tu kartavyo vaṃdhojālaṃ dharābhidhaḥ |  
kuṃbhakāṃte recakādau kartavyastuḍḍiyānakaḥ ||  
  
adhastā kuṃcane bhāśukaṃṭhasaṃkocane kṛte |  
madhyapaścimatānena syāt prāṇo madhyanāḍigaḥ ||  
  
apānamūrddhamutthāpya prāṇaṃ kaṃṭhādadho nayet |  
yogī jarāvimuktaśca ṣoḍaśābda vayo bhavet ||  
  
athāsane sukhādeva vadhvāvajrāsanaṃ tataḥ |  
dakṣaṇāḍyāsamākṛkhya vahisthāpavanaṃ śanaiḥ ||  
  
ākeśāgrānnakhāgraṃ ca śiropyavadhikuṃbhayet |  
kṛtvā vaivāmanāḍyā ca cālayet pavanaṃ śanaiḥ ||  
  
p. 161a)  
  
kapālaśodhanaṃ vāta doṣaghnaṃ kṛmināśanaṃ |  
punaḥ punaridaṃ sūrya bhedanaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
mukhaṃ sa yasya nāsābhyāṃ ākṛṣya pavanaṃ śanaiḥ |  
yadā ca gati kaṃṭhāṃtaṃ hṛtpadmavadhiśodhanaṃ ||  
  
pūrvavat kuṃbhayet prāṇāddrecayeditayā tataḥ |  
śleṣmādauṣaharaṃ deha valadīptivivarddhanaṃ ||  
  
kuṃbhaṃ kuryāt sadā vaktrād ghrāṇe caiva vijṛṃbhitaṃ |  
evamabhyāsayogena kāmadevo dvitīyakaṃ ||  
  
yogī cakraṃ samāsādya sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ |  
na kṣudhā na tṛṣā nidrā naivālasyaṃ tu jāyate ||  
  
bhaveśvachaṃda dehaśca sarvopadrava varjitaḥ |  
anena vidhinā satyaṃ yogīṃdro bhuvi maṃḍale ||  
  
rasanā tālu mūlena yaḥ prāṇaṃ satataṃ pibet |  
sa bhavet sarvasiddhīnāṃ bhājanaṃ nātrasaṃśayaḥ ||  
  
rasanā tālu mūlena yaḥ prāṇaṃ satataṃ pibet |  
abdārddhena bhavet tasya sarvagāṃ susthiraḥ kriyāṃ ||  
  
jihvāyā vāyumākṛṣya pūrvavat kuṃbhasādhanaṃ |  
prāṇaistu praṇaraṃdhrābhyāṃ recayedanilaṃ śanaiḥ ||  
  
gulma śleṣmādayo doṣāḥ jvarapittakṣudhā tṛṣā |  
etāni śītalī nāmaḥ kuṃbhako'yaṃ nihaṃti ca ||  
  
urvorupārasaṃsthāpya ubhe pādatale tathā |  
padmāsanaṃ bhavet samyak sarvapāpapraṇāśanaṃ ||  
  
samyak padmāsane vadhvā samagīvodaraḥ sudhī |  
  
p. 161b)  
  
mukhaṃ saṃyasya yatnena prāṇaṃ ghrāṇenda recayet |  
athaiva svaśarīrasthaṃ cārayet pavanaṃ sthalī ||  
  
sukhasaṃmyak prayatnena prāṇaṃ ghrāṇena recayet |  
yadā galati hṛtkaṃṭhe kapālapavanaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
vegena pūrayet kecid hṛtpadmāvadhimārutaṃ |  
puna virecayet tadvat purayecca punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
yathaiva lohakārāṇāṃ bhastrī vegena cārayet |  
tathaiva svaśarīrasthaṃ cālayet pavanaṃ śanaiḥ ||  
  
yadāśramo bhaven dehe tadā sūryeṇa recayet |  
athodaraṃ bhavet pūrṇaṃ recanaira tathā laghu ||  
  
dhārayennāsikā madhye aṃgulībhyāṃ tathā dṛḍhaṃ |  
kuṃbhakaṃ pūrvavat kṛtvā recayedvitrayā nila ||  
  
vātapitta śleṣma haraṃ śarīrāṇi vivarddhanaṃ |  
kuṃḍalī bodhakaḥ kuṃbho rogaghnaḥ sukhadaḥ śubhaḥ ||  
  
brahmanāḍī mukhe saṃsthaḥ kapālārgala nāśanaḥ |  
samyagsastrāsamudbhūto graṃthi traya vibhedakaḥ ||  
  
vegāddoṣaṃ pūrakaṃ bhṛṃganādaṃ bhṛṃgī nādaṃ recakaṃ maṃda   
maṃdaṃ |  
yogīṃdrāṇāmevamabhyāsayogācittai pātākā cidānandamūrchā ||  
  
pūrakāṃte vahutaraṃ vadhvā jālaṃdharai śanaiḥ |  
recayen mūrchanāsthoyaṃ manomūrchāsukhapradaḥ ||  
  
aṃtaḥ pravartitā dhāra mārutā pūritodaraḥ |  
sākṣāt payasya gādho'pi plavato brahmapatravat ||  
  
prāṇāyāmastridhā prokto recapūraka kuṃbhakaiḥ |  
  
p. 162a)  
  
sahitaḥ kevalaśceti kuṃbhako dvividho mataḥ |  
recakaḥ pūraka kārya sa vai sahita kuṃbhakaḥ ||  
  
yāvat kevala siddhi syāt tāvat sahitamaṃnyaset |  
recakaṃ pūrakaṃ muktvā mukhādvāyu nirodhanāt ||  
  
prāṇāyāmo'yamityuktaḥ sa vai kevala kuṃbhakaḥ |  
kevalakuṃbhake siddhe recaṃ pūraka varjitaṃ ||  
  
na tasya durlabhaṃ kiṃcit triṣu kāleṣu vidyate |  
śuddha kevala kuṃbhena yatheṣṭaṃ vāyu dhāraṇaṃ ||  
  
rājayoga padaṃ caiva labhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
haṭhaṃ vinā rājayogo rājayogaṃ vinā haṭha ||  
  
na siddhyati tato yugmanāniṣpatteḥ samabhyaset |  
kuṃbhakaḥ prāṇarecāṃte kuryātrittaṃ nirāmayaṃ ||  
  
evamabhyāsayogena rājayoga padaṃ vrajet |  
kuṃbhakāt kuṇḍalī bodhaḥ kuṃḍalo bodhato bhavet ||  
  
anurgatā suṣumnā ca haṭhasiddhiśca jāyate |  
vapuḥ kṛśatvaṃ vadane prasanna nādasphuṭatvaṃ nayane ca nirmale ||  
  
ārogyatāṃ bindu jayogni dīpanaṃ nāḍīṣu siddhirhaṭhasiddhilakṣaṇaṃ |  
  
sa śailavanadhātrīnāṃ yathādhāro hi kuṃḍalī |  
suptāguru prasādena yathā yāgarti kuṃḍalī ||  
  
tayā padmāni sarvāṇi bhidyaṃte graṃthayopi ca |  
prāṇasya śūnya padavī tadā rājapathāyate ||  
  
tathā citta nirālaṃbaṃ tathā kālasya vaṃdhanaṃ |  
  
p. 162b)  
  
suṣumnā śūnya padavī brahmaraṃdhraṃ mahāpathaḥ |  
śmaśānaṃ śāṃbhavī madhya mārgaścetyekakavācakā ||  
  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena prabodhayatumīśvarī |  
brahmadvāramukhasuptaṃ mudrābhyāsaṃ samācaret ||  
  
mahāmudrāmahāvaṃdho mahāvedhaṃśca khecarī |  
uḍḍiyānaṃ mūlabaṃdhaḥ tatojālaṃdharābhidhaḥ ||  
  
karaṇī viparītākhyā vajrolī śakti cālanaṃ |  
idaṃ ca mudrā daśakaṃ dharāmaraṇanāśanaṃ ||  
  
ādināthoditaṃ sarvaṃ aṣṭauśvarya pradāyakaṃ |  
vallabhaṃ sarvasiddhānāṃ vallabhaṃ manujāmapi ||  
  
gopanīyaṃ prayatnena yathāratna karaṃḍakaṃ |  
kasyacinnaiva vaktavyaṃ kulastrīsurataṃ yathā ||  
  
vajrolī ramarobhiśca sahajālistridhā matā |  
eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣya kartavyaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
pādamūlana vāmena yoni saṃpīḍyadakṣiṇaṃ |  
pādaṃ prasāritaṃ dhṛtvā karābhyāṃ dhāritatsukhaṃ ||  
  
kaṃṭhe vaṃdhaṃsamāropya dhārayedvāyumūrddhataḥ |  
yathādaṃḍāhataḥ sarpo daṃḍākāraḥ prajāyate ||  
  
ṛjvā bhūtā tathāśaktiḥ kuṇḍalī sahasā bhavet |  
tadasti mananāvasthā jāyate dvipuṭāśritā ||  
  
tataḥ śanaiśanaireva recayen na tu vegataḥ |  
iyaṃ khalu mahāmudrā mahāsiddhaiḥ praśasyate ||  
  
mahākleśādayo doṣā jāyaṃte maraṇādayaḥ |  
  
p. 163a)  
  
mahāmudrā ca te naiva vadaṃti vivudhottamā |  
caṃdrāsai ca samabhyasya sūryāśe punarabhyaset ||  
  
yāvat saṃkhyā bhavartulyā tato mudrāṃ visarjayet |  
nāpathyaṃ na hi pathyaṃ ca rasā sarve'pirīrasā ||  
  
api muktaṃ viṣaṃ ghoraṃ pīyūṣamiva jīryati |  
kṣayaṃ kuṣṭaṃ mudāvattaṃ tulyājīrṇa purogamāḥ ||  
  
doṣāḥ sarvakṣayaṃ yāṃti mahāmudrāṃ tu yo'bhyaset |  
kathiteyaṃ mahāmudrā mahāsiddhikarī nṛṇāṃ ||  
  
gaṃbhyanīyā prayatnena na deyā yasya kasyacit |  
rṣṇi bhāgena pādasya yoni sthānaṃ niyojayet ||  
  
vāmorūparisaṃsthāpya dakṣiṇaṃ caraṇaṃ tathā |  
pūrayitvā tato vāyuṃ hṛdayaṃ cibukaṃ dṛḍhaṃ ||  
  
nikṣipya yonimākuṃcya mano madhye niyojayet |  
dhārayitvā yathāśaktyā recayedanilaṃśanaiḥ ||  
  
saṃvyāgavasamabhyāsya dakṣiṇe naramabhyaset |  
matametaṃ tu keṣāṃcit kaṃṭhavaṃdhaṃ vivarjayet ||  
  
śatadaṃtasya jihvāyāṃ vaṃdhaḥ śastro bhavedvitaḥ |  
ayaṃ kila mahāvaṃdhaḥ mahāsiddhi pradāyakaḥ ||  
  
mahāmudrā ca te naiva vadaṃti vivudhottamā |  
caṃdrāsai ca samabhyasya sūryāśe punarabhyaset ||  
  
yāvat saṃkhyā bhavartulyā tato mudrāṃ visarjayet |  
nāpathyaṃ na hi pathyaṃ ca rasā sarve'pirīrasā ||  
  
p. 163b)  
  
api muktaṃ viṣaṃ ghoraṃ pīyūṣamiva jīryati |  
kṣayaṃ kuṣṭaṃ mudāvartaṃ tulyājīrṇapurogamāḥ ||  
  
doṣāḥ sarvakṣayaṃ yāṃti mahāmudrāṃ tu yo'nyaset |  
kathite yaṃ mahāmudrā mahāsiddhikarī nṛṇāṃ ||  
  
gaṃbhyanīyā prayatnena na deyā yasya kasyacit |  
pārṣṇi bhāgena pādasya yoni sthānaṃ niyojayet ||  
  
vāmorūparisaṃsthāpya dakṣiṇaṃ caraṇaṃ tathā |  
pūrayitvā tato vāyuṃ hṛdayaṃ cibukaṃ dṛḍhaṃ ||  
  
nikṣipya yonimākuṃcya mano madhye niyojayet |  
dhārayitvā yathāśaktyā recayedanilaṃśanaiḥ ||  
  
saṃvyāgavasamabhyāsya dakṣiṇe naramabhyaset |  
matametastu keṣāṃcit kaṃṭhaṃ vaṃdhaṃ vivarjayet ||  
  
śatadaṃ tasya jihvāyāṃ baṃdhaḥ śasto bhavedvitaḥ |  
ayaṃ kila mahāvaṃdhaḥ mahāsiddhi pradāyakaḥ ||  
  
kālapāśamahāvaṃdha vimocana vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
ayaṃ ca sarvanāḍīnāmūrddhnaṃ gati vibodhakaḥ ||  
  
triveṇī saṃgamaṃ dharte kedāraṃ pāpayet manaḥ |  
rūpalāvaṇya saṃpanna yathāstrī puruṣaṃ vinā ||  
  
mahāmudrā mahāvaṃdhau niḥphalau vedha varjitau |  
mahāvedhā sthito yogī kṛtvā pūrakamekadhīḥ ||  
  
vāyī nāmati māvṛttya nibhṛtaṃ kaṃṭhamudrayā |  
samahastā yugo bhūyo sphicau saṃtāḍayechanaiḥ ||  
  
puṭa dvayaṃ samākṛṣya vāyuḥ sphurati satvaraṃ |  
  
p. 164a)  
  
somasūryāgnisaṃbaṃdhā jāyate ca mṛtorjayaḥ |  
mṛtāvasthā samutpannā tato vāyuṃ virecayet ||  
  
mahāvedho yamabhyāsān mahāsiddhi pradāyakaḥ |  
valīpalitavaṃdhaghnaḥ sevyate sādhakottamaiḥ ||  
  
etat trayaṃ mahāmudrā jarāmṛtyuvināśinī |  
vahnivṛddhi karā caiva manimādi guṇapradaṃ ||  
  
aṣṭadhā kriyate caikaṃ yāmayāme dine dine |  
sarvasaṃcārasaṃdhāyī pāpaughābhiduraṃ sadā ||  
  
samyajijñāsatāmevaṃ svalpaṃ prathamasādhanaṃ |  
vahnistrī paṭhisevā nāmādau varjanamācaret ||  
  
chedanacālanadohaiḥ kalā krameṇa coddhayet |  
sāyāvadbhūmadhyaṃ ceti tadā khecara mudrayā ||  
  
kapālakuhare jihvā praviṣṭo viparītagā |  
bhrūvoraṃtargatā dṛṣṭirmudrā bhavati khecarī ||  
  
kalāṃ parāṃ mukhī * bhyakṣaṇārddhemapi tiṣṭhati |  
kṣaṇena mucyate yogī vyādhimṛtyujalādibhiḥ ||  
  
na rogo maraṇaṃ tasya na nidrā na kṣudhā tṛṣā |  
na ca mūrchā bhavet tasya yo mudrāṃ veṣṭi khecarī ||  
  
vādhyate na sa rogena lipyate na sa karmaṇā |  
bādhyate na sa kālena yo mudrāṃ vetti khecarī ||  
  
vittaṃ carati khe yasmājjihvā carati khegatā |  
te naiva khecarī mudrā sarvasiddhirnamaskṛtāḥ ||  
  
khecaryā mudritaṃ yena vivaralaṃbikorddhataḥ |  
tasya na kṣarate viṃduḥ kāminyā liṃga tasya ca ||  
  
p. 164b)  
  
caritopi yadā biṃduḥ saṃprāptaścāgni maṃḍalaṃ |  
brahmatyurddhaṃ haṭhāchaktyā nirodho yogamudrayā ||  
  
ūrddhajihvā sthito bhūtvā somapānaṃ karoti yaḥ |  
māsārddhena na saṃdeho mṛtyuṃjayati yogavat ||  
  
nitya somakalāpūrṇaṃ śarīraṃ yasya dehinaḥ |  
takṣakenāpi daṃṣṭasya viṣaṃ tasya na sarpati ||  
  
gomāṃsaṃ bhakṣayen nityaṃ pibedamaravāruṇīṃ |  
kulīnaṃ tamahaṃ vidyā itare kulaghātakāḥ ||  
  
gośabde noditā jihvā tatpraveśo hi tāluni |  
gomāṃsaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ tacca mahāpātakanāśanaṃ ||  
  
jihvā praveśanaṃ bhūtaṃ bahunātyāditaṃ khalu |  
caṃdrāt sravati yā samyak sāsyādamaravāruṇi ||  
  
mūrddhaṃ ṣoḍaśa padmapatra galitaṃ prāṇāṃdavāptaṃ haṭhādūrddhāsyo   
rasanāṃ vidhāya vipare śaktiṃ parāṃ ciṃtayet ||  
tatkallolajaḥ lākulaṃ suvimalaṃ dhārāmṛtaṃ yaḥ pibet nirdoṣaḥ samṛṇāla   
komala tanuryogī viraṃjī pati ||  
  
cuyaṃti yadi laṃbikāgramaniśaṃ jihvārasaspaṃdinī sa kṣārākaṭu *?   
dugdha sadṛśī sadhvājya tulyaṃ tathā ||  
vyādhīnāṃ haraṇaṃ jarāṃtakaraṇaṃ śāstrāgamodgīraṇaṃ tasya syādamaratva   
guṣṭhaguṇitaṃ siddhāṃ gaṇākarṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ sṛṣṭimayaṃ bīja ekāmudrā ca khecarī |  
eko devo nirālaṃba ekāvasthā manonmanī ||  
  
p. 165a)  
  
suciraṃ jñānajanakaṃ paṃcasrotaḥ samanvitaḥ |  
tiṣṭhaṃtī khecarī mudrā tasmin śūnyaniraṃjane ||  
  
yaprālepaṃ pihita sukhilaṃ merū mūrddhyā tathaitatasmiṃstatvaṃ pravadati sudhī   
castanmukha nimnagā caṃdrātsārasravati vapuṣastena mṛtyunnarāṇāṃta   
vahnīyādvaruṇamamṛtaṃ nānyathā kārya siddhi ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade ṣaḍviṃśati paṭalaḥ || 26 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
pārṣṇi bhāgena saṃpīḍye yonimākuṃcaya dṛḍhaṃ |  
apānamūrddhamākṛṣya mūlabaṃdhoyamucyate ||  
  
adhogatamakāraṃ vai ūrddhagaṃ kurute varāt |  
ākuṃcya tena taṃ prāhu mūlabaṃdha hi yoginaḥ ||  
  
gurupāṣṇyā tu saṃpīḍye vāyumākuṃcayadvalāt |  
vāraṃ vāraṃ tathā corddha samāyāti samīra ||  
  
prāṇāditodito binduḥ mūlabaṃdhena caikataḥ |  
tato yogasasaṃsiddhyai pramā tatra na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
apānaprāṇayoraikyākṣayo mūtra purīṣayoḥ |  
yuvā bhavati vṛddhau'pi satataṃ mūlabaṃdhanāt ||  
  
apāne corddha māyā te madhyataḥ nābhimaṃḍale |  
tathā nare śikhā dīrghā kriyate vāyunāhatā ||  
  
tato vāyu vahni yogau prāṇāyāma sa ucyate |  
tenātyaṃtaḥ pradīptastu kuto dehakṣayastadā ||  
  
tena kuṃḍalinī suptā saṃtatā saṃprabuddhyate |  
  
p. 165b)  
  
daṃḍāhatābhujaṃgīvaniśvasya ṛjunāyikā |  
vilaṃ pratiṣṭhācca tato brahmaṇāḍyaṃtare vrajet ||  
  
tasmān nityaṃ mūlabaṃdhaḥ kartavyo yogibhiḥ sadā |  
urddha sthitaḥ suṣumnāyāḥ prāṇastuḍḍīyate yataḥ ||  
  
tasmāt tve uḍḍiyānākhyā yogibhiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ |  
uḍaḍīnaṃ kurute yasmādaviśrāṃtaṃ mahākhagaḥ ||  
  
uḍḍiyānaṃ tadeyaṃ syāt kṣatrabaṃdho'bhidhīyate |  
uḍḍiyānaṃ tu sahajaṃ gurunā kathitaṃ sadā ||  
  
abhyase satataṃ yastu vṛddho'pi taruṇo bhavet |  
nābherurddhva madhaścāpitānaṃ kuryācca yaṃ nataḥ ||  
  
yogī samabhyaset mṛtyuṃjayatyevanna saṃśaya |  
ati vajrāsane pādau karābhyāṃ dhāraye dṛḍhaṃ ||  
  
gulphadaṃśasamīpaṃ ca kadaṃ tacca pravīcyate |  
paścimatānaṃmuparikārayeddhṛdaya gala ||  
  
śanaiḥ śanairyathā prāptaṃ tadā gaṃdhiṃ pragachati |  
sarveṣāmeva vaṃdhānāmuttamohuḍḍiyānakaḥ ||  
  
uḍḍiyāne dṛḍhe vaṃdhe muktiḥ svābhavikī bhavet |  
kaṃṭhamākuṃcya hṛdaye sthāpaye dṛḍhamichaya ||  
  
vaṃdhojāraṃ dharākhyoyaṃ jarāmṛtyuvināśakaḥ |  
vadhnāti hi śirājālaṃ adhogāni na bhojanaṃ ||  
  
tato jālaṃdharo baṃdhaḥ kaṃṭhaduḥkhāghanāśanaḥ |  
jālaṃdhare kṛte baṃdhe kaṃṭhasaṃkocalakṣaṇe ||  
  
maṃpīyūṣaṃyatatyagnau na ca vāyuḥ pradhāvati |  
  
p. 166a)  
  
saṃkocalakṣaṇe naiva dve nāḍyā staṃbhayed dṛḍhaṃ |  
madhyaṃ cakramidaṃ jñeyaṃ ṣoḍaśādhārabaṃdhanaṃ ||  
  
baṃdhatrayāmidaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mahāsiddhaiśca sevitaṃ |  
sarveṣāṃ yogataṃtrāṇāṃ sadhenaṃ yoginoṃ biduḥ ||  
  
adhasma kuṃcarenāśukaṃṭhasaṃkocane kṛte |  
madhyamaśvimatānena syāt prāṇāmadhyanāḍigaḥ ||  
  
iḍā ca piṃgalā caiva vāhayet paścimaṃ pathaṃ |  
brahmasthānasthitorodhaḥ prayāti pavanolayam ||  
  
tato na jāyate mṛtyurjarārogādikaṃ tathā |  
urddhvanābhi * raḥ stālururddhabhānuradhaḥ śaśī ||  
  
karaṇī viparītākhyā sarvavyādhivināśinī |  
nityamabhyāsayuktasya jaṭharāgni pravarddhinī ||  
  
āhārovahulastasya sampādyaḥ sādhakasya tu |  
alvāhāro nirāhāraḥ kṣudhālasya vasā bhavet ||  
  
addhāśiraścorddhapādau kṣaṇa syāt prathame dine |  
kṣaṇācca kiṃcidadhikaṃ abhyāse ca dine dine ||  
  
valitaṃ paritaṃ caiva ṣaṇmāsāṃ tu na dṛśyate |  
māsatrayaṃ tu yo nityamabhyase sa tu kālavit ||  
  
svecchāyā vartamāno'pi yogokairniyamarcinā |  
vajrolīya vijānāti sa yogī siddhimān bhavet ||  
  
tatra vastu dvayaṃ vakṣye durlabhaṃ yasya kasyacit |  
kṣīraṃ caiva dvitīyaṃ tu nārī ca vaśa vartinī ||  
  
meḍhrena vasanaiḥ samyak kṛtvā kuṃcanamabhyaset |  
  
p. 166b)  
  
puruṣo vāpi nārī vā vajrolī siddhimāpnuyāt |  
prayatnataḥ śiro jāle phaṭkāraḥ kaṃcukaṃ dhare ||  
  
śanaiḥ śanaiḥ prakurvaṃti vāyusaṃcāra kāraṇāt |  
bhāryā bhage patadviṃdurabhyāsenorddhamāharet ||  
  
valitaṃ valitaṃ viṃdumūrddhamākṛṣyarakṣayet |
