evaṃ rakṣati yo biṃduṃ mṛtyuṃ jayati yogavit ||  
  
maraṇaṃ biṃdupātena jīvitaṃ viṃdudhāraṇāt |  
sugaṃdhiryogino deho jāyate viṃdudhāraṇāt ||  
  
yāvad vindu sthito dehe tāvan mṛtyu bhayaṃ kutaḥ |  
cittāyattaṃ nṛṇāṃ śuklaṃ śukrāyattaṃ hi jīvitaṃ ||  
  
tasmācchukraṃ rajaścaiva rakṣaṇīyaṃ prayatnataḥ |  
biṃdumadhye rajo'pyevaṃ bījaṃ biṃdu ca rakṣayet ||  
  
meḍhremākuṃcayadūrddhaṃ samyagabhyāsa yogavit |  
aprayāsaḥ puṇyavataṃ dhanyānāṃ tatvadarśitaṃ ||  
  
nirma *? tsaraṇā siddhyaṃtana tu matsaraṇālināṃ |  
sahajolī cāmarolī vajrolyā ekabhedataḥ ||  
  
jaleṣu bhasmaniḥkṣipya dagdhamayasamudbhavaṃ |  
vajrolī maithunādūrddhaṃ strīpuṃsāḥ svāṃgalepanaṃ ||  
  
āsīnayoḥ sukhenaiva muktāvyāparayo kṣaṇaṃ |  
sahayolīriyaṃ proktā sādhyeyā yogibhiḥ sadā ||  
  
ayaṃ śubhaṃ karo yogo bhoge bhukte'pi muktidaḥ |  
viharye nityaṃ prathamāvadhārāṃ vihāya niḥsāratamāṃ'tyadhāraṃ ||  
  
p. 167a)  
  
niṣavyate śītalamadhyadhārāṃ kapālikaiḥ kuṇṭhamatairamedhyā |  
amarīyo piben nityaṃ nasyaṃ kuryād dine dine ||  
  
vajrālīmabhyaset satve amarolīti kathyate |  
puṃso viṃduṃ samākuṃce samyagabhyāsa pāṭavān ||  
  
yadi nārī rajo rakṣet saṃyogī cāsi yoginī |  
tasmā kiṃcid rajo nāśaṃ na gachati na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
tasyā śarīre nādastu biṃdunā śabda gachati |  
sa biṃdutadrajaścaiva ekībhūtaḥ svadehajaiḥ ||  
  
vajrolyābhyāsayogena sarvasiddhi prajāyate |  
meḍhrānākuṃcanādūrddhaṃ rajasāpi hi yoginī ||  
  
atīto nāgatavetti khecare ca bhavedruvaṃ |  
dehasiddhiṃ ca labhate vajrolyābhyāsa yogataḥ ||  
  
tasmādayaṃ sādhakānāṃ bhogamuktivimuktida |  
tasmāt puṇyavatāmeva yogoyaṃ saṃprasiddhyati ||  
  
kuṭilāṃgī kuṃḍalinī bhujaṃgī śaktimīśvarī |  
kuṇḍalyāruṃdha devīti śabdāḥ paryāya vācakā ||  
  
uddhāta yat kapāṭaṃ tu yathākuṃcitayā haṭhāt |  
kuṃḍalinyā tathā yogī mokṣadvāraṃ vibhedayet ||  
  
yena mārgeṇa gaṃtavyaṃ brahmasthānaṃ nirāmayaṃ |  
mukhenāchādyataddvāraṃ prasuptā parameśvarī ||  
  
kaṃdorddhakuṇḍalī śaktiraṣṭadhā kuṃtalākṛtiḥ |  
baṃdhanāya ca mūḍhānāṃ sadā mokṣāya yogināṃ ||  
  
aṃbhodi śailadvīpānāṃ ādhāraḥ śeṣa kuṃḍalī |  
  
p. 167b)  
  
aśeṣa yogataṃtrīṇāṃmādhāraḥ kuṇḍalī tathā |  
kuṇḍalī kuṭilānya?rāsarpavatparikīrtitā ||  
  
sā śaktiścālitā yena samukto nātrasaṃśayaḥ |  
gaṃgāyamunayormadhye vālaraṃḍātapasvinī ||  
  
jvālātkāreṇa gṛhnāyātadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃṣpadaṃ |  
iḍābhṛṃgavatī gaṃgā piṃgalā yamunā nadī ||  
  
iḍāpiṃgalayormadhye vālaraṃḍā sarasvatī |  
puchetpragṛhya bhujagī suptāśuddhodhayaṃvatāṃ ||  
  
nidrāṃ vihāyasya ṛjvī ūrddhamūrtiṣṭate hathāt |  
avasthitā vaiva phaṇāvatītāṃ prātaśca sāyaṃ praharārddhamātraṃ ||  
  
prasārya sūryāt paridhāna muktā pragṛhyate tatparivālanīyā |  
vitasti pramidaṃ dīrghaṃ vistāre caturaṃgulī ||  
  
mṛdulaṃ dhavalaṃ proktaṃ veṣṭanāṃvaralakṣaṇaṃ |  
vajrāsana sthito yogī pālayitvā ca kuṃḍalī ||  
  
kuryādanaṃtaraṃ bhastrī kuṃḍalīmāśu bodhayet |  
manorākuṃcane naiva kuṃḍalī cārayet tadā ||  
  
mṛtyorvaktragatasyāpi tasya mṛtyurbhayaṃ kuta |  
  
nāsādakṣiṇamārgavā hi pavanāt prāṇābhidīrghākṛtauścaṃdrābhaḥ   
paripūritā mṛtatanuḥ prāgghaṃṭikāyāstathā ||  
chinnātkālaviśālavahnivaśagābhrūraṃdhanāḍīgaṇāṃ tatkārya kurute   
punarnavataraṃ cinnadruma skaṃdhavat ||  
  
kuṃṇḍali cālayitvātha kuryādbhrastrī viśeṣataḥ |  
  
p. 138a)  
  
evamabhyasyate nityaṃ yaminastu kutoyama ||  
  
yadābhyaset sūryabhedamujjvayī vāpi śītalī |  
evamabhyāsayogena śamanoyaminā kutaḥ ||  
  
muhūrta dvaya paryaṃtaṃ nirbhayaṃ vā diśodaśaḥ |  
ūrddhamākṛṣyate kiṃcit suṣumnāyāḥ samuddhṛtaḥ ||  
  
tena kuṃḍalinī tasyāḥ suṣumnāyāḥ samuddhṛtā |  
jahāti tasmāt prāṇoyaṃ suṣumnā vrajaniścalā ||  
  
tasmāt saṃcālayennityaṃ sukhasuptāmaraṃdhatī |  
yasyāsaṃcālayenāśu yogī rogāt pramucyate ||  
  
yena saṃcālitā śaktiḥ sa yogī siddhibhājanaṃ |  
kimatravahunoktena kālaṃ vrajati līlayā ||  
  
brahmacaryarataṃ syevaṃ nityaṃ mitamitāsinaḥ |  
maṇḍalād dṛśyate siddhi kuṃḍalyābhyāsa yogataḥ ||  
  
abhyāseṃ vistṛtāṃ cāṃdrī vibhūtāṃ sahamiśrayet |  
tāṃ dhārayeduttamāṃge divyadṛṣṭi pradāyinī ||  
  
dvisaptati sahasrāṇāṃ nāḍīnāmalaśodhanaṃ |  
guḍaprakṣālanīpāyaḥ kuṇḍalibhyāsa iṣyate ||  
  
iti dvādaśadhā proktā ādi nāthena śaṃbhunā |  
kāraṇe sarvasiddhīnāmekaikāpi kṣameva sā ||  
  
rājayogaṃ vinā pṛthvī rājayogaṃ vinā niśā |  
rājayogaṃ vinā mudrā vicitrāpinu rājate ||  
  
mārutābhyāsanaṃ kiṃci māno yuktaṃ samācaret |  
itare'tra na kartavyā manovṛtti manīṣiṇā ||  
  
p. 168b)  
  
vināpi madhyamā nāḍī dṛḍhābhyāsena yoginaḥ |  
āsanaṃ prāṇasaṃyāma mudrābhi saralā bhavet ||  
  
abhyāsena hi mudrāṇāṃ taduteti samādhinā |  
mudrāṇāṃ cāparā mudrā bhadrāsiddhi prayachati ||  
  
upadeśaṃ hi mudrāṇāṃ yo dhatte sāṃpradāyakaṃ |  
sa eva śrī guruḥ svāmī sākṣādīśvara eva saḥ ||  
  
tasya vākya paro nityamathā * sa samāhitaḥ |  
animādi guṇaisvarya labhate kālapaṃcakaḥ ||  
  
namaḥ śivāya gurave nādaviṃdu kalātmane |  
niraṃjana padaṃ yāṃti yato yogī parāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
athedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi samādhi kramamuttamaṃ |  
mṛtyughnaṃ ca sukhopāyaṃ brahmānandakaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
rājayogasamādhiśca utmanīva * *? nī |  
amaraughārayastatra śūnyā chūnyaṃ paraṃ padaṃ ||  
  
amanaskaṃ tathā dvaitaṃ nirālaṃbaṃ niraṃjanaṃ |  
jīvanmukta * ? kti padaṃ śabda paryāya vācakaṃ ||  
  
salile saidhavaṃ yadva samyaṃ bhajati yogataḥ |  
yathātmamanasauraikyaṃ samā *? rabhidhīyate ||  
  
tatsamaṃ ca dvayoraikyaṃ jīvātmā paramātmanā |  
samastanaṣṭasaṃkalpaḥ samādhiso'bhidhīyate ||  
  
samādhistu tathā jñānaṃ karpūraṃ salile yathā |  
tathātmamanasauraikyaṃ samādhiḥ sābhidhīyate ||  
  
rājayogasya māhātmyaṃ koṭyajānāti tatvataḥ |  
  
p. 169a)  
  
jñānamukti sthiti siddhiḥ guruvākya na siddhyati |  
durlabho viṣaya tyāgo durlabhe tatva darśanaṃ ||  
  
durlabhā sahajāvasthā sadguroḥ karuṇāvinā |  
  
yāvatnaiva praviśaṃti caranmāruto madhyamārgaṃ yāvaviṃdurna bhavati   
dṛḍhaḥ prāṇavātaḥ prabuddhaḥ ||  
yāvadyaunnaḥ sahaja sadṛśaṃ jāyate naiva cittaṃ tāvajñānaṃ vadati yadidaṃ   
daṃbhamithyā pralāpaḥ ||  
  
vāyurmārgena saṃcāre sakalaṃ labhate mahaḥ |  
tathāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryaṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ varānane ||  
  
vividhai rasanaiḥ kuṃbhairvicitrakaraṇairapi |  
prabuddhāyāmādi śaktau prāṇaḥ śūnya vilīyate ||  
  
utpanna śakti bodhasya tyakta niḥśeṣa karmaṇāḥ |  
yoginaḥ sahajāvasthā svayameva prakāśate ||  
  
suṣumnā vāhinī prāṇe śūnyaviṃśati mārutaḥ |  
tadā sarvāṇi karmāṇi nirmūlayati yogavit ||  
  
amarāya namastubhyaṃ sopi kāla tvayāhataḥ |  
patitaṃ pavane yasya jagadetaccarācaraṃ ||  
  
citte samatvamāpanne vāyuvrajati madhyame |  
tathāmarolī vajrolī sahajolī matopi ca ||  
  
jñānaṃ kuto manasi jīvati dehi yāvat prāṇopi jīvama * nosni patena yāvat   
prāṇosano dvayamidaṃ vilayaṃ * yāti mokṣaṃ sa gachati naro na kathaṃ   
cidanyat ||  
  
jñātvā suṣumnā sadbhedaṃ kṛtvā vāyuṃ ca madhyagaṃ |  
  
p. 169b)  
  
sthitvā sadaidavasthāne prāṇaraṃdhraṃ nirodhayet ||  
  
sūryacaṃdrasamākṛtvā datvā kārāpi paṃjare |  
suṣumnāṃ śāṃbhavī śakti śeṣāstvevaṃ nirarthakāḥ ||  
  
vāyuḥ paricito yasmādanimāsahakuṃḍalī |  
atha ciṃtāṃtare'bhyāsa pratyāsā jīvayoginā ||  
  
pavaṃno vadhyate yena te naiva vadhyate manaḥ |  
hetu dvayaṃ tu cittasya vāsanā ca samīraṇe ||  
  
tayārvinaṣṭa ekasmin bhāvanāpi vinaśyataḥ |  
tatraiva līyate vāyuḥ manastatraiva līyate ||  
  
dugdhāṃvudhatsaṃmilitā vubhau tau tulya kriyau mānasamārutī hi |  
yato marunniṃdya manaḥ pravṛtti yato manastatra marunnivṛttiḥ ||  
  
ekasyanmasādaparasya nāśa tatraiva vṛtterapasya vṛttiḥ |  
adhastayośceṃdriya vargavṛttiḥ vijñātayormokṣa padasya siddhiḥ ||  
  
rasasya manasaścaiva caṃcaratvaṃ svabhāvataḥ |  
raso vaddho manovaddhaṃ kiṃ na siddhyati bhūtale ||  
  
mūrchito harate vyādhiṃ mṛto jīvayati svayaṃ |  
baddhaḥ khecarataṃ dhatte sa jīvaśo raseśvaraḥ ||  
  
vāyumārge ca saṃcāre saphalaṃ labhate mahaḥ |  
tato'ṣṭaguṇamaiśvarya satyamityāha śaṃkaraṃ ||  
  
manasthairya sthito vāyustato biṃdu sthiro bhavet |  
biṃdusthairyādayā satye piṃḍasthairya prajāyate ||  
  
iṃdriyāṇāṃ mano nāthe manonāthaśca mārutaḥ |  
  
p. 170a)  
  
mārutasya layonāthastannāthaṃ layamāśrayet |  
svayamevāmokṣasva'sti vāpi maṃtrāṃtaro manaḥ ||  
  
prāṇāpānamapānaṃ tāllayakāścitta vartite |  
pranaṣṭau chvāsaniḥśvāsaḥ pranaṣṭaviṣaya grahaḥ ||  
  
niścalo nirvikāraśca layo jayati yoginaḥ |  
uchinnasarvasaṃkalpo niḥśeṣāśeṣaveṣṭitaḥ ||  
  
svāvagamyo layaḥ ko'pi jāyate vāpi gocaraḥ |  
yatra dṛṣṭi layastatra bhūteṃdriya sanātanaḥ ||  
  
sā śaktirjīvabhūtānāṃ dṛṣṭillakṣyalayaṃ gate |  
vedaśāstrapurāṇāni sāmānyā gaṇikā iva ||  
  
ekaiva śāṃbhavī vidyā gopyākulavadhūriva |  
antallakṣamanodṛṣṭirnimeṣāṃ meṣavarjitā ||  
  
eṣā tu śāṃbhavī mudrā sarvamaṃtreṣu gopitā |  
  
anaṃtallakṣavilīna cittapavano yogī yathāvartate dṛṣṭvā niścalatārayā vahirataḥ   
paśyanna paśyannapi ||  
mudreyaṃ khecarī bhavati sāyuṣma prasādānguroḥ śūnyāśūnyavivarjitaṃ   
sthalati yattatvaṃ padaṃ śāṃbhavaṃ ||  
  
tārājyotiṣu saṃyojyo kiṃciduccārayedbhruvau |  
sūryagatasya mārgeṣu unmanī kālalakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
kecidāgamayogena kecinnigamasaṃkule |  
kecittarkena muhyaṃti naiva jānaṃti tārakam ||  
  
arddhoddhāṭita locana sthiramanonāśāgra datve kṣaṇaścaṃdrārkai ca   
vilīyatāṃtara gatau nikṣipya bhāsāṃtare ||  
  
p. 170b)  
  
jyotīrūpamaśeṣa vāhya rahitaṃ dedīpyamānaṃ paraṃ tatva paścaramaṃcavastu   
paramaṃ vācyaṃ kamatrādhikaṃ ||  
  
vāsare pūjayelliṃgaṃ rātrau caiva na pūjayet |  
satataṃ pūjayellingaṃ divārātrau na pūjayet ||  
  
sukhinaṃ jñānajanakaṃ paṃcastrotaḥ samanvitaṃ |  
tichate khecarī mudrā tasmin śūnyaniraṃjane ||  
  
savyadakṣiṇanāḍistho madhye vāhīta mārutaḥ |  
tiṣṭhaṃte khecarī mudrā tatra satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
somasūrya dvayormadhye nirālaṃbaṃ'tathā punaḥ |  
saṃsthitā vyomacakre yā sā mudrā nāma khecarī ||  
  
somayorbheditā dhāma sākṣād vai śivavallabhā |  
pūjayedatulāṃ divyā suṣumnā dakṣiṇe mukhe ||  
  
purastāccaiva pūryata niścitā khecarī bhavet |  
atyastā khecarī mudrā unmanī saṃprajāyate ||  
  
abhyaset khecarī mudrā tāṃvatsyād yoga nidratā |  
saṃprāpta yoganidrasya kālo nāsti kadācana ||  
  
bhruvormadhye śivasthānaṃ manastatra vilīyate |  
jñātavyaṃ tatpadaṃ turyaṃ tatra kālo na vidyate ||  
  
caṃdrasūrya dvayormadhye mudrāṃ dadyācca khecarī |  
nirālambe mahāśūnya vyomacakra vyavasthitaṃ ||  
  
nirālaṃbaṃ mana kṛtvā na kiṃcidapi ciṃtayet |  
sa vāhyābhyaṃtaraṃ vyomni ghaṭavartiṣṭhati dhruvaṃ ||  
  
p. 171a)  
  
vāhyavāyuryathā līnastathā madhye na saṃśayaḥ |  
svasthāna gachati prāṇaḥ sūryāngi pavane tathā ||  
  
evamabhyasya mānasya vāyumārgaṃ sadāniśaṃ |  
abhyāsājjāyate vāyu manastatra vilīyate ||  
  
ajaratvaṃ bhaved dehe āpadatalamastake |  
siddhyate ca mahāyogo mahāvalaparākramaḥ ||  
  
śaktimadhye manaḥkṛṣya śaktirmanasi madhyataḥ |  
manasā manasā lokye dhārayet paramaṃ padaṃ ||  
  
khamadhye kuru cātmānamātmamadhye ca svaṃ kuru |  
sarvaṃ mayaṃ ca khaṃ kṛtvā na kiṃcidapi cintayet ||  
  
antaḥ śūnyo vahiḥ śūnyo śūnyakuṃbha ivāmvare |  
aṃtaḥ pūrṇo vahiḥ pūrṇaḥ pūrṇakuṃbha ivārṇave ||  
  
vāhya ciṃtā na kartavyā tathaicāṃtaraciṃtanaṃ |  
sarvaciṃtā parityāryā na kiṃcidapi cintaye ||  
  
jñeyaṃ sarvamayī tañca jñānaṃ manasi ucyate |  
jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ manaścaiva nānyaḥ paṃtho dvitīyakaḥ ||  
  
manodṛśyamidaṃ sarvaṃ yatkiṃcit sa carācaraṃ |  
manaso hyunmanī bhāvo caitannevai pralabhyate ||  
  
jñeyavastu parityāgādvirayaṃ yāti mānasaṃ |  
mānaso vilaye yāte kaivalyamapi kalpate ||  
  
layo laya iti prāhuḥ kīdṛśaṃ layalakṣaṇaṃ |  
amunarvā sanotthānāddhṛttyayā viśvavismṛtaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ nānāvidho pāyāḥ samyak svānu bhavānvitā |  
samādhimārgā kathitāḥ pūrvācāryai mahātmabhiḥ ||  
  
p. 171b)  
  
aśakyaṃ tatvabodhīnāmūḍhānāmapi sarmataṃ |  
proktaṃ gorakṣanāthena nādopāsanamucyate ||  
  
śrī ādināthena sapādakoṭilayaḥ prakāraḥ kathitā jayaṃti |  
nādānusaṃdhānakameva dhānyaṃ manyāmaheratarnesaṃlayānāṃ ||  
  
śravaṇapuṭayanayugalanāsāmukharodhanenava kartavyaṃ śuddhasuṣumnāśaraṇe   
sphuṭe mamalaḥ śrūyate nādaḥ ||  
  
āraṃbhaśca ghaṭaṃścaivastathā paricayastataḥ |  
niṣpattiḥ sarvayogeṣu syādavasthā catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
brahmagraṃthi bhave bhinnā nādaḥ śūnyasamudbhavaḥ |  
vicitraṃ kuṇako dehe nāhataḥ śrūyate dhvani ||  
  
divyagaṃdhā divyacakṣustejasvī tu arogavān |  
saṃpūrṇa hṛdaya śūnya prāraṃbho yogavān bhavet ||  
  
dvitīya bhedayukte tu vāyurbhāvati madhyagaḥ |  
haṭhāsano bhaved yogī jñānī devasamastathā ||  
  
viṣṇugraṃthastathā bhedā paramānaṃdasūcakaḥ |  
ati śūnye visaṃ maṃdo bherīśabdastathā bhavet ||  
  
atha graṃthi trayaṃ bhitvā jāyate mardala dhvaniṃ |  
mahāśūnya samāyāti sarvasiddhi samāśrayaḥ ||  
  
vinā manastato jitvā sahajānaṃdasaṃbhavaḥ |  
doṣadvakhajarāmṛtyuḥ kṣudhā nidrā tṛṣā tathā ||  
  
rudragraṃthi tato bhitvā sarvapīṭhagato'nilaḥ |  
niṣpanno veṇavaḥ śabdo kvaṇannādo kvaṇo bhavet ||  
  
ekībhūtaṃ tathā cittaṃ rājayogābhidhānakaṃ |  
  
p. 172a)  
  
sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartāso yogīśvara samo bhavet |  
rājayogapadaṃ prastu mukhavāyau'lpa cetasāṃ ||  
  
sadyaḥ pratyūpasaṃdhāyī sevyate nādayo layaḥ |  
  
nādānusaṃdhānasamādhi bhājāṃ yogīśvarāṇāṃ hṛdi vaddhamānaṃ ||  
ānandamekaṃ vacasāmavācyaṃ jānātitaṃ śrīgurunātha eva ||  
  
muktāsanā sthito yogī mudrāsaṃdhāyaśāṃbhavī |  
śṛṇuyāddakṣiṇe karṇe nādamaṃtargate mahat ||  
  
abhyasya māno nādoyaṃ vācyamā śṛṇute dhvani |  
paścādvipakṣamakhilaṃ jitvā yogī sukhī bhavet ||  
  
śruyate prathamābhyāse nādo nāma vidho mahān |  
varddhamāne tato'bhyāse śrūyate śūkṣmaśūkṣmataḥ ||  
  
ādau jaladhijīmūta bharīnirbhara niḥsvanaḥ |  
madhyamardalaśaṃkhe ca ghaṃṭākolāhalastathā ||  
  
anye tu kiṃkiṇī vaṃśa vīṇābhramaraniḥsvana |  
iti nānāvidhānādā śrūyate yatra madhyataḥ ||  
  
mahātiśrūyamānepi meghabheryādika dhvanaiḥ |  
tatra śūkṣmaṃ nādamegha parito'pi parāmṛṇet ||  
  
dhvani mutsṛjya vā śūkṣme śūkṣmamutsṛjya vāyave |  
śmaśānamapi kṣiptaṃ ca mano netra pracārayet ||  
  
yatra kutrāpi vā nāde galati prathamaṃ manaḥ |  
tatraiva nicalo bhūtvā tena sārddhaṃ vilīyate ||  
  
koṣṭha pravartate vahni koṣṭhena sahasāmyati |  
nāde pravartate cittaṃ nādena saha līyate ||  
  
p. 172b)  
  
audāsīnya paro bhūtvā sadābhyāsena saṃśayaḥ |  
unmanī kārakaṃ sadyo nādamevādadhārayet ||  
  
jñātekācaupaṭī vā kuṭī vā pathyāhārogopayocāpayo vā bhojyaṃ bhuktaṃ   
cānnamākaṃdayāvā droṇī cāpya copa bhojyaiva pātraṃ ||  
  
sarvaciṃtāṃ samutsṛjya sarvaceṣṭāśca sarvadā |  
nādamevā na saṃdhatte yogasāmrājyamichati ||  
  
makaraṃdāmivaṃ bhṛṃgo gaṃdhanoppakṣate yathā |  
nādāśaktaṃ tathā cittaṃ viṣayā na hi kāṃkṣati ||  
  
vaddhaṃ vimuktaṃ cāvalyaṃ nādagaṃdhakarīraṇāt |  
manaḥ pāradamāpnoti nirālaṃbākhya khoṭanaṃ ||  
  
vaddhācennāda gaṃdhena sadyaḥ sa tyakta cāpale |  
prayāti sāśvatāścaiva vyupācha chinna idrumā ||  
  
nādaṃ praṇata nittasya maṃtaraṃgā bhujaṃgamaḥ |  
vismṛtya viśvamekāgraṃ kutracitta hi dhāvati ||  
  
manonmartagajeṃdrasya viṣayāpyanucāriṇaḥ |  
līyamānaḥ samarthoyaṃ nilādaniśitāṃkuśaṃ ||  
  
nādāṃtaraṃ tu saṃgasya cājinaḥ paridhāvate |  
aṃtaraṃga turaṃgasya rogo vā gīyate'pi ca ||  
  
anāhata dhvane cetarjñeyaṃ yatsūkṣmasūkṣmakaṃ |  
manastatra layaṃ yāti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ ||  
  
bhāvanākāśasaṃkalpo yāvachaṃdaḥ pravartate |  
niḥśabdaṃ tatparaṃ brahma paramātmānumīyate ||  
  
nādaḥ śaktiritikhyātā nādanāmaṃ sadāśivaṃ |  
  
p. 173a)  
  
nādajñānena naṣṭena tadunmanyeva śiṣyate ||  
  
nādāyāvanmanastāvannādāṃte tu manonmanī |  
sa śabda kathitaṃ vyoma niḥśabdaṃ brahma kathyate ||  
  
yadā nādānusaṃdhānāt saṃkṣīṇe vāsanodaye |  
nirañjane valīyante nisvare manasārute ||  
  
nādakoṭi sahasrāṇi bindukoṭi śatāni ca |  
sarve tatra layaṃ yāṃti yatra devo nirañjanaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ sṛṣṭimayaṃ bījaṃ ekāmudrā ca khecarī |  
eko devī nirālaṃba ekāvasthā manonmanī ||  
  
śaṃkhaduṃdubhinādaṃ ca na śṛṇoti kadācana |  
kāṣṭhavarjāyate deva unmanyā avasthā dhruvaṃ ||  
  
sarvāvasthā vinirmuktā sarvaciṃtā vivarjitāḥ |  
mṛtavattiṣṭhate yogī samukto nātrasaṃśayaḥ ||  
  
avadhyaḥ sarvaśastrāṇāṃmavadhyaḥ sarvadehināṃ |  
agrā * maṃtratantrāṇāṃ yogī yuktasamādhinā ||  
  
praveśe nirgame caiva dakṣiṇe corddhamadhyamaḥ |  
na paśyavāyurvahati samukto nātrasaṃśayaḥ ||  
  
cittaṃ na suptaṃ no jāgrat smṛti vastu ca nānyathā |  
nāsti meti na codeti yathāsau mukta evasaḥ ||  
  
sṛṣṭiḥ sthirā yasya vinaiva dṛśyaṃ vāyu sthiroya vinā prayatnataḥ citta sthiraṃ   
yasya vināvalaṃvanaṃ sa eva muktaḥ sa guruḥ sa sevyaḥ ||  
  
vidyā tīrthe jagati vivudhā sādhavaḥ satya tīrthe gaṃgātīrthe malina manaso yogino   
jñāna tīrthe ||  
p. 173b)  
dhārātīrthe dharaṇi patano dānatīrtheśca bhaktyāḥ lajjātīrthaḥ kulayuvatayaḥ   
pātakaṃ kṣālayaṃti ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade saptaviṃśatitama paṭalaḥ || 27 ||  
  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi ṣoḍaśamātṛkāṃvikā |  
vārāhī nīlakālī ca kathayāmi yathākramaṃ ||  
  
gaurī padmā śacī medhā sāvitrī vijayā jayā |  
devasenā svadhā svāhā mātaro lokamātaraḥ ||  
  
hṛṣṭi puṣṭistathā tuṣṭi tathātmakuladevatā |  
dhammillasaṃyataṃkevā vidhoścādho mukhī galāṃ ||  
  
keśāṃte tilakasyārddhaṃ dadhatī sumanoharā |  
maṇikuṇḍalasaṃghṛṣṭa gaṃḍāmukuṭamaṇḍitā ||  
  
sa jyotiḥ karṇapurāmbā karṇā vā pūrya saṃgatā |  
suvarṇamaṇimāṇikya nāgahāravirājitā ||  
  
sadā sugaṃdhibhiḥ padmai rasānairati suṃdarī |  
mālāṃ vibharti grīvāyāṃ ratnakeyūra dhāriṇī ||  
  
mṛṇālāyata vṛttaistu vāhubhiḥ komalaiḥ śubhaiḥ |  
rājatī kaṃcukopeta pīnonnata payodharā ||  
  
kṣīṇamadhyāpītavastrā trivalī madhya bhūṣitāṃ |  
śūlaṃ vajraṃ ca vānaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ śaktiṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
dakṣiṇaiḥ pāṇibhirdevī gṛhītvāditya pūjitā |  
  
p. 174a)  
  
gadāṃ ghaṃṭhāṃ ca cāpaṃ ca carmaṃ śaṃkhaṃ tathaiva ca |  
ūrddhādi kramato devī dadhatī vāmapāṇibhiḥ ||  
  
siṃhasyopari tiṣṭhaṃti vyāghracarmāṇi kauśikī |  
vibhratīrūpamatulaṃ sasurāsuramohanaṃ ||  
  
nīlotpaladalaśyāmā caturvāhu samanvitā |  
khaṭvāṃgaṃ caṃdrahāsaṃ ca vibhratī dakṣiṇe kare ||  
  
vāme carma ca pāśaṃ ca ūrddhādho bhāvataḥ punaḥ |  
dadhatī muṃḍamālāṃ ca vyāghracarmadharāsurā ||  
  
kṛśāṃgī dīrghadaṃṣṭrā ca ati dīrghoti bhīṣaṇā |  
lolajihvā nimnarakta nayanārārabhīṣaṇā ||  
  
kavaṃdhavāhanāsīnā vistāri śravanānanā |  
eṣā kālī samākhyātā cāmuṃḍeti ca kathyate ||  
  
jayaṃtī mangalā kālī bhadrakālī kapālinī |  
durgākṣamāśivādhātrī svāhā svadhā namostute ||  
  
anenaiva tu maṃtreṇa japahomau tu kārayet |  
gaṃdhapuṣpe tathā dhūpo dīpo naivedyameva ca ||  
  
yasya yaddīyate vastramalaṃkārādi kiṃcana |  
teṣāndaivatamuccārya kṛtvā prokṣaṇa pūjayet ||  
  
utsṛjyamūlamaṃtreṇa pratināmnā nivedayet |  
yaddīyate vadevebhyo gaṃdhapuṣpādikaṃ tathā ||  
  
arghapātra sthitaistoyairabhiṣiṃcya tadutsṛjet |  
vinā pātreṇa ya kuryāt pratiṣṭhāṃ yājñikī kriyāṃ ||  
  
viphalā jāyate sarvā vāhanādi dhanāpahā |  
  
p. 174b)  
  
valihīne tu durbhikṣaṃ gaṃdhahīne ca śokatāṃ |  
dhūpahīne tathodvegaṃ vastrahīne dhanakṣayaṃ ||  
  
ratnahīne mriyedbhāryā vipatākecanāyakaḥ |  
chatrahīne harechatraṃ vitāne maraṇo bhavet ||  
  
vedahīne tu nāśaḥ syān nagarasya purasya ca |  
kalaśairvaṃdunāśaśca bhaved vai muni ukta ca ||  
  
toraṇānāsabhāvāttu hanyājñāti sa bāṃdhavān |  
dakṣiṇā vahite sarvaṃ vyarthaṃ syānnātrasaṃśayaḥ ||  
  
maṃtravidyā vihīnaṃ tu saṃpūrṇamapi naśyati |  
pātramaṃtrasamāyuktaṃ sarvadoṣāharaṃ bhavet ||  
  
rātrāvudaṃ mukhaḥ kuryād devakāryaṃ sa deva hi |  
śivārcanaṃ samāpye śuciḥ kuryādudaṃmukhaḥ ||  
  
śuciḥ vastra * dhṛk prājño maunī dhyānaṃ parāyaṇaḥ |  
gatakāmabhaye dvaṃdvo rāgamotsarya varjitaḥ ||  
  
ātmānaṃ pūjayitvā ca sugaṃdhasitavāsasā |  
sarvamūrte yajed devān svakīyāmanasaṃsthitān ||  
  
sarveṣu gaṃdhajāteṣu praśastoṃ malayodbhavaḥ |  
tasmāt sarvaṃ prayatnena dadyāmalayajaṃ sadā ||  
  
ghṛtatilāśca homārthe madaścaivānulepanaṃ |  
caṃdanāgurukarpūraṃ nakhaṃ dhūpe varaṃ mataṃ ||  
  
caṃdrākhyaṃ lepanaṃ deyaṃ sarvasiddhi pradāyakaṃ |  
kṛṣṇāguruḥ sa karpūraḥ sahito malayodbhavaiḥ ||  
  
kuṃkumāgurukastūrī caṃdrabhāgaiḥ samīkṛtaiḥ |  
gaṃdhaprīti pradādevyā durgāyāḥ saha śaṃbhunā ||  
  
p. 175a)  
  
madakarpūrakāśmīra rocanānāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ |  
etena lepayed devīṃ sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt ||  
  
puṣpairaraṇyasaṃbhūtaiḥ patrairvā giri saṃbhavaiḥ |  
aparyaṣita niśchidraiḥ prokṣitairjaṃtu varjitaiḥ ||  
  
ansarāmodbhavairvāpi puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjaye chivāṃ |  
sa tu kālodbhavaiḥ puṣpaimallikājāti kubjakaiḥ ||  
  
sitaraktaistathā padmainnīlapadmaiśca pāṇḍuraiḥ |  
kiṃśukaistagaraiścaiva kiṃkirātaiḥ sa campakaiḥ ||  
  
vakulaiścaiva maṃdāraiḥ kundapuṣpaistirīṭakaiḥ |  
karavīrārkapuṣpaiśca śāṃśasaiścāparājitaiḥ ||  
  
sitaraktaistathā pītaiḥ kṛṣṇaiścaiva caturvidhaiḥ |  
dhuttūrakāṃti muktaiśca baṃdhūkāgastisaṃbhavaiḥ ||  
  
madanaiḥ siṃduvāraiśca surabhīmuruvakaistathā |  
latābhirbrahmavṛkṣasya durvāṃkuraiśca komalaiḥ ||  
  
maṃjarībhiḥ kuśānāṃ ca vilvapatraiḥ śuśobhanaiḥ |  
uktānuktaistathā sarverjalajaisthalasaṃbhavaiḥ ||  
  
patraiḥ puṣpairyathā lābhaṃ sarvoṣadhayataiḥ śubhai |  
dhānyānāṃ sarvapatraiśca puṣpaiścaiva prapūjayet ||  
  
alābhe puṣpa jātīnāṃ patrāṇyapi nivedayet |  
patrāṇāmapyalābhe tu oṣadhīśca nivedayet ||  
  
oṣadhīnāmalābhe tu bhaktyā bhavati pūjitā |  
kadaṃvairarcayed rātrau mallikā ubhayoḥ smṛtā ||  
  
divāvāyāṇi puṣpāṇi yathālābhaṃ prapūjayet |  
  
p. 175b)  
  
keśakīṭopaviddhāni śīrṇaparyuṣitāni ca |  
svayaṃ patitapuṣpāṇi tyajedupahatāni ca ||  
  
mukulairnārcayed devīmapakvaṃ na nivedayet |  
phalaṃ kathita viddhaṃ ca kālāpakvamapi tyajet ||  
  
sarveṣāṃmeva dhūpānāṃ durgāyo gugguluḥ priye |  
ghṛtayukto viśeṣeṇa satataṃ prīti varddhanaḥ ||  
  
kṛṣṇā guruḥ sa karpūro mahāmāyā priyaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
dhūpaḥ kalyāṇa nāmā tu nityaṃ devyāḥ priyā nṛpa ||  
  
nāsākṣi raṃdhra sukhadaḥ sugandhāti manohara |  
dahyamānasya kāṣṭhasya priyatasyetarasya vā ||  
  
parāgasyāthavādhūpo nistāpo yasya jāyate |  
sa dhūpa iti vijñeyo devānāṃ tuṣṭi dāyakaṃ ||  
  
rāgī kṛtairna caikatra tairdravyaiḥ paridhūpayet |  
medomajjasamāyuktānna dhupānvinivedayāt ||  
  
parakīyāstathā ghrātān steyī kṛtyābhimāṃkitān |  
puṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ ca gaṃdhaṃ ca upacārāstathā parān ||  
  
ghrāṇānnivedya devebhyo naronarakamāpnuyāt |  
na bhūmau vitaveddhūpaṃ nāśanena yute tathā ||  
  
yathā tathā dhāvaśataṃ kṛtvā tāṃ vinivedayet |  
ghṛtadīpaḥ prathamatastilatailodbhavastataḥ ||  
  
sārṣapaḥ phalaniryāsa jāto vārājikodbhavaḥ |  
dadhijaścānnajaścaiva dīpāsapta prakīrtitā ||  
  
haviṣā prathamaḥ kalpo dvitīyaścauṣadhī rasaiḥ |  
vasāmedāsthi niryāsainna kāryaḥ puṣṭimichatā ||  
  
p. 176a)  
  
netrā hlādakaraṃ svarcirdūratā parivarjitaḥ |  
svaśikhaḥ śabdarahito nirddhūmonati hrasvakaḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇe dīpavṛkṣastu pradīpaḥ śrī savṛddhaye |  
suvṛttavarti sa snehaṃ pātrabhavayudarśane ||  
  
pradīpa vṛkṣakoṭau tu dīpandadyān prayatnataḥ |  
labhyate yasya tāpastu dīpasya caturangulāt ||  
  
na sa dīpa iti khyāte osu vahnistu saṃbhṛtaḥ |  
vṛkṣapradīpo dātavyo na tu bhūmau kadācana ||  
  
sarvaṃ sahāvasumatī saha tena dvidaṃ dvayaṃ |  
svakāyapādaghātaṃ tu dīpaghāta tathaiva ca ||  
  
na miśrīkṛtya dadyāt tu dīpasnehān ghṛtādikān |  
kṛtvā miśrī kṛtasnehaṃ tāmisraṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
padmasūtra bhavo darbha garbhasūtrabhavāthavā |  
gaṇajāvādarāvāpi phalokoṭidbhavāpi vā ||  
  
vartikā dīpa kṛtyeṣu sadā paṃca vidhā smṛtā |  
śānaṃ vādaravastraṃ ca jīrṇaṃ malinameva ca ||  
  
upayuktaṃ tu nādadyādvartikārthaṃ kadācana |  
naiva nirvāpayed dīpaṃ devārthamupa kalpitaṃ ||  
  
dīpahartā bhavedaṃdhaḥ kāṇonirvāpanā bhavet |  
naivedyaṃ suprabhṛtaṃ ca deya devyāḥ subhānvitau ||  
  
paramānnaṃ piṣṭakaṃ ca yāvakaṃ kṛśavaṃ tathā |  
modakaṃ prthukādīnikaṃdu parvāṇi cotsṛjet ||  
  
haviḥ śālyodanaṃ divyamāhyayuktaṃ sa śarkaraṃ |  
nivedayet mahādivyai sarvāṇi vyaṃjanāni ca ||  
  
kṣīrādīnpathagavyāni mahīṣāṇi ca sarvaśaḥ |  
kapitthaṃ lāṃgalaṃ caiva drākṣākramukameva ca ||  
  
vakulaṃ ca madhukaṃ ca rasālāsrotake tathā |  
auduṃvaraṃ ca punnāgaṃ karuṇaṃ karkaṭī phalaṃ ||  
  
hanītakīmāmalakaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ nāgaraṃgakaṃ |  
mātuluṃgaṃ ca kuṃcakadalīkaramardakaṃ ||  
  
śṛṃgāṭakaṃ kaśeraṃ ca śālūkaṃ ca mṛṇālakaṃ |  
kumudānī paṃkajālāṃ phalāni vinivedayet ||  
  
vānapriyaiśca naivedyailājākṣata phalādibhiḥ |  
ikṣudaṃḍiḥ sitābhiścalavatīnāgaraṃgakaiḥ ||  
  
pūjayejjagatāṃ dhātrī sarvakāmārtha siddhaye |  
paṃcābdaṃ lakṣaṇopetaṃ gaṃdhadhūpasugaṃdhitaṃ ||  
  
vidhivat kālikālikālīti japtvā khaḍgena ghātayet |  
paṃcābdaṃ paṃcavārṣīkaṃ mahiṣamajameṣa ca ||  
  
tadusyaṃ rudhiraṃ māṃsaṃ gṛhītapūtanādiṣu |  
nair-ṛtebhyaḥ pradātavyaṃ mahākauśikamaṃtritaṃ ||  
  
tasyāgrato nṛpaḥ snāyāchatruṃ kṛtvātha piṣṭakaṃ |  
khaḍgena ghātayitvā tu dadyā skaṃda viśākhayāḥ ||  
  
tato devīṃ snāpaye ca kṣīrasarpi jalādibhiḥ |  
kuṃkumā gurukarpūra caṃdanaiśca prapūjayet ||  
  
hemādi puṣparatnāni vāsāṃsinnahatāni ca |  
naivedyaṃ suprabhṛtaṃ ca deyaṃ devyāḥ svabhāvitaiḥ ||  
  
devī bhaktāśca pūjyaṃte kanyakāḥ prathamādayaḥ |  
  
p. 177a)  
  
dvijadīnānupākhāṃḍānannadānena toṣayet |  
nandabhaktā na vāye tu mahāvrata dharāścaye ||  
  
pūjayet tātviśeṣeṇa yasmāt tad rupamāmnikaṃ |  
mātṛkāṇāṃ ca devānāṃ pūjākāryā tadā niśi ||  
  
dhvajachatrapaṭākādi uchayeccaṃḍikā gṛhe |  
rajayātrāṃ valikṣepa vaṭukādyaśca pūjayet ||  
  
kārayet tuṣyate yena nānāpaśunipātanaiḥ |  
aśvamedhamavāpnoti bhaktitaḥ surasattamaḥ ||  
  
mahānavamyāṃ pūjaye ca sarvakāma pradāyakā |  
sarveṣu vatsavarṇeṣu tava bhaktyā prakīrtitā ||  
  
kṛtvāpnoti yaśorājya putrāyuddha na sampadaḥ |  
kanyāyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe tu pūjayitvā prabhe divā ||  
  
navamyāṃ bodhayed devīṃ gītavādita nisvanaiḥ |  
śuklapakṣe caturthyāṃ tu devīkeśavimocanaṃ ||  
  
prātareva tu paṃcamyāṃ snāpayet suśubhai jalaiḥ |  
saptamyāṃ patrikā pūjā aṣṭamyāṃ cappupoṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
pūjā ca jāgaraścaiva navamyāṃ vidhivad valiḥ |  
sapreṣaṇaṃ daśamyāṃ tu krīḍākautukamangalaiḥ ||  
  
nīrājanaṃ daśamyāṃ tu valivṛddikaraṃ mahat |  
rāmasyānu grahārthāya rāvaṇasya ca dhāya ca ||  
  
rātrāmeva mahākālī brāhmaṇāvodhitā purā |  
tatastu tyakta nidrā sā naṃdayāmāśvine site ||  
  
rāmārāvaṇayoryuddhaṃ saṣmahaṃ sāmyayojayet |  
vyatīte saptarātre tu navamyāṃ rāvaṇaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
p. 177b)  
  
rāmaṇe ghātayā māsa mahāmāyā jagatmayī |  
yāvat tayāḥ svayaṃ devī yuddhakolimudaikṣata ||  
  
tāvat tu saptarātrāṇi sarvadevaiḥ supūjitā |  
nihate rāvaṇe vīra navamyāṃ sakalaiḥ suraiḥ ||  
  
viśeṣapūjāṃ durgāyāḥ cakre loka pitāmahaḥ |  
tataḥ saṃpreṣitā devī daśamyāṃ śāvarotsavaiḥ ||  
  
tathaiva ca narāḥ sarve kuryupūjāṃ yathāvidhi |  
valanīrājanaṃ rājā kuryādvavalavṛddhaye ||  
  
dikpālaṃ kārayuktābhiḥ kāśinībhiḥ pravartanaṃ |  
kartavyaṃ gītavādyādi krīḍākautuka maṃgalaṃ ||  
  
keśasaṃskāradravyāṇi pradadyāt pratipaddine |  
ṣaḍgādānaṃ dvitīyāyāṃ keśasapa hetave ||  
  
darpaṇaṃ ca tṛtīyāyāṃ siṃdurānaktakaṃ tathā |  
madhuparkaṃ caturthyaṃ tu tilakaṃ netramaṃḍalaṃ ||  
  
paṃcamyā yadgarāgaṃ ca śaktyālaṃkaraṇāni ca |  
ṣaṣṭyāṃ vilvatarau bodhaṃ sāyaṃ saṃdhyāsu kārayet ||  
  
saptamyāṃ prātarānīya gṛha * dhye prapūjayet |  
upoṣaṇamathāṣṭamyāṃ sāṣṭaśakteśca pūjanaṃ ||  
  
navamyāṃmugracaṃḍāyāstadvadevārcanaṃ divā |  
pūjā ca validānaṃ ca tadvatyā tu prapūjayet ||  
  
kumārī pūjanīyāvabhūṣaṇīyā ca bhūṣaṇaiḥ |  
saṃpūjya preṣaṇaṃ kuryād daśamyāṃ śāvalotsavaiḥ ||  
  
anena vidhinā yastu devīṃ prīṇayate naraḥ |  
skandavat pālayet tastu devī sarvāpadi sthitaṃ ||  
  
p. 178a)  
  
putradāradhanarddhīrāṃ saṃkhyā tasya na vidyate |  
bhuktveha paramān bhogān pretya devagaṇo bhavet ||  
  
bodhayodvilvaśākhāyāṃ ṣaṣṭhyāndevī phaleṣu ca |  
saptamyāṃ bilvaśākhāṃtāmāhṛtya pratipūjayet ||  
  
punaḥ pūjāṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ viśeṣeṇa samācaret |  
jāgaraṃ ca svayaṃ kuryād validānaṃ mahāniśi ||  
  
prabhūtavalidānaṃ tu navamyāṃ vidhivarcayet |  
dhyāyed daśabhujān devīṃ durgātaṃtreṇa pūjayet ||  
  
visarjanaṃ daśamyāṃ tu kuryād vai śāvarotsavaiḥ |  
kṛtvā visarjanaṃ tasyāṃ tasyānaktaṃ samācaret ||  
  
antapādo divābhāge praṇavasya yadā bhavet |  
tadā saṃpreṣaṇaṃ devyā daśamyāṃ śāvarotsavaiḥ ||  
  
vāṇinībhiḥ kumārībhiḥrveśyābhirnnartakaistathā |  
śaṃkhatūryaninādeśca mṛdangai paṭahaistathā ||  
  
dhvajairastrairvahuvidhairlāja puṣpa prakīrtikaiḥ |  
dhūlikardamavikṣepaiḥ krīḍākautukamaṃgalaiḥ ||  
  
bhagaliṃgobhidhānaiśca bhagaliṃgapragītakaiḥ |  
bhagaliṃgakriyābhiśca krīḍaye yuvalaṃjanāḥ ||  
  
parairnākṣipyate yastu yaḥ paraṃ nākṣipatyapi |  
tasya kruddhā bhagavatī śāpaṃ dadyāt sudāruṇaṃ ||  
  
mūlaṃ prāpya prathama caraṇebhyarcanaṃ caṇḍikāyāḥ   
kṛtvāṣṭamyāmaśanarahitastyakta nidraśca pūjāṃ prātaḥ kāle paśuvalividhiḥ   
snānadānaṃ navamyāṃ nirmālyaṃ tu śravaṇadaśamīvāsavarkṣeṣujatyāt ||  
  
p. 178b)  
  
mūlena pratipūjayed bhagavatīṃ caṃḍīṃ pracaṇḍā kṛtiṃ   
cāṣṭamyāmupavāsasadgatatayā bhaktyā samārādhayet ||  
  
nānāpāśavamajjamāṃsarudhiraiḥ kṛtvā navamyāṃ valiṃ nakṣatraśravaṇa   
tithiṃ ca daśamī saṃprāpya saṃpreṣayet ||  
  
ṛkṣatraye ca mūlādau saptamyāmāśvinesite |  
caṇḍikāmupahāraiśca pūjayedrāṣṭavṛddhayet ||  
  
kuryājjāgaramaṣṭamyāṃ navamyāṃ vidhivadvaliṃ |  
daśamyāṃ valavṛddhyarthaṃ kuryānnīrājanaṃ priye ||  
  
mūlena bodhayed devī pūrveṇa pratipūjayet |  
uttareṇārcanaṃ kṛtvā śravaṇena visarjayet ||  
  
tithiḥ śaraṃtithireva kāraṇaṃ tithiḥ pradhānaṃ tithireva sādhanaṃ |  
tithiṃ vinānaiva ca dṛśyate śaśī vineṃdunānaiva ca karmasiddhiḥ ||  
  
tithinakṣatrayoryoge dvayorevānu lepanaṃ |  
yogābhāve tithi grāhyā devyāḥ pūjanakarmaṇi ||  
  
umā yā navamī proktā harasya tithiraṣṭamī |  
dvayoraikya mahāpuṇyā umāmāheśvarī tithi ||  
  
aṣṭamyāṃ navamī yuktā navamyā cāṣṭamī yuta |  
arddhanārīśvara prāyātithiḥ sarvavratādiṣu ||  
  
āśvinasya site pakṣe yā tusyā tithiraṣṭamī |  
tasya rātrau pūjanīyā mahāvibhavavistarai ||  
  
yo mohādatha vānasyaddevī durgā mahotsave |  
  
p. 179a)  
  
na pūjayati daṃbhādvādvevyādvāpyatha bhairava |  
kruddhā bhagavatī tasya kāmānniṣṭhānnihaṃti vai ||  
  
paratra ca mahāmāyā valirbhūtvā sa jāyate |  
tasmālloka hitārthāya sarvalokavibhūtaye ||  
  
durgātaṃtreṇa maṃtreṇa pūjitasya ubhe api |  
bhadrakālī cogracaṇḍī mahāmāyai mahotsave ||  
  
prāguttareṇa tasmācca dadhyakṣata samanvitaṃ |  
cūtapallavasaṃchannaṃ phalavastrayugānvitaṃ ||  
  
paṃcaratnasamāyuktaṃ paṃcabhaṃgadalānvitaṃ |  
sthāpayedatraṇaṃ kuṃbhaṃ varuṇaṃ tatra vinyaset ||  
  
gaṃgādyāḥ saritaḥ sarvāḥ samudrāṃśca sarāṃsi ca |  
gajāśca rathyāvalmīkasaṃgamādvadaśo kulāt ||  
  
mṛdamānīya vipreṃdra sarvauṣadhi jalānvitaṃ |  
snānārthaṃ vinyaset tatra yajamānasya dharmacit ||  
  
sarve samudrāḥ saritaḥ sarāṃsi vanadā hradāḥ |  
āyāṃ tu yajamānasya duritaḥ kṣayakārakāḥ ||  
  
śrīkāmastulya sanmyaka deśavṛddhikaraṃ śubhaṃ |  
kāṃcanaṃ ghṛtagodhūmān dūrvārocanayā saha ||  
  
agnirbrahma bhavānī ca gajavaktro mahoragaḥ |  
skaṃdobhānurmātṛgaṇo digpālāśca navagrahāḥ ||  
  
eṣāṃ ghaṭeṣu pratyekaṃ pūjayitvā yathāvidhi |  
mūrtipavitramekaikaṃ dadyādebhyaḥ samāhitaḥ ||  
  
kadalī dāḍimī dhānyaṃ haridrāmānakaṃkacuḥ |  
vilvāśākhā jayaṃtī ca vijñeyānavapatrikā ||  
  
p. 179b)  
  
brahmāṇī kadalīkāṃḍe dāḍime rakta caṃḍikā |  
dhānyalakṣmīrharidrāyāṃ durgāmānaka patrake ||  
  
cāmuṃḍākālikāṃ kacyāṃ śivāvilvapratiṣṭhitā |  
aśokaśokarahitā jayaṃtyāṃ kārtikīṣṭhitāṃ ||  
  
tasmin devī prakartavyā haimī vārājatī tathā |  
mṛdvākṣī lakṣaṇopetā bilva khaḍge ca pūjayet ||  
  
tatrāṣṭamyāṃ bhadrakālī dakṣayakṣa vināśinī |  
prādurbhūtā mahāghorā yoginī koṭibhiḥ saha ||  
  
atārthaṃ pūjanīyā sā tasminnahanimānavaiḥ |  
upoṣitairvastradhūpamālyaratnonulepanaiḥ ||  
  
dīpairnaraistathā bhakṣyaiḥ phalairmalaiśca dhānyakaiḥ |  
āmiṣairvividhaiḥ śokaiḥ homairbrāhmaṇa tarpaṇaiḥ ||  
  
bilvapatraiḥ śrīphalaiśca caṃdanena ghṛtena ca |  
paśubhiḥ pānakairhṛdyairātrijāgaraṇena ca ||  
  
durgā gṛhe tu śastrāṇi pūjanīyāni paṃḍitaiḥ |  
vādyabhāṃḍāni cihnāni kavacānyāyudhāni ca ||  
  
rātrau ca śilpibhistāni svāni pūjyāni sarvadā |  
kanyāsthe ravayaścaiva śuklāṣṭamyāṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
sopavāso niśārddhaṃ tu mahāvibhavavistaraiḥ |  
pūjāṃ samārabheddevyā nakṣatre vāruṇepi vā ||  
  
paśughātaśca kartavyo gavalājavadhastathā |  
valikṣepaṃ sureśānāṃ kṛtvā sarvaṃ niśāṃtaye ||  
  
p. 180a)  
  
kanyāsaṃsthe ravī vatsa śuklāṣṭamyāṃ prapūjayet |  
sopavāso niśārddhe tu mahāvibhavavistaraiḥ ||  
  
pūjāṃ samārabheddevya rakṣarkṣavāribheyi vā |  
paśorghātaḥ prakartavyo gavadojavadhastathā ||  
  
valikṣepastu rakṣobhyaḥ kāryaḥ sarvāriśāṃtaye |  
kanyāsaṃstheravā viṣeyā śuklātithiraṣṭamī ||  
  
tasyāṃ rātrau pūjitavyā mahāvibhavavistaraiḥ |  
navamyāṃ validānaṃ tu kartavyamvai yathāvidhi ||  
  
japahomaṃ ca vidhivat kuryāt tatra vibhūtaye |  
mātṛṇāṃ caiva devīnāṃ pūjākāryā tadā niśi ||  
  
hataghore mahāvīre surāsurabhayaṃ kare |  
devyā upāsakā devāḥ prabhutārākṣasāstathā ||  
  
āgatā ghātitaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahiṣaṃ taṃ sudurjayaṃ |  
brahmāviṣṇusureśānāṃ iṃdracaṃdrayamānilāḥ ||  
  
ādityā vasavo rudrā grahānāgaḥ sa guhyakāḥ |  
samabhya sarvadevāste devī bhaktyā pratuṣṭuvuḥ ||  
  
caraṃ ca sarvalokānāṃ pradadau bhayanāśinī |  
valiṃduduśca bhūtānāṃ mahiṣājāniṣeṇa ca ||  
  
praṇeduḥśaṃkhabhedaiśca śamaśodha sahasraśaḥ |  
hatādvaṃdvabhinādāśca paṭṭaśabdāḥ samardanā ||  
  
patākā dhvajasaṃchannaṃ ghaṃṭācāmaraśobhitaṃ |  
taddinaṃ kārayāmāsurdevī bhaktāḥ surottamāḥ ||  
  
kṛtvā ca sarvadevaiśca mahāpūjā ca śāśvatī |  
  
p. 180b)  
  
āśvine māsi meṣāṃte mahiṣāriṇi varhiṇīṃ |  
devīṃ saṃpūjayitvāya arddharātreṣṭamīṣu ca ||  
  
ghātayaṃti paśun bhaktyā te bhavaṃti mahāvalāḥ |  
valiṃ ca ye prayachaṃti sarvabhūtavināśanaṃ ||  
  
teṣāṃ tu tuṣyate devī yāvat kalpaṃ tu śāṃkaraṃ |  
krīḍaṃti vividhairbhogairdevaloke sudurlabhe ||  
  
nādhayo vyādhayasteṣāṃ na ca śakra bhayaṃ bhavet |  
na ca deva grahā daityā nāsurā na ca pannagāḥ ||  
  
pīḍayaṃti surādhyakṣa devī pādau samākṣitān |  
yāvadurvāyuvākāśaṃ jalaṃ vahni śaśi grahāḥ ||  
  
tāvacca caṇḍikā pūjā bhaviṣyati sadā bhuvi |  
prāvṛkāle viśeṣeṇa āśvine hyaṣṭamīṣu ca ||  
  
mahāśabdo navamyāṃ ca lokekhyātiṃ gamiṣyasi |  
etat te devarājeṃdra svargavāsaphalapradaṃ ||  
  
prarāparā vibhāgena kriyāyogā ca kīrtitaṃ ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade aṣṭāviṃśati paṭalaḥ || 28 ||  
  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
navapadmātmake sthāne pūjā durgāḥ svamūrtitaḥ |  
ādau madhye tatheṃdrādau navatatvākṣaraiḥ kramāt ||  
  
aṣṭādaśabhujaiḥ kāṃta pīnavakṣasthalorūkā |  
mūrddhajaṃ kheṭakaṃ ghaṃṭhāmādarśaṃ tarjanīṃ dhanuḥ ||  
  
dhvajaṃ ḍamarukaṃ pāśaṃ vibhratī vāmake tataḥ |  
śaktimudgara śūlaṃ ca vajraṃ khaḍgamathāṃkuśa ||  
  
raśaraṃ cakralokāṃ ca etairevāyudhairyutāḥ |  
  
p. 181a)  
  
śeṣāḥ ṣoḍaśahastā ca tarjanīṃ ḍamaruṃ vinā |  
rudracaṃḍā pracaṃḍā ca caṃḍogrā caṃḍanāyikā ||  
  
caṇḍācaṃḍavatī caiva caṃḍarūpāti caṃḍikā |  
navamī cogracaṃḍā ca madhyasthā ca prakīrtitā ||  
  
rocanāṃgāruṇā kṛṣṇā nīlāśuklā ca dhūmrikā |  
pītā ca pāṃḍaroraktā anīṭasthā hari sthitā ||  
  
mahiṣotha mahāśastrī tatkeca grahamuṣṭikā |  
sthāpyāvṛtte ca paṃktyā ca ityuktaṃ skaṃda yāmale ||  
  
mahiṣaghnirmahāmāya cāmuṃḍe muṃḍamālinī |  
dravyamārogya vijayaṃ dehi devi namaḥ sadā ||  
  
rūpaṃ dehi yaśo dehi bhagaṃ bhagati de hime |  
putrā dehi dhanaṃ dehi sarvān kāmān prade hime ||  
  
ādau prathamataḥ padma madhya sthitvā ca caṃḍikā |  
puṣpamāropya hastena śāradāmaṃbikenmuhu ||  
  
ehyehi parameśāni sānnidhyamiha kalpayā |  
pūjābhāgaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ durge devi namostute ||  
  
durge durge ihā gacha gaṇaiḥ parikaraiḥ saha |  
pūjā bhāgaṃ gṛhāṇesaṃ makharakṣa namostute ||  
  
nārāyaṇyai vidmahe * caṇḍikāyai tu dhīmahi |  
śeṣabhāge tu gāyatryāstanna caṃḍī pracodayāt ||  
  
datvā snānamanenaiva durgā taṃtreṇa vai punaḥ |  
caturakṣaramaṃtreṇa pādyādīnatha ṣoḍaśa ||  
  
vitaredupacārāśca pūrvoktaṃścaiva bhairava |  
  
p. 181b)  
  
durgātaṃtreṇa maṃtreṇa devyā aṃgāni pūjayet |  
durge anena hṛdayaṃ para durge anenakaṃ ||  
  
śikhā kavaca netrāṇi vāhu?pādāṃśca paṃcabhiḥ |  
vādipaṃcākṣaraiḥ śeṣaiḥ pūjayet kramaśaḥ sudhī ||  
  
pūrvabhāge maṃḍalasya devyāḥ śaktīśca pūjayet |  
ugracaṃḍā pracaṃḍāṃ ca caṃḍogrāṃ caṃḍanāyikāṃ ||  
  
caṃḍāṃ ca davatīṃ caiva caṇḍarūpāṃ ca caṃḍikāṃ |  
devyāstu kara gṛhyāṇi śastrāstrādīni vāhanaṃ ||  
  
paṃcānanaṃ kāmasaraṃ ca daityamagre ca pūjayet |  
japtvā stutvā valiṃ dadyān namaskṛtvāvaguṇṭhya ca ||  
  
yonimudrāṃ pradaśyārtha nirmālyaṃ diśi śūlinaḥ |  
caṃḍeśvaryai nama iti nivāpya ca visarjayet ||  
  
ugracaṃḍādikāḥ pūjyā yoginyoṣṭau tathā śubhāḥ |  
yoginīśca catuḥṣaṣṭhiṃ tathā vai koṭi yoginī ||  
  
navadurgāstathābhyarcyaddevyāḥ sannihitāḥ śubhāḥ |  
jayaṃtyādyāgaṃdhapuṣpaistāddevyā mūrtayo yataḥ ||  
  
devyāḥ śastrāṇi cāstrāṇi bhūṣaṇāni tathaiva ca |  
aṃgapratyaṃgayuktāni vāhanaṃ siṃhameva ca ||  
  
mahiṣāsuramardinyāḥ pūjayed bhaktaye sadā |  
grahāśca daśadikpālān pūrvoktena krameṇa tu ||  
  
pūrvavatpūjayeddhīmān bhairavaṃ bhairavīmapi |  
dakṣiṇe pūjayedetāścatuḥṣaṣṭhiśca yoginī ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi catuḥṣaṣṭhikarūpakaṃ |  
mahābhāgyaṃ viśeṣeṇa dhanadharmasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
p. 182a)  
  
pūjayed vijayāṃ devīṃ śūlapadmākṣadhāriṇīṃ |  
varodyatāṃ siṃhasaṃsthāṃ sarvasiddhipradāyinīṃ ||  
  
maṃgalāṃ pūjayed devīṃ sarvasiddhi pradāyinīṃ |  
siṃhapadmāsanāṃ saumyāṃ jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
śūlākṣasūtravaradāmabhayaṃ dakṣaṇe kare |  
bhadrāṃ tu pūjayed devīṃ bhadrāsana vyavasthitāṃ ||  
  
nīlotpalakarāṃ śūlākṣasūtravaradhāriṇīṃ |  
dhṛtisaṃpūjayed devīṃ caṃḍāsana vyavasthitāṃ ||  
  
padmadarpaṇadhāriṇīṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāṃ |  
śāṃtiḥ śāṃti pradākāryā padmāsana vyavasthitā ||  
  
akṣasūtradharā devī varado vāmapāṇikā |  
śivāvṛṣāsanāṃ kāryā trinetrāvarapāṇikā ||  
  
ḍamaruragadhāriṇī sa śūlā cābhaya pradā |  
jaṭāmukuṭakhaṃḍendu vāsuki kṛtakaṃkaṇā ||  
  
kṣamāpadmāsanasthā tu pratisūryopapāṇikā |  
mekhalāśūlasaṃyuktā yogapaṃttottarīyakā ||  
  
siddhiścaṃḍāsamākāryā siddhārthake varapradā |  
atha padmāsanasthā tu pratisūryopaśobhitā ||  
  
tuṣṭiṃ ca pūjayed devīṃ kalaśoparisaṃsthitāṃ |  
pāśāṃkuśadharāṃ saumyā padmasvastika dhāraṇīṃ ||  
  
umāpadmāsanā kāryā mṛgasiṃhaparāvṛtā |  
yogapaṭṭottarāsaṃgā kamaṃḍalukarā śubhā ||  
  
varādyatatriśūlājya jayādyaiḥ parivāritā |  
gahamālāvirājaṃtī padmakuṃḍaladhāriṇī ||  
  
p. 142b)  
  
śivārcanaratā devī puṣṭiḥ kāryā yathā śṛṇu |  
khaḍgahastā mahārūḍhā carmamudgaradhāriṇī ||  
  
aśvārūḍhā svarūpādyā puṣṭivevaṃ vidhā bhavet |  
śriyā padmāsanā kāryā padmaśrīphaladhāriṇī ||  
  
gajairbhūhītakalaśaiḥ snāpyamānāsuśobhanā |  
ṛddhiṃ pūjaya padmasthāṃ varadābhaya pāṇikāṃ ||  
  
dānodyata karāṃ devīṃ vyāharaṃtīṃ śubhāni ca |  
vīṇāvādyena padmasthā ratiḥ kāryā sulocanā ||  
  
dīptā caṃḍāsanākāryā kiraṇojjvaladhāriṇī |  
siṃhāsanā gadā vāpi padmahastā suśobhanā ||  
  
nīlotpala sthitā kāṃtiḥ kamalotpaladhāriṇī |  
muḍmālāṃ bhūṣitā devī sarvābharaṇa carcitā ||  
  
paryaṃkodara saṃsthā ca yaśāḥ kāryāsuśobhanā |  
śaṃkhapustakadhārī ca sunmālā bharaṇojvalā ||  
  
lakṣmīḥ padmāsanā kāryā padmaśrīphaladhāriṇī |  
īśvarī vṛṣabhasthā tu jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇī ||  
  
caṃdrārddhaśekharā devī triśūloraṃgabhūṣaṇā |  
kalasthā * bhavedvarddhirbījapūrakadhāriṇī ||  
  
yogapaṭṭottarāsaṃkā ratnamālā dharā śubhā |  
śākrī gajāsanā kāryā vajrahastāsuśobhanā ||  
  
jayāvatī siṃhasaṃsthā śaraśṛṃgadharā śubhā |  
haṃsāsanā bhaved brāhmī muṃjamekhaladhāriṇī ||  
  
caturvaktrā svarūpādyā daṃḍakāṣṭhaṃ kamaṃḍaluṃ |  
  
p. 183a)  
  
akṣasūtraṃ ca vibhrāṇā sruca hastājya dhāriṇī |  
yogapaṭṭakakhaṭvāṃgī sarvado giraṇānanā ||  
  
jayaṃtī nakulasthā ca kuṃḍaśūlakarā śubhā |  
khaḍgakheṭakarākāryā varadābhaya pāṇikā ||  
  
aparājitā tu kartavyā siṃhārūḍho mahāvalā |  
pinākaśarahastā tu khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇī ||  
  
trinetrā sa jaṭājūṭā kṛtavāsuki dhāriṇī |  
padmāṃkuśakarā devī ajitāmakarāsanā ||  
  
rathasthāmānasī kāryā ghaṃṭāmudgaradhāriṇī |  
vajrāṃkuśadharā devī sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā ||  
  
śvetāpaṃkajasaṃsthā tu daṃḍākṣasūtradhāriṇī |  
ditirdaṃḍadharā kāryā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā ||  
  
phalanīlotpalavarā utsaṃge vālakānvitā |  
māyā pāśāṃkuśavarā māyā vāmaradhāriṇī ||  
  
śūkarasthā mahāmāyā mohayaṃtī carācaraṃ |  
mohanī mṛgayā rūḍhā dhvajaśūlākṣadhāriṇī ||  
  
veṇuhastāsurāpātra hārakeyūrabhūṣitā |  
lālasāgajasaṃsthā tu malādarpaṇadhāriṇī ||  
  
tārākaraśamārūḍhā vimalā hṛdyacarcasā |  
muktākṣasūtradhāri ca kamaṃḍalu kalā śubhā ||  
  
gaurī padmāsanasthāṃ tu varadābhaya pāṇakā |  
akṣasūtrakarā devī kamaṃḍalu dharā śubhā ||  
  
śaraṇyā siṃhamāsīnā varadābhayapāṇikā |  
kauśikī kauśikārūḍhā triśūlamuṃḍadhāriṇī ||  
  
p. 183b)  
  
kapālakartikā hastā ghorarūpā mahāvalā |  
matimanasthā kartavyā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā ||  
  
vīṇāvādanaśīrā ca nṛtyamānā suśobhanā |  
durgādidya * mastrāṇi pṛṣṭagā ripu suṃdanī ||  
  
pinākaśaracarmāsi dhāriṇī mahiṣāpahā |  
tachīrṣottha mahākāryaistadbhaṭaiḥ parivāritā ||  
  
raktasrudrakta netraiśca tajitā tanmahāvalaiḥ |  
veṣṭitānāgapāśena kacikecchigatāsavaḥ ||  
  
devī śūlagatāḥ kāryāḥ sarvate saṃmukhāna *? |  
pādīpadmāsane caikamekaṃ mihaniveśitaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ vidhena rūpeṇa durgākāryāmacānyathā |  
vaṭṭoparisamāsīnā kriyākāryāsuśobhanā ||  
  
puṣpamālāvirājaṃtī prabhāmaṃḍalabhūṣitā |  
sravamekhanadhārī ca sarvaśobhāsamanvitā ||  
  
vratasthā ruṃdhatī kāryā puṣpodakarā śubhā |  
ghaṃṭhāṃ tu pūjaye devī ghaṃṭhahastāṃ triśūlinīṃ ||  
  
karṇā svarūpā kartavyā sa kartā tu suśobhanā |  
padmākṣasūtradhārī ca mahāvrata dharā śubhā ||  
  
kapālinī sadā kāryā kapālaśūladhāriṇī |  
rudrarūpā tathā raudrī vṛṣasaṃsthā suśobhanā ||  
  
jaṭāmukuṭasārddheṃ duḥkṛta vāsukikaṃkaṇā |  
rathasthāṃ pūjayet kālīṃ kapālaśūladhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
mayūrī śikhi saṃsthā ca pāśaśaktiṃ dharā śubhā |  
trinetrā śakrakartavyā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā ||  
  
daṇḍāsana samārūḍhaṃ padmasvastikadhāriṇī |  
  
p. 184a)  
  
svarūpāṃ pūjayed devīṃ hārakeyūrabhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
śūlakhaḍgadharā devīṃ vahurūpāṃ narāsanāṃ |  
trinetrāṃ pūjayed devīṃ śūlapaṭṭisadhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
jaṭoragaśiraścaṃdra bhūṣitāṃ śivarūpiṇīṃ |  
ripuhāśatru nāśārthaṃ vajracakradhanurddharā ||  
  
aśvārūḍhā tathā pūjyā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā |  
aṃbikāṃ śūlasūtrākṣa dhāriṇīṃ pūjayet tadā ||  
  
padmāsanasthāṃ deveṃdra carcikāṃ sāṃprataṃ śṛṇu |  
pretārūḍhāṃ mahādevīṃ nāgābharaṇabhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
ūrddhakeśī karālīṃ tu muṃḍakartikadhāriṇīṃ |  
surapūjitā tu kartavyā gajārūḍhā mahāvalā ||  
  
vajrāṃkuśadharāṃ devī tathā vaivasvatīṃ śṛṇu |  
kāpāladaṃḍahastāṃ tu śūkarāsyāṃ yamāsanāṃ ||  
  
kaumārī pūjyate devī mayūrāsana śakti bhūt |  
tridaṃḍī vānarūpā tu raktamālyā sa kukkuṭā ||  
  
māheśvarī vṛṣārūḍhā trinetrāśūladhāriṇī |  
vīṇāvādanaśīlā ca hārakeyūrabhūṣitā ||  
  
śaṃkhacakradharā pūjyā vaiṣṇavī garuḍāsanā |  
vanamālā dharādevī mahālakṣmīstathā śṛṇu ||  
  
gagaṇodbhisi śūlāṃ ca nṛtyamānāṃ kapālinīṃ |  
saumyānanāṃ susaṃpūrṇā trinetrāmuṃḍabhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
tasyāḥ saṃmukhagākāryā kārtikī pretasaṃsthitā |  
śivadūtī ca kartī ca yauvanā bharaṇojjvalā ||  
  
śivāvajrāṃkuśadharānirmāṃsā koṭare kṣaṇā |  
  
p. 184b)  
  
aviralau tathaivoṣṭhau vikeśānāgavaṃdhanā |  
mudrālaṃkṛtakarṇā tu vāmorukarasaṃsthitā ||  
  
pīṭhasaṃsthena yāmye ca tathāṭhavikṛtānanā |  
cāmuṃḍā pūjyate devī ūrddhakeśī bhayānakā ||  
  
pretāsanasthā nirmāṃsā mālākhaṭvāṃgadhāriṇī |  
kapālaśūlahastā ca karṇikā bharaṇojjvalā ||  
  
mudrāvasthe dhare cauṣṭhe saṃsthitā vāmakāṃguliḥ |  
gajacarmāsurā raudrī nāgābharaṇabhūṣitā ||  
  
catuḥṣaṣṭhestu devīnāṃ rūpakaṃ kathitaṃ tava |  
sāṃprataṃ ca sudhādhyakṣa mahābhāgyaṃ vadāmyahaṃ ||  
  
yathā śivasya naivāṃto vidyate devi pūjane |  
tathā cāṃtaṃ na paśyāmi catuḥṣaṣṭhestu pūjanāt ||  
  
suvarṇabhūmidānasya godānasya ca yatphalaṃ |  
phalaṃ tadadhikaṃ devi catuḥṣaṣṭhi smṛteriha ||  
  
prāsāde maṃḍape gehe citre vastre valārthatā |  
catuḥṣaṣṭhirmahābhāga pūjitārājyadā śubhā ||  
  
catuḥṣaṣṭhi pratiṣṭhāpya dvātriṃśaṣoḍaśāthavā |  
vasusaṃkhyāmathā devi sarvaṃ tarati dukṛtaṃ ||  
  
mātṝṇāṃ lakṣyaṇaṃ vakṣye yathāvadana pūrvaśaḥ |  
brahmāṇī brahmasadṛśī caturvaktrā caturbhujā ||  
  
haṃsādhirūḍhākartavyā sākṣasūtrakamaṃḍaluḥ |  
maheśvarī svarūpeṇa tathā māheśvarī matā ||  
  
jaṭāmukuṭasaṃyuktā vṛṣasthā caṃdraśekharā |  
kapālaśūlakhaṭvāṃga varadātha caturbhujā ||  
  
p. 185a)  
  
kumārarūpākaumārī mayūravaravāhinī |  
raktavastradharā tadvachūlaśakti dharā matā ||  
  
hārakeyūrasampannā kṛkaṃrākuṭharā tathā |  
vaiṣṇavī viṣṇu sadṛśī garuḍāsanasaṃsthitā ||  
  
caturbāhuśca varadā śaṃkhacakragadādharā |  
siṃhāsana gatā vāpi cālakena samanvitā ||  
  
vārāhī ca pravakṣyāmi mahiṣā parisaṃsthitā |  
vārāha sadṛśīṃ devīṃ ghaṃṭācāmaradhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
gadācakradharā tadvad dānaveṃdra vināśinīṃ |  
iṃdrāṇīmiṃdrasadṛśīṃ vajraśūlagadādharāṃ ||  
  
gajārūḍhāstutāṃ devīṃ locanairvahubhirvṛtāṃ |  
taptakāṃcanavarṇābhāṃ vastrābharaṇabhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
tīkṣṇakhaṭvāṃgadharāṃ tadva yogīśvaraṃ mimāṃ śubhāṃ |  
dīrghajihvāmurddhakeśīmachikhaṇḍeśca maṃḍitāṃ ||  
  
daṃṣṭrā karālavadanāṃ kuryād vai ca kuśodarīṃ |  
kapālamālinīṃ devīṃ muṇḍamālāvibhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
kapālaṃ vāmahaste tu māṃsaśoṇitapūritaṃ |  
sa keśaṃ ca śirotyasmin śastrikāṃ dakṣiṇe tathā ||  
  
gṛdhrasthā vā śavāsthā vā nirmāṃsā vigatādarī |  
karālavadanā tadvat kartavyā sā tilocanā ||  
  
cāmuṇḍā ca dvaghaṃṭhā ca dvīpi carmadharā śivā |  
digvāsā kālikā tadvadrāsabhasthā kapālinī ||  
  
surakta puṣpā bharaṇā varddhanī dhvaja saṃyutā |  
  
p. 185b)  
  
vināyakaṃ ca kurvīta mātṛṇā maṃtrike tathā |  
vīreśvaraśca bhagavān vṛṣārūḍho jaṭādharaḥ ||  
  
vīṇāhasta triśūlī ca mātṝṇāṃ purato bhavet |  
mātaraḥ pūjanīyāstu dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa phalārthinā ||  
  
gaṃdhanaivedyadhūpena valimālāvibhūṣaṇaiḥ |  
tathā mātṛgaṇaṃ pūjya devaṃ bhairavarūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
strīsaṃyukanyakā viprāḥ pūjanīyāśca śaktitaḥ |  
brāhmī māheśvarī caiva kaumāri vaiṣṇavī smṛta ||  
  
vārāhya na ta candrāṇī cāmuṇḍā saptamī satā |  
aṣṭamī syān mahālakṣmīḥ proktāḥ syuḥ viśvamātaraḥ ||  
  
caṃḍikā taṃtra maṃtrasya yoginyoṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ |  
brahmaṇī prathamā proktā tato māheśvarī para ||  
  
kaumārī vaiṣṇavī caiva vārāhī ca tathā parā |  
nārasiṃhī tathaicendrī śivadūtī tathāṣṭamī ||  
  
bhairavaḥ pāṇḍanāthaśca raktagauraścaturbhujaḥ |  
gadāpadmaṃ ca śaktiṃ ca cakraṃ cāpi kareṣu ca ||  
  
vibhra devyāḥ purābhāge pūjyoyaṃ viṣṇu rūpadhṛk |  
mama pravartate pūjā yatra yatra ca tatra te ||  
  
pūjyaściṃtyataśca tatraiva kāyoyaṃta ca dānava |  
triśūlaṃ dakṣiṇe dadyāt khaḍgacarmaṃ tathorddhataḥ ||  
  
tīkṣṇavāṇaṃ tathāśaktiṃ vāmatopi nibodhate |  
kheṭakaṃ pūrṇacāpaṃ ca pāśamaṃkuśameva ca ||  
  
ghaṇṭhā vā paraśuṃ vāpi vā medhaḥ sa niveśayet |  
  
p. 186a)  
  
dvibhujā divyavastrāṇi khaḍgakheṭakadhāstathā |  
divyasuṃdariṃ rūpā ca pāśaśūladharāstathā ||  
  
dhanurvāṇadharācānyā ghaṃṭhācakrakarodyatā |  
vajradaṇḍadharā devīṃ daśavāhurathā parā ||  
  
kartikāṃ madgaraṃ kuṃbhaṃ kuṭhāraṃ tarjanī puraḥ |  
ḍamaruṃ dhārayaṃtī ca śakti hastā mahāvalāḥ ||  
  
padmābhaya karā devī tarpaṇaṃ viṃśakekare |  
evaṃ vidha svarūpā tu siṃhasyoparisaṃsthitā ||  
  
mahāmāyā prakartavyā siṃhayugmagatāthavā |  
padmāsanasthā varadā navayauvanabhāvitā ||  
  
sarvāvayavaśobhāḍhyā jayādyarūpaśobhitā |  
atha vā yudhyamānā tu mahiṣāsuraghātinī ||  
  
dhyātā prapūjitā nityaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradā |  
na tathā tuṣpatte devi homadānajapena tu ||  
  
kumārī pūjane nātra yathā devī prasīdati |  
pitaro vasavo rudrā ādityāgaṇalokapāḥ ||  
  
śuklāṣṭamī caturdaśyā navamyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |  
kṛṣṇapakṣe viśeṣeṇa bhojayet tu kumārikāḥ ||  
  
prakṣālyapādau sarvāsāṃ kumārīṇāṃ ca vāsava |  
svalipte bhūtale divya tatratā āsane sthitā ||  
  
pūjayed gaṃdhapuṣpaiśca prāgbhavaścāpi nanārasaiḥ |  
pūjayitvā vidhānena bhojanaṃ tālu dāpayet ||  
  
p. 186b)  
  
khaṇḍala tu guḍaṃ sarpirdadhīkṣīraṃ sa mākṣikaṃ |  
tāsāṃ deyaṃ kumārīṇāṃ sanairbhañjāpayeccatāḥ ||  
  
pānīyaṃ yācitandeya matramvā yācitaṃ śubhaṃ |  
tāsbhṛptāstu yadā sarvāstadā svācanaṃ dadet ||  
  
ācamyatākṣatān sarvān datvā tvayākṣataṃ tata |  
dātuḥ śirasi dātavyāḥ kanyakābhirathākṣatāḥ ||  
  
tenapi praṇipātaṃntu kartavyo bhaktipūrvakaḥ |  
anena vidhināścaiva devī kṣipraṃ prasīdati ||  
  
dadāti vividhān kāmān manobhīṣṭān surādhipa |  
rājyaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ paścād devalokaṃ ca gacchati ||  
  
prabhūtavalidānaṃ ca navamyāṃ vidhiva caret |  
valiṃ ca ye prayachakti sarvabhūtavināśanaṃ ||  
  
tapyantu tuṣyeteddevī yāvat kalpantu śādkuraṃ(?) |  
sarvabhūtavināśānāṃ mahiṣā chedanaṃ ||  
  
navadhā paśughātantu mahiṣā jāyo vighātanaṃ |  
kartavyaṃ bhūtavetāla navamyāṃ nātmikāmyayā ||  
  
pakṣi *? kachapā grāhā varāhāsdvo?galāstathā |  
mahiṣo godhikā meṣastathā navavidhāmṛgā ||  
  
navavidhāmṛgāḥ kṛṣṇā sāraruru prabhūtayaḥ |  
dadatuṣṭau valiṃ caiva nija gātrā sṛgukṣitaṃ ||  
  
sahasraṃ bhṛpti māyāti svadehaṃ rudhireṇa tu |  
tarpitā vidhivadurgā bhitvā vāhuṃ ca jaṃghake ||  
  
ajaśva mahiṣaścaiva naraścaiva yathā kramāt |  
valirmahāvaliśca ti valiśveti prakīmbhatāḥ |  
  
p. 187a)  
  
nāreśaśirasāvīra pūjitā vidhivannṛpa |  
tṛṣṇābhūtaṃ bhaved dūrgā varṣāṇāṃ lakṣameva ca ||  
  
śonitaṃ maṃtra pūtantu śārṣapīyuṣamucyate |  
tasmāt tu pūjane dadyād valaḥ śīrṣaṃ ca śāṇitaṃ ||  
  
pūjayed vidhivad bhaktyā cāmuṇḍasūdinīṃ |  
rudhireṇa tathā vīra śiro hivvividhi nṛpaḥ ||  
  
ajāri mahiṣāṇāṃśca svadehasya ca bhedanāt |  
chinnalāṅgulakarṇākṣi bhagnadanta tathaiva ca ||  
  
bhagnaśṛṃgādikaṃ cāpi na dadyāt tu kadācana |  
kāśavyaṃgañcāpi vṛddhaṃ rogiṇañca galad vraṇaṃ ||  
  
klivaṃdīnāṅgamaṃthavā viddha liṅgaṃ sravat kakaṃ |  
na ca traimāsikā nyunaṃ paśun dadyāchivāvaliṃ ||  
  
na ca traipakṣikānnyunaṃ pradyād vai ṣatatriṇaṃ |  
paśūnā pakṣināmnāpi narānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
striyanna dadyābhuvaliṃ datvā narakamāpnuyāt |  
anuktaṃ nāpi dadyāt tathā'jñātā ṛgadvijāna ||  
  
pṃcābdaṃ lakṣaṇopetaṃ vidhivat kālikā vali |  
vidhivatkālikāsini japtvā khaḍgena ghātayet ||  
  
uttarābhimukho bhūtvā valiṃ pūrvamukhaṃ tathā |  
nirīkṣāsādhakaḥ paśvādimaṃmantamudīrayet ||  
  
narastvaṃ valirūpeṇa mama bhāgyadupasthitaḥ |  
praṇamāmi tataḥ sarva rūpiṇaṃ valirūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
caṃḍikā prīti dānena dāturāpadviśana |  
cāmuṃḍā valirūpāṃ yaṃ vale tubhyaṃ namostute ||  
  
yajñārthe valayaḥ sṛṣṭaḥ svayameva svayaṃbhuvā |  
  
p. 187b)  
  
atastvāṃ ghātayāmpadya tasmād yajñepadho'vadhaḥ |  
e& hrī& śrī& miti maṃtreṇa valiṃmetasvarūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
cintayitvā nyaset puṣpaṃ mūrddhitasya tu bhairava |  
tato devo samuddiśya kāmamuddiśya cātmanaḥ ||  
  
abhiṣicyata tathā kṛṣṇaṃ pinākapāṇi ca kālarātri svarūpiṇaṃ |  
ugraṃ raktāsya nayanaṃ raktamālyānulepanaṃ ||  
  
raktāvaradharaṃ caika pāśahastraṃ kuṭumvitaṃ |  
picamānaṃ ca rudhiraṃ bhujānaṃ dravyasaṃhitaṃ ||  
  
asirviśasanaḥ khaḍgastīkṣṇadhārīdarā sahaḥ |  
śrīgarho vijayaṃścaiva dharmapāla namostute ||  
  
pūjayitvā tataḥ khaḍgaṃ ā& hu& phaḍiti maṃtrakaiḥ |  
gṛhītvā vimalaṃ khaḍgaṃ chedayed valimuttamaṃ ||  
  
oṃ e& hrī& kauśikīti rudhiraṃṇāpyāyatāmiti |  
sthāna niyojayed raktaṃ śiraśca saptadīpakaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ datvā valiṃ pūrṇa phalaṃ prāpnoti sādhakaḥ |  
hīnantu syād vinaṃtāyāṃ niṣkalaṃ syād viparyayāt ||  
  
anyeṣāṃ mahīṣādīnāṃ valināmatha pūjayet |  
kāyo madhyatvamāyāti raktaṃ gṛhnāti vai śivā ||  
  
validāne tu durgāyāḥ sarvatrāyamvidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
daityānāṃ matsyamāṃsāni devīnāṃ palanaudanaṃ ||  
  
kuṣmāṇḍamikṣudaṇḍaśca madyamāṃsa vayaṃ va ca |  
eta valiṃ samājñayāsbhṛptau chāgasamāsamāḥ ||  
  
caṃdrahāsena kartārai chedanaṃ saṃkhyamiṣyate |  
  
p. 188a)  
  
dātrāsidhenukrakavaśaṭkulābhistu madhyanaṃ ||  
  
asidhenuḥ chariśaṃ cakralāvartatathaiva ca |  
kartarīkṣura bhagnaśca adhamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
etyaunyaiḥ śaktiśūlādyaiḥ valichedyaḥ kadāpi naḥ |  
nāsti devīṃ valiṃ tantu dātā mṛtyu navāpnuyāt ||  
  
validāne valiṃ chitvā khaṃgaiste rudhiraiḥ sakaiḥ sarvaṃ vaśya na maṃtreṇa   
lalāṭe tilakaṃ nyasyet ||  
  
rājā vā rājaputre vā striyo vā yakṣarākṣasāḥ |  
sarva tasya vaśaṃ yānti bhūtagrāmaścaturvidhaḥ ||  
  
ajānāṃ mahiṣānāñca meṣāṇāṃ ca tathā vadhāt |  
prīṇayed vidhivad durgā māṃsaśoṇitatarpaṇeḥ ||  
  
ahanya hani yo durgā pūjayed radhirādibhiḥ |  
kulānāṃ śatamuddhṛbhyaṃ brahme loke mahīyate ||  
  
svamekamekaṃ varadā bhṛptā bhavati caṇḍikā |  
rudhireṇoraṇasyeha tarpitā vidhivannṛpa ||  
  
ajaspada varṣāṇi rudhireṇa sutarpitā |  
mahiṣeṇa śataṃ vīra bhṛptā bhavati caṇḍikā ||  
  
sahasraṃ bhṛpti māyāti svadeharudhireṇa tu |  
tarpitā vidhivad durgā bhitvā vāhu ca jaṃghake ||  
  
nareṇa śirasā vīra pūjitā vidhivan nṛpa |  
bhṛptārāved dṛśa durgā varvāṇāṃ lakṣameva tu ||  
  
chitvā bhitvā ca bhūtāni hatvā sarvamidaṃ jigat |  
praṇamya śirasā devīḥ sa pāpaistu na lipyate ||  
  
durgāyā darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ darśanādabhivaṃdanaṃ |  
  
p. 188b)  
  
vandanā sparśanaṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sparśanādabhi pūjanaṃ |  
pūjanāt snapanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ snapanārtarpaṇaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
tarpaṇānmāṃsa dānaṃ tu mahiṣājanipātanaṃ |  
sarvayajñopavāseṣu sarvatīrtheṣu yatphalaṃ ||  
  
tatphalaṃ labhate vīra praṇamya śirasā * sīṃ |  
saṃprasārita deho yo daṇḍavat patito bhuvi ||  
  
caṃḍikā purato vīra sa yāti paramāṃ gatiṃ |  
tapatīrtha pradānaiśca yajñairvā vahu dakṣiṇaiḥ ||  
  
na tādgatiṃ labhaṃte trayāṃstu tvā ca sureśvarīṃ |  
āyurārogyasauṣyāni sampado dayitāstriyaḥ ||  
  
bhavaṃti tasya yasmaiti devīṃ vāsava bhairavīṃ |  
caṇḍikāṃ pūjayitvā tu prahṛṣṭenāṃ narātmanā ||  
  
kṛtāṃjaliṃ puṭo bhūtvā idaṃ stotramudīrayet |  
oṃ durgāṃ śivāṃ śāṃti karīṃ brahmāṇīṃ brahmaṇaḥ priyāṃ ||  
  
sarvalokapraṇetrī ca praṇamāmi sadā śivāṃ |  
maṃgalāṃ śobhanāṃ siddhāṃ niḥkalāṃ paramā kalāṃ ||  
  
viśveśvarīṃ viśva mātāṃ caṃḍikāṃ praṇamāmyahaṃ |  
sarvadevamayīṃ devīṃ sarvarogabhayāpahāṃ ||  
  
brahmeśaviṣṇu namitāṃ praṇamāmi sadā umāṃ |  
viṃdhyasthā viṃdhyanilayāṃ divyasthānanivāsinīṃ ||  
  
yoginīṃ yogamātāṃ ca caṇḍikā praṇamāmyahaṃ |  
īśānamātaraṃ devīmīśvarīmīśvara priyāṃ ||  
  
praṇatosmi sadā durgā saṃsārārṇava tāriṇīṃ |  
ya idaṃ paṭhati stotraṃ śṛṇuyādvāpi yo naraḥ ||  
  
p. 189a)  
  
sa muktaḥ sarvapāpaistu modate durgayā saha |  
maṃtreṇānena vṛttāre prārthayet tāṃ sureśvarī ||  
  
mahiṣagni mahāmāye cāmuṇḍe muṃḍamālinī |  
dravyamārogya vijayaṃ dehi devi namostute ||  
  
bhūtapreta piśācebhyo rakṣobhyośca maheśvari |  
devebhyo mānuṣebhyaśca mayābhyo rakṣamāṃ sadā ||  
  
sarvamaṃgalamāṅgalya śive sarvārthasādhike |  
umā brahmāṇi kaumāri viśvarūpa prasīda me ||  
  
rūpaṃ dehi yaśo dehi bhagaṃ bhavati dehi me |  
putrān dehi dhanan dehi sarvān kāmān prasīda me ||  
  
caṃdanena samālabdhe kuṃkumena vilepite |  
bilva patra kṛtā pīḍe durgehaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade unatriṃśa paṭalaḥ || 29 ||  
  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
durgā gṛhe tu śastrāṇi pūjanīyāni paṃḍitaiḥ |  
vādyabhāṃḍāni cihnāni kavacānyā yudhāni ca ||  
  
aśirvisasanaḥ khaḍgastīkṣṇadhārodvarāsanaḥ |  
śrīgarbho vijayaścaiva dharmadhārastathaiva ca ||  
  
ityaṣṭau tava nāmāni prayamuktā nivedhasā |  
na kṣetraṃ kṛttikā te tu guru devā maheśvarā ||  
  
rohiṇyaśca śarīraṃte daivataṃ ca janārdanaḥ |  
pitāpitāmahādevastvaṃmāṃpānaya sarvadā ||  
  
nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśastīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāḥ kṛśodaraḥ |  
bhāvaśuddhomarṣaṇaśca ati tejāstathaiva ca ||  
  
iyaṃ yena dhṛtākṣoṇī hatayaśca mahāsuraḥ |  
  
p. 189b)  
  
tīkṣṇadhārāya śuddhāya tasmai khaḍgāya te namaḥ ||  
  
sarvāyudhānāṃ prathamaṃ nirmitāsi pinākinā |  
śūlāyuddhādviniṣkṛṣya kṛtvāmuṣṭi gṛhaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
caṃḍikāyāḥ pradattāni sarvaduṣṭanivarhiṇī |  
tayā vistāritā cāgni devānāṃ pratipāditā ||  
  
sarvasatvāṃga bhūtāni sarvāśubhanivarhiṇī |  
churike rakṣamānnityaṃ śāṃtiyecha namostute ||  
  
rakṣāṃgāni grajānrakṣa rakṣavājidhanāni ca |  
mama dehaṃ sadārakṣa kaṭṭāraka namostute ||  
  
sarvāyudha mahāmātra sarvadevārisūdana |  
cāpamāṃsamarerakṣa śākaṃ śaravarairiha ||  
  
dhūtaṃ kṛṣṇena rakṣārthaṃ saṃhārāya hareṇa ca |  
trayī mūrti gataṃ devaṃ dhanurastraṃ namāmyahaṃ ||  
  
prāṇān pātaya śatrūṇāmanayātīkṣṇa dhārayā |  
gṛhāṇa jīvitaṃ teṣāṃ kuṃtasyainpaṃca rakṣa me ||  
  
śarmapradastvaṃ samare varman sainya yaśodyamāṃ |  
rakṣamāṃ rakṣaṇīyohaṃtāpaneya namostute ||  
  
śaśāṃkakarasaṃkāśa himadiṃḍirapāṃḍara |  
protsāraya tvaṃduritaṃ cāmacāmara vallabhaḥ ||  
  
yathāṃvudaśchāda yajña śivāyamāṃ vasuṃdharāṃ |  
tathāmāṃchādaya chatrayuddhe dhvani gataṃ sadā ||  
  
śakraketo mahāvīryaḥ svayaṃ tustvāṃ samāśritaḥ |  
pakṣirojāvainateyastathā nārāyaṇadhvajaḥ ||  
  
kāśyapayo mṛtāhartā nāgārirviṣṇuvāhanaḥ |  
aprameyo durādharṣo raṇadevāni sūdanaḥ ||  
  
p. 190a)  
  
garutmān māruta gati tvayi sannihitaḥ sthitaḥ |  
sāśca carmāyudhān yodhān yodhān rakṣātmakaṃ ripuṃ ||  
  
hutabhūgvasavo rudrā vāyuḥ somāmaharṣayaḥ |  
nāgakiṃnaragaṃdharvāyakṣabhūtamahoragāḥ ||  
  
pramathāśca mahādevyai bhūtaśāmātṛbhiḥ saha |  
sakrasenāpatiskaṃda varuṇaścāśritastvayi ||  
  
pratihaṃtu ripun sarvān rājavijayamṛchatu |  
yāni prayuktānyaribhirduṣaṇāni samaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
nihatāni sadātāni bhavaṃ tu tava tejasā |  
kālanemi vadhe yuddhe yuddhe tripuraghātine ||  
  
hiraṇyakaśipo yuddhe yuddhe devāsure yathā |  
śobhitāsi tathaivādya śobhasuramayaṃ smara ||  
  
raktāṃ nīlāṃsitāṃ dṛṣṭvā naścattvāśumamārayaḥ |  
duṃdubhe tvaṃ sapatnānāṃ ghoṣāvṛdaya kampanaḥ ||  
  
bhavabhūmipasainyānāṃ tathā vijayavarddhanaḥ |  
yathā jīmūtaghoṣeṇa hṛṣyaṃti varavāraṇāḥ ||  
  
tathāstu tava śabdena harṣosmākaṃ jayāpahaḥ |  
yathājīmūtaśabdena strīṇāṃ trāsobhijāyate ||  
  
tathā tatra ca śabdena tasyaṃtvasmād dviṣoraṇe |  
puṇyastvaṃ śaṃkhapuṇyānāṃ maṃgalānāṃ ca maṃgalaṃ ||  
  
viṣṇunātvaṃ dhṛto nityaṃ mataḥ śāṃtiṃ prayacha me |  
vijayo jayadojetāripu bhettābhayaṃkaraḥ ||  
  
duḥkhahāśarmadaḥ śāṃtaḥ sarvāriṣṭavināśanaḥ |  
ityaṣṭau tava nāmāni yasmāt siṃhaparākramaḥ ||  
  
p. 190b)  
  
tena siṃhāsane titvaṃ nāmnā deveṣu gīyate |  
tvayi sthitaḥ śivaḥ śākṣāstvayi śakraḥ sureśvaraḥ ||  
  
tvayi sthite haridevaṃstvadarthaṃ tanyate tapaḥ |  
samasta sarvato bhadra śivo bhava mahīpate ||  
  
trailokya vijaya sarvaṃ siṃhāsana namostute |  
turaṃgamaciraṃ jīva paraśastraiva lakṣitaḥ ||  
  
sadāmāṃsamarerakṣa svāmi kāryaṃ sadā kuru |  
gaṃdharva kulajātosi sā bhūyā kuladūṣakaḥ ||  
  
brāhmaṇaḥ satya vākyena somasya varuṇasya ca |  
tejasī caiva sūryasya munīnāṃ tapasā tathā ||  
  
rudrasya brahmacaryeṇa pavanasya valena ca |  
prabhāvācca hutāśasya varddhasuddhaṃ turaṃgamaḥ ||  
  
smaratvaṃ rājaputrāsi kaustubhaṃjamaṇiṃ smara |  
surāsurairmadhyamānāt kṣīrodādamṛtādibhiḥ ||  
  
jāta uccaiḥ śravāḥ pūrvaṃ tena jātosi tatsara |  
yāṃ gatiṃ brahmahā gachet pitṛhā mātṛhā tathā ||  
  
bhūmyarthe nṛtavādī caraṇeyaśca parāṃmukhaḥ |  
sūryācaṃdramasau vāyuryāvat paśyaṃti duḥkṛtāṃ ||  
  
tāṃ gatiṃ vrajasi kṣipraṃ tacca pāpaṃ bhavai bhuva |  
vikṛtiṃ yadi gachethā yuddhe dhvaṃni turaṃgama ||  
  
ripun vijinya samare sahabhattā sukhī bhave |  
śivāḥ kaṃkāla vetālāḥ pūtanā jaṃbhakādayaḥ ||  
  
te sarve tṛptimāyāṃ tu validānena toṣitā |  
yojāgaraṇaṃ girisutābhirato dadāti caitrotsavādi divase vyadhidūryanādaṃ ||  
  
p. 191a)  
  
vīṇāsureṇu madhurasurabhāṣiṇībhiḥ saṃgīyate sahi kṛśodara kinnaraṃbhiḥ |  
  
gītavādya pradānena saukhyaṃ prāpnotyanuttamaṃ |  
pradakṣiṇa pradānena rūpavānami jāyate ||  
  
māsi cāśvayute vīraḥ śuklapakṣe triśūlinīṃ |  
navamyāṃ pūjayed yastu tasya puṇyaṃ phalaṃ śṛṇu ||  
  
aśvamedha sahasrasya vājapeyaśatasya ca |  
tatphalaṃ labhate vīra dividevagaṇairddhṛtaḥ ||  
  
ajānāṃ mahiṣāṇāṃ ca meṣāṇāṃ ca tathā vadhāt |  
prīṇayed vidhivad durgāṃ māsaśoṇita tarpaṇaiḥ ||  
  
uttiṣṭha devi caṃḍeśi śubhāṃ pūjā pragṛhya ca |  
kuruṣva mama kalyāṇamaṣṭābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ saha ||  
  
gacha gacha parasthānaṃ svasthānaṃ devi caṃḍike |  
vajrasoto jalavṛddhyai tiṣṭha gehe ca bhūtaye ||  
  
oṃ durge devī jaganmātaḥ svasthānaṃ gacha pūjite |  
saṃvatsare vyatīte tu punarāgamanāya vai ||  
  
imāṃ pūjāṃ mayā devī yathāśaktyā niveditāṃ |  
rakṣaṇārthaṃ samādāya vrajasusthānamuttama ||  
  
caturbhujāṃ pītavastrāṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāṃ |  
  
dakṣiṇavāmayo rūpari talahastayoḥ khaḍgacarmadharāṃ madhastana   
hastayorvarābhayaṃ cihnaṃ trinetrāṃmīṣat prahasita vadaṃ nāma parājitāṃ   
cāruṇāmukhapadmena vicitrakanako jvalā ||   
  
jayā devi śive bhaktā sarvān kāmāṃ dadātu me |  
kāṃcanena vicitreṇa karpūreṇa vibhūṣitā ||  
  
p. 191b)  
  
jayāpradā mahāmāyā śivabhāvita cetasā |  
vijayāva sadābhāgāṃ dadātu vijayaṃ mama ||  
  
hāreṇa suvicitreṇa bhāsvat kanaka mekhala |  
aparājitā rudraratā karotu vijayaṃ mama ||  
  
iti stutvā haridrā ca pītopacāra pūjayet |  
sadā parājitā yasmāt tvaṃ latāsūka mātṛtā ||  
  
sarvākāmārtha siddhārtha kasmāt svādhārayāmyahaṃ |  
bhavā parājite devi mama sarvārtha mṛddhaye ||  
  
pūjitāyāṃ tvayi śrayo mamāstu duritaṃ hataṃ |  
oṃ jaya devaradedevi daśamyāma parājite ||  
  
dhārayāmi bhujaṃ dakṣa jalalābhābhivṛddhaye |  
valamādhe hi valayaṃ mayi śatroḥ parājaya ||  
  
tvaddhāraṇādbhaveyurmedhanadhānyasamṛddhaye |  
surāstvāmabhi * cestu brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ||  
  
vāsudevo jagannāthastathā saṃkarṣaṇo vibhuḥ |  
pradyumnaśca niruddhaśca bhavaṃ tu vijayāyate ||  
  
ākhaṇḍalāgni bhagavān yame vai nirmatistathā |  
varuṇāḥ pavanaścaiva dhatodhyakṣastathā śivaḥ ||  
  
brahmaṇā sahitāḥ śeṣāṃ digpālāḥ pāṃtu te sadā |  
kīrti lakṣmīrddhṛtirmedhā puṣṭiḥ śraddhājiyāmati ||  
  
buddhirlajjā vapuḥ śāṃtistuṣṭiḥ kāṃtiśca mātaraḥ |  
etāstvāmaṃbhiṣiṃcaṃ tu devāpanyaḥ samāgatāḥ ||  
  
āditya caṃdramāsomo budhajīvasitārkaṭāḥ |  
gṛhāstvamabhiṣiṃcaṃtu rāhuketuśca tarpitāḥ ||  
  
p. 192a)  
  
datvādānavagaṃdharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ |  
ṛṣayo mānavo gāvo devāmāṃgala eva ca ||  
  
deva patnyo umānāgā debhyāścāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ |  
astrāṇi sarvaśāstrāṇi rājano vāhanāni ca ||  
  
oṣadhāni ca ratnāni kālasyā vayavāḥścaye |  
saritaḥ sāgarāśailāstīrthāni jaladānavāḥ ||  
  
etāstu mabhiṣiṃcaṃ tu sarvakāmārthasiddhaye |  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi prāyaścittavidhiṃ tava |  
gurutyāga karaḥ śiṣyaḥ prāyaścitti bhaveddhruvaṃ ||  
  
lakṣaṃ śrīpādukāṃ japtvā tasmāt pāpād viśuddhyati |  
maṃtratyāgakaro yastu tatsaṃgaṃ varjayet priye ||  
  
lakṣamekaṃ japen maṃtraṃ homatarpaṇataḥ śuciḥ |  
nityādi kramadoṣāṇāṃ śāṃtyaṃ vidyāśataṃ japet ||  
  
naimittikāti kramaṇe sahasraṃ prajapenmanuṃ |  
madhulobhādyathā bhṛṃgaḥ puṣpāt puṣpāṃtaraṃ vrajet ||  
  
gurulubdhāstathā śiṣyo gurorgurvataraṃ vrajet |  
yadi daivāt paśorvidyā labhyate kulajairnaraiḥ ||  
  
dvijaṃ tu kaulikaṃ prāpya punarvidyāmupālabhet |  
śakalo jīvahīnastu saṃdigdho niṃditastathā ||  
  
manavastu na siddhyaṃti guruḥ syādbrahmaghātakaḥ |  
tadā taṃ sahasā jñātvā maṃtraṃ deva guruṃ tyajet ||  
  
kṣamasvamātastatpāpaṃ haradevi kṛpāṃ kuru |  
anekadhā paśo ratnaṃ bhuṃjate ye tu kaulikāḥ ||  
  
lakṣatrayaṃ japellopāṃ lakṣaṃ vāpya japāṃ japet |  
  
p. 192b)  
  
homayeddhaviṣāntena niḥpāpaḥ syāt tathā dhruvaṃ |  
ekapātro pibed dravyaṃ vīro māheśvaro yadi ||  
  
śvānocchiṣṭaṃ bhavet pāpaṃ prāyaścittaṃ sa kaulikaḥ |  
gāyatryāstu sahasreṇa upavāsa trayeṇa ca ||  
  
samyak śodhita cittastu suvarṇaṃ guruve dadet |  
valāt svarasato vāpi yoramenmaṃtra mātaraṃ ||  
  
daśalakṣaṃ manuṃ japtvā tuṣānalaṃ samācaret |  
maṃtraputryāḥ svaputryāśca bhaginyāśca kulastriyaḥ ||  
  
ramaṇāllakṣajāpena pūto bhavati kaulikaḥ |  
maṃtra putrī putratvenapyupadeśobhidhānataḥ ||  
  
kṛtvā vīravadhaṃ maṃtrī vṛthāpānaṃ guro * *? |  
japet ||  
  
anasthi prāṇisaṃghātaṃ hatvā ca narakaṃ vrajet |  
caikādaśaṃ japet ||  
  
sarpamārjāranakulamūṣamuṣṭrakharaṃ hayaṃ |  
gajādyāśca * * * * * * * * * * *   
  
validānaṃ * * * * * * * * * * *   
  
|  
go vadhe daśabhi * * * * * * * * *   
  
guruhatvā prasādena paṃcalakṣairbhaved * *? ||  
  
  
p. 193a)  
  
pramādāt patite vipre lakṣairviṃśatibhiḥ śubhiḥ |  
kṣetrādayo yathoktena mucyaṃte kilviṣāditaḥ ||  
  
brāhmaṇasya vadhelakṣaṃ kṣetriye dviguṇaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
vaiśya triguṇamuddiṣṭaṃ pādaje ca caturguṇaṃ ||  
  
arhadvauddhavadhe maṃtrī khāddhilakṣaṃ manuṃ japet |  
vabhrośca śūkarāṇāṃ ca vadhe paṃca sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
pakṣiṇāṃ hanane maṃtrī dvisahasreṇa śuddhyati |  
sarpamārjāramatsyānāṃ vadhe vedasahasrakaṃ ||  
  
devadrohād gurudrohāttriṃśatkoṭi manuṃ japet |  
niṃdate samayānāṃ ca yoginī vīrayoḥ śivaḥ ||  
  
śāstrāṇāṃ maṃtriṇāṃ strīṇāṃ sahasraṃ japamācaret |  
vāmadakṣiṇasiddhāṃte śaiva vrata dhare hate ||  
  
catuḥkoṭimitāṃ maṃtrī japan śuddhyati kilviṣāt |  
ādyādinīṃdane maṃtrī daśāvartena śuddhyati ||  
  
arghāmṛtaṃ pibet pūrvaṃ devīmutthāpayet tataḥ |  
paśupānaṃ bhavet tasya tatkṣayo lakṣato bhavet ||  
  
vīrapatnīṃ vṛthāpānaṃ vīrapatnīsnuṣe tathā |  
prāyaścittaṃ caren maṃtrī divyavīrārcanādikaṃ ||  
  
dīpanāśe pātranāśe pātrapraskhalane tathā |  
pūjayitvā mahādevīṃ japedaṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ ||  
  
ajñānādetaduddiṣṭaṃ jñānato dviguṇaṃ bhavet |  
bhagnaṃ ca sphuṭitaṃ yaṃtraṃ hṛtaṃ caureṇa vā priye ||  
  
upavāsaṃ prakurvīta dinamekamateṃdritaḥ |  
lakṣamātraṃ japed vidyāṃ homatarpaṇapūrvikāṃ ||  
  
p. 193b)  
  
sadbhaktyā ca guruṃ toṣya brāhmaṇānapi bhojayet |  
kadācillupta cihnaṃ vā sphuṭitādi vibhūṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
bhagnaṃ karoti yo martyo mṛtyustasya bhaveddhruvaṃ |  
tasmāt sa tīrtharāje vā gaṃgādi saritāṃvare ||  
  
samudre vā kṣiped devi anyathā duḥkhamāpnuyāt |  
āṃbike yo yadā maṃtrī dehadharmamupāśritaḥ ||  
  
aṃtyaṣṭistatra kartavyā tacchiṣyādyairvidhānataḥ |  
kartā nitya kriyāṃ kṛtvā paṃcaratnairviśodhayet ||  
  
pretaṃ netrādi mārgeṇa lokāṃtaravinirgataṃ |  
ākṛṣya sthāpayet prete jīvātmānaṃ guruktitaḥ ||  
  
paṃcapraṇava yogena viyadvahya nilātmakaiḥ |  
mokṣade padamuccārya cakṣurādi samuccaret ||  
  
pretanāmasamuccārya vadedāvāhayāmi ca |  
anenāvāhayet pretaṃ tatra prāṇāśca vinyaset ||  
  
aṃgaprakalpanaṃ kuryā māyayā dīrghasaṃyutā |  
pratiṣṭhāpya ghaṭaṃ maṃtrī paretaṃ snāpayet sudhīḥ ||  
  
paṃcagavyairaghoreṇa varddhinyā tvabhiṣicyataṃ |  
śuddhatoyena saṃsnāpya bhasmanāsnāpayet punaḥ ||  
  
pretaṃ dakṣiṇamūrddhānaṃ nyasedarbhāstane sudhīḥ |  
navavastrasragā lepairalaṃkṛtyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ ||  
  
abhyarcya gaṃdhapuṣpādyairmūlamaṃtreṇa sādhakaḥ |  
samyak vimānaṃ saṃkalpā mṛtakaṃ tatra vinyaset ||  
  
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇī kurvan śaṃkhabheryādi nisvanaiḥ |  
pretasthānaṃ samāviśya dakṣiṇottaramāyataṃ ||  
  
upaviśyasamāṃ bhūmiṃ tatra lājātilākṣatān |  
  
p. 194a)  
  
vikiret sarṣapo petān vimānamathavinyaset |  
saṃsthāpya tatra cityagniṃ paristīrya vilomataḥ ||  
  
pāvāṇyāsādayen maṃtrī dakṣiṇe viṣṇu devataṃ |  
praṇīta pātramāsādya saṃpūjya kusumādibhiḥ ||  
  
darbherāchādite maṃtrī vahnikoṇe pravinyaset |  
dakṣabhāge yajed devaṃ bhairavaṃ maṃḍalaṃ kramāt ||  
  
uktena vidhinā kṛtvā vahne jihvādi kalpanaṃ |  
tilataṃḍulasaṃmiśraṃ śravayeccarumuttamaṃ ||  
  
mṛtyuṃjayena maṃtreṇa śatamaṣṭottaraṃ sudhīḥ |  
sāccena caruṇāhutvā paṃcaratnarviśeṣataḥ ||  
  
juhuyānmūlamaṃtreṇa kramādāvaraṇāṃtikaṃ |  
evaṃ vilomatā homān sarvamaṃtrān gurostanau ||  
  
krameṇa vilayaṃ nītvā juhuyād vāgbhavena ca |  
hutvātha mūlamaṃtreṇa preta dehi vilomataḥ ||  
  
tatvāni vilayaṃ nītvā sarvamātma niyojayet |  
puṇyapāpe tasya juhuyān maṃtramuccaran ||  
  
tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ datvā yojayet paramaṃ pade |  
śivaśaktyātmake śuddhe punarāvṛddhi varjite ||  
  
saccitsukhamaye sākṣāt tatvātīte nirākule |  
iti saṃyojitaḥ pretaḥ śiṣyena parame pade ||  
  
saṃpūjyamalakāluṣyaṃ śastu bhāvāya kalpane |  
ājyena juhuyādvahnāvaghorāstreṇa mūlataḥ ||  
  
anulomavidhānena prāyaścittāya sādhakaḥ |  
paretadehamānena śayanaṃ parikalpayet ||  
  
vahnerdakṣiṇa digbhāge kulavṛkṣasamudbhavaiḥ |  
  
p. 194b)  
  
śaṃkubhirdakṣiṇāgraistu bilvajairvākuśaistathā |  
āstīrya śayanaṃ maṃtrī triguṇī kṛti taṃtunā ||  
  
saṃveṣṭya pūjayed gaṃdha puṣpādyairupacārakaiḥ |  
āchādyanaṃ vā vastreṇa tatra yaṃtraṃ likhet sudhīḥ ||  
  
padmaṃ trikoṇa ṣaṭkoṇa karṇikaṃ sāṣṭa patrakaṃ |  
sārddharekhaṃ tatastatra puṣpāṇyākīrya sarvataḥ ||  
  
pretaṃ dakṣiṇamūrddhānaṃ vinyasediha sādhakaḥ |  
rakṣāmaṃtreṇa saṃkalpya jvalāmālini vidyayā ||  
  
prajvālyā ghoramaṃtreṇa dahet pādādito budhaḥ |  
aghorāstreṇa maṃtreṇa maṃtrī pāśupatena vā ||  
  
yāvadbhasmī bhavatyeṣa tāvaddhomaṃ karotviha |  
stotra maṃtra japaṃ kuryat samayajñāḥ samāgatāḥ ||  
  
bhasmībhūte pare tesmin devā samyak samarcayet |  
ciṃtyagniṃ rakṣayen maṃtrī saṃprāpte saptame hani ||  
  
nirvāpaya sasāsthīni veṣṭayet nava vāsasā |  
tadbhasma niḥkṣipet kvāpi viśuddhe salilāsayet ||  
  
asthikūṭaṃ khanen maṃtrī devamātṛ gṛhe'thavā |  
svagṛhe vā nikhanyeta trisaṃdhyaṃ pūjayedidaṃ ||  
  
pūrvapūjāṃ mṛtadine pratimāsaṃ prakalpayet |  
saṃpūrṇa vatsare kuryāt mahotsava mataṃdritaḥ ||  
  
tatosti kūṭamuddhṛtya nadyāṃ vā vidhisaṃspṛśi |  
  
kenāpikīkase nāsya pratimāṃ pāduke'tha vā |  
kṛtvā saṃpūjayet maṃtrī gurubhaktiparāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
p. 195a)  
  
deśāṃtaramṛtānāṃ ca jīvatāmapi sādhakaḥ |  
darbhapūjaiḥ palāśairvā śālipiṣṭhena vā punaḥ ||  
  
dehaṃ kṛtvā yathā pūrvaṃ śeṣaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
athavā manasā kuryādekāṃte svayamāstikaḥ ||  
  
vāgbhavaṃ dīpinī jvālā mālinīti padaṃ tataḥ |  
krodha haṃsenduhet parṇān saṃpuṭatvena yojayet ||  
  
etāni tatra bījāni praṇavo jīvakeśavai |  
haṃseṃdugāṃta kuṭilavahni biṃdun bhagāśritān ||  
  
śivaśakti kṣameṃdrāṃvu vahnivātārghisaṃcayaṃ |  
jvālāmālini maṃtroyaṃ kathito maṃtrako vidaiḥ ||  
  
māyābījaṃ sphuradvaṃdvaṃ prasphūra dvitayaṃ tathā |  
ghoraghorataretyaṃte tanurūpa padaṃ vadet ||  
  
caṭapracaṭa dvitayaṃ kathitoyaṃ mahāmanuḥ |  
kaha dvaṃdva samuccārya ghātaye dvayamuccaret ||  
  
varmāṃtāstrassamuddiṣṭo varṇāmaghoramaṃtrakaḥ |  
tāriṇīṃ paśuvarṇāte kavacāstrākṣaro vadet ||  
  
manuḥ pāśupatāstroyaṃ kṣudragrahanivārakaḥ |  
paṃcātakeṃdu pārśvārṇānyamadhāṃtasamanvitān ||  
  
iṃdrārūḍhāt sudhīḥ kuryād vāmakarṇeṃdu saṃyutān |  
paṃcaratnamidaṃ proktaṃ manobhilaṣita pradam ||  
  
iti śrīvārāhītaṃtre dakṣiṇāmnāyanirvāṇapade triṃśa paṭalaḥ || 30 ||  
  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
kurukṣetre prayāge ca gaṃgāsāgarasaṃgame |  
mahākāle ca kāśyāṃ ca dīpasthānaṃ na ciṃtayet ||  
  
p. 195b)  
  
niyamaḥ puruṣe jñeyo na yoṣitsu kadācana |  
na nyāso yoṣitāṃ cātra na dhyānaṃ na ca pūjanaṃ ||  
  
kevalaṃ japamātreṇa maṃtrāt siddhyaṃti yoṣitāṃ |  
puraścaraṇa kāle ca paraśaktiṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
dīkṣito vastrapuṣpādyairbhojyaiḥ pāyasasaṃbhavaiḥ |  
śūnyagehe samānīya arghodakaṃ viśodhitaṃ ||  
  
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā śaktīrabhi mukhaṃ nayet |  
arghodakena sarvāstāssaṃprayokṣya vidhi pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ kuryāt sakalī karaṇaṃ tataḥ |  
athāṣṭa kanyakā vakṣye devī rūpadharāyataḥ ||  
  
brāhmaṇī kṣatriyā vaiśyā śūdrāllakulabhūṣaṇā |  
veśyānāpita kanyā ca rajakī yoginī tathā ||  
  
viśeṣa vai dagdhā yutāḥ sarvaṣṭavaśubhāṃganāḥ |  
aṣṭakanyārūpabhedaṃ vilokyāmarṣaceṣṭitaṃ ||  
  
brāhmaṇyādyaṣṭaśaktīnāṃ nāmabhiḥ kṛtasaṃjñakāḥ |  
gaurakṛṣṇādikaṃ rūpaṃ saumyatvaṃ ca guṇādikaṃ ||  
  
āsanaṃ prathamaṃ datvā svāgataṃ ca vadet punaḥ |  
arghyapādyaṃ ca pānīyaṃ madhuparkaṃ jalaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
snāpayed gaṃdhapuṣpābhiḥ keśasaṃskāramācaret |  
dhūpayitvā tataḥ keśaṃ kauśeyaṃ vinivedayet ||  
  
tataḥ snānottare pīṭhamāstīrya pādukā dvayaṃ |  
datvā tatra samāsīnāṃ nānālaṃkārabhūṣaṇaiḥ ||  
  
bhūṣayitvānulepaṃ ca gaṃdhamālyaṃ nivedayet |  
tāṃ tāṃ śaktiṃ samāvāhya mūrddhni tāsāṃ samānayet ||  
  
p. 196a)  
  
bhojyamaṃḍapamadhye tu svarṇapātre suśobhane |  
cavyaṃ coṣyaṃ lehyapeyaṃ bhojyaṃ caiva hi bhakṣakaṃ ||  
  
adīkṣitā yadā syustu tadā māyā nivedayet |  
tatrāsāṃsavyakarṇenu tataḥ stotraṃ samācaret ||  
  
mātardevi namaste'stu brahmaputri dhare'naghe |  
kṛpayā haravighnaṃ me maṃtrasiddhiṃ prayacha me ||  
  
māheśi varade devi paramānandarūpiṇī |  
kṛpayā haravighnaṃ me maṃtrasiddhiṃ prayacha me ||  
  
kaumāri sarvavighneśi kumārakrīḍane vane |  
kṛpayā haravighnaṃ me maṃtrasiddhiṃ prayacha me ||  
  
viṣṇurūpa dhare devi vinatāsutavāhini |  
kṛpayā haravighnaṃ me maṃtrasiddhiṃ prayacha me ||  
  
vārāhi varade devi daṃṣṭroddhṛta vasuṃdhare |  
kṛpayā haravighnaṃ me maṃtrasiddhiṃ prayacha me ||  
  
śakrarūpadhare devi śakrādi surapūjite |  
kṛpayā haravighnaṃ me maṃtra siddhiṃ prayacha me ||  
  
cāmuṇḍe muṃḍamālā sṛk carcite vighnanāśini |  
kṛpayā haravighnaṃ me maṃtrasiddhiṃ prayacha me ||  
  
mahālakṣmi mahāmokṣa kṣobhasaṃtāpanāśini |  
kṛpayā haravighnaṃ me maṃtrasiddhiṃ prayacha me ||  
  
miti mātṛmaye devi miti mātṛ vahiḥ kṛte |  
eke vahutare devi viśvarūpe namo'stute ||  
  
etat stotraṃ paṭhed yastu maṃtrāraṃbheṣu saṃyutaḥ |  
vidagdhāṃ vā samālokya tasya vighnaṃ na jāyate ||  
  
yadi krīḍāparāstāstu bhojane tadgṛhādvahiḥ |  
sthitaḥ stotraṃ paṭhet tāvad yāvat tṛptiḥ prajāyate ||  
  
p. 196b)  
  
ācamya mukhavāsādi tāṃbūlaṃ ca nivedayet |  
tato dadyāt punarmālyaṃ caṃdanaṃ paṃktitaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
visṛjya pradakṣiṇī kṛtya varaṃ prārthya sukhī bhavet |  
jyoti paśyati sarvatra śarīraṃ vā prakāśa yuk ||  
  
nijaṃ śarīramathavā devatā mayameva hi |  
krūrakarmasu deveśi karma kṛtvā yathāvidhi ||  
  
tailātyaktaḥ punaḥ snātaḥ sāṃgāṃ sāvaraṇāṃ budhaḥ |  
abhyarcya devatāsiṣṭāmātmarakṣārthamaṃtrike ||  
  
japen maṃtraṃ praśannātmā sahasraṃ sāṣṭakaṃ priye |  
māṃ rakṣa rakṣa cetyuktā praṇamya visṛjecchive ||  
  
anyaiḥ suhṛdbhiḥ susnigdhairātmarakṣāṃ tu kārayet |  
mṛtyuṃjayādibhirdevi prayogāstreṇa cāṇunā ||  
  
japahomārcanādyaiśca brāhmaṇārādhanādibhiḥ |  
prayogāṃte tathā cakra pūjāṃ maṃtrī samācaret ||  
  
ekalakṣaṃ japenmaṃtrī dhyāna nyāsa samanvitaḥ |  
prayogādoṣaśāṃtyarthamātmarakṣārthameva ca ||  
  
na cenna phalamāpnoti devatā śāpamāpnuyāt |  
praṇavādyā muktikarī śrībījādyādhanāgame ||  
  
hṛllekhādyā mahāsiddhikarī sarvavaśaṃkarī |  
vāgbhavādyā caradvidyāṃ kāmādyā jamaraṃjinī ||  
  
ūrddhadṛṣṭirjapecchāṃntā vadho dṛṣṭistu mohane |  
samadṛṣṭisnaṃpane ca pārśvato darśana kramāt ||  
  
virodhe ca samuccāṭa māraṇe sūrya darśanaḥ |  
  
p. 197a)  
  
vidyārthaṃ jalamadhyastho bhānumaṃḍaladarśanāt |  
bhrūmadhya darśanād devi sarvatraśubhakarmaṇi ||  
  
nityaṃ japaṃ kare kuryān na prayoge kadācana |  
prayoge vihitā mālā tat tat karmānurūpataḥ ||  
  
homamudrā trayaṃ proktaṃ sṛṃgīhaṃsī ca śūkarī |  
śūkarī karasaṃkocī mṛgīmuktakaniṣṭhikā ||  
  
haṃsī syāt tarjanī muktā tridhā mudrā prakīrtitā |  
śāṃtike pauṣṭike caiva māraṇoccāṭane tathā ||  
  
vidveṣe staṃbhane caiva vaśye ca parameśvari |  
śāṃtike ca mṛgī jñeyā haṃsī pauṣṭika karmaṇi ||  
  
abhicāre śūkarī syād vidveṣoccāṭanādiṣu |  
na devāḥ pratigṛhnaṃti mudrāhīnāmathāhutiṃ ||  
  
mudrāhīnāṃ tu yo mohāddhottumichati maṃdadhīḥ |  
vaśyaśāṃtyoḥ svarṇapātraṃ mṛtpātraṃ staṃbhane mataṃ ||  
  
vidveṣe ṣādiraṃ pātramuccāṭe lauhanirmitaṃ |  
māraṇe kukkuṭāṃḍaṃ syāt pātrāṇī mani tarpaṇe ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
bhagavan sarvatatvajño lokānugrahakāraka |  
kenopāyena deveśa dehaśuddhiḥ prajāyate ||  
  
tanme kathaya sarvajña yadi snehosti māṃ prati |  
  
īśvara uvāca ||  
  
deveśi bhakti surabhe auṣadhaṃ kathayāmi te |  
na prakāśyamidaṃ kvāpi triṣu lokeṣu durlabhaṃ ||  
  
kumārīṃ chatradhārīṃ ca rājamāṣeṇa peṣayet |  
ekavarṇagavākṣīrai raṃbhābījena meva ca ||  
  
p. 197b)  
  
prabhāte lepayedaṃgaṃ vaśyasiddhiḥ prajāyate |  
śvetāparājitā mūlaṃ sadhunā saha bhakṣayet ||  
  
śvetakuṣṭavināśaṃ ca lepayitvā raverdine |  
aśokasya phalaṃ puṣpaṃ meraṃḍasya phalaissaha ||  
  
nimaṃtrayet pūrvadine bhakṣayedaparehani |  
vātāṃjīrṇa bhave rogastasya dehena jāyate ||  
  
dvādaśādhāramādāya tadgraṃthiṃ paribhedayet |  
tasmājjihvāgramānīya dīpākāraṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
lakṣamekamidaṃ japtvā sarvapāpāni nirdahet |  
tataścarācaraṃ sarvaṃ jñātvā sarvajñatāṃ labhet ||  
  
tato japet mahāvidyāṃ vākyatirjāyate naraḥ |  
vādesadasiyā vākya staṃbhinī prativādinī ||  
  
tatpaṃḍita ghaṭāṭopa tato pratihata prabhaḥ |  
sa tarkapadavākyārtha śabdālaṃkārasāravit ||  
  
jihvāyāṃ nyasanā deva mukopi sukavirbhavet |  
sukumāratarasphāra śabdālaṃkārasāravit ||  
  
tato * *? samudrosmi mālā tulyai rūpanyaset |  
padaguptairmahākāvyaṃ varakārapitā bhavet ||  
  
avyāhatāmati śāstre vijayo vākyateriva |  
vālakasya tu jihvāyāṃ tridinābhyaṃtare likhet ||  
  
suvarṇamayyālekhinyāmadhunā śveta durvayā |  
vāgbhavādyāṃ likhed vidyāṃ samārādhya prajapya ca ||  
  
sa eva paṇḍitaḥ śrīmān na tu mūrkhaḥ kadācana |  
  
p. 198a)  
  
etad vāgīśvarī vidyāṃ vāriśasyāpi mūrddhani |  
karaṃ datvā japed vidyāṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ naraḥ ||  
  
sopi ślokānaśeṣāstu karoti vākya tiryathā |  
jihvāyāṃ bhāvayed yastu tāriṇī dīpasannibhāṃ ||  
  
vṛhaspati samastasya kavitā śukranirjitā |  
brāhme muhūrte cosyāya kṛtā vaśyaḥ sasaṃyutaḥ ||  
  
jihvāyā bhāvayan vidyāṃ tato rūpāṃ japet sudhīḥ |  
amṛtasaṃdinī tasya vāṇī sarvavidhā bhavet ||  
  
prātarvidyāṃ vibhāvyaiva jihvāyāṃ dīparūpiṇī |  
mātṛkāṃ sahitāṃ vidyāṃ trirāvartya jalaṃ pibet ||  
  
jalapānavidhānena mukopi sūkavirbhavet |  
jihvāyāṃ ciṃtanā deva trikālajño bhaven naraḥ ||  
  
yastu vidyāmabhedena ciṃtayet sādhakottamaḥ |  
jīvanmukto vimuktaśca aṃte sopi bhaveddhruvaṃ ||  
  
madhunā tarpaṇa devyāssarvakāmaphalapradaṃ |  
aṣṭasiddhikaraṃ sākṣāt mahāpātakanāśanaṃ ||  
  
haviṣyāśī muktakeśo japedayutamādarāt |  
gadyapadya mayī vāṇī tasya sarvavidhā bhavet ||  
  
śatābhijaptamātreṇa rocanā tilakaṃ naraḥ |  
kṛtvā paśyati yaṃ maṃtrī taṃ kuryād dāsavad vaśaṃ ||  
  
puṣkariṇyāṃ jale gāḍhe yaṣṭikāṣṭhaṃ tamo grahe |  
daṃtenānīyatattūrṇaṃ kīlakaṃ tena kārayet ||  
  
te naiva madhunoktena padminī patramātrake |  
likhed vajrāvalī madhye mūlamaṃtraṃ tu siddhidaṃ ||  
  
p. 198b)  
  
amukaṃ kurumāyāṃte vadet sādhaka sattamaḥ |  
tatkuṃḍa caturasre tu niḥkṣipya juhuyād dadhi ||  
  
sahasraṃ kṣīranīrakta padmāṃ māṃ lohita tviṣaṃ |  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuccārya padme yugalameva ca ||  
  
mahāpadme padaṃ brūyāt padmāvati padaṃ tataḥ |  
hu& hu& svāheti maṃtreṇa yathāpūrvaṃ valiṃ haret ||  
  
evaṃ yaḥ kurute karma sasyādruta kaviddhruvaṃ |  
arddharātre tato nityaṃ baliṃ dadyāccatuḥ paṭhe ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya hṛllekhāṃ ca tataḥ paraṃ |  
ekajaṭe padāṃte tu mahāśabdamudīrayet ||  
  
yakṣādi padamābhāṣya mataye ca tato mama |  
upanīta padaṃ coktvādvaliṃ gṛhneti ṭhadvidhā ||  
  
gṛhnāpaya dvidhāṭhoktā mama sarva padaṃ tataḥ |  
śāṃtiṃ kuru padaṃ caiva paravidyā manaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
dvidhā kṛtvetiṭha brūyātruṭa chiṃdhī ca tadvidhā |  
māyā svāheti maṃtroyaṃ valyādau buddhisiddhidaḥ ||  
  
parasainyagrahāriṣṭa rogakṛtyāvināśanaḥ |  
prayoge valimaṃtroyaṃ prayogāt sādhayed yadi ||  
  
arddharātre gate nityaṃ valiṃ dadyāccatuḥpathe |  
parasainya grahāriṣṭa rogakṛtyāvināśanaḥ ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuccārya cogratāre tataḥ paraṃ |  
vikaṭadaṃṣṭre parapakṣaṃ kṣobhaya dvayamuccaret ||  
  
khādaya dvaya paṭhamaṭhya tathā dvayaṃ dvayaṃ vadet |  
ye māṃ hiṃsi tu mudyaṃtāstathā niṃditumudyatā ||  
  
yoginī cakrasahitaistānnāśaya hū& phaṭ svāhā ||  
  
p. 199a)  
  
paravidyāmākarṣaya chedaya svāhā kapile gṛhna 2 svāhā |  
athavā madhulājābhyāṃ jihvāyāṃ vālakasya ca ||  
  
nādī chedāt tadā pūrvaṃ likheddhema śalākayā |  
mūlamaṃtraṃ likhen maṃtrī yadveṣṭo śveta durvayā ||  
  
vākyoccāraṇato vālo vāgmīdrutakavirbhavet |  
janmasaṃskārakaṃ sadyaḥ putre jāte praśasyate ||  
  
jihvāyāṃ tu likhen maṃtrī yajñadāru śalākayā |  
vāratrayaṃ tu saṃpūjya dakṣiṇe naiva pāṇinā ||  
  
maṃtramuccārya pratyekaṃ paṃktiṃ kuryāt suśobhanaṃ |  
ādau kṛtvā tu saṃskāraṃ udaṃte vilikhen manuṃ ||  
  
gaṃdha caṃdanapuṣpaiśca pūjayet tāriṇīṃ śivāṃ |  
uttarābhimukho bhūtvā sthāpayet pīṭhamuttamaṃ ||  
  
pūjayet tāriṇīṃ devīṃ nānā bhakṣaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ |  
kavirvāgbhī bhavet putrassatyavādīj iteṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
kuśamūlena madhunā likhenmaṃtraṃ prayatnataḥ |  
piturbhrātāthavā maṃtraṃ māturbhrātāthavā punaḥ ||  
  
pitā vā vilikhen maṃtraṃ nānya eva kadācana |  
atha bhrātā praśastaśca agrajaśca bhavet sadā ||  
  
tasmād devi nyasen maṃtraṃ sarvakāmaphalapradaṃ |  
mātuḥ kroḍe tu saṃsthāpya darbhā nāstīrya yatnataḥ ||  
  
śāṃtiṃ kuryād vālakasya sādhakaiḥ sahasaṃyutaḥ |  
mātuḥ savye tu karṇe ca pūrvaḥ stotraṃ samācaret ||  
  
brāhmī bhayā vacā vāsā pippalī madhusaṃyutā |  
  
p. 199b)  
  
asya prayogāt saptāhā kinnaraiḥ saha gīyate |  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
jihvā mārjanakaṃ dravyaṃ svābhi rakṣā ca kīdṛśa |  
putra rakṣā ca kiṃ deva veśma rakṣā kimauṣadhaṃ ||  
  
śrotumicchāmyahaṃ deva kathyatāṃ tadanugrahāt |  
  
īśvara uvāca ||  
  
kṛṣṇā jayaṃtī puṣpaṃ ca apāmārgasya mūlakaṃ |  
lepayitvā ca jihvāyāṃ ṣaṣṭhe ca divase sutaṃ ||  
  
rakṣā dravyaṃ ca jānīyād yajjanma divase kṛtaṃ |  
vipradārupadmamūlaśuṣkagomuṇḍameva ca ||  
  
sthāpayed dvāha deśe ca nāsti kiṃcid bhayaṃ tadā |  
jaṃbutvacaṃśimbi patraṃ jaṭānāṃ dhārayecchire ||  
  
rākṣasānāṃ bhayaṃ nāsti roga kṛtyādikaṃ tathā |  
catuḥkoṇe tu gehasya ropayitvā tu pippalaṃ ||  
  
vahiḥ saṃsthāpayed dvāre vadhniyācchāgalaṃ kapiṃ |  
raṃbhāmūlaṃ dvayaṃ rohe ṣaṣṭhe ca divase niśi ||  
  
tatraiva sthāpayet khaḍgaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ ca suśobhanaṃ |  
vṛddhāṃstriyaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya śyālaṃ vā vinayānvitaṃ ||  
  
jayaṃtyāḥ surase naiva kumāraṃ snāpayet tataḥ |  
jayaṃtī ghṛtayogena codakena ca siṃcayet ||  
  
aṣṭapatre pratiṣṭhāpya suputro matimān bhavet |  
nāgeśvarasya mūlaṃ ca tvaca mānīya yatnataḥ ||  
  
pūrṇaṃ kṛtvā ghṛtāktaṃ ca vartikāṃ kārayet tataḥ |  
dīpaṃ kṛtvā tu maṃtrajñaḥ putranāḍīṃ tu chedayet ||
